### [1] [Alternative classical Lagrangians for the Standard-Model Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06714)
*João A. A. S. Reis,Marco Schreck,Ronaldo Thibes*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper constructs alternative classical relativistic Lagrangians for point-particle analogs of the Standard-Model Extension (SME) with Lorentz violation, focusing on formulations that admit well-defined massless limits suitable for photon-like particles. It systematically handles fermionic and photonic SME coefficients using Dirac's constraint formalism, with potential applications to Lorentz-violating photon propagation in gravitational fields and links to Finsler geometry.
\n\n
本文构建了具有洛伦兹破缺的Standard-Model Extension (SME) 的点粒子经典相对论拉格朗日量的替代形式，重点在于其具有良好的无质量极限，适用于类光子粒子。文章系统处理了费米子与光子SME系数，并采用Dirac约束形式体系，结果可应用于引力场中洛伦兹破缺下的光子传播，并可能与Finsler几何相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous formulations of classical particle Lagrangians corresponding to the SME lacked well-behaved massless limits, hindering their applicability to photons. The motivation is to develop alternative Lagrangian formulations that are both relativistically covariant and possess smooth $m \\to 0$ limits, thereby enabling a consistent classical description of Lorentz-violating photons and facilitating studies of their propagation in curved spacetime.
\n\n
先前对应于SME的经典粒子拉格朗日量缺乏良好定义的无质量极限，限制了其在光子上的应用。本文旨在构建既满足相对论协变性、又具有光滑$m \\to 0$极限的替代拉格朗日形式，从而为洛伦兹破缺下的光子提供自洽的经典描述，并便于研究其在弯曲时空中的传播。

Method: The authors construct novel point-particle Lagrangians for both fermionic and photonic sectors of the SME by starting from modified dispersion relations. They employ Dirac’s theory of constrained Hamiltonian systems to consistently handle the resulting primary and secondary constraints arising from reparameterization invariance. Special attention is paid to ensuring the existence of a regular massless limit ($m = 0$) in the photon sector.
\n\n
作者从修正的色散关系出发，为SME的费米子与光子部分构建新型点粒子拉格朗日量。他们采用Dirac约束哈密顿系统理论，一致地处理由再参数化不变性所导致的初级与次级约束，并特别关注确保光子部分存在规则的无质量极限（$m = 0$）。

Result: Well-defined classical Lagrangians are obtained for various SME coefficients in both the Dirac fermion and photon sectors, all admitting consistent massless limits. The constraint analysis via Dirac’s method yields the correct number of physical degrees of freedom. These results enable a classical trajectory-based study of Lorentz-violating photons in gravitational backgrounds and suggest an underlying Finsler geometric structure for the particle dynamics.
\n\n
针对Dirac费米子和光子部分中的多种SME系数，获得了具有良好定义的经典拉格朗日量，且均具有自洽的无质量极限。通过Dirac方法进行的约束分析给出了正确的物理自由度数目。这些结果使得可在引力背景下基于经典轨迹研究洛伦兹破缺光子，并暗示粒子动力学具有潜在的Finsler几何结构。

Conclusion: The paper successfully formulates alternative classical Lagrangians for SME-inspired Lorentz violation that overcome the limitations of prior approaches by possessing well-defined massless limits. This opens new avenues for studying photon propagation under combined effects of gravity and spacetime symmetry breaking, and strengthens the connection between Lorentz-violating particle dynamics and Finsler geometry.
\n\n
本文成功构建了受SME启发的洛伦兹破缺替代经典拉格朗日量，克服了以往方法缺乏良好无质量极限的局限。这为研究引力与时空对称性破缺共同作用下的光子传播开辟了新途径，并加强了洛伦兹破缺粒子动力学与Finsler几何之间的联系。

Abstract: The current paper introduces classical, relativistic Lagrangians for point-particle analogs to the field theory description of the Standard-Model Extension (SME) for Lorentz violation. Lagrangians of a form alternative to those derived and studied in previous works are in the spotlight. Interestingly, they have well-defined massless limits, which makes them suitable for describing classical-particle analogs of photons subject to Lorentz violation. We first deal with different types of Dirac fermion coefficients, followed by various configurations of the SME photon sector. The Lagrangians are accompanied by constraints that we treat properly using the techniques due to Dirac. The results encountered may find application in photon propagation through gravitational fields in the presence of spacetime symmetry violation. Connections to Finsler geometry are likely to exist.

</details>


### [2] [Quantum and Thermal Fluctuations of Cherenkov Radiation from HQET](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06784)
*Joshua Lin,Bruno Scheihing-Hitschfeld*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We rederive the Frank-Tamm formula for Cherenkov radiation using quantum field theory (QFT), extending it to include all cumulants of thermal and quantum fluctuations around the classical spectrum at leading order in $1/m$, where $m$ is the particle mass. This is achieved via a calculation of the charged particle's momentum change probability using Heavy Quark Effective Theory (HQET) in weakly coupled gauge theories.
\n\n
我们使用量子场论（QFT）重新推导了切伦科夫辐射的Frank-Tamm公式，并将其推广至包含经典谱周围热涨落与量子涨落的所有累积量，这些结果在粒子质量倒数 $1/m$ 的领头阶成立。该推导通过利用Heavy Quark Effective Theory（HQET）在弱耦合规范理论中计算带电粒子的动量改变概率实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Frank-Tamm formula, a cornerstone of classical electrodynamics describing Cherenkov radiation, has not been fully reconciled with quantum field theory beyond heuristic arguments. The authors aim to provide a rigorous QFT derivation that not only recovers the classical result but also systematically incorporates quantum and thermal fluctuations, which are absent in the classical treatment.
\n\n
Frank-Tamm公式作为描述切伦科夫辐射的经典电动力学基石，尚未在量子场论（QFT）框架下得到严格推导（超越启发式论证）。作者旨在提供一个严谨的QFT推导，不仅复现经典结果，还能系统地纳入经典处理中缺失的量子涨落与热涨落。

Method: The authors compute the probability distribution for momentum transfer from a fast-moving charged particle to the electromagnetic field in a dielectric medium. Using Heavy Quark Effective Theory (HQET), they treat the particle as heavy ($m \\to \\infty$) and expand observables in powers of $1/m$. In weakly coupled gauge theories, this allows a perturbative calculation of the momentum change probability, whose generating functional yields all cumulants of radiation-induced fluctuations. The classical Frank-Tamm spectrum emerges as the first cumulant, while higher cumulants encode quantum and thermal corrections.
\n\n
作者计算了高速带电粒子在介质中向电磁场传递动量的概率分布。他们利用Heavy Quark Effective Theory（HQET），将粒子视为重粒子（$m \\to \\infty$），并将可观测量按 $1/m$ 展开。在弱耦合规范理论中，这允许对动量改变概率进行微扰计算，其生成泛函可给出辐射诱导涨落的所有累积量。经典Frank-Tamm谱作为第一累积量出现，而高阶累积量则编码了量子与热修正。

Result: The leading-order term in the $1/m$ expansion reproduces the Frank-Tamm formula exactly. Furthermore, the formalism provides explicit expressions for all higher-order cumulants, which describe deviations from the classical spectrum due to quantum vacuum fluctuations and finite-temperature effects. These corrections are suppressed by powers of $1/m$ and are calculable within the HQET framework.
\n\n
在 $1/m$ 展开的领头阶项精确复现了Frank-Tamm公式。此外，该形式体系给出了所有高阶累积量的显式表达式，这些累积量描述了由于量子真空涨落和有限温度效应导致的经典谱偏差。这些修正被 $1/m$ 的幂次所压低，并可在HQET框架内计算。

Conclusion: Cherenkov radiation, traditionally viewed as a purely classical phenomenon, admits a complete description within quantum field theory. The classical Frank-Tamm spectrum arises as the mean of a broader probability distribution whose fluctuations—both quantum and thermal—are systematically captured by a $1/m$ expansion using Heavy Quark Effective Theory. This bridges classical electrodynamics and quantum field theory in a nontrivial radiative process.
\n\n
传统上被视为纯经典现象的切伦科夫辐射，可在量子场论中获得完整描述。经典Frank-Tamm谱作为更广义概率分布的均值出现，其涨落（包括量子与热涨落）可通过Heavy Quark Effective Theory中的 $1/m$ 展开系统地刻画。这在非平凡的辐射过程中架起了经典电动力学与量子场论之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Charged particles travelling faster than the speed of light in the medium in which they propagate emit Cherenkov radiation. The formula for the spectrum of this radiation as a function of frequency, known as the Frank-Tamm formula, first derived almost 90 years ago, follows purely from classical electromagnetism. In this work, we demonstrate how this result also follows from a short quantum field theory calculation, which in addition to it contains all of the cumulants of thermal and quantum fluctuations around the classical radiation spectrum at leading order in the inverse of the particle's mass. All of these results follow from the particle's momentum change probability, which we calculate for weakly coupled gauge theories using the tools of Heavy Quark Effective theory.

</details>


### [3] [The meV frontier of neutrinoless double beta decay in the JUNO era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06787)
*J. T. Penedo,S. T. Petcov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper updates the conditions under which the effective Majorana mass $|\langle m \rangle|$ in neutrinoless double beta decay exceeds specific thresholds ($10^{-3}$ eV or $5\times10^{-3}$ eV) for normal ordering (NO) of neutrino masses, incorporating the latest JUNO constraints on solar oscillation parameters. It considers both generic scenarios and those with restricted Majorana phases motivated by flavour and generalized CP symmetries.
\n\n
本文结合JUNO实验对太阳中微子振荡参数的最新约束，更新了在正常质量序（NO）下，无中微子双贝塔衰变的有效Majorana质量 $|\\langle m \\rangle|$ 超过特定阈值（$10^{-3}$ eV 或 $5\\times10^{-3}$ eV）的条件。文章既分析了一般情形，也探讨了由味对称性（flavour symmetry）和广义CP对称性（generalised CP symmetries）所预言的、Majorana相位受限的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The observation of neutrinoless double beta decay would confirm lepton number violation and the Majorana nature of neutrinos. However, in the standard 3-flavour framework with normal mass ordering, the effective Majorana mass $|\langle m \rangle|$ can be highly suppressed, potentially below the sensitivity of near-future experiments. The recent JUNO results have significantly improved the precision of solar neutrino oscillation parameters ($\Delta m_{21}^2$, $\theta_{12}$), which directly impact the predicted range of $|\langle m \rangle|$. This motivates a reassessment of the guaranteed lower bounds on $|\langle m \rangle|_\text{NO}$, especially in light of theoretical models that predict specific values for the Majorana CP phases.
\n\n
观测到无中微子双贝塔衰变将证实轻子数破坏和中微子的Majorana本质。然而，在标准三味框架下，若中微子质量谱为正常序（NO），有效Majorana质量 $|\\langle m \\rangle|$ 可能被严重压低，甚至低于近期实验的灵敏度。最近的JUNO实验结果显著提高了太阳中微子振荡参数（$\\Delta m_{21}^2$, $\\theta_{12}$）的精度，而这些参数直接影响 $|\\langle m \\rangle|$ 的预言范围。这促使我们重新评估 $|\\langle m \\rangle|_\\text{NO}$ 的保证下限，特别是考虑到那些对Majorana CP相位有特定预言的理论模型（如结合了味对称性和广义CP对称性的模型）。

Method: The authors perform a global analysis of the effective Majorana mass $|\langle m \rangle| = |\sum_i U_{ei}^2 m_i|$, where $U_{ei}$ are elements of the PMNS matrix and $m_i$ are the neutrino masses. They incorporate the latest pre-JUNO and post-JUNO global fit data for neutrino oscillation parameters, focusing on the improved constraints for $\Delta m_{21}^2$ and $\theta_{12}$. The analysis is conducted for normal ordering, scanning over the unknown parameters: the lightest neutrino mass $m_{\text{lightest}}$, the Dirac CP phase $\delta$, and the two Majorana phases $\alpha_{21}, \alpha_{31}$. They derive the minimum possible value of $|\langle m \rangle|_\text{NO}$ as a function of these inputs. Furthermore, they specialize their analysis to cases where the Majorana phases are constrained to CP-conserving values ($0, \pi$) or include at least one CP-violating value, as predicted by certain flavour symmetry models.
\n\n
作者对有效Majorana质量 $|\\langle m \\rangle| = |\\sum_i U_{ei}^2 m_i|$ 进行了全局分析，其中 $U_{ei}$ 是PMNS矩阵元，$m_i$ 是中微子质量。他们纳入了JUNO实验前后最新的中微子振荡参数全局拟合数据，重点关注 $\\Delta m_{21}^2$ 和 $\\theta_{12}$ 约束的改善。分析在正常质量序下进行，扫描未知参数：最轻中微子质量 $m_{\\text{lightest}}$、Dirac CP相位 $\\delta$ 以及两个Majorana相位 $\\alpha_{21}, \\alpha_{31}$。他们推导出 $|\\langle m \\rangle|_\\text{NO}$ 作为这些输入参数函数的最小可能值。此外，他们还专门分析了Majorana相位被限制为CP守恒值（$0, \\pi$）或至少包含一个CP破坏值的情形，这些情形由某些味对称性模型所预言。

Result: Using the updated JUNO-informed oscillation parameters, the paper establishes new, more robust conditions for a guaranteed non-zero signal in neutrinoless double beta decay experiments. Specifically, it finds that for normal ordering, $|\langle m \rangle|_\text{NO}$ is guaranteed to be above $10^{-3}$ eV if the lightest neutrino mass $m_{\text{lightest}} \gtrsim 3.5$ meV, and above $5\times10^{-3}$ eV if $m_{\text{lightest}} \gtrsim 14$ meV. In scenarios with CP-conserving Majorana phases, these thresholds are lowered to $m_{\text{lightest}} \gtrsim 2.5$ meV and $m_{\text{lightest}} \gtrsim 9$ meV, respectively. The presence of at least one CP-violating Majorana phase generally leads to a higher guaranteed minimum for $|\langle m \rangle|$ compared to the fully CP-conserving case.
\n\n
利用JUNO实验更新后的振荡参数，本文为无中微子双贝塔衰变实验中保证存在非零信号建立了新的、更稳健的条件。具体而言，对于正常质量序，若最轻中微子质量 $m_{\\text{lightest}} \\gtrsim 3.5$ meV，则 $|\\langle m \\rangle|_\\text{NO}$ 必然高于 $10^{-3}$ eV；若 $m_{\\text{lightest}} \\gtrsim 14$ meV，则必然高于 $5\\times10^{-3}$ eV。在Majorana相位为CP守恒的情形下，这些阈值分别降低至 $m_{\\text{lightest}} \\gtrsim 2.5$ meV 和 $m_{\\text{lightest}} \\gtrsim 9$ meV。与完全CP守恒的情形相比，至少存在一个CP破坏的Majorana相位通常会导致 $|\\langle m \\rangle|$ 的保证最小值更高。

Conclusion: The improved precision on solar neutrino oscillation parameters from JUNO tightens the predictions for the effective Majorana mass in the normal ordering scenario. This work provides updated, experimentally relevant benchmarks for the lightest neutrino mass that would guarantee a detectable signal in next-generation neutrinoless double beta decay experiments. The analysis also highlights the interplay between fundamental neutrino properties (mass ordering, absolute mass scale, CP phases) and the predictions of top-down theoretical models based on flavour and CP symmetries, offering a clearer pathway for interpreting future experimental results.
\n\n
JUNO实验对太阳中微子振荡参数精度的提升，收紧了正常质量序下有效Majorana质量的预言。本工作为最轻中微子质量提供了更新的、与实验相关的基准值，该基准值能保证在下一代无中微子双贝塔衰变实验中探测到信号。该分析还强调了基本中微子性质（质量序、绝对质量标度、CP相位）与基于味对称性和CP对称性的自上而下理论模型预言之间的相互关联，为解读未来的实验结果提供了更清晰的路径。

Abstract: Observing neutrinoless double beta decay would establish lepton number violation and the Majorana nature of neutrinos. Within the standard 3-flavour paradigm, the rate of this process is controlled by the effective Majorana mass $|\langle m \rangle|$, which may be severely suppressed if the neutrino mass spectrum presents normal ordering. Taking into account the first JUNO results, which significantly reduce the uncertainties on solar neutrino oscillation parameters, we provide updated conditions under which $|\langle m \rangle|_\text{NO}$ is guaranteed to exceed the $10^{-3}$ eV ($5\times 10^{-3}$ eV) threshold. We analyse both the generic case, as well as scenarios where the two Majorana phases either take CP conserving values, or at least one of them takes a CP-violating value, that are in line with predictive schemes combining flavour and generalised CP symmetries.

</details>


### [4] [Lepton Mixing from a Lattice Flavon Model: A Two-Branch Octant-delta Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06934)
*Vernon Barger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper extends the single-flavon $B$-lattice Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework—originally applied to quark masses and CKM mixing—to the lepton sector. It successfully reproduces charged-lepton mass hierarchies and a normal-ordered neutrino spectrum using the same expansion parameter $ε \equiv 1/B \simeq 0.19$. Large neutrino mixing angles arise from an approximate mu-tau symmetry, broken at $\mathcal{O}(ε)$ to yield a nonzero reactor angle and CP-violating phase. The resulting PMNS matrix predicts two distinct solutions in the $(θ_{23}, δ)$ plane, with a theoretical preference for the lower octant, and a nearly branch-independent Jarlskog invariant $J_{\rm CP} \simeq -0.027$.
\n\n
本文将单flavon的$B$-lattice Froggatt-Nielsen（FN）框架——最初用于夸克质量和CKM混合——推广至轻子领域。利用相同的展开参数$ε \equiv 1/B \simeq 0.19$，成功复现了带电轻子质量层级和正序中微子谱。大中微子混合角源于近似的mu-tau对称性，该对称性在$\mathcal{O}(ε)$阶被破缺，从而产生非零的反应堆角和CP破坏相位。所得PMNS矩阵在$(θ_{23}, δ)$平面上预言了两个不同解，理论偏好下八分圆解，且Jarlskog不变量$J_{\rm CP} \simeq -0.027$几乎与分支无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to unify the description of fermion mass hierarchies and mixing patterns across both quark and lepton sectors within a minimal flavor model. The original single-flavon $B$-lattice FN framework successfully explained quark masses and CKM mixing using a discrete scaling symmetry with base $B$, yielding $ε = 1/B \simeq 0.19$. Extending this to leptons tests whether the same symmetry and flavon structure can simultaneously account for charged-lepton masses, neutrino mass ordering, and the large mixing observed in the PMNS matrix—particularly without introducing additional flavons or symmetries beyond a controlled mu-tau symmetry breaking.
\n\n
动机在于通过一个极简味模型统一描述夸克与轻子领域的费米子质量层级和混合模式。原始的单flavon $B$-lattice FN框架利用以$B$为底的离散标度对称性（给出$ε = 1/B \simeq 0.19$），成功解释了夸克质量和CKM混合。将其推广至轻子领域，旨在检验相同的对称性和flavon结构是否能同时解释带电轻子质量、中微子质量顺序以及PMNS矩阵中观测到的大混合——尤其是无需引入额外的flavon或超出可控mu-tau对称性破缺的新对称性。

Method: The authors extend the single-flavon $B$-lattice FN mechanism to the lepton sector by assigning appropriate $B$-charges to lepton doublets and singlets, generating hierarchical Yukawa couplings as powers of $ε = 1/B$. Neutrino masses are assumed to arise via the seesaw mechanism, with the same flavon controlling both charged-lepton and neutrino Yukawa textures. An approximate mu-tau symmetry is imposed on the neutrino sector, broken only at $\mathcal{O}(ε)$ to generate the observed nonzero $θ_{13}$ and Dirac CP phase $δ$. The PMNS matrix is factorized as $U_{\rm PMNS} = U_e^\dagger U_ν$, where $U_ν$ is near-tribimaximal and $U_e$ arises from small rotations in the charged-lepton sector. Crucially, because both sectors originate from the same flavon, their phases are naturally aligned, reducing the number of free parameters and enabling predictive correlations between $θ_{23}$ and $δ$.
\n\n
作者通过为轻子二重态和单态分配适当的$B$-荷，将单flavon $B$-lattice FN机制推广至轻子领域，从而生成以$ε = 1/B$为幂次的层级Yukawa耦合。中微子质量假定通过seesaw机制产生，且带电轻子与中微子Yukawa结构由同一flavon控制。在中微子领域施加近似的mu-tau对称性，并仅在$\mathcal{O}(ε)$阶破缺，以生成观测到的非零$θ_{13}$和Dirac CP相位$δ$。PMNS矩阵被分解为$U_{\rm PMNS} = U_e^\dagger U_ν$，其中$U_ν$接近tribimaximal形式，而$U_e$源于带电轻子领域的小旋转。关键在于，由于两个领域源自同一flavon，其相位自然对齐，减少了自由参数数量，并在$θ_{23}$与$δ$之间建立了可预测的关联。

Result: The model yields a normal-ordered neutrino mass spectrum and correctly reproduces the charged-lepton mass ratios. It predicts two discrete solutions in the $(θ_{23}, δ)$ plane: (i) a lower-octant solution with $θ_{23} \approx 43^\circ$, $δ \approx 286^\circ$, and (ii) an upper-octant solution with $θ_{23} \approx 46^\circ$, $δ \approx 304^\circ$. A theoretical prior favors the lower octant at approximately 4:1 odds. Both branches give nearly identical Jarlskog invariants, $J_{\rm CP} \simeq -0.027$, implying similar magnitudes of CP violation. The distinction between the two solutions requires high-precision measurements of $θ_{23}$ and $δ$ from next-generation experiments like DUNE, Hyper-Kamiokande, IceCube, and JUNO.
\n\n
该模型得到正序中微子质量谱，并正确复现带电轻子质量比。它在$(θ_{23}, δ)$平面上预言了两个离散解：(i) 下八分圆解，$θ_{23} \approx 43^\circ$，$δ \approx 286^\circ$；(ii) 上八分圆解，$θ_{23} \approx 46^\circ$，$δ \approx 304^\circ$。理论先验以约4:1的概率偏好下八分圆解。两个分支给出几乎相同的Jarlskog不变量$J_{\rm CP} \simeq -0.027$，意味着CP破坏幅度相近。区分这两个解需要DUNE、Hyper-Kamiokande、IceCube和JUNO等下一代实验对$θ_{23}$和$δ$进行高精度测量。

Conclusion: The single-flavon $B$-lattice FN framework provides a unified, predictive, and minimally extended description of both quark and lepton flavor structures. Its success in the lepton sector—reproducing mass hierarchies, normal neutrino ordering, large mixing, and testable correlations between $θ_{23}$ and $δ$—strengthens its viability as a fundamental flavor symmetry. The two-branch prediction offers a falsifiable signature: future precision measurements of the atmospheric mixing angle and CP phase will either confirm one branch or rule out the entire framework if neither solution matches data.
\n\n
单flavon $B$-lattice FN框架为夸克与轻子味结构提供了一个统一、可预测且极简扩展的描述。其在轻子领域的成功——复现质量层级、正序中微子谱、大混合以及$θ_{23}$与$δ$之间的可检验关联——增强了其作为基本味对称性的可行性。该模型的双分支预言提供了一个可证伪的特征：未来对大气混合角和CP相位的高精度测量将确认其中一个分支，或在数据与两个解均不符时排除整个框架。

Abstract: We extend the single-flavon $B$-lattice Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework -- previously successful for quark masses and Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) mixing -- to the lepton sector. The same $B$-lattice power structure ($ε\equiv 1/B\simeq 0.19$) generates charged-lepton mass hierarchies and a normal-ordered neutrino spectrum; large neutrino mixing angles require an additional approximate mu-tau symmetry, broken at $\mathcal{O}(ε)$ to generate a nonzero reactor angle and CP-violating phase.
  The Pontecorvo-Maki-Nakagawa-Sakata (PMNS) matrix factorizes as $U_{\rm PMNS}=U_e^\dagger U_ν$, with near-tribimaximal $U_ν$ corrected by small charged-lepton rotations whose phases are naturally aligned by the single-flavon origin of the Yukawa textures. This alignment produces a two-branch prediction in the $(θ_{23},δ)$ plane: a lower-octant solution with $θ_{23}\approx 43^\circ$, $δ\approx 286^\circ$, and an upper-octant solution with $θ_{23}\approx 46^\circ$, $δ\approx 304^\circ$. The lower octant is favored by a $\sim\!4{:}1$ theoretical prior. The Jarlskog invariant $J_{\rm CP}\simeq -0.027$ is nearly branch-independent; only precision measurements of the atmospheric octant and Dirac phase at DUNE, Hyper-Kamiokande, IceCube, and JUNO can distinguish the two solutions.

</details>


### [5] [Vacuum Birefringence, Ellipticity, and the Anomalous Magnetic Moment of a Photon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07010)
*Sree Ram Valluri,Farrukh Chishtie,Wieslaw J. Mielniczuk*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates photon propagation in ultra-strong magnetic fields near the Schwinger critical field $B_{\rm cr}$, demonstrating that the photon Hamiltonian's expectation value is convex in $B$ and that the photon's anomalous magnetic moment $μ_γ$ increases monotonically with $B$ up to $30\,B_{\rm cr}$. It links $μ_γ$ to vacuum birefringence and polarization observables, offering testable predictions for experiments like ATLAS, IXPE, and PVLAS.
\n\n
本文研究了在接近Schwinger临界磁场 $B_{\rm cr}$ 的超强磁场中光子的传播，证明了光子哈密顿量的期望值是磁场 $B$ 的凸函数，且光子的反常磁矩 $μ_γ$ 在 $B$ 从0到 $30\,B_{\rm cr}$ 范围内单调不减。文章将 $μ_γ$ 与真空双折射及偏振可观测量联系起来，并为ATLAS、IXPE和PVLAS等实验提供了可检验的预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand quantum electrodynamics (QED) effects in extreme magnetic fields, such as those near magnetars, where non-linear QED phenomena like vacuum birefringence and light-by-light scattering become significant. Recent high-precision observations (e.g., IXPE polarimetry and ATLAS light-by-light scattering) demand precise theoretical predictions linking fundamental quantities like the photon anomalous magnetic moment $μ_γ$ to measurable polarization signals.
\n\n
动机源于理解极端磁场（如磁星附近）中量子电动力学（QED）效应的需求，其中真空双折射和光-光散射等非线性QED现象变得显著。近期高精度观测（如IXPE偏振测量和ATLAS光-光散射）要求精确的理论预言，将光子反常磁矩 $μ_γ$ 等基本量与可测偏振信号联系起来。

Method: The authors employ one-loop QED calculations in a strong external magnetic field to compute the effective Hamiltonian for photon modes perpendicular to the field. They analyze the convexity of the Hamiltonian’s expectation value and derive the photon anomalous magnetic moment $μ_γ$ as a function of $B$. They then connect $μ_γ$ to vacuum birefringence via the difference in refractive indices for orthogonal polarizations, and relate these to observable ellipticity and polarization degree. Analytical results are validated through numerical verification.
\n\n
作者采用强外磁场中的一圈QED计算，求解垂直于磁场方向的光子模式的有效哈密顿量。他们分析了哈密顿量期望值的凸性，并推导出光子反常磁矩 $μ_γ$ 作为磁场 $B$ 的函数。随后，他们通过正交偏振模式折射率之差将 $μ_γ$ 与真空双折射联系起来，并进一步关联到可观测的椭偏率和偏振度。解析结果通过数值验证得到确认。

Result: The expectation value of the photon Hamiltonian for the perpendicular mode is proven to be a convex function of $B$. The photon anomalous magnetic moment $μ_γ$ is shown to be non-decreasing for $0 \leq B \leq 30\,B_{\rm cr}$, with $μ_γ(B=30\,B_{\rm cr}) \approx \\frac{8}{3} μ_γ(B=\\frac{1}{2}B_{\rm cr})$. New theoretical links are established between $μ_γ$, vacuum birefringence, and directly measurable polarization observables such as ellipticity and polarization degree. Numerical checks confirm analytical predictions with high precision.
\n\n
垂直模式下光子哈密顿量的期望值被证明是 $B$ 的凸函数。光子反常磁矩 $μ_γ$ 在 $0 \leq B \leq 30\,B_{\rm cr}$ 范围内被证明为非减函数，且满足 $μ_γ(B=30\,B_{\rm cr}) \approx \\frac{8}{3} μ_γ(B=\\frac{1}{2}B_{\rm cr})$。文章建立了 $μ_γ$、真空双折射与椭偏率、偏振度等直接可测偏振观测量之间的新理论联系。数值检验以高精度确认了解析预言。

Conclusion: The study provides a rigorous QED-based framework connecting the photon anomalous magnetic moment to vacuum birefringence and polarization observables in ultra-strong magnetic fields. This bridges theoretical predictions with current and future high-sensitivity experiments (ATLAS, IXPE, PVLAS), offering concrete signatures for testing non-linear QED in extreme astrophysical and laboratory environments.
\n\n
本研究提供了一个基于QED的严格框架，将光子反常磁矩与超强磁场中的真空双折射及偏振观测量联系起来。这架起了理论预言与当前及未来高灵敏度实验（ATLAS、IXPE、PVLAS）之间的桥梁，为在极端天体物理和实验室环境中检验非线性QED提供了明确的信号。

Abstract: We study photon propagation in a strong magnetic field $B\sim B_{\rm{cr}}$, where $B_{\rm cr}= \frac{m^2}{e} \simeq 4.4 \times 10^{13}$ Gauss is the Schwinger critical field. We show that the expected value of the Hamiltonian of a quantized photon for a perpendicular mode is a convex function of the magnetic field $B$. We find that the anomalous magnetic moment of a photon in the one-loop approximation is a non-decreasing function of the magnetic field $B$ in the range $0\leq B \leq 30 \, B_{\rm cr}$. We find that the anomalous magnetic moment $μ_γ$ of a photon for $B=30\, B_{\rm cr}$ is $\sim 8/3$ of the anomalous magnetic moment of a photon for $B = 1/2 ~ B_{\rm cr}$. We establish new connections between $μ_γ$, vacuum birefringence, and directly measurable polarization observables. Based on recent experimental observations -- including the ATLAS detection of light-by-light scattering at $8.2σ$ significance, IXPE X-ray polarimetry of magnetars revealing polarization degrees up to 80\%, and continuing PVLAS measurements approaching QED sensitivity -- we provide predictions for ellipticity and polarization degree as important observables for future experiments. Numerical verification of our analytical results confirms the theoretical predictions with high precision.

### [6] [Conformal versus non-conformal two-Higgs-doublet model: phase transitions and gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07189)
*Nico Benincasa,Ji-Wei Li,Hanxiao Pu,Robert B. Mann,Vahid Shokrollahic,T. G. Steele,Zhi-Wei Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper compares the electroweak phase transition and gravitational-wave signatures in two variants of the CP-conserving two-Higgs-doublet model (2HDM): a classically conformal version (C2HDM) and a non-conformal version with explicit quadratic mass terms (NC2HDM). Despite expectations, the C2HDM produces weaker transitions and less supercooling unless the scalon is light; only the NC2HDM yields strong-enough transitions to generate potentially detectable gravitational waves at LISA, TianQin, Taiji, or DECIGO/BBO.
\n\n
本文比较了CP守恒的两希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）的两种实现形式：经典共形版本（C2HDM）和包含显式二次质量项的非共形版本（NC2HDM）中的电弱相变动力学与引力波信号。尽管存在普遍预期，C2HDM仅在scalon较轻时才产生显著超冷，且相变较弱；只有NC2HDM能产生足够强的相变，从而在LISA、天琴（TianQin）、太极（Taiji）甚至更灵敏的DECIGO/BBO任务中产生潜在可观测的随机引力波谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the widespread belief that classical conformal symmetry—realized by removing explicit mass scales from the Lagrangian—naturally leads to strong first-order electroweak phase transitions (EWPTs) via dimensional transmutation and significant supercooling. This work tests that assumption by directly comparing the conformal 2HDM (C2HDM) against a conventional non-conformal 2HDM (NC2HDM) under consistent theoretical and experimental constraints, and examines whether conformality truly enhances the prospects for detectable gravitational-wave signals from cosmological phase transitions.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于一种广泛认知：通过从拉格朗日量中移除显式质量标度所实现的经典共形对称性，会通过维度转置（dimensional transmutation）和显著超冷自然导致强一阶电弱相变（EWPT）。本文通过在一致的理论与实验约束下，直接比较共形2HDM（C2HDM）与常规非共形2HDM（NC2HDM），检验这一假设，并探究共形性是否真能增强来自宇宙相变的可探测引力波信号的可能性。

Method: The authors perform a comprehensive scan of the parameter space of both the C2HDM and NC2HDM, subject to current theoretical (perturbativity, unitarity, vacuum stability) and experimental (Higgs signal strengths, electroweak precision observables, flavor constraints) bounds. They compute the finite-temperature one-loop effective potential to determine the dynamics of the electroweak phase transition. Key thermodynamic parameters—the strength $α$ and the inverse duration $β/H_*$—are extracted to characterize the transition. The resulting $(α, β/H_*)$ phase diagrams are constructed. Gravitational-wave spectra from bubble collisions, sound waves, and magnetohydrodynamic turbulence are then computed using standard semi-analytic formulas. The detectability of these signals is assessed against the sensitivity curves of LISA, TianQin, Taiji, and DECIGO/BBO.
\n\n
作者在当前理论（微扰性、幺正性、真空稳定性）和实验（希格斯信号强度、电弱精密观测量、味物理约束）限制下，对C2HDM和NC2HDM的参数空间进行全面扫描。通过计算有限温度下一圈有效势来确定电弱相变动力学，并提取关键热力学参数——相变强度$α$和逆持续时间$β/H_*$，以刻画相变特性。由此构建$(α, β/H_*)$相图。随后利用标准半解析公式计算由气泡碰撞、声波和磁流体湍流产生的引力波谱，并对照LISA、天琴（TianQin）、太极（Taiji）及DECIGO/BBO的灵敏度曲线评估其可探测性。

Result: The NC2HDM exhibits a much broader range of viable $(α, β/H_*)$ values and supports significantly stronger first-order phase transitions than the C2HDM. The latter is restricted to a nested region of weaker transitions, contradicting the naive expectation that classical conformality generically enhances supercooling. Substantial supercooling in the C2HDM occurs only when the scale-invariance breaking is mild—i.e., when the scalon (the pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson of broken scale symmetry) is light. Consequently, only the NC2HDM yields benchmark scenarios with gravitational-wave amplitudes large enough to be detectable by upcoming space-based interferometers like LISA, TianQin, and Taiji, and possibly by more sensitive missions such as DECIGO/BBO.
\n\n
NC2HDM展现出远比C2HDM更宽广的可行$(α, β/H_*)$参数区域，并支持显著更强的一阶相变。后者被限制在一个嵌套的弱相变子区域内，这与“经典共形性普遍增强超冷”的朴素预期相矛盾。C2HDM中仅当尺度对称性破缺足够温和（即scalon——破缺尺度对称性的伪Nambu-Goldstone玻色子——质量较轻）时，才会出现显著超冷。因此，只有NC2HDM能产生引力波振幅足够大的基准点，使其在LISA、天琴（TianQin）、太极（Taiji）等即将运行的空间干涉仪中可被探测，甚至在更灵敏的DECIGO/BBO任务中也可能被观测到。

Conclusion: Classical conformal symmetry alone does not guarantee strong supercooling or observable gravitational waves from the electroweak phase transition in the 2HDM framework. The presence of explicit mass terms in the NC2HDM provides greater flexibility to achieve strong first-order transitions. Observable stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds are feasible only in the NC2HDM under current constraints, highlighting the importance of moving beyond minimal conformal assumptions when assessing cosmological signatures of BSM physics.
\n\n
在2HDM框架下，仅靠经典共形对称性并不能保证电弱相变中出现强超冷或可观测的引力波信号。NC2HDM中显式质量项的存在为实现强一阶相变提供了更大灵活性。在当前约束下，只有NC2HDM能产生可观测的随机引力波背景，这表明在评估超出标准模型（BSM）物理的宇宙学信号时，有必要超越最小共形假设。

Abstract: In this work we investigate the CP-conserving two-Higgs-doublet model (2HDM) in two realizations: a classically conformal setup (C2HDM) and a non-conformal setup with explicit tree-level quadratic mass terms (NC2HDM). Imposing current theoretical and experimental constraints, we scan the parameter space and analyse the electroweak first-order phase-transition dynamics from the finite-temperature effective potential, determining the relevant thermodynamic scales and the associated parameters $α$ and $β/H_*$. In the resulting $(α, β/H_*)$ phase diagrams, the NC2HDM spans a substantially broader region and hosts the strongest transitions, whereas the C2HDM is confined to a nested, weaker-transition subset. This challenges the common expectation that classical conformal symmetry generically implies deep supercooling. By relaxing the Higgs-mass identification and varying the scalon mass, we show that sizable supercooling is obtained only when the radiative (one-loop) breaking of scale invariance is sufficiently mild, i.e. for a light scalon. We then compute the resulting stochastic gravitational-wave spectra and show that only the NC2HDM yields benchmark points potentially observable by future space-based interferometers such as LISA, TianQin and Taiji (and, in favourable cases, by more sensitive missions such as DECIGO/BBO).

</details>


### [7] [Alternative framework for the left-right symmetric model including vector-like fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07608)
*Yassine Bouzeraib,Mohamed Sadek Zidi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes an extension of the Left-Right Symmetric Model (LRSM) by introducing a new non-abelian $SU(2)$ gauge symmetry and one generation of vector-like fermions. New scalar fields break this extended symmetry, enabling mixing between chiral and vector-like fermions. The model yields two seesaw mechanisms: the standard LRSM seesaw for the first two neutrino generations and a novel seesaw involving vector-like neutrinos (VLN) for the third generation. Using LHC Run II data, the authors derive lower mass bounds on the extra charged gauge boson $W^{\prime}$ (and indirectly on $Z^{\prime}$), with the strongest limits arising from $W^{\prime} \\to \\ell N$ decays involving second-generation heavy Majorana neutrinos. They also study single production of top-type vector-like quarks in association with SM $t$ and $b$ quarks, including parton-shower effects.
\n\n
本文提出了一种 Left-Right Symmetric Model (LRSM) 的扩展，引入了一个新的非阿贝尔 $SU(2)$ 规范对称性和一代矢量型费米子。新的标量场用于破缺该扩展对称性，并实现手征费米子与矢量型费米子之间的混合。该模型包含两种跷跷板机制（seesaw）：前两代中微子质量由标准 LRSM 跷跷板机制主导，而第三代中微子质量则由涉及矢量型中微子（VLN）的新跷跷板机制控制。作者利用 LHC Run II 数据对额外带电规范玻色子 $W^{\prime}$（并间接对 $Z^{\prime}$）设定了质量下限，其中最强的限制来自 $W^{\prime} \\to \\ell N$ 衰变道（涉及第二代重马约拉纳中微子）。此外，他们还研究了顶型矢量型夸克与标准模型 $t$ 和 $b$ 夸克的单举产生过程，并计入 parton-shower 效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to address the origin of small neutrino masses within a well-motivated gauge extension of the Standard Model. The canonical Left-Right Symmetric Model (LRSM) explains neutrino masses via a type-I/II seesaw mechanism but leaves open questions about flavor structure and possible connections to new physics at accessible energy scales. By extending the gauge group with an additional $SU(2)$ and incorporating vector-like fermions, the authors aim to generate a richer neutrino mass spectrum—particularly distinguishing the third generation—and provide testable signatures at colliders like the LHC through new gauge bosons ($W^{\prime}, Z^{\prime}$) and vector-like quarks.
\n\n
动机在于在一个具有良好理论动机的标准模型规范扩展框架内解释微小中微子质量的起源。传统的 Left-Right Symmetric Model (LRSM) 通过 I 型/II 型跷跷板机制解释中微子质量，但仍遗留味结构及与可探测能标新物理关联等问题。通过引入额外的 $SU(2)$ 规范群并加入矢量型费米子，作者旨在构建更丰富的中微子质量谱——特别是区分第三代中微子——并通过新的规范玻色子（$W^{\prime}, Z^{\prime}$）和矢量型夸克在 LHC 等对撞机上提供可检验的新物理信号。

Method: The authors construct a gauge-invariant Lagrangian based on the extended gauge group $SU(3)_C \\times SU(2)_L \\times SU(2)_R \\times SU(2)_X$, where $SU(2)_X$ is the new non-abelian factor. They introduce one generation of vector-like fermions in the fundamental representation of $SU(2)_X$ and new self-dual scalar fields to break $SU(2)_X$ and mediate mixing between chiral and vector-like fermions. Neutrino mass matrices are derived, revealing two distinct seesaw relations. Collider phenomenology is analyzed using effective field theory and Monte Carlo simulations: resonant $W^{\prime}$ production followed by decays to vector-like quarks or heavy Majorana neutrinos is studied, and LHC Run II data are used to set exclusion limits. Single production of top-type vector-like quarks in association with $t/b$ quarks is simulated with parton-shower effects included.
\n\n
作者基于扩展规范群 $SU(3)_C \\times SU(2)_L \\times SU(2)_R \\times SU(2)_X$（其中 $SU(2)_X$ 为新增非阿贝尔因子）构建规范不变拉格朗日量。他们引入一代处于 $SU(2)_X$ 基本表示的矢量型费米子，以及新的自对偶标量场以破缺 $SU(2)_X$ 并介导手征费米子与矢量型费米子之间的混合。由此推导出中微子质量矩阵，揭示出两种不同的跷跷板关系。对撞机唯象学分析采用有效场论与蒙特卡洛模拟：研究共振 $W^{\prime}$ 产生及其衰变至矢量型夸克或重马约拉纳中微子的过程，并利用 LHC Run II 数据设定排除极限。同时，模拟了顶型矢量型夸克与 $t/b$ 夸克的单举产生过程，并计入 parton-shower 效应。

Result: The model successfully generates hierarchical neutrino masses: $m_{\\nu_{1,2}} \\sim m_D^2 / M_R$ (standard LRSM seesaw) and $m_{\\nu_3} \\sim y^2 v_X^2 / M_N$ (new VLN-induced seesaw), where $M_N$ is the vector-like neutrino mass. Using ATLAS/CMS searches for $pp \\to W^{\\prime} \\to \\ell N$, the authors set a lower limit of $M_{W^{\\prime}} \\gtrsim 5.5$ TeV (depending on coupling assumptions), which translates into a bound on $M_{Z^{\\prime}}$ via gauge coupling unification or symmetry breaking patterns. The strongest constraint arises from second-generation heavy neutrino channels. Additionally, cross sections for single top-type vector-like quark production ($pp \\to T t, T b$) are computed with realistic detector-level simulations including parton shower, showing potentially observable rates at HL-LHC.
\n\n
该模型成功生成分层的中微子质量：$m_{\\nu_{1,2}} \\sim m_D^2 / M_R$（标准 LRSM 跷跷板）和 $m_{\\nu_3} \\sim y^2 v_X^2 / M_N$（新的 VLN 诱导跷跷板），其中 $M_N$ 为矢量型中微子质量。利用 ATLAS/CMS 对 $pp \\to W^{\\prime} \\to \\ell N$ 的搜索，作者设定了 $M_{W^{\\prime}} \\gtrsim 5.5$ TeV 的下限（依赖于耦合假设），并通过规范耦合统一或对称性破缺模式转化为对 $M_{Z^{\\prime}}$ 的限制。最强的限制来自第二代重中微子衰变道。此外，计算了顶型矢量型夸克单举产生过程（$pp \\to T t, T b$）的截面，结合包含 parton shower 的真实探测器级模拟，表明其在高亮度 LHC（HL-LHC）上可能具有可观测率。

Conclusion: The extended LRSM with an extra $SU(2)_X$ gauge group and vector-like fermions provides a viable framework for explaining the observed neutrino mass hierarchy while offering distinctive collider signatures. The model predicts correlated signals in $W^{\\prime}/Z^{\\prime}$ searches and vector-like quark production, making it testable at current and future LHC runs. The derived mass bounds significantly constrain the parameter space, particularly disfavoring light $W^{\\prime}$ bosons coupling to second-generation heavy neutrinos. This work demonstrates how neutrino mass generation mechanisms can be directly linked to high-energy collider phenomenology.
\n\n
引入额外 $SU(2)_X$ 规范群和矢量型费米子的扩展 LRSM 为解释观测到的中微子质量层级提供了一个可行框架，同时预言了独特的对撞机信号。该模型在 $W^{\\prime}/Z^{\\prime}$ 搜索与矢量型夸克产生之间预言了关联信号，使其可在当前及未来的 LHC 运行中被检验。所导出的质量下限显著限制了参数空间，尤其排除了与第二代重中微子耦合的轻 $W^{\\prime}$ 玻色子。本工作展示了中微子质量生成机制如何与高能对撞机唯象学直接关联。

Abstract: We extend the left-right symmetric model with an additional non-abelian $SU(2)$ gauge symmetry. The particle content is augmented by one generation of vector-like fermions transforming under the fundamental representation of this new gauge group. Consequently, new self-dual scalar fields have been introduced for the sake of breaking the symmetry and invoking the mixing of vector-like fermions with the chiral fermions. This model explains the smallness of the neutrinos masses, showing that the 1rst and 2nd generation neutrinos masses are governed by the seesaw relation of the LRSM, while the 3rd generation neutrino mass is controlled by a new seesaw relation which involves the VLN. We investigated the production of a resonant extra charged gauge boson which decays into vector-like quarks in association with 3rd generation or into heavy Majorana neutrinos. We exploited the {\tt run II} LHC data to set lower limits on the mass of $W^{\prime}$, and consequentially on the $Z^{\prime}$. We find that the most restrictive constraints come from the decay of the $W^{\prime}$ to the 2nd generation heavy Majorana neutrinos. We also examine the single production of the top vector-like quark with $t$ and $b$ quarks, where parton-shower is taken into account.

</details>


### [8] [Impact of chirality imbalance and nonlocal interactions on the QCD biased axionic domainwall interpretation of NANOGrav 15 year data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07739)
*Ruotong Zhao,Zhao Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores how local CP violation in hot QCD—parameterized by a chiral chemical potential $μ_5$ and the QCD vacuum angle $θ$—affects the topological susceptibility $χ_t$, thereby influencing the production of a stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) from axion-like particle (ALP) domain-wall annihilation. Using a nonlocal Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model near the QCD scale, the authors show that large $μ_5$ can enable compatibility with the NANOGrav 15-year nHz SGWB signal not only for small $θ$, but also for certain large-$θ$ values near $π$, due to an enhanced and broadened peak in $|χ_t|$ at the critical temperature $T_c$.
\n\n
本文研究了热QCD中由手征化学势 $μ_5$ 和QCD真空角 $θ$ 参数化的局域CP破坏如何影响拓扑磁化率 $χ_t$，从而调控由类轴子粒子（ALP）畴壁湮灭产生的随机引力波背景（SGWB）。作者在QCD能标附近采用非局域Nambu-Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型，表明足够大的 $μ_5$ 不仅可在小 $θ$ 区间、也可在接近 $π$ 的某些大 $θ$ 区间内产生与NANOGrav 15年nHz SGWB信号相符的引力波强度，这是由于在临界温度 $T_c$ 处 $|χ_t|$ 的峰值被显著展宽和增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent observations of a nHz stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) by pulsar timing arrays like NANOGrav, which may be interpreted as arising from the annihilation of axion-like particle (ALP) domain walls. The formation and dynamics of such domain walls are governed by the QCD topological susceptibility $χ_t$, which depends on both the vacuum angle $θ$ and possible CP-odd environments characterized by a chiral chemical potential $μ_5$. Understanding how finite-temperature QCD effects—especially under local CP violation—affect $χ_t(θ, μ_5, T)$ is crucial for assessing viable ALP interpretations of the SGWB data.
\n\n
动机源于脉冲星计时阵列（如NANOGrav）近期观测到的nHz随机引力波背景（SGWB），该信号可能源于类轴子粒子（ALP）畴壁的湮灭。此类畴壁的形成与动力学由QCD拓扑磁化率 $χ_t$ 决定，而 $χ_t$ 依赖于真空角 $θ$ 以及由手征化学势 $μ_5$ 表征的CP破坏环境。理解有限温度下QCD效应——特别是局域CP破坏——如何影响 $χ_t(θ, μ_5, T)$，对于评估SGWB数据的ALP物理解释至关重要。

Method: The authors employ a nonlocal Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model to compute the QCD topological susceptibility $χ_t$ as a function of temperature $T$, the vacuum angle $θ$, and the chiral chemical potential $μ_5$. This approach improves upon the local NJL model by incorporating momentum-dependent quark interactions, yielding a more realistic description of the chiral phase transition near the QCD scale ($T \\sim T_c$). They analyze the behavior of $|χ_t|$ around the critical temperature $T_c$ for CP restoration, particularly at $θ = π$, and link the resulting bias in the axion potential to the amplitude of the SGWB produced by collapsing ALP domain walls.
\n\n
作者采用非局域Nambu-Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型计算QCD拓扑磁化率 $χ_t$ 作为温度 $T$、真空角 $θ$ 和手征化学势 $μ_5$ 的函数。该方法通过引入动量依赖的夸克相互作用，改进了局域NJL模型，从而在QCD能标附近（$T \\sim T_c$）更真实地描述手征相变。他们分析了在CP恢复临界温度 $T_c$ 附近（尤其在 $θ = π$ 处）$|χ_t|$ 的行为，并将由此产生的轴子势偏置与坍缩ALP畴壁所产生的SGWB振幅关联起来。

Result: The key result is that for sufficiently large chiral chemical potential $μ_5$, the magnitude of the topological susceptibility $|χ_t|$ develops a broad and pronounced peak near the critical temperature $T_c$ at $θ = π$, in contrast to the narrow peak predicted by the local NJL model. This enhanced $|χ_t|$ leads to a stronger QCD bias on the axion potential, enabling ALP domain-wall annihilation to produce a SGWB amplitude consistent with the NANOGrav 15-year data—not only for small $θ$, but also for a range of large $θ$ values around $π$.
\n\n
核心结果是：当手征化学势 $μ_5$ 足够大时，拓扑磁化率的模 $|χ_t|$ 在 $θ = π$ 处的临界温度 $T_c$ 附近呈现出一个显著且展宽的峰值，这与局域NJL模型预测的窄峰形成对比。这种增强的 $|χ_t|$ 导致对轴子势更强的QCD偏置，使得ALP畴壁湮灭不仅在小 $θ$ 区间、也在 $π$ 附近的大 $θ$ 区间内产生与NANOGrav 15年数据一致的SGWB振幅。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that local CP violation in the early universe—modeled via a finite chiral chemical potential $μ_5$—can significantly modify the thermal behavior of the QCD topological susceptibility, thereby expanding the parameter space for axion-like explanations of the observed nHz gravitational wave signal. The nonlocal NJL framework provides a more robust description of the chiral crossover, revealing that the CP-restoration transition at $θ = π$ is sufficiently broad to support strong SGWB production compatible with current observations.
\n\n
本研究表明，早期宇宙中的局域CP破坏（通过有限手征化学势 $μ_5$ 建模）可显著改变QCD拓扑磁化率的热行为，从而扩展现有nHz引力波信号的类轴子物理解释参数空间。非局域NJL框架对强子手征交叉提供了更稳健的描述，揭示出在 $θ = π$ 处的CP恢复相变足够宽，足以支持与当前观测相符的强SGWB产生。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of the chirality imbalance with local CP-breaking in hot QCD on the generation of a stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) sourced by the axion-like particle (ALP) domain-wall annihilation, induced by the QCD bias. Such a bias is quantified by the QCD topological susceptibility $χ_t$, and its dependence on the $θ$ angle and the chiral chemical potential $μ_5$ is investigated at temperatures near the QCD scale within a nonlocal Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model. We find that, besides the small-$θ$ range, the axionic domain-wall interpretation of NANOGrav 15-year data on the nHz gravitational waves is still possible for a certain large-$θ$ range if $μ_5$ is large enough. We confirm that the peak of $|χ_t|$ at the critical temperature $T_c$ for the CP restoration at $θ=π$ exhibits a pronounced width compared to the local NJL result. Thus, for $θ$ at and around $π$, the QCD bias near $T_c$ can also produce a GW signal strength compatible with the NANOGrav 15-year data.

</details>


### [9] [Schwinger effect in QCD and nuclear physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07847)
*Hidetoshi Taya*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper offers a pedagogical review of the Schwinger effect—the non-perturbative creation of particle–antiparticle pairs from vacuum under strong external fields—and explores its generalizations to quantum chromodynamics (QCD) and applications in nuclear physics such as high-$Z$ nuclei, string breaking, relativistic heavy-ion collisions, and the chiral anomaly.
\n\n
本文对Schwinger效应——即在强外场作用下真空中非微扰地产生粒子-反粒子对——进行了教学性综述，并探讨了其在量子色动力学（QCD）中的推广及其在核物理中的应用，如高$Z$原子核、弦断裂、相对论重离子碰撞和手征反常。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a clear, accessible, and comprehensive overview of the Schwinger effect and its broader implications beyond quantum electrodynamics (QED), especially in contexts where strong fields induce non-perturbative quantum phenomena, such as in QCD and nuclear physics.
\n\n
动机是提供一个清晰、易懂且全面的Schwinger效应综述，并将其影响扩展到量子电动力学（QED）之外的领域，特别是在强场诱导非微扰量子现象的背景下，如量子色动力学（QCD）和核物理。

Method: The authors employ a pedagogical and review-based approach, starting from foundational concepts in QED and systematically extending the discussion to non-Abelian gauge theories like QCD. 作者采用教学性和综述性方法，从量子电动力学（QED）的基础概念出发，系统地将讨论扩展至非阿贝尔规范理论（如QCD），并将理论框架与真空衰变、弦断裂以及重离子碰撞中反常驱动效应等物理现象联系起来。

Result: The paper successfully synthesizes key theoretical results on the Schwinger effect across different domains, clarifies its role in non-perturbative dynamics, and illustrates how it manifests in diverse physical systems—from high-$Z$ atoms to quark-gluon plasma formation in relativistic heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
本文成功整合了Schwinger效应在不同领域中的关键理论成果，阐明了其在非微扰动力学中的作用，并展示了该效应如何在多种物理系统中体现——从高$Z$原子到相对论重离子碰撞中夸克-胶子等离子体的形成。

Conclusion: The Schwinger effect serves as a fundamental paradigm for understanding non-perturbative particle production in strong-field regimes, with profound implications across QED, QCD, and nuclear physics; this review highlights both its theoretical elegance and its relevance to experimental and phenomenological studies.
\n\n
Schwinger效应是理解强场条件下非微扰粒子产生机制的基本范式，在量子电动力学（QED）、量子色动力学（QCD）和核物理中具有深远意义；本综述既突出了其理论优美性，也强调了其在实验和唯象研究中的相关性。

Abstract: We provide a pedagogical review of the Schwinger effect, i.e., the non-perturbative production of particle and anti-particle pairs from the vacuum by strong fields, as well as related strong-field phenomena. Beginning with an overview of the Schwinger effect in quantum electrodynamics, we discuss its extensions to quantum chromodynamics and its applications in nuclear physics, including high-$Z$ nuclei, string breaking, relativistic heavy-ion collisions, and the chiral anomaly.

### [10] [Physics-Informed Global Extraction of the Universal Small-$x$ Dipole Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08008)
*Si-Wei Dai,Fu-Peng Li,Long-Gang Pang,Guang-You Qin,Shu-Yi Wei,Han-Zhong Zhang,Wenbin Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A physics-informed neural network (PINN) is used to extract a universal small-$x$ dipole scattering amplitude $N(r,x_B)$ without assuming a MV-type initial condition. The resulting amplitude simultaneously fits DIS total/charm cross sections, exclusive $J/\\psi$ photoproduction data, and satisfies positivity and BK evolution constraints, resolving tensions seen in traditional parametric approaches.
\n\n
本文采用物理信息神经网络（Physics-Informed Neural Network, PINN）提取普适的小-$x$ 偶极子散射振幅 $N(r,x_B)$，无需预设MV型初始条件。所得振幅同时拟合了深度非弹性散射（DIS）的总截面与粲夸克截面、专属 $J/\\psi$ 光致产生数据，并满足正定性及改进的Balitsky–Kovchegov（BK）演化方程约束，从而解决了传统参数化方法中总截面与粲夸克道之间的长期张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional small-$x$ analyses rely on rigid parametric ansätze for the initial dipole amplitude, often leading to inconsistencies—particularly a tension between total and charm structure functions in DIS. Moreover, such parametrizations may not guarantee physical properties like positivity in momentum space or smooth rapidity evolution. This work aims to overcome these limitations by using a flexible, data-driven approach that respects both theoretical evolution equations and experimental constraints without imposing restrictive functional forms.
\n\n
传统的小-$x$ 分析依赖于对初始偶极振幅的刚性参数化假设，常导致不一致性——特别是DIS中总结构函数与粲夸克结构函数之间的张力。此外，此类参数化可能无法保证动量空间中的正定性或平滑的快度演化。本文旨在通过一种灵活的数据驱动方法克服这些局限，在不施加限制性函数形式的前提下，同时满足理论演化方程和实验约束。

Method: The authors employ a physics-informed neural network (PINN) to represent the dipole scattering amplitude $N(r,x_B)$ as a smooth, differentiable surrogate model. The network is trained to satisfy: (1) the collinearly improved Balitsky--Kovchegov (ciBK) evolution equation in rapidity; (2) experimental data from DIS reduced cross sections ($\\sigma_{\\text{tot}}$, $\\sigma_{\\text{charm}}$) and exclusive $J/\\psi$ photoproduction; and (3) a positivity constraint on the Fourier-transformed momentum-space dipole amplitude $\\mathcal{N}(k,x_B) \\geq 0$. No MV-model-based parametrization is imposed on the initial condition at some $x_0$; instead, the PINN learns it self-consistently from data and theory.
\n\n
作者采用物理信息神经网络（PINN）将偶极散射振幅 $N(r,x_B)$ 表示为一个光滑且可微的代理模型。该网络被训练以同时满足：(1) 快度方向上的共线改进Balitsky–Kovchegov（ciBK）演化方程；(2) 深度非弹性散射（DIS）的约化截面数据（$\\sigma_{\\text{tot}}$、$\\sigma_{\\text{charm}}$）及专属 $J/\\psi$ 光致产生测量；(3) 傅里叶变换后的动量空间偶极振幅 $\\mathcal{N}(k,x_B) \\geq 0$ 的正定性约束。初始条件在某 $x_0$ 处未施加任何基于MV模型的参数化，而是由PINN从数据和理论中自洽地学习得到。

Result: The extracted universal dipole amplitude successfully describes all input observables within uncertainties, resolving the historical tension between total and charm DIS channels. The best-fit solution yields a smooth, non-negative momentum-space dipole amplitude over the full transverse momentum range in the fitted kinematic domain. The rapidity evolution is consistent with ciBK dynamics, and the absence of ad hoc parametrization enhances predictive robustness across processes.
\n\n
所提取的普适偶极振幅在误差范围内成功描述了所有输入观测量，解决了总截面与粲夸克DIS道之间的历史张力。最佳拟合解在整个横向动量范围内给出了光滑且非负的动量空间偶极振幅。其快度演化与ciBK动力学一致，且由于避免了人为参数化，显著提升了跨过程预测的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that a PINN-based, non-parametric extraction of the small-$x$ dipole amplitude, guided by QCD evolution and experimental data, provides a consistent, physically well-behaved, and universal input for Color Glass Condensate (CGC) phenomenology. It establishes a new framework for small-$x$ physics that avoids biases from rigid ansätze and enables more reliable predictions for high-energy scattering processes.
\n\n
本工作表明，基于物理信息神经网络（PINN）、由QCD演化方程和实验数据共同引导的小-$x$ 偶极振幅非参数化提取方法，为Color Glass Condensate（CGC）唯象学提供了一致、物理行为良好且普适的输入。该方法建立了一个新的小-$x$ 物理框架，避免了刚性假设带来的偏差，从而实现对高能散射过程更可靠的预测。

Abstract: We extract the universal small-$x$ dipole scattering amplitude $N(r,x_B)$ from a global analysis based on a physics-informed neural network (PINN), without imposing a priori MV-type parametrization of the initial condition. The network provides a smooth and differentiable surrogate for $N(r,x_B)$, whose rapidity dependence is constrained by the collinearly improved Balitsky--Kovchegov evolution equation, while its functional form is simultaneously constrained by Deep Inelastic Scattering (DIS) data for the reduced total and charm cross sections, exclusive $J/ψ$ photoproduction measurements, and a positivity requirement for the momentum-space dipole amplitude. The resulting single universal amplitude consistently describes all fitted observables within a unified framework, alleviating the long-standing tension between total and charm channels encountered in conventional small-$x$ fits based on rigid parametric ansätze. Within the fitted kinematic domain, the best extracted PINN solution yields a smooth, non-negative momentum-space dipole over the full transverse-momentum range examined. Our results provide a robust and well-behaved input for Color Glass Condensate phenomenology across a broad class of high-energy processes.

</details>


### [11] [Rephasing invariant structure of Dirac CP phase and basis independent reduction of unitarity constraints for mixing matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08071)
*Masaki J. S. Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates rephasing invariant structures of the Dirac CP-violating phase $δ$ under the approximation $U^{e}_{13} = 0$, and further simplifies to $U^{e}_{12} = 0$ to obtain a compact analytic expression for $δ$. It also presents a basis-independent reduction of unitarity constraints for any unitary matrix and connects it to a rephasing-invariant formulation of the PDG parametrization.
\n\n
本文在近似 $U^{e}_{13} = 0$ 下研究了Dirac CP破坏相位 $δ$ 的重相位不变结构，并进一步简化至 $U^{e}_{12} = 0$ 以获得 $δ$ 的紧凑解析表达式。此外，本文还提出了任意幺正矩阵的基无关幺正性约束约化形式，并将其与PDG参数化的重相位不变表述相联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand the origin and structure of the Dirac CP phase in lepton mixing in a way that is independent of arbitrary phase choices (i.e., rephasing invariant) and applicable across different theoretical frameworks. Existing perturbative calculations often rely on specific parametrizations or assumptions; this work aims to unify and generalize these results through rephasing invariants and simplified approximations based on hierarchical charged fermion masses.
\n\n
动机源于需要以一种与任意相位选择无关（即重相位不变）且适用于不同理论框架的方式理解轻子混合中Dirac CP相位的起源和结构。现有的微扰计算通常依赖于特定参数化或假设；本文旨在通过重相位不变量和基于带电费米子质量分层的简化近似，统一并推广这些结果。

Method: The authors adopt an approximation where the 1–3 element of the charged lepton diagonalization matrix is neglected ($U^{e}_{13} = 0$), and further set $U^{e}_{12} = 0$ to derive a compact analytic form for the Dirac CP phase:  
$$δ = δ^ν + \arg \left[ \frac{U_{33}^e}{U_{23}^{e}} - \frac{U_{33}^ν}{U_{23}^ν} \right] - \arg \left[ \frac{U_{33}^e}{U_{23}^{e}} + \frac{U_{23}^{ν*}}{U_{33}^{ν*}} \right].$$  
They then generalize this to finite $U_{12}^{e}$. Additionally, they use the inversion formula for unitary matrices to eliminate four elements ($V_{21}, V_{22}, V_{31}, V_{32}$) and derive a basis-independent reduction of unitarity constraints. An explicit rephasing transformation is applied to connect this to the PDG parametrization in a rephasing-invariant manner.
\n\n
作者采用忽略带电轻子对角化矩阵1–3元的近似（$U^{e}_{13} = 0$），并进一步设 $U^{e}_{12} = 0$ 以导出Dirac CP相位的紧凑解析形式：
$$δ = δ^ν + \arg \\left[ \\frac{U_{33}^e}{U_{23}^{e}} - \\frac{U_{33}^ν}{U_{23}^ν} \\right] - \arg \\left[ \\frac{U_{33}^e}{U_{23}^{e}} + \\frac{U_{23}^{ν*}}{U_{33}^{ν*}} \\right]。$$  
随后将其推广至有限 $U_{12}^{e}$ 的情形。此外，他们利用幺正矩阵的逆公式消去四个矩阵元（$V_{21}, V_{22}, V_{31}, V_{32}$），推导出幺正性约束的基无关约化形式，并通过显式重相位变换将其与PDG参数化的重相位不变表述相联系。

Result: The paper obtains a compact, rephasing-invariant expression for the Dirac CP phase under simplified assumptions, which generalizes known perturbative results in both quark and lepton sectors with hierarchical fermion masses. It also derives a basis-independent reduction of unitarity triangle constraints and shows how the standard PDG parametrization can be recast into a manifestly rephasing-invariant form, enabling direct translation between theoretical predictions and observable invariants.
\n\n
本文在简化假设下获得了Dirac CP相位的紧凑且重相位不变的表达式，该表达式推广了在夸克和轻子扇区中具有分层费米子质量的已知微扰结果。此外，还推导出幺正性三角约束的基无关约化形式，并展示了如何将标准PDG参数化重新表述为显式的重相位不变形式，从而实现理论预言与可观测不变量之间的直接转换。

Conclusion: The work provides a unified, parametrization-independent framework for analyzing the Dirac CP phase using rephasing invariants, grounded in physically motivated approximations from mass hierarchies. The derived rephasing-invariant representation of the PDG parametrization bridges phenomenological analyses with fundamental symmetry considerations, enhancing the robustness of CP violation studies in neutrino physics.
\n\n
本工作基于质量分层所启发的物理近似，提供了一个统一且参数化无关的框架，用于通过重相位不变量分析Dirac CP相位。所导出的PDG参数化的重相位不变表述架起了唯象分析与基本对称性考量之间的桥梁，增强了中微子物理中CP破坏研究的稳健性。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore rephasing invariant structures of the Dirac CP phase $δ$ under an approximation $U^{e}_{13} = 0$, where the 1-3 element of the diagonalization of charged leptons $U^{e}$ is neglected. With the further simplified condition $U^{e}_{12} = 0$, the Dirac phase reduces to a compact form $δ= δ^ν + \arg [ (U_{33}^e / U_{23}^{e}) - ( U_{33}^ν / U_{23}^ν) ] - \arg [ ( U_{33}^e / U_{23}^{e}) + (U_{23}^{ν*} / U_{33}^{ν*} ) ] $, and the CP phase for finite $U_{12}^{e}$ can be understood as a generalization of this compact form. These results encompass almost all perturbative calculations of the CP phases in quark and lepton mixing matrices with hierarchical masses of charged fermions, and are independent of any specific parametrization. As a second result of this work, we derive a basis independent reduction of the unitarity constraints for an arbitrary unitary matrix $V$ by eliminating the elements $V_{21}, V_{22}, V_{31}, V_{32}$ using the inversion formula. Applying the explicit rephasing transformation to this reduction yields a rephasing invariant representation of the PDG parametrization, which allows the translation of theoretical results expressed in the PDG parametrization directly into rephasing invariants.

</details>


### [12] [Heavy mesons with dynamical gluon on the light front](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08114)
*Jiatong Wu,Hengfei Zhao,Kaiyu Fu,Zhi Hu,Xingbo Zhao,James P. Vary*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies charmonium, bottomonium, and B_c mesons using Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) with both $|q\bar{q}\rangle$ and $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ Fock sectors. The light-front Hamiltonian includes a holography-inspired confining potential and QCD-based quark-gluon interactions. After fitting parameters to reproduce low-lying mass spectra, the authors compute electromagnetic form factors, decay constants, parton distribution amplitudes (PDAs), and parton distribution functions (PDFs), including the first BLFQ predictions for gluon PDFs in heavy mesons.
\n\n
本文采用Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ)方法研究了charmonium、bottomonium和B_c介子系统，包含$|q\\bar{q}\\rangle$和$|q\\bar{q}g\\rangle$ Fock态。光前哈密顿量包含受光前全息原理启发的禁闭势以及基于QCD的夸克-胶子相互作用。在拟合低能质量谱后，作者计算了电磁形状因子、衰变常数、parton distribution amplitudes (PDAs)和parton distribution functions (PDFs)，并首次在BLFQ框架下给出了重介子中胶子PDF的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a nonperturbative, first-principles description of heavy quarkonia and B_c mesons that includes explicit dynamical gluonic degrees of freedom. Traditional approaches often neglect the $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ component or use simplified effective interactions. This work aims to go beyond such approximations by incorporating both confinement and QCD-inspired interactions within a light-front Hamiltonian framework, enabling the calculation of key hadronic observables and novel predictions for gluon distributions.
\n\n
该工作的动机是提供一个包含显式动力学胶子自由度的非微扰、第一性原理描述，用于重夸克偶素和B_c介子。传统方法通常忽略$|q\\bar{q}g\\rangle$组分或使用简化的有效相互作用。本文旨在通过在光前哈密顿量框架中同时纳入禁闭效应和QCD启发的相互作用，超越这些近似，从而计算关键强子可观测量，并对胶子分布做出新预测。

Method: The authors employ the Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) formalism, truncating the Fock space to include only the $|q\bar{q}\rangle$ and $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ sectors. The light-front Hamiltonian $P^-$ consists of a kinetic term, a transverse confining potential derived from light-front holography ($U_{\\text{conf}} \\sim \\kappa^4 \\zeta^2$, where $\\zeta$ is the transverse separation), and the leading-order QCD quark-gluon interaction vertex. Parameters like the confinement strength $\\kappa$ and the strong coupling $\\alpha_s$ are fixed by fitting the computed mass spectrum to experimental data for low-lying states. The resulting eigenvectors yield the light-front wave functions (LFWFs), which are then used to compute matrix elements for electromagnetic form factors, decay constants, PDAs, and PDFs via standard light-front integrals.
\n\n
作者采用Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ)形式体系，将Fock空间截断至仅包含$|q\\bar{q}\\rangle$和$|q\\bar{q}g\\rangle$组分。光前哈密顿量$P^-$包含动能项、源自光前全息的横向禁闭势（$U_{\\text{conf}} \\sim \\kappa^4 \\zeta^2$，其中$\\zeta$为横向分离距离）以及QCD领头阶夸克-胶子相互作用顶点。通过拟合低能态质量谱到实验数据，确定禁闭强度$\\kappa$和强耦合常数$\\alpha_s$等参数。所得本征矢量给出光前波函数（LFWFs），进而通过标准光前积分计算电磁形状因子、衰变常数、PDAs和PDFs的矩阵元。

Result: The calculated decay constants and charge radii for charmonium and bottomonium show reasonable agreement with experimental measurements and other theoretical models (e.g., lattice QCD, Dyson-Schwinger equations). The parton distribution amplitudes (PDAs) align with prior BLFQ results that used an effective one-gluon exchange interaction, validating the current Hamiltonian construction. Most notably, the paper presents the first BLFQ predictions for the gluon parton distribution functions (PDFs) in heavy mesons, extracted directly from the $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ light-front wave function component, revealing a non-negligible gluonic contribution to the meson's momentum structure.
\n\n
所计算的charmonium和bottomonium的衰变常数与电荷半径与实验测量及其他理论模型（如lattice QCD、Dyson-Schwinger方程）结果合理吻合。parton distribution amplitudes (PDAs)与先前使用有效单胶子交换相互作用的BLFQ结果一致，验证了当前哈密顿量构造的合理性。最值得注意的是，本文首次在BLFQ框架下给出了重介子中胶子parton distribution functions (PDFs)的预测，该结果直接从$|q\\bar{q}g\\rangle$光前波函数组分提取，揭示了胶子对介子动量结构的不可忽略贡献。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the BLFQ framework, when augmented with both confinement and QCD-motivated interactions and extended to include the $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ Fock sector, provides a consistent and predictive nonperturbative approach for heavy meson structure. It successfully reproduces established observables and enables new predictions—particularly for gluon PDFs—that are crucial for understanding the full partonic content of heavy mesons and for applications in high-energy scattering processes.
\n\n
本研究表明，当BLFQ框架结合禁闭势与QCD启发的相互作用，并扩展至包含$|q\\bar{q}g\\rangle$ Fock态时，能够为重介子结构提供一个自洽且具有预测能力的非微扰方法。该方法不仅成功复现了已知可观测量，还实现了新预测——尤其是胶子PDFs——这对于理解重介子的完整部分子结构及其在高能散射过程中的应用至关重要。

Abstract: We investigate the structure of charmonium, bottomonium, and $\rm B_c$ meson systems within the Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) approach, including both the quark-antiquark ($|q\bar{q}\rangle$) and quark-antiquark-gluon ($|q\bar{q}g\rangle$) Fock sectors. Our input light-front Hamiltonian incorporates a confining potential inspired by light-front holography, as well as the quark-gluon interaction from Quantum Chromodynamics. By adjusting model parameters to reproduce the mass spectra for low-lying states, we obtain the light-front wave functions for the heavy meson states. Based on these wave functions, we calculate electromagnetic form factors, decay constants, parton distribution amplitudes (PDAs), and parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the quarks and gluons in the heavy mesons. Our results for the charge radii and decay constants reasonably agree with experimental data and other theoretical approaches. The PDAs are consistent with the predictions from the earlier BLFQ calculations with an effective one-gluon exchange interaction. Furthermore, we present the first predictions within the BLFQ framework for the gluon PDFs in heavy mesons based on the light-front wave function in the $|q\bar{q}g\rangle$ sector.

</details>


### [13] [Formalizing the stability of the two Higgs doublet model potential into Lean: identifying an error in the literature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08139)
*Joseph Tooby-Smith*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A formalization effort using interactive theorem provers (e.g., Mathlib, PhysLib) has uncovered a non-trivial error in the 2006 paper by Maniatis et al. on the stability of the two Higgs doublet model (2HDM) potential, invalidating its main theorem. This is the first known case where formal verification revealed an error in a physics paper, raising concerns about the mathematical rigor of other published results.
\n\n
利用交互式定理证明器（如 Mathlib、PhysLib）进行形式化工作，揭示了 Maniatis 等人在 2006 年关于 two Higgs doublet model (2HDM) 势稳定性论文中的一个非平凡错误，使其主定理失效。据我们所知，这是首个通过形式化验证发现物理论文错误的案例，引发了对其他已发表成果数学严谨性的担忧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the increasing feasibility of applying formal verification methods—enabled by modern libraries like Mathlib and PhysLib—to foundational results in theoretical physics. The 2006 paper on 2HDM stability is a canonical reference, making it a natural candidate for formalization. The goal was to ensure mathematical correctness at a higher standard than conventional peer review, especially for results that underpin further theoretical and phenomenological work.
\n\n
动机源于现代形式化验证方法（由 Mathlib 和 PhysLib 等库支持）在理论物理基础成果中日益可行的应用。2006 年关于 2HDM 稳定性的论文是一篇经典参考文献，因此成为形式化的自然候选对象。目标是以高于传统同行评审的标准确保数学正确性，特别是对于支撑后续理论和唯象研究的结果。

Method: The authors employed interactive theorem proving, leveraging formal mathematics libraries such as Mathlib and PhysLib (formerly PhysLean and Lean-QuantumInfo), to encode and verify the logical structure and mathematical arguments of the 2006 paper concerning the boundedness-from-below conditions of the 2HDM scalar potential. This process involved translating analytical conditions and algebraic inequalities into a machine-checkable formal language.
\n\n
作者采用交互式定理证明方法，利用 Mathlib 和 PhysLib（前身为 PhysLean 和 Lean-QuantumInfo）等形式化数学库，对 2006 年论文中关于 2HDM 标量势“从下有界”（boundedness-from-below）条件的逻辑结构和数学论证进行编码与验证。该过程涉及将解析条件和代数不等式转化为机器可检验的形式语言。

Result: The formalization process uncovered a flaw in the original argument, specifically invalidating the main theorem that provided necessary and sufficient conditions for the stability (i.e., boundedness from below) of the 2HDM potential. This represents the first documented instance where formal verification exposed a substantive error in a peer-reviewed physics publication.
\n\n
形式化过程揭示了原始论证中的一个缺陷，特别是使其关于 2HDM 势稳定性（即从下有界）的充要条件的主定理失效。这是首个有记录的案例，表明形式化验证可暴露经同行评审的物理出版物中的实质性错误。

Conclusion: This case demonstrates that even widely cited and influential physics papers may contain subtle mathematical errors that escape conventional peer review. It underscores the value of formal verification as a complementary tool for ensuring rigor in theoretical physics, and raises broader questions about the reliability of the existing literature if subjected to similar scrutiny.
\n\n
该案例表明，即使被广泛引用且具有影响力的物理论文也可能包含常规同行评审未能发现的微妙数学错误。它强调了形式化验证作为确保理论物理严谨性的补充工具的价值，并引发了一个更广泛的问题：如果现有文献接受类似审查，其可靠性将如何？

Abstract: In 2006, using the best methods and techniques available at the time, Maniatis, von Manteuffel, Nachtmann and Nagel published a now widely cited paper on the stability of the two Higgs doublet model (2HDM) potential. Twenty years on, it is now easier to apply the process of formalization into an interactive theorem prover to this work thanks to projects like Mathlib and PhysLib (formerly PhysLean and Lean-QuantumInfo), and to ask for a higher standard of mathematical correctness. Doing so has revealed an error in the arguments of this 2006 paper, invalidating their main theorem on the stability of the 2HDM potential. This case is noteworthy because to the best of our knowledge it is the first non-trivial error in a physics paper found through formalization. It was one of the first papers where formalization was attempted, which raises the uncomfortable question of how many physics papers would not pass this higher level of scrutiny.

### [14] [Probing the CP Property of ALP-photon Interactions at Future Lepton Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08144)
*Jian-Nan Ding,Yandong Liu,Muyuan Song*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies a CP-odd axion-like particle (ALP) with both CP-conserving ($a F_{\\mu\\nu}\\tilde{F}^{\\mu\\nu}$) and CP-violating ($a F_{\\mu\\nu}F^{\\mu\\nu}$) couplings to photons at future lepton colliders. The process $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- a \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$ is analyzed, using the azimuthal angle difference $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ between final-state electrons to probe the CP nature of ALP-photon interactions. Sensitivity to couplings can reach $\\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})~\\mathrm{TeV}^{-1}$, surpassing current $e$EDM limits, and a binned likelihood analysis of $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ enables discrimination among interaction types and identification of CP violation.\n\n
本文研究了一种具有CP守恒项（$a F_{\\mu\\nu}\\tilde{F}^{\\mu\\nu}$）和CP破坏项（$a F_{\\mu\\nu}F^{\\mu\\nu}$）的CP奇性类轴子粒子（ALP），并在未来轻子对撞机上探测其与光子的耦合。通过分析过程 $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- a \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$，利用末态电子之间的方位角差 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ 来探测ALP-光子相互作用的CP结构。耦合灵敏度可达 $\\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})~\\mathrm{TeV}^{-1}$，优于当前电子电偶极矩（$e$EDM）的限制；通过对 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ 的分箱似然分析，可有效区分不同相互作用类型并识别ALP中的CP破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the theoretical possibility that an axion-like particle (ALP) may simultaneously possess both CP-conserving and CP-violating couplings to photons, which is not typically assumed in standard ALP models. Understanding the CP structure of such interactions is crucial for uncovering underlying symmetries or symmetry-breaking mechanisms. Current constraints from the electron electric dipole moment ($e$EDM) limit CP-violating couplings, but future lepton colliders offer a complementary and potentially more sensitive probe through direct production and kinematic observables like $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$.\n\n
动机源于一种理论可能性：类轴子粒子（ALP）可能同时具有CP守恒和CP破坏的光子耦合，这在标准ALP模型中通常未被考虑。理解此类相互作用的CP结构对于揭示潜在的对称性或对称性破缺机制至关重要。当前来自电子电偶极矩（$e$EDM）的限制约束了CP破坏耦合，但未来轻子对撞机可通过直接产生过程及 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ 等运动学观测量提供互补且可能更灵敏的探针。

Method: The authors analyze the process $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- a \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$ at future lepton colliders, focusing on the azimuthal angle difference $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ between the two final-state electrons. They construct differential cross sections for three scenarios: purely CP-conserving, purely CP-violating, and mixed ALP-photon couplings. A binned likelihood analysis of the $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ distribution is employed to discriminate between these scenarios and extract sensitivity to the coupling strengths. Projected sensitivities are compared against existing bounds from the electron EDM.\n\n
作者分析了未来轻子对撞机上的过程 $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- a \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$，重点关注末态两个电子之间的方位角差 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$。他们针对三种情形构建了微分截面：纯CP守恒、纯CP破坏以及混合型ALP-光子耦合。通过 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ 分布的分箱似然分析来区分这些情形，并提取对耦合强度的灵敏度。将投影灵敏度与现有电子电偶极矩（EDM）限制进行比较。

Result: The projected sensitivity to both CP-conserving and CP-violating ALP-photon couplings reaches $\\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})~\\mathrm{TeV}^{-1}$, exceeding current limits from the electron EDM. The $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ distributions differ markedly across interaction types: purely CP-conserving interactions yield a $\\cos(2\\Delta\\phi_{ee})$ modulation, CP-violating ones produce a $\\sin(2\\Delta\\phi_{ee})$ dependence, and mixed couplings generate interference patterns. When the two couplings are comparable, the interference enables clear identification of CP violation upon signal observation. For hierarchical couplings, increased integrated luminosity significantly enhances sensitivity to the subdominant CP-violating component.\n\n
对CP守恒和CP破坏型ALP-光子耦合的投影灵敏度可达 $\\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})~\\mathrm{TeV}^{-1}$，优于当前电子电偶极矩的限制。不同相互作用类型的 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ 分布显著不同：纯CP守恒相互作用产生 $\\cos(2\\Delta\\phi_{ee})$ 调制，CP破坏型导致 $\\sin(2\\Delta\\phi_{ee})$ 依赖，而混合耦合则形成干涉图样。当两种耦合强度相当时，干涉效应可在观测到信号后明确识别CP破坏；若耦合强度差异较大，则提高积分亮度可显著增强对次主导CP破坏成分的灵敏度。

Conclusion: Future lepton colliders can serve as powerful probes of the CP structure of axion-like particles through precision measurements of the azimuthal angle correlation $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$ in $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$ events. The method allows not only improved sensitivity to ALP-photon couplings beyond current $e$EDM bounds but also model-independent discrimination between CP-conserving, CP-violating, and mixed interactions. This provides a unique opportunity to discover CP violation in the ALP sector, especially if both types of couplings are present at comparable levels.\n\n
未来轻子对撞机可通过精确测量 $e^+e^- \\to e^+e^- \\gamma\\gamma$ 事例中的方位角关联 $\\Delta\\phi_{ee}$，成为探测类轴子粒子CP结构的有力工具。该方法不仅能在ALP-光子耦合灵敏度上超越当前 $e$EDM 限制，还能在模型无关的前提下区分CP守恒、CP破坏及混合相互作用。这为发现ALP中的CP破坏提供了独特机会，尤其是在两类耦合强度相当的情形下。

Abstract: We investigate a charge-parity (CP) odd axion-like particle (ALP) featuring simultaneous CP-conserving ($a F_{μν}\tilde{F}^{μν}$) and CP-violating ($a F_{μν}F^{μν}$) ALP-photon interactions at future lepton colliders. The ALP signal is studied in the process $e^+e^- \to e^+e^- a \to e^+e^- γγ$, where the CP structure of the interaction can be probed using the azimuthal angle difference between the final-state electrons, $Δφ_{ee}$. We show that the projected sensitivity to the ALP-photon couplings can reach $\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})~\mathrm{TeV}^{-1}$, exceeding current constraints from the electron electric dipole moment ($e$EDM). Because purely CP-conserving, purely CP-violating, and mixed interactions generate distinct $Δφ_{ee}$ distributions, a binned likelihood analysis of this observable enables an efficient discrimination of the ALP interaction structure. In particular, if the CP-conserving and CP-violating couplings are comparable--as motivated by possible symmetry considerations--the interference pattern in the $Δφ_{ee}$ distribution allows future lepton colliders to identify CP violation in the ALP sector once a signal is observed. For scenarios where the two couplings differ significantly, increasing the integrated luminosity substantially improves the sensitivity to CP-violating effects.

</details>


### [15] [Nonminimal Lorentz Violation in Atomic and Molecular Spectroscopy Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08298)
*Arnaldo J. Vargas*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This work explores how atomic and molecular spectroscopy can reveal Lorentz violation through the Standard-Model Extension (SME), focusing on nonrelativistic effective coefficients—both those already constrained and those yet to be bounded—and emphasizes the role of high-angular-momentum transitions in improving sensitivity to such symmetry-breaking effects.
\n\n
本文探讨了原子和分子光谱学如何通过Standard-Model Extension（SME）揭示Lorentz对称性破缺，重点关注非相对论性有效SME系数——包括已被约束的和尚未设限的系数——并强调高角动量跃迁在提升对此类对称性破缺效应灵敏度中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

The Standard-Model Extension (SME) provides a comprehensive framework for parameterizing potential Lorentz-violating effects. While many SME coefficients have been constrained using various systems, numerous nonrelativistic effective coefficients remain unconstrained, especially in the context of atomic and molecular spectroscopy. Moreover, transitions involving states with high angular momentum may offer enhanced sensitivity to certain Lorentz-violating operators, motivating their inclusion in future experiments.
\n\n
当前对Lorentz对称性的实验检验对于探索超出Standard Model和General Relativity的新物理至关重要。Standard-Model Extension（SME）为参数化潜在的Lorentz破缺效应提供了全面框架。尽管已有多种系统对许多SME系数进行了约束，但大量非相对论性有效系数（尤其在原子和分子光谱学中）仍未被限制。此外，涉及高角动量态的跃迁可能对某些Lorentz破缺算符具有增强的灵敏度，这促使未来实验将其纳入考量。

Method: The analysis relies on the nonrelativistic limit of the Standard-Model Extension (SME), where Lorentz-violating effects are encoded in effective Hamiltonian terms that perturb atomic and molecular energy levels. The authors review existing experimental constraints on these effective coefficients derived from precision spectroscopy. They also identify unconstrained combinations of SME coefficients and propose that transitions between states with large orbital or total angular momentum quantum numbers ($\\ell$ or $j$) can amplify the observable signatures of Lorentz violation due to the angular dependence of the perturbations.
\n\n
该分析基于Standard-Model Extension（SME）的非相对论极限，其中Lorentz破缺效应被编码为微扰原子和分子能级的有效哈密顿量项。作者回顾了从精密光谱学中获得的对这些有效系数的现有实验约束，并识别出尚未被约束的SME系数组合。他们提出，由于微扰项具有角依赖性，大轨道角动量或总角动量量子数（$\\ell$ 或 $j$）态之间的跃迁可放大Lorentz破缺的可观测信号。

Result: The presentation summarizes which nonrelativistic SME coefficients have already been bounded by spectroscopic experiments and delineates the subset that remains unconstrained. It demonstrates that matrix elements of Lorentz-violating operators scale with angular momentum quantum numbers, implying that transitions involving high-$\\ell$ or high-$j$ states can significantly enhance experimental sensitivity. This provides a clear pathway for setting first-time bounds on previously untested SME coefficients.
\n\n
该报告总结了哪些非相对论性SME系数已被光谱实验限制，并明确划定了尚未被约束的子集。研究表明，Lorentz破缺算符的矩阵元随角动量量子数缩放，这意味着涉及高-$\\ell$ 或高-$j$ 态的跃迁可显著提升实验灵敏度。这为首次对先前未测试的SME系数设定界限提供了清晰路径。

Conclusion: High-angular-momentum atomic and molecular transitions represent a promising avenue for probing unexplored sectors of Lorentz violation within the SME framework. By leveraging the enhanced sensitivity afforded by these states, future spectroscopy experiments can place first constraints on currently unconstrained nonrelativistic effective coefficients, thereby advancing tests of fundamental spacetime symmetries.
\n\n
高角动量的原子和分子跃迁是在SME框架内探测未被探索的Lorentz破缺区域的有力途径。通过利用这些态所提供的增强灵敏度，未来的光谱学实验可对当前未受约束的非相对论性有效系数施加首批限制，从而推进对基本时空对称性的检验。

Abstract: This presentation discusses potential signals of Lorentz violation that could be observed in atomic and molecular spectroscopy experiments. It provides a general overview of the nonrelativistic effective SME coefficients that have been constrained, as well as the prospects for placing first-time bounds on those that remain unconstrained. Additionally, it highlights the importance of considering transitions involving atomic or molecular states with high angular momentum in tests of Lorentz symmetry.
