### [16] [Connecting baryon light-front wave functions to quasi-transverse-momentum-dependent correlators in lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08405)
*S. Rodini,A. Schiavi,B. Pasquini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a method to extract baryonic light-front wave functions (LFWFs) from equal-time correlators accessible in Lattice QCD. It establishes factorization of these correlators into the physical LFWF, a lattice-specific residual factor, and a soft subtraction factor, and verifies the renormalizability and scale evolution of the LFWF up to next-to-leading order.
\n\n
本文提出了一种从格点QCD可计算的等时关联函数中提取重子（如质子）的光前波函数（LFWFs）的方法。文章建立了关联函数的因子化形式，将其分解为物理LFWF、格点特有的剩余因子和一个软减除因子，并在次领头阶验证了LFWF的可重整性及其标度演化方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Light-front wave functions (LFWFs) provide a complete description of hadron structure in terms of partonic degrees of freedom, but they are not directly accessible in Euclidean-space Lattice QCD due to their Minkowski-space nature. The motivation is to bridge this gap by constructing a rigorous connection between LFWFs and equal-time correlators that can be computed on the lattice, enabling first-principles nonperturbative calculations of hadronic structure.
\n\n
光前波函数（LFWFs）以部分子自由度完整描述强子结构，但由于其闵可夫斯基空间本质，无法直接通过欧几里得空间的格点QCD获得。本文旨在建立LFWFs与可在格点上计算的等时关联函数之间的严格联系，从而弥合这一鸿沟，使强子结构能够通过第一性原理的非微扰方法进行计算。

Method: The authors employ an operator product expansion (OPE) to analyze a specific equal-time three-quark correlator designed for Lattice QCD. They demonstrate its factorization into three components: (i) the physical three-quark color-singlet LFWF, (ii) a residual lattice factor encoding UV-sensitive short-distance physics specific to the lattice regulator, and (iii) a soft factor that subtracts additional divergences introduced by the factorization procedure. The renormalization properties and scale dependence of the LFWF are then analyzed using standard renormalization group techniques at next-to-leading order (NLO) in perturbation theory.
\n\n
作者采用算符乘积展开（OPE）分析一种专为格点QCD设计的三夸克等时关联函数。他们证明该关联函数可因子化为三个部分：(i) 物理的三夸克色单态LFWF，(ii) 一个包含格点正规化方案下紫外敏感短程物理的剩余格点因子，以及(iii) 一个用于减除因子化过程中引入的额外发散的软因子。随后，利用标准的重整化群技术，在微扰论的次领头阶（NLO）分析了LFWF的重整化性质及其标度依赖性。

Result: The paper proves the factorization formula for the lattice-accessible correlator, explicitly identifying the LFWF as a separate, universal component. It verifies that the LFWF is independently renormalizable, confirming its status as a well-defined physical object. Furthermore, the authors derive the explicit evolution equations that dictate how the baryonic LFWF changes with the renormalization scale $\\mu$, providing a crucial tool for connecting lattice results at a low scale to phenomenological applications at higher scales.
\n\n
本文证明了格点可及关联函数的因子化公式，明确将LFWF识别为一个独立的普适组分。文章验证了LFWF具有独立的可重整性，确认了其作为良定义物理对象的地位。此外，作者推导出了支配重子LFWF随重整化标度$\\mu$变化的显式演化方程，为连接低能标下的格点结果与高能标下的唯象应用提供了关键工具。

Conclusion: This work provides a theoretically sound and practical framework for extracting fundamental light-front wave functions of baryons from Lattice QCD simulations. By establishing a clear factorization and renormalization program, it paves the way for ab initio calculations of hadron structure in terms of quark and gluon degrees of freedom, which is essential for a deeper understanding of QCD and for making precise predictions for high-energy experiments.
\n\n
本工作为从格点QCD模拟中提取重子的基本光前波函数提供了一个理论严谨且实用的框架。通过建立清晰的因子化与重整化方案，它为基于夸克和胶子自由度的强子结构从头算（ab initio）计算铺平了道路，这对于深入理解QCD以及为高能实验做出精确预言至关重要。

Abstract: Within light-front quantization, hadrons can be represented on a Fock-space basis of configurations of elementary partons. The coefficients of the expansion are called light-front wave functions (LFWFs), and encode all the dynamical degrees of freedom. We show how to extract the LFWFs of baryons, such as the proton, from equal-time correlators suitable for Lattice QCD simulations. Using an operator product expansion, we prove the factorization of the relevant correlator in the three-quark color-singlet LFWF, a residual lattice factor, and a soft factor that systematically subtracts the additional divergences arising from the factorization. We verify up to next-to-leading order the independent renormalizability of the LFWF, and we derive the evolution equations that govern its scale dependence.

</details>


### [17] [The Dark Photon: a 2026 Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08430)
*Andrea Caputo,Rouven Essig*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper provides a pedagogical introduction to dark photons, covering their theoretical framework, significance in particle physics, and experimental search strategies across laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological domains.
\n\n
本文对暗光子（dark photons）进行了教学式综述，涵盖了其理论框架、在粒子物理中的重要性，以及在实验室、天体物理和宇宙学领域中的探测策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dark photons are a well-motivated extension of the Standard Model that could explain dark matter or mediate interactions in a hidden sector; understanding them is crucial for addressing fundamental questions in particle physics and cosmology, necessitating a clear pedagogical synthesis of current knowledge.
\n\n
暗光子是标准模型（Standard Model）的一个理论动机充分的扩展，可能解释暗物质或作为隐藏扇区（hidden sector）中的相互作用媒介；理解暗光子对于回答粒子物理与宇宙学中的基本问题至关重要，因此有必要对现有知识进行清晰的教学式整合。

Method: The paper employs a review-based approach, synthesizing established theoretical formulations of dark photons—including their kinetic mixing with ordinary photons—and summarizing diverse experimental and observational techniques such as beam-dump experiments, stellar cooling arguments, cosmic microwave background (CMB) constraints, and big bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) limits.
\n\n
本文采用综述方法，整合了暗光子的既有理论表述——包括其与普通光子的动能混合（kinetic mixing）——并总结了多种实验与观测技术，例如束流倾倒实验（beam-dump experiments）、恒星冷却论证、宇宙微波背景（CMB）约束以及大爆炸核合成（BBN）限制。

Result: The overview clarifies the parameter space of dark photon models (mass $m_{A'}$ and mixing parameter $\epsilon$), identifies current experimental bounds from various probes, and highlights complementarities among laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological searches.
\n\n
该综述阐明了暗光子模型的参数空间（质量 $m_{A'}$ 与混合参数 $\epsilon$），梳理了各类探针给出的当前实验限制，并强调了实验室、天体物理与宇宙学搜寻之间的互补性。

Conclusion: Dark photons remain a compelling target for new physics; coordinated efforts across multiple observational frontiers are essential to fully explore their viable parameter space and test their role in fundamental physics.
\n\n
暗光子仍是新物理的一个引人注目的目标；要全面探索其可行参数空间并检验其在基础物理中的作用，必须在多个观测前沿开展协同努力。

Abstract: We give a pedagogical overview of dark photons. We describe the theory and their importance in particle physics research, and discuss searches using laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological probes.

</details>


### [18] [Precise Predictions for Hadronic Higgs Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08517)
*Elliot Fox*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This work presents high-precision theoretical predictions for hadronic Higgs decays at future $e^+e^-$ Higgs factories, comparing the dominant $H\to b\bar{b}$ and subdominant $H\to gg$ channels using the generalised antenna formalism up to NNLO, with selected observables matched to NNLL resummation.
\n\n
本文利用新发展的“广义天线形式”（generalised antenna formalism），在未来的 $e^+e^-$ 希格斯工厂背景下，对主导的 $H\to b\bar{b}$ 与次主导的 $H\to gg$ 强子衰变道进行了高精度理论计算，达到 NNLO 精度，并对部分观测量匹配至 NNLL 重求和，以获得背对背极限下的可靠预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Future electron-positron colliders functioning as "Higgs factories" will enable ultra-precise measurements of Higgs boson properties in a clean environment. To fully exploit this experimental potential, precise theoretical predictions for hadronic Higgs decay observables—especially distinguishing between different production mechanisms like Yukawa-driven $H\to b\bar{b}$ and gluonic $H\to gg$—are essential. Current theoretical uncertainties limit the interpretation of such data, motivating higher-order calculations.
\n\n
未来的电子-正电子对撞机作为“希格斯工厂”，将在干净的实验环境中实现对希格斯玻色子性质的超高精度测量。为充分利用这一潜力，必须提供精确的强子衰变可观测量理论预言，特别是区分由 Yukawa 耦合主导的 $H\to b\bar{b}$ 与胶子诱导的 $H\to gg$ 衰变机制。当前理论不确定性限制了实验数据的解释，因此亟需更高阶的微扰计算。

Method: The authors employ the newly developed "generalised antenna formalism" to compute jet rates and classical QCD event-shape observables for $H\to b\bar{b}$ and $H\to gg$ decays at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) in perturbative QCD. For certain infrared-sensitive observables, they further match the fixed-order NNLO results to next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic (NNLL) resummation to correctly describe the back-to-back (soft/collinear) emission limit.
\n\n
作者采用新发展的“广义天线形式”（generalised antenna formalism），在微扰 QCD 的 NNLO 精度下计算 $H\to b\bar{b}$ 与 $H\to gg$ 衰变的喷注率和经典 QCD 事例形状观测量。对于某些红外敏感的观测量，他们进一步将固定阶 NNLO 结果与 NNLL 重求和（resummation）匹配，以正确描述背对背（软/共线）辐射极限。

Result: The calculation provides NNLO-accurate predictions for a range of jet and event-shape observables that clearly differentiate between the $H\to b\bar{b}$ and $H\to gg$ decay topologies. When matched to NNLL resummation, the predictions remain reliable even in kinematic regions where emissions are soft or collinear (i.e., the back-to-back limit), significantly reducing theoretical uncertainties.
\n\n
该计算为多种喷注和事例形状观测量提供了 NNLO 精度的预言，能清晰区分 $H\to b\bar{b}$ 与 $H\to gg$ 衰变的拓扑结构。当与 NNLL 重求和匹配后，即使在软或共线辐射区域（即背对背极限），预言依然可靠，显著降低了理论不确定性。

Conclusion: High-precision NNLO (+NNLL) theoretical predictions for hadronic Higgs decays are now achievable using the generalised antenna formalism, enabling robust discrimination between different Higgs coupling structures at future Higgs factories. This paves the way for precision tests of the Standard Model and potential discovery of new physics through deviations in Higgs decay patterns.
\n\n
利用广义天线形式，现已可实现强子希格斯衰变的高精度 NNLO（+NNLL）理论预言，使得在未来希格斯工厂中能够稳健地区分不同的希格斯耦合结构。这为通过希格斯衰变模式的偏差进行标准模型的精密检验乃至新物理的发现铺平了道路。

Abstract: The prospect of future electron-positron colliders operating as "Higgs factories" in a clean experimental environment presents one of the most promising avenues for Higgs precision measurements. In order to capitalise on this, we need to have good theoretical control over these observables. In this talk, I will report on recent calculations in Hadronic Higgs decays, focusing in particular on the variations between the dominant $H\to b \bar{b}$ channel via a Yukawa interaction, and the sub-dominant $H\to gg$ channel. Using the newly-developed "generalised antenna formalism", we have been able to calculate jet-rates and classical QCD event-shape observables up to NNLO accuracy, providing us with the means to quantify the differences between the two decay modes. For a subset of observables, we also match these NNLO results to NNLL resummation to obtain valid predictions even in the back-to-back limit.

</details>


### [19] [Radiative corrections to the nucleon isovector $g_V$ and $g_A$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08596)
*Oleksandr Tomalak,Yi-Bo Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Electroweak, QCD, and QED radiative corrections to nucleon low-energy couplings $g_V$ and $g_A$ are enhanced by large logarithms across scales; incorporating these yields a 3.5(2.1)% (or 5.6(7)%) correction, predicting $g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.265(26)$ or $1.240(9)$ depending on input assumptions.
\n\n
电弱、QCD 和 QED 对核子低能耦合常数 $g_V$ 和 $g_A$ 的辐射修正因跨越电弱尺度、强子尺度和 MeV 低能尺度之间的大对数而被增强；综合这些效应后，得到 3.5(2.1)%（或 5.6(7)%）的总修正，预测 $g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.265(26)$ 或 $1.240(9)$，具体取决于是否结合格点 QCD 与数据驱动输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The physical axial-vector coupling $g_A$ extracted from neutron beta decay differs from the value computed in lattice QCD due to missing higher-order electroweak, QCD, and QED radiative corrections, as well as pion-mass splitting effects. These corrections involve large logarithms between widely separated energy scales, necessitating a consistent effective field theory treatment to bridge lattice results and physical observables.
\n\n
从自由中子β衰变提取的物理轴矢耦合常数 $g_A$ 与格点 QCD 计算结果存在差异，原因在于缺失了高阶电弱、QCD 和 QED 辐射修正以及π介子质量劈裂效应。这些修正包含跨越电弱、强子和 MeV 尺度之间的大对数项，因此需要一致的有效场论处理以连接格点计算与物理观测量。

Method: The authors employ a multi-scale matching framework within an effective field theory (EFT) approach, systematically resumming large logarithms via renormalization group evolution from the electroweak scale down to the hadronic and then to the MeV scale. They incorporate isospin-breaking corrections from pion-mass splitting using chiral perturbation theory ($\\chi$PT), and combine lattice-QCD inputs with phenomenological data to relate the bare lattice axial charge to its physical value.
\n\n
作者采用多尺度匹配框架，在有效场论（EFT）方法中通过重整化群演化系统地重求和从电弱尺度到强子尺度再到 MeV 尺度的大对数项。他们利用手征微扰理论（$\\chi$PT）纳入由π介子质量劈裂引起的同位旋破缺修正，并结合格点 QCD 输入与唯象数据，将裸格点轴矢荷关联到其物理值。

Result: The total radiative correction to $g_A$ is found to be $3.5(2.1)\%$ when combining lattice and data-driven inputs, and $5.6(7)\%$ when using only data-driven inputs. This yields predicted lattice-QCD values of $g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.265(26)$ and $1.240(9)$, respectively, improving the consistency between lattice computations and experimental measurements.
\n\n
对 $g_A$ 的总辐射修正被确定为：当结合格点与数据驱动输入时为 $3.5(2.1)\%$，仅使用数据驱动输入时为 $5.6(7)\%$。由此分别预测格点 QCD 值为 $g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.265(26)$ 和 $1.240(9)$，从而改善了格点计算与实验测量之间的一致性。

Conclusion: A consistent inclusion of multi-scale radiative corrections and isospin-breaking effects resolves part of the tension between lattice-QCD calculations and experimental determinations of $g_A$. Future improvements in chiral perturbation theory, lattice systematics, and phenomenological inputs will further refine the precision of this fundamental parameter.
\n\n
一致地纳入多尺度辐射修正和同位旋破缺效应可部分缓解格点 QCD 计算与 $g_A$ 实验测定之间的张力。未来在手征微扰理论、格点系统误差和唯象输入方面的改进将进一步提升这一基本参数的精度。

Abstract: Electroweak, QCD, and QED radiative corrections to the nucleon low-energy coupling constants $g_V$ and $g_A$ are enhanced by large perturbative logarithms between the electroweak and hadronic scale, as well as between the hadronic scale and the low-energy MeV scale. Additionally, higher-order pion-mass splitting corrections to the nucleon axial-vector charge might be large. By consistently incorporating these effects, we provide an updated relation between the lattice-QCD and physical $g_A$, finding a total radiative correction of $3.5(2.1)\%$ ($5.6(7)\%$). This leads to an expected lattice-QCD result of $g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.265(26)$ ($g^{\mathrm{QCD}}_A = 1.240(9)$) when based on a combination of lattice-QCD and data-driven (or only data-driven) inputs, respectively. Future phenomenological, chiral perturbation theory, and lattice-QCD studies can improve both the central value and the uncertainty of this estimate.

</details>


### [20] [Cobimaximal mixing pattern from a $Δ(27)$ inverse seesaw model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08625)
*A. E. Cárcamo Hernández,Ivo de Medeiros Varzielas,Nicolás A. Pérez-Julve*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose an inverse seesaw model using $\\Delta(27)$ and Abelian discrete symmetries that generates realistic neutrino masses and cobimaximal leptonic mixing, and successfully explains the baryon asymmetry via leptogenesis only in the normal mass hierarchy scenario.
\n\n
我们提出了一种基于 $\\Delta(27)$ 和阿贝尔离散对称性的逆跷跷板模型，该模型生成了符合实际的中微子质量和 cobimaximal 轻子混合，并且仅在正常质量序情形下通过轻子生成机制成功解释了宇宙重子不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to address the origin of neutrino mass hierarchies and the observed pattern of leptonic mixing angles, particularly within the framework of the cobimaximal mixing paradigm. It also seeks to provide a viable mechanism for generating the baryon asymmetry of the Universe through leptogenesis, while being consistent with current neutrino oscillation data.
\n\n
本文旨在解决中微子质量等级结构和观测到的轻子混合角模式（特别是 cobimaximal 混合范式）的起源问题。同时，它试图提供一种通过轻子生成（leptogenesis）产生宇宙重子不对称性的可行机制，并与当前中微子振荡数据保持一致。

Method: The authors construct an inverse seesaw model incorporating the non-Abelian flavor symmetry $\\Delta(27)$ along with additional Abelian discrete symmetries. These symmetries constrain the structure of the Yukawa couplings and the mass matrices. A specific pattern of symmetry breaking is introduced to yield the cobimaximal mixing pattern—characterized by maximal atmospheric mixing ($\\theta_{23} = \\pi/4$), maximal CP violation ($\\delta = \\pm \\pi/2$), and zero reactor angle ($\\theta_{13} = 0$)—which is then perturbed to accommodate nonzero $\\theta_{13}$ consistent with observations. Leptogenesis is analyzed within this framework, focusing on the decay of heavy sterile neutrinos in the early Universe.
\n\n
作者构建了一个包含非阿贝尔味对称性 $\\Delta(27)$ 及额外阿贝尔离散对称性的逆跷跷板模型。这些对称性约束了汤川耦合和质量矩阵的结构。通过引入特定的对称性破缺模式，得到 cobimaximal 混合模式——其特征为最大大气混合角（$\\theta_{23} = \\pi/4$）、最大 CP 破坏（$\\delta = \\pm \\pi/2$）和零反应堆角（$\\theta_{13} = 0$）——随后引入微扰以容纳与观测一致的非零 $\\theta_{13}$。在此框架下分析了轻子生成机制，重点关注早期宇宙中重惰性中微子的衰变。

Result: The model successfully reproduces the observed neutrino oscillation parameters under the cobimaximal mixing ansatz with small corrections. Leptogenesis yields the correct order of magnitude for the baryon asymmetry of the Universe, but only when the light neutrino masses follow a normal hierarchy; the inverted hierarchy scenario fails to produce sufficient asymmetry.
\n\n
该模型在 cobimaximal 混合假设下通过小修正成功复现了观测到的中微子振荡参数。轻子生成机制能给出正确量级的宇宙重子不对称性，但仅当轻中微子质量遵循正常序；反常序情形无法产生足够的不对称性。

Conclusion: The inverse seesaw model based on $\\Delta(27)$ and discrete Abelian symmetries provides a theoretically motivated framework that simultaneously explains neutrino masses, cobimaximal mixing (with realistic corrections), and the baryon asymmetry via leptogenesis—but only in the normal neutrino mass hierarchy. This links flavor symmetry, neutrino phenomenology, and cosmology in a testable way.
\n\n
基于 $\\Delta(27)$ 和离散阿贝尔对称性的逆跷跷板模型提供了一个理论上有动机的框架，能够同时解释中微子质量、cobimaximal 混合（含符合实际的修正）以及通过轻子生成产生的重子不对称性——但仅限于正常中微子质量序。这以一种可检验的方式将味对称性、中微子唯象学和宇宙学联系起来。

Abstract: We present an inverse seesaw model based on the $Δ(27)$ symmetry and Abelian discrete symmetries, which account for the mass hierarchies and, through a specific pattern of symmetry breaking, leads to viable leptonic mixing angles according to the cobimaximal mixing pattern. In the model, leptogenesis successfully accounts for the observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe for a large range of the parameter space, only for the scenario of normal neutrino mass hierarchy.

### [21] [Flash from the Past: New Gamma-Ray Constraints on Light CP-even Scalar from SN1987A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08695)
*Yue Yu,Writasree Maitra,P. S. Bhupal Dev,Jean-Franccois Fortin,Steven P. Harris,Kuver Sinha,Yongchao Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper derives new constraints on light CP-even scalars by reanalyzing archival gamma-ray data from the Solar Maximum Mission (SMM) satellite toward SN1987A. The absence of an observed gamma-ray excess following the neutrino burst implies limits on the scalar–Higgs mixing angle.
\n\n
本文通过重新分析Solar Maximum Mission（SMM）卫星对SN1987A方向的历史伽马射线数据，推导出对轻CP-even标量粒子的新约束。在中微子暴发后未观测到伽马射线超出，从而对CP-even标量与Standard Model Higgs玻色子的混合角设定了新限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Light CP-even scalars, which may arise in extensions of the Standard Model, can be copiously produced in supernova cores through nucleon bremsstrahlung and subsequently decay into photons. The non-detection of such a signal from SN1987A provides a powerful probe of their coupling to the Standard Model, specifically via the mixing angle with the Higgs boson.
\n\n
轻CP-even标量粒子可能出现在Standard Model的扩展模型中，可通过核子轫致辐射过程在超新星核心大量产生，并随后衰变为光子。SN1987A方向未探测到此类信号，为它们与Standard Model的耦合（特别是通过与Higgs玻色子的混合角）提供了强有力的探针。

Method: The authors compute the production rate of light CP-even scalars in the SN1987A core via nucleon bremsstrahlung ($N + N \\to N + N + s$), model their escape and subsequent decay into photons (either directly $s \\to \\gamma\\gamma$ or via $s \\to \\ell^+\\ell^- \\to \\gamma\\gamma$), and compare the predicted gamma-ray flux with the SMM observational upper limits following the 1987 neutrino burst.
\n\n
作者计算了SN1987A核心中通过核子轫致辐射（$N + N \\to N + N + s$）产生的轻CP-even标量粒子产率，建模其逃逸及后续衰变为光子的过程（直接衰变$s \\to \\gamma\\gamma$或通过$s \\to \\ell^+\\ell^- \\to \\gamma\\gamma$），并将预测的伽马射线流量与SMM在1987年中微子暴发后观测到的上限进行比较。

Result: The non-observation of an excess gamma-ray signal by SMM leads to stringent new upper bounds on the mixing angle $\\sin\\theta$ between the CP-even scalar and the Standard Model Higgs boson, particularly for scalar masses in the MeV–GeV range.
\n\n
SMM未观测到伽马射线超出信号，从而对CP-even标量与Standard Model Higgs玻色子之间的混合角$\\sin\\theta$给出了新的严格上限，尤其适用于MeV–GeV质量区间的标量粒子。

Conclusion: Archival gamma-ray data from SN1987A remain a valuable resource for constraining light beyond-the-Standard-Model scalars. This work improves existing limits on Higgs-portal CP-even scalars by leveraging the high sensitivity of SMM to transient gamma-ray signals.
\n\n
SN1987A的历史伽马射线数据仍是限制轻超出Standard Model标量粒子的宝贵资源。本工作通过利用SMM对瞬态伽马射线信号的高灵敏度，改进了对Higgs-portal型CP-even标量粒子的现有约束。

Abstract: We derive new constraints on light CP-even scalars using old gamma-ray observations in the direction of SN1987A by the Solar Maximum Mission (SMM) satellite. Light scalars can be abundantly produced in the supernova core via the nucleon bremsstrahlung process, can stream out of the supernova-environment and decay into photons -- either primary photons or secondary photons from lepton-antilepton pairs -- thus leading to a gamma-ray signal. From the non-observation of excess photon flux by SMM after the detection of the neutrino burst from SN1987A, we set new constraints on the mixing angle of the CP-even scalar with the Standard Model Higgs boson.

</details>

### [22] [Fundamental Limits of Quantum Sensors for Gravitational Wave Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06772)
*Sergio Gaudio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Quantum sensors (optical clocks, squeezed light, quantum magnetometers) cannot directly detect gravitational waves unless they exploit the light propagation coupling mechanism; only this mechanism—used by laser and atom interferometers—provides sufficient transducer gain. Quantum enhancements are limited by classical noise: modest ($\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$) for LISA, but larger ($\mathcal{E} = 1.8$–$2.4$) for ground-based detectors in shot-noise-limited regimes.
\n\n
量子传感器（光钟、压缩光、量子磁力计）除非利用光传播耦合机制，否则无法直接探测引力波；只有激光干涉仪和原子干涉仪所采用的这一机制能提供足够的换能增益。量子增强受限于经典噪声：对LISA而言较小（$\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$），但在散粒噪声主导的地基探测器中较大（$\mathcal{E} = 1.8$–$2.4$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The rapid progress in quantum sensing technologies—such as optical clocks with $5.5\times10^{-19}$ systematic uncertainty, frequency-dependent squeezing below the standard quantum limit, and quantum magnetometers nearing fundamental sensitivity bounds—has prompted the question of whether these can be used to detect gravitational waves (GWs) either directly or by enhancing current GW detectors. This motivates a rigorous analysis of how GWs couple to quantum sensors at the fundamental level.
\n\n
量子传感技术的快速进展——如系统不确定度达 $5.5\times10^{-19}$ 的光钟、低于标准量子极限的频率相关压缩态、以及逼近基本灵敏度极限的量子磁力计——引发了以下问题：这些技术能否直接探测引力波（GWs），或用于增强现有引力波探测器？这促使人们从基本层面严格分析引力波如何与量子传感器耦合。

Method: The authors start from the tidal Hamiltonian in Fermi normal coordinates within linearized general relativity and non-relativistic quantum mechanics. They systematically identify and analyze three distinct physical coupling mechanisms between gravitational waves and quantum sensors: (1) internal atomic coupling (tidal distortion of electronic wavefunctions), (2) center-of-mass coupling (Doppler shifts due to geodesic deviation), and (3) light propagation coupling (phase accumulation over macroscopic paths). For each, they compute the transducer gain $G$, which quantifies the sensor's response per unit GW strain. They then evaluate the potential quantum enhancement $\mathcal{E}$ by analyzing the noise architecture of existing detectors (e.g., LISA and ground-based interferometers).
\n\n
作者从线性化广义相对论和非相对论量子力学框架下的Fermi正则坐标系中的潮汐哈密顿量出发，系统识别并分析了引力波与量子传感器之间的三种不同物理耦合机制：(1) 原子内禀耦合（电子波函数的潮汐形变），(2) 质心耦合（测地线偏离引起的多普勒频移），(3) 光传播耦合（宏观路径上的相位累积）。针对每种机制，他们计算了换能增益 $G$（即单位引力波应变下传感器的响应）。随后，通过分析现有探测器（如LISA和地基干涉仪）的噪声架构，评估了潜在的量子增强因子 $\mathcal{E}$。

Result: The three coupling mechanisms yield vastly different transducer gains: internal atomic coupling gives $G_A = 2.4\times10^{-20}$, with vanishing first-order energy shifts for $J=0$ clock states—rendering it ineffective for GW detection (a deficit of $\sim10^{35}$ compared to interferometry). Center-of-mass coupling achieves strain sensitivity $\sim10^{-18}$, still $10^4$ times worse than LISA’s requirement. Only light propagation coupling provides the large gain necessary for viable GW detection, which is why laser and atom interferometers work. Quantum enhancements are constrained by classical noise: LISA’s noise budget is $\sim91\%$ classical, limiting $\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$, while shot-noise-dominated ground-based detectors achieve $\mathcal{E} = 1.8$–$2.4$. Atom interferometers using this third mechanism uniquely access the 0.01–10 Hz band.
\n\n
三种耦合机制产生的换能增益差异巨大：原子内禀耦合给出 $G_A = 2.4\times10^{-20}$，且对所有 $J=0$ 钟态的一阶能量移动为零——使其无法用于引力波探测（相比干涉仪存在约 $10^{35}$ 的增益赤字）。质心耦合达到应变灵敏度 $\sim10^{-18}$，仍比LISA需求差 $10^4$ 倍。唯有光传播耦合能提供足够大的增益，使激光和原子干涉仪成为可行方案。量子增强受经典噪声限制：LISA的噪声预算中约91%为经典噪声，导致 $\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$；而散粒噪声主导的地基探测器可实现 $\mathcal{E} = 1.8$–$2.4$。利用第三种机制的原子干涉仪可独特覆盖0.01–10 Hz频段。

Conclusion: Direct gravitational wave detection with quantum sensors like optical clocks or magnetometers is fundamentally limited by weak coupling mechanisms; only detectors exploiting light propagation coupling (i.e., interferometers) achieve sufficient sensitivity. Quantum enhancements are possible but modest in space-based missions like LISA due to dominant classical noise, while more significant gains are achievable in ground-based detectors operating in the quantum-limited regime. Atom interferometers offer a promising path to the mid-frequency GW band (0.01–10 Hz) by leveraging the same high-gain coupling mechanism as optical interferometers.
\n\n
利用光钟或磁力计等量子传感器直接探测引力波在根本上受限于微弱的耦合机制；只有利用光传播耦合的探测器（即干涉仪）才能获得足够灵敏度。量子增强虽可能，但在LISA等空间任务中因经典噪声主导而效果有限，而在量子噪声主导的地基探测器中可获得更显著提升。原子干涉仪通过利用与光学干涉仪相同的高增益耦合机制，为探测中频段（0.01–10 Hz）引力波提供了有前景的路径。

Abstract: Recent advances in quantum sensing -- optical clocks at $5.5\times 10^{-19}$ systematic uncertainty, frequency-dependent squeezing below the standard quantum limit, quantum magnetometers approaching fundamental sensitivity limits -- raise a natural question: can these technologies detect gravitational waves directly, or enhance existing detectors beyond current capabilities? We show that the answer is primarily determined by the \emph{coupling mechanism} between the gravitational wave and the sensor. Starting from the tidal Hamiltonian in Fermi normal coordinates, we identify three physically distinct coupling mechanisms and derive their transducer gains within linearized general relativity and non-relativistic quantum mechanics. Internal atomic coupling (tidal distortion of electronic wavefunctions) yields a transducer gain $G_A = 2.4\times 10^{-20}$, with vanishing first-order energy shifts for all $J=0$ clock states -- a $\sim\!10^{35}$ deficit relative to laser interferometry that exceeds any projected quantum enhancement. Center-of-mass coupling (Doppler shifts from geodesic motion) reaches strain sensitivities of $\sim\!10^{-18}$, still $10^4$ above LISA requirements. Light propagation coupling (phase accumulation over macroscopic baselines) provides the enormous transducer gain that makes laser interferometry -- and atom interferometry -- viable. For detectors exploiting this third mechanism, we quantify how much improvement quantum sensors can provide through the detector's noise architecture: LISA's noise budget is $\sim\!91\%$ classical, limiting combined quantum enhancement to $\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$, while ground-based detectors in the shot-noise-dominated regime achieve $\mathcal{E} = 1.8$--$2.4$. Atom interferometers exploit the same light-propagation mechanism to uniquely access the 0.01--10~Hz band.

</details>


### [23] [Spectral sirens cosmology from binary black holes populations with sharper mass features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06792)
*Tom Bertheas,Vasco Gennari,Danièle Steer,Nicola Tamanini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Spectral-sirens inference using structured binary black hole mass models applied to GWTC-4.0 yields a 23% precise measurement of $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$, a ~50% improvement over previous BBH-only analyses, and competitive constraints on modified gravitational-wave propagation, highlighting the critical role of accurate population modeling in cosmological inference from gravitational waves.
\n\n
使用具有结构的双黑洞质量模型对GWTC-4.0进行Spectral-sirens推断，得到哈勃常数 $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$ 的23%精度测量，比以往仅用双黑洞（BBH）的分析提升约50%，并对修改的引力波传播给出有竞争力的限制，凸显了在引力波宇宙学推断中精确种群模型的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard siren cosmology typically requires electromagnetic counterparts or galaxy catalogs to break degeneracies between luminosity distance and redshift. Spectral-sirens circumvent this by exploiting the redshift-induced distortion of the observed black hole mass spectrum, which depends on both the intrinsic mass distribution and the cosmological model. However, this method is highly sensitive to assumptions about the binary black hole (BBH) population model. Previous analyses used overly simplistic mass functions, limiting cosmological precision. This work aims to improve spectral-sirens inference by introducing more flexible, physically motivated parametric mass models that better capture the observed structure in the BBH mass spectrum, thereby enabling more robust and precise cosmological constraints from gravitational-wave data alone.
\n\n
标准“标准汽笛”宇宙学通常需要电磁对应体或星系目录来打破光度距离与红移之间的简并。Spectral-sirens方法通过利用红移引起的黑洞质量谱形变（该形变同时依赖于本征质量分布和宇宙学模型）来规避这一需求。然而，该方法对双黑洞（BBH）种群模型的假设高度敏感。以往分析采用过于简化的质量函数，限制了宇宙学精度。本文旨在通过引入更灵活、更具物理动机的参数化质量模型（能更好捕捉BBH质量谱中的观测结构），改进spectral-sirens推断，从而仅从引力波数据中获得更稳健、更精确的宇宙学限制。

Method: The authors develop new parametric models for the intrinsic binary black hole primary mass function that incorporate features like peaks and breaks, going beyond simple power laws. They apply the spectral-sirens framework to the GWTC-4.0 catalog. In this framework, the observed redshifted mass distribution $p(m_{\\rm obs})$ is related to the intrinsic mass distribution $p(m)$ and the cosmological model via $p(m_{\\rm obs}) \\propto \\int p(m) p(z(m_{\\rm obs}, m)) \\frac{dV_c}{dz} \\frac{1}{(1+z)} dz$, where the mapping between observed mass $m_{\\rm obs}$, intrinsic mass $m$, and redshift $z$ is $m_{\\rm obs} = m(1+z)$. They perform a joint Bayesian inference of the population hyperparameters and cosmological parameters (e.g., $H_0$, parameters for modified GW propagation $\\Xi_0, n$). Model comparison is done using Bayesian evidence. Forecasts for the O5 observing run are generated using simulated populations.
\n\n
作者开发了新的双黑洞主质量本征分布参数化模型，包含峰和截断等特征，超越了简单的幂律。他们将spectral-sirens框架应用于GWTC-4.0目录。在此框架中，观测到的红移质量分布 $p(m_{\\rm obs})$ 通过公式 $p(m_{\\rm obs}) \\propto \\int p(m) p(z(m_{\\rm obs}, m)) \\frac{dV_c}{dz} \\frac{1}{(1+z)} dz$ 与本征质量分布 $p(m)$ 和宇宙学模型相关联，其中观测质量 $m_{\\rm obs}$、本征质量 $m$ 和红移 $z$ 的关系为 $m_{\\rm obs} = m(1+z)$。他们对种群超参数和宇宙学参数（如 $H_0$、修改引力波传播参数 $\\Xi_0, n$）进行联合贝叶斯推断。模型比较采用贝叶斯证据。O5观测运行的预测基于模拟种群生成。

Result: Using their improved mass models on GWTC-4.0, they measure the Hubble constant as $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$ (23% precision at 68% CL), a ~50% improvement over the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA BBH-only analysis. The new mass models are moderately favored by Bayesian evidence over simpler power-law models. They place competitive constraints on parameters of modified gravitational-wave propagation ($\\Xi_0, n$), but find uninformative bounds on dark energy equation-of-state parameters ($w_0, w_a$). Forecasts for the O5 run predict significant improvements in the precision of $H_0$ and modified propagation parameters due to a larger sample of higher-redshift events.
\n\n
利用其改进的质量模型分析GWTC-4.0，他们测得哈勃常数为 $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$（68%置信度下精度为23%），比LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA仅用双黑洞的分析提升约50%。新质量模型在贝叶斯证据上略优于简单的幂律模型。他们对修改引力波传播参数（$\\Xi_0, n$）给出了有竞争力的限制，但对暗能量状态方程参数（$w_0, w_a$）的限制则不具信息量。对O5运行的预测表明，由于更高红移事件样本量的增加，$H_0$ 和修改传播参数的精度将显著提高。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the precision of cosmological inference from gravitational waves via the spectral-sirens method is critically dependent on the fidelity of the assumed binary black hole population model. By employing more realistic mass functions that capture spectral features, they achieve a significant improvement in the constraint on $H_0$ from BBH data alone, rivaling results that require additional information from neutron stars or galaxy catalogs. This underscores that accurate astrophysical modeling is not just a systematic to be marginalized over, but a key ingredient for unlocking the full cosmological potential of current and future gravitational-wave observations.
\n\n
本研究表明，通过spectral-sirens方法从引力波进行宇宙学推断的精度，关键取决于所假设的双黑洞种群模型的保真度。通过采用能捕捉谱特征的更现实质量函数，他们仅用双黑洞数据就显著改进了对 $H_0$ 的限制，其效果可与需要中子星或星系目录额外信息的结果相媲美。这强调了精确的天体物理建模不仅是需要被边缘化的系统误差，更是释放当前及未来引力波观测全部宇宙学潜力的关键要素。

Abstract: Spectral-sirens inference enables the extraction of cosmological parameters from gravitational-wave data alone, without electromagnetic counterparts or galaxy catalogs. We introduce new parametric mass functions for the binary black hole population that capture significant structure across the mass spectrum and are moderately favoured by Bayesian evidence over simpler models. Analysing the latest gravitational-wave transient catalog, GWTC-4.0, we show that powerlaws-only population models constrain the Hubble constant to $23\%$ precision, $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$ at $68\%$ confidence level. This represents a $\sim 50\%$ improvement over the corresponding binary black hole-only analysis by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration, achieving precision comparable to their joint analyses including neutron stars and galaxy catalogs. We further test alternative cosmological models, establishing competitive constraints on modified gravitational-wave propagation, while bounds on the dark energy equation-of-state parameters remain uninformative. Projecting to future O5 observing run, we forecast substantial improvements in $H_0$ and modified propagation parameters with larger datasets at higher redshifts. Our results highlight the strong interplay between the black hole mass distribution and inferred cosmology, underscoring the need for suitable population models to fully exploit gravitational-wave data.

### [24] [Stationary Particle Creation and Entanglement in the Rotating Teo Wormhole: A Quantum Mode-Mixing Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06822)
*Ramesh Radhakrishnan,Gerald Cleaver,William Julius*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a quantum field theoretic analysis of massless scalar fields in the rotating Teo wormhole spacetime, revealing that geometric asymmetry due to rotation and frame dragging induces non-reciprocal vacuum mode mixing. This leads to exact analytic expressions for Bogoliubov coefficients, particle production, and entanglement entropy, interpreted as a stationary geometric analogue of the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect (ADCE).
\n\n
本文对旋转Teo虫洞时空中的无质量标量场进行了量子场论分析，揭示了由旋转和参考系拖曳引起的几何不对称性导致非互易的真空模混合。由此获得了Bogoliubov系数、粒子产生和纠缠熵的精确解析表达式，并将其解释为非对称动力学Casimir效应（ADCE）的一种静态几何类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand quantum effects in horizonless, rotating spacetimes—specifically how frame dragging and rotation induce vacuum polarization, particle creation, and entanglement without event horizons or explicit time dependence. The rotating Teo wormhole provides a clean theoretical laboratory to isolate these effects from black hole physics.
\n\n
动机在于理解无视界、旋转时空中的量子效应——特别是参考系拖曳和旋转如何在没有事件视界或显式时间依赖的情况下诱导真空极化、粒子产生和纠缠。旋转Teo虫洞提供了一个干净的理论实验室，可将这些效应与黑洞物理分离。

Method: The authors employ quantum field theory in curved spacetime, using the Bogoliubov transformation formalism. They define ``in'' and ``out'' vacuum modes on the two asymptotically flat regions of the rotating Teo wormhole. The effective radial potential, shaped by rotation and frame dragging, forms an asymmetric barrier, allowing exact calculation of scattering amplitudes via the WKB-like barrier-penetration exponent. This yields closed-form Bogoliubov coefficients $\\alpha_{\\omega\\omega'}$, $\\beta_{\\omega\\omega'}$, from which particle number $\\langle N_\\omega \\rangle = \\int |\\beta_{\\omega\\omega'}|^2 d\\omega'$ and two-mode entanglement entropy are derived.
\n\n
作者采用弯曲时空中的量子场论方法，使用Bogoliubov变换形式体系。他们在旋转Teo虫洞的两个渐近平直区域上定义“入”态和“出”态真空模。由旋转和参考系拖曳形成的径向有效势构成一个不对称势垒，可通过类似WKB的势垒穿透指数精确计算散射振幅。由此得到闭合形式的Bogoliubov系数$\\alpha_{\\omega\\omega'}$、$\\beta_{\\omega\\omega'}$，并进一步导出粒子数$\\langle N_\\omega \\rangle = \\int |\\beta_{\\omega\\omega'}|^2 d\\omega'$和双模纠缠熵。

Result: The paper derives exact analytic expressions for the Bogoliubov coefficients, mean particle number, and two-mode entanglement entropy as functions of the rotation parameter. It shows that co-rotating and counter-rotating modes scatter asymmetrically, leading to non-reciprocal quantum amplification. Crucially, particle creation arises purely from geometric asymmetry and boundary conditions in a stationary spacetime, not from time-dependent backgrounds. This effect is identified as a stationary geometric analogue of the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect (ADCE), where rotation replaces moving boundaries as the source of vacuum squeezing.
\n\n
论文推导出Bogoliubov系数、平均粒子数和双模纠缠熵关于旋转参数的精确解析表达式。结果表明，顺转和逆转模式经历不对称散射，导致非互易的量子放大。关键的是，粒子产生完全源于静态时空中的几何不对称性和边界条件，而非时变背景。该效应被识别为非对称动力学Casimir效应（ADCE）的一种静态几何类比，其中旋转取代了运动边界，成为真空压缩的来源。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that stationary, horizonless rotating wormholes can generate quantum particle production and entanglement through geometric asymmetry alone. This establishes a novel connection between frame-dragging-induced vacuum effects and the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect, highlighting that non-reciprocity and amplification can emerge in static spacetimes without horizons or time dependence, solely due to asymmetric scattering geometry.
\n\n
研究表明，静态、无视界的旋转虫洞仅通过几何不对称性即可产生量子粒子产生和纠缠。这建立了参考系拖曳诱导的真空效应与非对称动力学Casimir效应（ADCE）之间的新联系，表明非互易性和放大效应可在无视界、无时间依赖的静态时空中，仅由不对称散射几何而产生。

Abstract: Rotating traversable wormholes allow the effects of frame dragging and rotation to be studied in the absence of event horizons. We develop a quantum field theoretic treatment of massless scalar perturbations in the rotating Teo spacetime. This spacetime is an exact, stationary, horizonless wormhole connecting two asymptotically flat regions. Using the Bogoliubov transformation formalism, we construct ``in'' and ``out'' mode solutions defined on the two asymptotic regions and compute the Bogoliubov coefficients that quantify vacuum mode mixing.
  The effective radial potential induced by rotation and frame dragging forms an asymmetric scattering barrier. This geometric asymmetry allows an exact analytic evaluation of reflection and transmission amplitudes via the barrier-penetration exponent. This results in closed-form expressions for the Bogoliubov coefficients, the mean particle number, and the two-mode entanglement entropy as functions of the rotation parameter. The resulting amplification arises at the level of quantum Bogoliubov mode mixing and vacuum squeezing, rather than classical superradiant flux enhancement.
  Since this spacetime is stationary, particle creation originates from geometric asymmetry and boundary conditions, and not from explicit time dependence. Co-rotating and counter-rotating modes experience inequivalent scattering. This renders the process intrinsically non-reciprocal. We identify this mechanism as a stationary, geometric analogue of the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect (ADCE). In the rotating Teo geometry, rotation and frame dragging play the role that moving boundaries play in the dynamical Casimir effect, acting as the source of asymmetric vacuum mode mixing.

### [25] [Constraint Analysis and Quantization of Anomalous 2-D Thomas-Whitehead Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06995)
*Eric Biedke,Salvatore Quaid,Vincent Rodgers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the Hamiltonian structure and quantization of two-dimensional Thomas-Whitehead gravity, which extends the Polyakov action by promoting the diffeomorphism field—associated with Virasoro coadjoint orbits—to a dynamical variable. This modification resolves the issue of vanishing Hamiltonians present in conventional 2D gravity formulations across both light-cone and ADM formalisms.
\n\n
本文研究了二维Thomas-Whitehead引力的哈密顿结构与量子化，该理论通过将与Virasoro代数余伴随轨道相关的diffeomorphism场提升为动力学变量，从而推广了Polyakov作用量。这一修改解决了传统二维引力在light-cone和ADM形式体系下哈密顿量恒为零的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In standard two-dimensional gravity models derived from the Polyakov effective action—such as those arising from string theory or 2D fermions coupled to gravity—the reparameterization invariance leads to constraints that render the total Hamiltonian identically zero, even when analyzed in different gauges like the dynamical light-cone or ADM formalism. This obstructs meaningful physical evolution and quantization. The motivation is to resolve this degeneracy by embedding the theory into the Thomas-Whitehead gravity framework, where the coadjoint orbit representative (the diffeomorphism field) becomes dynamical, thereby potentially yielding a nontrivial Hamiltonian.
\n\n
在由Polyakov有效作用量导出的标准二维引力模型中（例如源于弦论或二维费米子耦合引力的情形），由于重参数化不变性，约束条件导致总哈密顿量恒为零，即使在dynamical light-cone或ADM形式等不同规范下亦如此。这阻碍了物理演化和量子化的实现。本文的动机是将理论嵌入Thomas-Whitehead引力框架，其中余伴随轨道的代表元（即diffeomorphism场）被提升为动力学变量，从而可能产生非平凡的哈密顿量。

Method: The authors perform a detailed constraint analysis using Dirac’s algorithm within both the dynamical light-cone gauge and the ADM (Arnowitt–Deser–Misner) formalism for 2D metrics. They start from the Thomas-Whitehead action, which generalizes the Polyakov action by introducing a dynamical diffeomorphism field $\\phi(x)$ tied to the projective connection on the Virasoro coadjoint orbit. The action includes terms like $\\int d^2x \\sqrt{-g} \\left( \\phi R + \\frac{1}{2}(\\nabla \\phi)^2 \\right)$, where $R$ is the Ricci scalar. They then derive the canonical momenta, identify primary and secondary constraints, and compute the total Hamiltonian. The analysis is repeated on a fixed Minkowski background to isolate gravitational dynamics from spacetime curvature effects.
\n\n
作者在dynamical light-cone规范和ADM（Arnowitt–Deser–Misner）形式下，使用Dirac约束算法对二维度规进行详细约束分析。他们从Thomas-Whitehead作用量出发，该作用量通过引入一个与Virasoro余伴随轨道上的射影联络相关的动力学diffeomorphism场$\\phi(x)$来推广Polyakov作用量。作用量包含形如$\\int d^2x \\sqrt{-g} \\left( \\phi R + \\frac{1}{2}(\\nabla \\phi)^2 \\right)$的项，其中$R$为Ricci标量。随后推导正则动量，识别初级与次级约束，并计算总哈密顿量。分析还在固定的Minkowski背景上重复进行，以分离引力动力学与时空曲率效应。

Result: The constraint analysis reveals that in the standard Polyakov theory, the Hamiltonian vanishes due to first-class constraints associated with diffeomorphism invariance. However, in the Thomas-Whitehead extension, the diffeomorphism field $\\phi$ acquires its own kinetic term, breaking the pure gauge nature of the symmetry. Consequently, the total Hamiltonian no longer vanishes; instead, it becomes a nontrivial functional of the canonical variables $(g_{ij}, \\pi^{ij}, \\phi, \\pi_\\phi)$. The algebra of constraints remains consistent, and the system admits a well-defined phase space suitable for quantization. This holds in both the light-cone and ADM formulations, and even when the background metric is fixed to Minkowski space.
\n\n
约束分析表明，在标准Polyakov理论中，由于与diffeomorphism不变性相关的一类约束，哈密顿量恒为零。然而，在Thomas-Whitehead推广中，diffeomorphism场$\\phi$获得了自身的动能项，打破了对称性的纯规范性质。因此，总哈密顿量不再为零，而是成为正则变量$(g_{ij}, \\pi^{ij}, \\phi, \\pi_\\phi)$的非平凡泛函。约束代数保持自洽，系统具有适合量子化的良定义相空间。这一结论在light-cone和ADM形式下均成立，即使背景度规固定为Minkowski时空亦然。

Conclusion: By promoting the diffeomorphism field—originally a parameter labeling Virasoro coadjoint orbits—to a dynamical degree of freedom via the Thomas-Whitehead formalism, the pathological vanishing of the Hamiltonian in two-dimensional gravity is resolved. This yields a consistent constrained Hamiltonian system amenable to canonical quantization, offering a novel pathway to define quantum gravity in two dimensions beyond the limitations of the Polyakov action.
\n\n
通过Thomas-Whitehead形式将原本仅作为Virasoro余伴随轨道标签的diffeomorphism场提升为动力学自由度，成功解决了二维引力中哈密顿量病态消失的问题。由此得到一个自洽的约束哈密顿系统，适用于正则量子化，为超越Polyakov作用量局限的二维量子引力提供了新路径。

Abstract: The two-dimensional effective Polyakov action is often realized as the anomalous contributions of string theories and fermions coupled to gravity in two-dimensions. However, as a result of the reparameterization invariance, one finds that the effective action produces vanishing Hamiltonians as constraints even in disparate gauges such as the dynamical light-cone and the ADM formalism of the metric. On the other hand, two-dimensional gravitational theories naturally arise as geometric actions on the coadjoint orbits of the Virasoro algebra. The Thomas-Whitehead gravity formalism extends the effective Polyakov action in such a way that the defining coadjoint element for the orbit becomes a dynamical field, viz the diffeomorphism field. In this work, we examine the constraint analysis and quantization of the Hamiltonian in the context of Thomas-Whitehead gravity using both the dynamical light-cone and the ADM formalisms of the metric. Constraint analysis is then repeated in a Minkowski background and with a dynamical action for the diffeomorphisms field arising from the Thomas-Whitehead action. Adding dynamics to the diffeomorphism field subsequently removes the vanishing Hamiltonians.

</details>


### [26] [Black hole solutions surrounded by an anisotropic fluid in a Kalb--Ramond two--form background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07052)
*Y. Sekhmani,A. Al-Badawi,Mohsen Fathi,A. Vachher,Sushant G. Ghosh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs exact static, spherically symmetric black hole solutions in a theory where gravity is non-minimally coupled to a Kalb--Ramond (KR) two-form field that spontaneously breaks Lorentz symmetry, with the spacetime also filled by an anisotropic fluid obeying $w_1 = -1$ and arbitrary $w_2$. The authors analyze curvature singularities, energy conditions, photon spheres, black hole shadows, and both weak and strong gravitational lensing. They find that the KR field and anisotropic fluid jointly enhance light deflection, especially for dark-energy-like fluids ($w_2 = -1/2$), and predict measurable deviations in SDL observables for Sgr A$^*$ and M87$^*$, offering new observational tests for string-motivated gravity and anisotropic dark matter.
\n\n
本文构建了在引力与Kalb--Ramond（KR）二形式场非最小耦合且该场自发破缺Lorentz对称性的理论中，精确的静态球对称黑洞解，其中时空还填充了满足 $w_1 = -1$ 且 $w_2$ 任意的各向异性流体。作者分析了曲率奇点、能量条件、光子球、黑洞阴影以及弱和强引力透镜效应。研究发现，KR场与各向异性流体共同增强光线偏折，尤其在类暗能量流体（$w_2 = -1/2$）背景下更为显著，并预测Sgr A$^*$和M87$^*$的强偏折极限（SDL）可观测量存在可测偏差，为弦论启发的KR引力和各向异性暗物质晕提供了新的观测检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring gravitational theories beyond General Relativity that are motivated by quantum gravity and string theory, specifically those involving spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking via antisymmetric tensor fields like the Kalb--Ramond (KR) field. Additionally, the presence of anisotropic matter distributions—such as those possibly describing dark matter halos or exotic compact objects—necessitates studying their interplay with modified gravity. The paper aims to derive exact black hole solutions in this context and identify unique observational signatures, particularly in gravitational lensing and shadow imaging, which can be tested with current (e.g., EHT) and future telescopes.
\n\n
动机源于探索受量子引力和弦论启发的广义相对论之外的引力理论，特别是通过Kalb--Ramond（KR）场等反对称张量场实现的自发Lorentz对称性破缺。此外，各向异性物质分布（如可能描述暗物质晕或奇异致密天体的分布）的存在，要求研究其与修改引力的相互作用。本文旨在推导此类背景下的精确黑洞解，并识别独特的观测特征，尤其是在引力透镜和阴影成像方面，这些特征可通过当前（如EHT）及未来望远镜进行检验。

Method: The authors consider a gravitational action with a non-minimal coupling between the Ricci scalar and the kinetic term of the Kalb--Ramond (KR) field, which triggers spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking. They assume a static, spherically symmetric ansatz and introduce an anisotropic fluid with equation of state $p_r = w_1 \\rho$, $p_t = w_2 \\rho$, setting $w_1 = -1$ while keeping $w_2$ arbitrary. Solving the modified Einstein equations yields exact black hole metrics parameterized by the KR coupling constant $\\ell$, fluid density scale $K$, and $w_2$. They compute curvature invariants (e.g., Kretschmann scalar) to verify singularities, check energy conditions, and determine event horizons. For lensing, they use the Gibbons--Werner method: applying the Gauss-Bonnet theorem to the optical metric to compute the weak deflection angle $\\hat{\\alpha}$, and employ the strong deflection limit (SDL) formalism to calculate observables like the angular radius of the relativistic images for Sgr A$^*$ and M87$^*$.
\n\n
作者考虑一个引力作用量，其中Ricci标量与Kalb--Ramond（KR）场的动能项非最小耦合，从而触发自发Lorentz对称性破缺。他们采用静态球对称度规假设，并引入满足状态方程 $p_r = w_1 \\rho$、$p_t = w_2 \\rho$ 的各向异性流体，设 $w_1 = -1$ 而 $w_2$ 任意。求解修正的Einstein方程得到由KR耦合常数 $\\ell$、流体密度参数 $K$ 和 $w_2$ 参数化的精确黑洞度规。他们计算曲率不变量（如Kretschmann标量）以验证奇点，检查能量条件并确定事件视界。在透镜分析中，采用Gibbons--Werner方法：将Gauss-Bonnet定理应用于光学度规以计算弱偏折角 $\\hat{\\alpha}$，并使用强偏折极限（SDL）形式计算Sgr A$^*$和M87$^*$的相对论性像角半径等可观测量。

Result: The paper obtains exact black hole solutions for various $w_2$ values (dust: $w_2=0$, radiation: $w_2=1/3$, dark energy-like: $w_2=-1/2$). Curvature analysis confirms a true central singularity. Energy conditions and global geometry depend critically on $\\ell$, $K$, and $w_2$. The photon sphere and shadow radii are modified compared to Schwarzschild. Using the Gauss-Bonnet theorem on the optical metric, the weak deflection angle is found to increase due to both the KR field and anisotropic fluid, with maximal enhancement for $w_2 = -1/2$. In the strong deflection limit, the logarithmic divergence coefficients ($\\bar{a}, \\bar{b}$) and resulting observables (angular separation, magnification) for Sgr A$^*$ and M87$^*$ show measurable deviations from GR predictions, scaling with $\\ell$ and $K$.
\n\n
论文获得了多种 $w_2$ 值下的精确黑洞解（尘埃：$w_2=0$，辐射：$w_2=1/3$，类暗能量：$w_2=-1/2$）。曲率分析确认存在真实的中心奇点。能量条件和整体几何结构强烈依赖于 $\\ell$、$K$ 和 $w_2$。光子球和阴影半径相较于Schwarzschild解发生改变。通过对光学度规应用Gauss-Bonnet定理，发现弱偏折角因KR场和各向异性流体而增大，在 $w_2 = -1/2$ 时增强效应最大。在强偏折极限下，Sgr A$^*$和M87$^*$的对数发散系数（$\\bar{a}, \\bar{b}$）及相应可观测量（角间距、放大率）均显示出相对于广义相对论预测的可测偏差，且偏差随 $\\ell$ 和 $K$ 变化。

Conclusion: The interplay between spontaneous Lorentz violation induced by a string-theoretic Kalb--Ramond field and anisotropic matter leads to black hole geometries with distinct observational imprints in both weak and strong gravitational lensing. These deviations—particularly enhanced light bending and altered SDL observables—provide concrete, testable signatures for probing fundamental physics beyond GR, including the nature of dark matter halos (if anisotropic) and the viability of KR gravity. Future high-resolution observations of black hole shadows and lensing by EHT and next-generation instruments can constrain the parameters $\\ell$ and $K$, thereby testing this class of modified gravity theories.
\n\n
弦论启发的Kalb--Ramond场诱导的自发Lorentz破缺与各向异性物质的相互作用，导致黑洞几何在弱和强引力透镜中产生独特的观测印记。这些偏差——尤其是增强的光线偏折和改变的强偏折极限（SDL）可观测量——为探测广义相对论之外的基本物理提供了具体且可检验的信号，包括暗物质晕（若为各向异性）的本质及KR引力的可行性。未来EHT及下一代仪器对黑洞阴影和透镜效应的高分辨率观测可约束参数 $\\ell$ 和 $K$，从而检验此类修改引力理论。

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric black hole spacetimes induced by the spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking of a Kalb--Ramond (KR) two-form field non--minimally coupled to gravity, coexisting with an anisotropic fluid. By adopting a general equation of state where the radial pressure relates to the energy density via $w_1 = -1$ and the tangential pressure via an arbitrary parameter $w_2$, we derive exact analytical solutions representing black holes surrounded by diverse matter fields, including dust ($w_2=0$), radiation ($w_2=1/3$), and dark energy-like distributions ($w_2=-1/2$). A rigorous analysis of curvature invariants confirms a genuine core singularity, while the global geometry and adherence to standard energy conditions are shown to be highly sensitive to the interplay between the KR coupling ($\ell$), the fluid density parameter ($K$), and $w_2$. Furthermore, we analyse null geodesics in detail to determine the photon sphere and shadow radii. Using the Gibbons--Werner geometrical approach and the Gauss-Bonnet theorem applied to the optical metric, we compute the weak deflection angle of light, demonstrating that both the KR field and the anisotropic fluid significantly enhance light bending, particularly in dark-energy-like backgrounds. Finally, we evaluate strong deflection limit (SDL) observables for the supermassive black holes Sgr A$^*$ and M87$^*$, revealing quantifiable deviations from standard Schwarzschild geometries. These results offer novel astrophysical signatures for constraining string-inspired KR gravity and anisotropic dark matter halos using current and future observations.

### [27] [Frozen Motion: Why Single Carrollian Scalars Cannot Propagate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07081)
*Andrew James Bruce*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper constructs intrinsic first-order scalar field theories on the Carrollian plane, minimally coupled to a Carrollian connection and invariant under extended Carrollian symmetries including supertranslations. While such symmetries permit a broad class of Lagrangians (requiring only spacetime coordinate independence), invariance under supertranslations enforces a static energy density and vanishing momentum density, thereby forbidding on-shell field propagation. Propagating dynamics thus require moving beyond minimally coupled single-field setups.
\n\n
本文构建了内生于Carrollian平面的一阶标量场理论，这些理论最小耦合于Carrollian联络，并在包含超平移（supertranslations）的扩展Carrollian变换下保持不变。尽管此类对称性允许一大类拉格朗日量（仅需不显含时空坐标），但超平移不变性强制能量密度静态、动量密度为零，从而禁止了壳层上的场传播。因此，若要获得具有传播性的动力学，必须超越最小耦合的单场理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore intrinsically defined field theories on Carrollian geometries—without taking ultra-relativistic limits of Lorentzian theories—and to understand how extended Carrollian symmetries, particularly supertranslations, constrain the dynamics of such theories. This addresses foundational questions about the viability of propagating degrees of freedom in non-Lorentzian settings relevant to holography, asymptotic symmetries, and flat space physics.
\n\n
动机在于探索内生于Carrollian几何的场论——而非通过Lorentzian理论的超相对论极限获得——并理解扩展的Carrollian对称性（尤其是超平移）如何约束此类理论的动力学。这涉及非Lorentzian背景下可传播自由度的可行性问题，与全息原理、渐近对称性及平直时空物理密切相关。

Method: The authors define first-order scalar field actions directly on the Carrollian plane, minimally coupled to a Carrollian connection. They impose invariance under the extended Carrollian group, which includes spatial rotations, time translations, and supertranslations (with boosts realized as linear supertranslations). The constraints imposed by these symmetries on the Lagrangian density and resulting conservation laws are analyzed using Noether’s theorem and geometric considerations.
\n\n
作者直接在Carrollian平面上定义一阶标量场作用量，其最小耦合于Carrollian联络。他们要求作用量在扩展Carrollian群下不变，该群包含空间旋转、时间平移和超平移（其中boost作为线性超平移实现）。通过Noether定理和几何分析，研究了这些对称性对拉格朗日密度及守恒律所施加的约束。

Result: Invariance under supertranslations forces the energy density $\\mathcal{E}$ to be time-independent ($\\partial_t \\mathcal{E} = 0$) and the momentum density $\\mathcal{P}_i$ to vanish identically. Consequently, the equations of motion admit no on-shell propagating solutions for a single minimally coupled scalar field. The most general allowed Lagrangian depends only on the field and its spatial derivatives, but cannot support wave-like dynamics.
\n\n
超平移不变性强制能量密度 $\\mathcal{E}$ 不随时间变化（$\\partial_t \\mathcal{E} = 0$），且动量密度 $\\mathcal{P}_i$ 恒为零。因此，单个最小耦合标量场的运动方程不存在壳层上的传播解。所允许的最一般拉格朗日量仅依赖于场及其空间导数，但无法支持波动型动力学。

Conclusion: Truly dynamical, propagating field theories on Carrollian spacetimes cannot be realized within the framework of single, minimally coupled first-order scalar fields respecting extended Carrollian symmetry. To achieve propagation, one must consider either non-minimal couplings, higher-derivative terms, multiple fields, or relax certain symmetry assumptions—highlighting a fundamental tension between Carrollian supertranslation invariance and local dynamics.
\n\n
在Carrollian时空中，若要求满足扩展Carrollian对称性，则单个最小耦合的一阶标量场无法实现真正具有传播性的动力学。要获得传播行为，必须考虑非最小耦合、高阶导数项、多场体系，或放松某些对称性假设——这揭示了Carrollian超平移不变性与局域动力学之间的根本张力。

Abstract: We investigate a class of first-order scalar field theories minimally coupled to a Carrollian connection that are defined intrinsically on the Carrollian plane, i.e., the theories are not defined via limits of Lorentzian theories. The theories built are invariant under the extended Carrollian transformations which include supertranslations. The symmetry allows for a large class of Lagrangians, independence of spacetime coordinates is all that is required. However, invariance under supertranslations (which include boosts as linear supertranslations) forces the energy density to be static and the momentum density to vanish -- this precludes on-shell propagation of fields. Thus, to have propagating theories, one must move beyond single field theories that are minimally coupled to the geometry.

### [28] [Bounding the number of spacetime dimensions from precessing black hole binaries with the third-generation gravitational-wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07102)
*Xu-Jie Zhu,Ji-Yu Song,Tao Zhu,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detectors—Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer—can constrain extra-dimensional theories by analyzing precessing binary black hole mergers. By combining luminosity distance measurements from GWs with redshift information from galaxy catalogs (dark siren method), the authors show that orbital precession significantly sharpens distance and redshift estimates, leading to tighter bounds on the number of spacetime dimensions $D$ and the screening scale $R_{\rm c}$. They forecast $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ and $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$ at 68% credibility, improving prior constraints by an order of magnitude.
\n\n
本文研究了第三代引力波（GW）探测器——爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和宇宙探索者（Cosmic Explorer）——如何通过分析进动双黑洞并合事件来限制额外维度理论。作者结合引力波的光度距离测量与星系目录提供的红移信息（即“暗标准汽笛”方法），表明轨道进动显著提高了距离和红移估计的精度，从而对时空维度数 $D$ 和额外维度的屏蔽尺度 $R_{\rm c}$ 给出更紧的限制。他们预测在68%可信度下 $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ 且 $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$，比此前基于GWTC-3的分析提升约一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the fact that in models with extra spatial dimensions, gravitational waves can propagate into these extra dimensions, causing a faster-than-expected amplitude decay compared to four-dimensional general relativity. This modifies the inferred luminosity distance of GW sources. By comparing the GW-inferred luminosity distance with the electromagnetic redshift (or statistical redshift from galaxy catalogs), one can test deviations from standard 4D gravity and thus probe the existence and properties of extra dimensions. Third-generation detectors offer unprecedented sensitivity, making it timely to assess their potential for such fundamental tests using realistic signal populations, particularly those including spin-induced orbital precession which enhances parameter estimation accuracy.
\n\n
动机源于额外空间维度模型中引力波可泄漏至额外维度，导致其振幅衰减快于四维广义相对论的预期，从而修正引力波源的光度距离。通过比较引力波推断的光度距离与电磁红移（或来自星系目录的统计红移），可检验对标准四维引力的偏离，进而探测额外维度的存在及其性质。第三代探测器具有前所未有的灵敏度，因此有必要评估其利用真实信号样本（特别是包含自旋诱导轨道进动的系统，因其可提升参数估计精度）进行此类基础物理检验的潜力。

Method: The authors simulate a one-year dataset of detectable precessing binary black hole merger signals for the Einstein Telescope–Cosmic Explorer network. They perform parameter estimation using the Fisher information matrix formalism, which approximates the posterior distribution around the true parameters. Redshift information is incorporated via the “dark siren” approach: instead of assuming perfect redshift knowledge, they use a hierarchical Bayesian framework that marginalizes over possible host galaxies in a catalog, assigning redshift probabilities based on sky localization and distance estimates. The modified luminosity distance in $D$-dimensional gravity is modeled as $d_L^{\rm GW} \propto d_L^{\rm EM}^{(D-2)/(D-3)}$, where $d_L^{\rm EM}$ is the electromagnetic luminosity distance. The screening scale $R_{\rm c}$ enters as a cutoff below which extra-dimensional effects are suppressed; for sources at distances $\ll R_{\rm c}$, standard 4D behavior is recovered.
\n\n
作者模拟了爱因斯坦望远镜–宇宙探索者探测器网络在一年内可探测到的进动双黑洞并合信号数据集。他们采用Fisher信息矩阵方法进行参数估计，该方法在真实参数附近近似后验分布。红移信息通过“暗标准汽笛”方法引入：不假设完美红移知识，而是在分层贝叶斯框架下对星系目录中可能的宿主星系进行边缘化，根据天区定位和距离估计分配红移概率。在 $D$ 维引力中，引力波光度距离被建模为 $d_L^{\rm GW} \\propto d_L^{\rm EM}^{(D-2)/(D-3)}$，其中 $d_L^{\rm EM}$ 为电磁光度距离。屏蔽尺度 $R_{\rm c}$ 作为截断尺度引入——当源距离远小于 $R_{\rm c}$ 时，额外维度效应被抑制，恢复标准四维行为。

Result: The inclusion of orbital precession significantly improves the measurement precision of the luminosity distance and reduces the uncertainty in the inferred redshift range. This leads to substantially tighter constraints on the extra-dimensional parameters. The projected constraints from one year of observation are $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ and $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$ at the 68% credible level. These results represent an improvement by approximately one order of magnitude compared to current constraints derived from the GWTC-3 catalog using second-generation detectors.
\n\n
引入轨道进动显著提高了光度距离的测量精度，并缩小了推断红移范围的不确定性，从而对额外维度参数给出更紧的限制。基于一年观测的预测结果为：在68%可信度下 $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ 且 $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$。相比当前基于第二代探测器和GWTC-3目录所得的限制，该结果提升约一个数量级。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that third-generation gravitational wave observatories, when combined with galaxy catalogs and analyses that account for spin precession, will be powerful probes of extra-dimensional physics. The improved angular resolution and distance precision from precessing systems enable stringent tests of deviations from four-dimensional general relativity. The projected sensitivities provide a benchmark for future tests of fundamental gravity and highlight the importance of including higher-order waveform effects like precession in cosmological and theoretical studies with gravitational waves.
\n\n
本工作表明，第三代引力波天文台结合星系目录及考虑自旋进动的分析方法，将成为探测额外维度物理的有力工具。进动系统带来的更高角分辨率和距离精度，使得对四维广义相对论偏离的检验更加严格。所预测的灵敏度为未来基础引力理论的检验提供了基准，并强调了在引力波宇宙学和理论研究中纳入进动等高阶波形效应的重要性。

Abstract: In the theories with extra dimensions, gravitational waves can leak into extra dimensions, resulting in a reduction in the amplitude of the observed gravitational waves. Such an effect modifies the standard luminosity distance of gravitational wave sources, which enables constraining extra dimensions by measuring both the luminosity distance and redshift from gravitational wave events. The main purpose of this paper is to assess the capacity of the third-generation gravitational wave detector network, Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer, to constrain the theory of extra dimensions through observations of precessing binary black hole mergers. To this end, we generate a dataset of signals of precessing binary black hole mergers detectable by the detector network with one year of observations. We then employ the Fisher information matrix method for parameter estimation, together with a dark siren approach that obtains the redshift information from the galaxy catalog within a hierarchical Bayesian framework. Our results show that the precession in the binary system can significantly improve the precision of the luminosity distances and narrow their redshift ranges, thus leading to a tighter constraint on the extra dimensions. Based on this approach, we constrain the number of spacetime dimensions $D$ and the screening scale $R_{\rm c}$ of the extra dimensions, obtaining $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ and $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$ at $68\%$ credible level. This result improves previous ones from an analysis with GWTC-3 by about one order of magnitude. This work provides theoretical foundations and projected sensitivities for future third-generation gravitational wave observations in exploring the effects of extra dimensions.

</details>


### [29] [Dyonic black holes from dimensional reduction of five-dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07125)
*Z. Belkhadria,S. Mignemi,F. Paderi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates black hole solutions in dimensionally reduced five-dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, revealing novel features such as extremal mass in neutral configurations and modified thermodynamics where extremal black holes possess nonzero temperature and entropy.
\n\n
本文研究了五维Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet引力经维度约化后的黑洞解，揭示了中性情形下存在极值质量等新特征，并发现极值黑洞具有非零温度和熵，表明热力学性质被显著修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how higher-curvature corrections—specifically the Gauss-Bonnet term—in five dimensions affect black hole physics upon dimensional reduction to four dimensions, particularly in comparison with standard Kaluza-Klein theory which lacks such corrections.
\n\n
动机在于探索高阶曲率修正（特别是Gauss-Bonnet项）在五维引力中如何通过维度约化影响四维黑洞物理，尤其是与不含此类修正的标准Kaluza-Klein理论进行对比。

Method: The authors perform a dimensional reduction of five-dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, yielding an effective four-dimensional theory comprising gravity, a $U(1)$ gauge field (electromagnetism), and a scalar dilaton-like field, with nonlinear interactions and nontrivial couplings induced by the Gauss-Bonnet term. They then solve the resulting field equations to obtain static, spherically symmetric black hole solutions parameterized by mass $M$, electric charge $Q_e$, and magnetic charge $Q_m$.
\n\n
作者对五维Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet引力进行维度约化，得到一个包含引力、$U(1)$规范场（电磁场）和类dilaton标量场的有效四维理论，其中Gauss-Bonnet项诱导出非线性相互作用和非平凡耦合。随后求解所得场方程，获得由质量$M$、电荷$Q_e$和磁荷$Q_m$参数化的静态球对称黑洞解。

Result: The solutions exhibit distinct properties compared to standard Kaluza-Klein black holes: even neutral black holes ($Q_e = Q_m = 0$) admit an extremal limit with a minimum mass, and extremal black holes possess nonzero Hawking temperature $T \\neq 0$ and finite entropy $S > 0$, violating the usual extremality condition $T = 0$.
\n\n
所得解与标准Kaluza-Klein黑洞相比具有显著差异：即使中性黑洞（$Q_e = Q_m = 0$）也存在一个具有极小质量的极值极限；且极值黑洞具有非零Hawking温度$T \\neq 0$和有限熵$S > 0$，违背了通常的极值条件$T = 0$。

Conclusion: The inclusion of the Gauss-Bonnet term fundamentally alters the structure and thermodynamics of black holes in dimensionally reduced theories, demonstrating that higher-curvature corrections can lead to qualitatively new phenomena not captured by conventional Kaluza-Klein reductions.
\n\n
引入Gauss-Bonnet项从根本上改变了维度约化理论中黑洞的结构与热力学性质，表明高阶曲率修正可导致标准Kaluza-Klein约化无法捕捉的全新物理现象。

Abstract: We study the general black hole solutions of dimensionally reduced five-dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. The reduced theory contains gravity, electromagnetism and a scalar field, with nonlinear corrections to the action and nontrivial couplings. The solutions can be classified through mass and electric and magnetic charge. They present peculiar features with respect to the solutions of the standard Kaluza-Klein theory without Gauss-Bonnet corrections, like the existence of an extremal mass even in the neutral case. Also the thermodynamics is affected, for example, extremal black holes display nonvanishing temperature and entropy.

</details>


### [30] [Periodic Orbits and Gravitational Radiation from Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals as Probes of Black Hole Quantum Hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07168)
*Yiru Zhang,Meirong Tang,Zhaoyi Xu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how quantum hair—a small near-horizon correction to classical black hole geometry induced by quantum vacuum polarization—affects orbital dynamics and gravitational-wave emission in extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs). It shows that the quantum hair parameter $\\gamma$ shifts key orbital radii (MBO and ISCO), modifies the $E$-$L$ phase space, enhances zoom-whirl behavior, and induces measurable gravitational-wave phase dephasing, offering a potential observational signature for quantum gravity with future detectors.
\n\n
本文研究了量子毛发（quantum hair）——由量子真空极化在黑洞视界附近引入的微小几何修正——如何影响极端质量比旋进系统（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）中的轨道动力学和引力波辐射。研究表明，量子毛发参数 $\\gamma$ 会移动关键轨道半径（边际束缚轨道 MBO 和最内稳定圆轨道 ISCO），改变能量-角动量（$E$-$L$）相空间结构，增强 zoom-whirl 轨道行为，并导致可测量的引力波相位失配（phase dephasing），为未来探测器检验量子引力效应提供了潜在观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical no-hair theorem implies that black holes are featureless except for mass, charge, and angular momentum, leaving no room for probing their microscopic or quantum structure through external observations. However, quantum effects such as vacuum polarization may generate 'quantum hair'—small deviations from the classical metric near the horizon—which could encode information about quantum gravity. The motivation is to explore whether such quantum corrections leave detectable imprints on orbital motion and gravitational-wave signals from EMRIs, thereby enabling empirical tests of quantum gravity with next-generation observatories like LISA.
\n\n
经典无毛定理（no-hair theorem）表明黑洞仅由质量、电荷和角动量完全刻画，无法通过外部观测探知其微观或量子结构。然而，量子效应（如真空极化）可能在视界附近产生“量子毛发”——即对经典度规的微小偏离——其中可能蕴含量子引力的信息。本文旨在探究此类量子修正是否会在极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）系统的轨道运动和引力波信号中留下可观测印记，从而为利用LISA等下一代空间引力波天文台检验量子引力提供理论依据。

Method: The authors model the spacetime of a quantum-corrected Schwarzschild black hole using a metric that includes a quantum hair parameter $\\gamma$, derived from effective field theory considerations of vacuum polarization. They compute modifications to the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) by analyzing the effective potential for timelike geodesics. Orbital dynamics are classified using the rational number $q = \\Delta \\phi / (2\\pi)$, where $\\Delta \\phi$ is the azimuthal angle advance per radial period, to identify zoom-whirl behavior. Gravitational-wave waveforms are generated via the Numerical Kludge approach, which maps geodesic motion onto flat-spacetime radiation formulas, allowing them to quantify frequency drifts and phase dephasing due to $\\gamma$.
\n\n
作者采用一个包含量子毛发参数 $\\gamma$ 的度规来描述量子修正的Schwarzschild黑洞时空，该度规源于真空极化的有效场论（effective field theory）考虑。他们通过分析类时测地线的有效势，计算了边际束缚轨道（MBO）和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）的修正。利用有理数 $q = \\Delta \\phi / (2\\pi)$（其中 $\\Delta \\phi$ 为每个径向周期的方位角增量）对轨道动力学进行分类，以识别 zoom-whirl 行为。引力波波形通过 Numerical Kludge 方法生成，该方法将测地线运动映射到平直时空的辐射公式上，从而量化由 $\\gamma$ 引起的基频漂移和相位失配。

Result: The quantum hair parameter $\\gamma$ causes measurable shifts in the radii and specific angular momenta of both the MBO and ISCO: for positive $\\gamma$, these orbits move outward compared to the classical Schwarzschild case. This expands the allowed region in the energy-angular momentum ($E$-$L$) phase space for bound orbits. Furthermore, quantum corrections increase the prevalence of zoom-whirl orbits (characterized by rational $q$ values close to integers). Gravitational-wave modeling shows that $\\gamma$ modifies the effective potential, leading to small but cumulative changes in the three fundamental frequencies ($\\Omega_r, \\Omega_\\theta, \\Omega_\\phi$), which manifest as phase dephasing $\\Delta \\Phi \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1)$ over long EMRI waveforms—potentially detectable by LISA-like missions.
\n\n
量子毛发参数 $\\gamma$ 导致 MBO 和 ISCO 的轨道半径及单位质量角动量发生可观测的偏移：当 $\\gamma > 0$ 时，这些轨道相比经典 Schwarzschild 情况向外移动，从而扩大了束缚轨道在能量-角动量（$E$-$L$）相空间中的允许区域。此外，量子修正增强了 zoom-whirl 轨道（对应于接近整数的有理数 $q$）的出现概率。引力波建模表明，$\\gamma$ 改变了有效势，引起三个基本频率（$\\Omega_r, \\Omega_\\theta, \\Omega_\\phi$）的微小但累积性变化，进而在长时间 EMRI 波形中产生 $\\Delta \\Phi \\sim \\mathcal{O}(1)$ 量级的相位失配——这一效应有望被 LISA 类任务探测到。

Conclusion: Quantum hair introduces theoretically consistent and observationally relevant modifications to black hole spacetimes, altering both orbital structure and gravitational-wave signatures in EMRIs. These effects provide a concrete dynamical fingerprint of quantum-gravitational corrections near the event horizon. Future space-based interferometers like LISA could constrain or detect the quantum hair parameter $\\gamma$, thereby offering an unprecedented opportunity to test semi-classical quantum gravity in the strong-field regime.
\n\n
量子毛发在理论上自洽且具有观测意义，它改变了黑洞时空的轨道结构和 EMRI 系统的引力波特征，为事件视界附近的量子引力修正提供了明确的动力学指纹。未来的空间干涉仪（如 LISA）有望限制或探测量子毛发参数 $\\gamma$，从而为在强场区域检验半经典量子引力理论提供前所未有的机会。

Abstract: The classical no-hair theorem states that stationary black holes in general relativity can be completely described by only a small set of global parameters. Within this framework, no additional geometric structures are expected to persist outside the event horizon. However, quantum vacuum polarization may introduce small modifications to the near-horizon geometry, effectively giving rise to what is known as quantum hair. Such corrections may provide a possible window into the microscopic structure and thermodynamic properties of black holes. In this work, we examine how the quantum hair parameter γ influences the periodic orbital dynamics of test bodies in extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and their associated gravitational-wave emission. We find that γ significantly modifies the characteristic radii and angular momenta of two important circular orbits, namely the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), leading to a shift in the allowed region of the energy-angular momentum (E-L) phase space. Based on the rational number q classification, we further show that quantum corrections tend to enhance the zoom-whirl orbital behavior.Gravitational-wave calculations using the Numerical Kludge approach indicate that quantum hair alters the effective spacetime potential, produces small drifts in the fundamental orbital frequencies, and consequently leads to observable phase dephasing in longduration signals. These results provide a dynamical signature for distinguishing quantum-corrected black holes from classical Schwarzschild ones and offer theoretical motivation for testing quantum gravity effects with future space-based gravitational-wave observatories.

</details>


### [31] [Gravitational waves from warm inflation in the weak dissipative regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07662)
*Orlando Luongo,Tommaso Mengoni,Paulo M. Sá*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper extends the study of gravitational-wave background generation in a unified warm inflation and dark sector model to the weak dissipation regime, showing enhanced detectability by future observatories compared to the strong dissipation case.
\n\n
本文将统一暖暴胀与暗区模型中引力波背景生成的研究扩展到弱耗散区域，表明与强耗散情形相比，其未来探测器的可观测性有所增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous studies demonstrated that a two-scalar-field cosmological model unifying warm inflation and the dark sector can produce a potentially detectable stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB). However, these analyses were limited to the strong dissipation regime of warm inflation. The motivation here is to explore whether the weak dissipation regime—characterized by different thermal and quantum dynamics—can yield distinct or enhanced gravitational-wave signatures that improve detection prospects with next-generation detectors like LISA, BBO, or DECIGO.
\n\n
先前研究表明，统一暖暴胀与暗区的双标量场宇宙学模型可产生潜在可探测的随机引力波背景（SGWB），但这些分析仅限于暖暴胀的强耗散区域。本文旨在探索弱耗散区域——其具有不同的热力学与量子动力学特性——是否能产生独特或增强的引力波信号，从而提升LISA、BBO或DECIGO等下一代探测器的探测前景。

Method: The authors compute the full gravitational-wave energy spectrum $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$ in the weak dissipation regime of warm inflation using the formalism of continuous Bogoliubov coefficients. This approach accounts for the time-dependent particle production during inflation due to interactions between the inflaton, radiation, and metric perturbations. The model involves two scalar fields: one driving warm inflation and the other acting as a dark sector component, with dissipative dynamics governed by a friction coefficient $\\Upsilon$ satisfying $\\Upsilon \\ll 3H$ (weak dissipation). The resulting tensor power spectrum is integrated over the inflationary history and converted into $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$, which is then compared against sensitivity curves of future gravitational-wave observatories.
\n\n
作者采用连续Bogoliubov系数形式计算暖暴胀弱耗散区域中的完整引力波能量谱 $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$。该方法考虑了暴胀期间由于暴胀子、辐射与度规扰动相互作用导致的时变粒子产生。模型包含两个标量场：一个驱动暖暴胀，另一个作为暗区成分，其耗散动力学由摩擦系数 $\\Upsilon$ 控制，满足 $\\Upsilon \\ll 3H$（弱耗散）。所得张量功率谱在暴胀历史中积分并转换为 $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$，随后与未来引力波天文台的灵敏度曲线进行比较。

Result: The analysis reveals that the weak dissipation regime produces a gravitational-wave spectrum with enhanced amplitude at certain frequencies compared to the strong dissipation regime. This enhancement arises from the interplay between thermal fluctuations and the slower decay of the inflaton’s energy density, leading to a more efficient amplification of tensor modes. When benchmarked against detector sensitivities (e.g., LISA, BBO), the weak dissipation scenario yields a signal-to-noise ratio that improves the likelihood of detection, making it a more promising target for observational cosmology.
\n\n
分析表明，与强耗散区域相比，弱耗散区域在某些频率上产生的引力波谱振幅更强。这种增强源于热涨落与暴胀子能量密度较慢衰减之间的相互作用，从而更有效地放大张量模。当与探测器灵敏度（如LISA、BBO）对比时，弱耗散情形的信噪比更高，提升了探测可能性，使其成为观测宇宙学中更具前景的目标。

Conclusion: The weak dissipation regime in unified warm inflation–dark sector models offers a viable and observationally favorable pathway for generating a detectable primordial gravitational-wave background. This work underscores the importance of dissipation dynamics in shaping the SGWB and suggests that future gravitational-wave missions should prioritize parameter regions associated with weak dissipation in warm inflation scenarios.
\n\n
在统一暖暴胀–暗区模型中，弱耗散区域为产生可探测的原初引力波背景提供了一条可行且观测上更有利的路径。本工作强调了耗散动力学在塑造随机引力波背景（SGWB）中的关键作用，并建议未来的引力波任务应优先关注暖暴胀情景中与弱耗散相关的参数区域。

Abstract: Previous work on the gravitational-wave background generated in a two-scalar-field cosmological model, in which warm inflation and the dark sector are unified within a single framework, has shown that the resulting spectrum could be potentially detectable by planned next-generation gravitational-wave observatories. In this work, we extend this analysis to the weak dissipation regime of warm inflation, highlighting how the features of the inflationary scenario play a crucial role in the production of gravitational waves. The full gravitational-wave energy spectrum is calculated using the formalism of continuous Bogoliubov coefficients. By comparing our results with those obtained in the strong dissipation regime and with the sensitivity curves of future detectors, we find that the weak dissipation regime improves the prospects for observational detection.
