### [32] [Shadows and Polarization Images of a Four-dimensional Gauss-Bonnet Black Hole Irradiated by a Thick Accretion Disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07185)
*Xiao-Xiong Zeng,Huan Ye,Muhammad Israr Aslam,Rabia Saleem*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate shadows and polarized images of spherically symmetric Gauss-Bonnet (GB) black holes surrounded by thick accretion flows using general relativistic ray-tracing. Two emission models—phenomenological RIAF-like and analytical Hou disk—are employed. The GB coupling parameter $λ$ and observer inclination $θ$ significantly affect image morphology, brightness, and polarization. In the RIAF-like model, larger $λ$ shrinks and dims higher-order images, while larger $θ$ distorts their shape and obscures the horizon silhouette. Anisotropic emission induces vertical stretching, yielding elliptical higher-order rings. In the Hou disk model, higher-order images narrow with increasing $λ$, and $θ$ boosts direct emission brightness without altering higher-order ring size—contrasting sharply with RIAF behavior. Polarization patterns in the Hou model trace emission structure and encode spacetime geometry via $λ$ and $θ$. These findings demonstrate that intensity and polarization in thick-disk scenarios serve as powerful diagnostics for GB gravity and near-horizon accretion physics.\n\n我们采用广义相对论光线追踪方法研究被几何厚吸积流包裹的球对称Gauss-Bonnet（GB）黑洞的阴影和偏振图像。使用两种辐射模型：唯象的RIAF类模型和解析的Hou盘模型。GB耦合参数$λ$和观测倾角$θ$显著影响图像形态、亮度和偏振。在RIAF类模型中，更大的$λ$会缩小并变暗高阶图像，而更大的$θ$会扭曲其形状并遮蔽视界轮廓；各向异性辐射导致高阶图像在垂直方向拉伸，呈现椭圆形态。在Hou盘模型中，随着$λ$增大，高阶图像变得更窄；而$θ$增强高阶图像外直接辐射的亮度，却几乎不改变高阶图像尺寸——这与RIAF模型形成鲜明对比。Hou盘产生的偏振图样追踪亮度结构，并受$λ$和$θ$调制，反映时空的内禀几何。这些结果表明，在厚盘模型中，强度和偏振可作为探测GB黑洞及近视界吸积动力学的有效探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to explore observational signatures of modified gravity—specifically Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) theory—through black hole imaging. While EGB gravity introduces a dimensionless coupling $λ$ that alters spacetime near compact objects, its imprints on realistic accretion environments remain underexplored. Traditional thin-disk models are inadequate for capturing strong-gravity effects in low-luminosity systems like Sgr A*. Thus, the authors adopt geometrically thick accretion flow models (RIAF-like and Hou disk) to assess how $λ$ and viewing angle $θ$ influence shadow morphology, higher-order photon rings, and polarized emission—key observables for next-generation Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) campaigns.\n\n本文旨在通过黑洞成像探索修改引力理论（特别是Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet（EGB）理论）的观测特征。EGB引力引入无量纲耦合参数$λ$，改变致密天体附近的时空结构，但其在真实吸积环境中的印记尚未充分研究。传统薄盘模型不足以刻画如Sgr A*等低光度系统中的强引力效应。因此，作者采用几何厚吸积流模型（RIAF类和Hou盘），评估$λ$和观测角$θ$如何影响阴影形态、高阶光子环和偏振辐射——这些是下一代事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测的关键可观测量。

Method: The authors employ general relativistic ray-tracing in the spacetime of spherically symmetric Gauss-Bonnet black holes. They compute null geodesics backward from the observer’s camera to the emission region, incorporating both intensity and polarization transport. Two accretion models are used: (1) a phenomenological RIAF-like model with radially dependent emissivity and optional anisotropic emission; (2) an analytical Hou disk based on a conical approximation, which yields a geometrically thick but locally thin structure in certain regions. The polarization is calculated using the geodesic deviation of the polarization vector parallel-transported along null rays. Key parameters varied are the GB coupling $λ$ and observer inclination $θ$, with analysis focused on direct images, higher-order lensed images, and associated polarization patterns.\n\n作者在球对称Gauss-Bonnet黑洞时空中进行广义相对论光线追踪，从观测者相机反向计算零测地线，并包含强度与偏振的传输。采用两种吸积模型：(1) 一个具有径向依赖发射率且可选各向异性辐射的唯象RIAF类模型；(2) 基于锥形近似的解析Hou盘模型，该模型在某些区域呈几何厚但局部薄的结构。偏振通过沿零测地线平行输运的偏振矢量的测地线偏离计算。关键变量为GB耦合参数$λ$和观测倾角$θ$，分析聚焦于直接图像、高阶透镜图像及其关联的偏振图样。

Result: In the RIAF-like model, increasing $λ$ reduces the size and brightness of higher-order images; increasing $θ$ distorts their shape and masks the black hole shadow boundary. Anisotropic emission causes vertical elongation, producing elliptical high-order rings. In contrast, the Hou disk model shows that higher-order images become narrower with larger $λ$, and $θ$ enhances the brightness of direct emission outside the photon ring without significantly changing the ring size—diverging from RIAF predictions. Moreover, the Hou disk generates polarization maps that closely follow the brightness distribution and are modulated by $λ$ and $θ$, directly encoding spacetime curvature effects. These differences highlight model-dependent signatures of GB gravity in thick accretion flows.\n\n在RIAF类模型中，增大$λ$会减小高阶图像的尺寸和亮度；增大$θ$会扭曲其形状并掩盖黑洞阴影边界。各向异性辐射导致垂直方向拉伸，形成椭圆高阶环。相比之下，Hou盘模型显示：随着$λ$增大，高阶图像变得更窄；而$θ$增强光子环外直接辐射的亮度，却几乎不改变环尺寸——与RIAF预测明显不同。此外，Hou盘产生的偏振图样紧密跟随亮度分布，并受$λ$和$θ$调制，直接编码时空曲率效应。这些差异凸显了厚吸积流中GB引力的模型依赖性特征。

Conclusion: Intensity and polarization imaging of geometrically thick accretion flows around Gauss-Bonnet black holes provide distinct, measurable signatures of modified gravity. The dependence of image morphology and polarimetric structure on the GB coupling $λ$ and observer angle $θ$ varies significantly between accretion models (RIAF-like vs. Hou disk), underscoring the necessity of accurate accretion physics in interpreting EHT observations. Future high-resolution polarimetric measurements can thus constrain $λ$ and discriminate between gravity theories, provided that realistic emission models are employed.\n\n对Gauss-Bonnet黑洞周围几何厚吸积流的强度与偏振成像提供了修改引力的独特可观测特征。图像形态和偏振结构对GB耦合参数$λ$及观测角$θ$的依赖性在不同吸积模型（RIAF类 vs. Hou盘）间存在显著差异，这强调了在解释EHT观测时必须采用精确的吸积物理模型。因此，未来的高分辨率偏振测量可在采用真实辐射模型的前提下约束$λ$并区分不同引力理论。

Abstract: We adopt a general relativistic ray-tracing approach to study the shadows and polarization images of spherically symmetric Gauss-Bonnet (GB) black holes enveloped by geometrically thick accretion flows. Specifically, we adopt a phenomenological RIAF-like model and an analytical Hou disk model. In the RIAF-like model, increasing the GB coupling parameter $λ$ reduces both the size and brightness of the higher-order image, while increasing $θ$ alters the shape of the higher-order image and obscures the horizon's outline. The main difference between isotropic and anisotropic emission is that the latter produce distortion of the high-order image in the vertical direction, leading to an elliptical morphology. For the Hou disk model, due to specific regions being geometrically thinner with the conical approximation, the high-order images are narrower with the increase in $λ$ than the RIAF model. While increasing $θ$ enhances the brightness of the direct images outside the higher-order images, but hardly changes the size of the higher-order images, which is in sharp contrast to the RIAF model. Meanwhile, the Hou disk produces polarization patterns that trace the brightness configuration and are affected by $λ$ and $θ$, reflecting the intrinsic structure of spacetime. These results illustrate that intensity and polarization in thick-disk models provide probes of GB black holes and near-horizon accretion dynamics.

### [33] [Black Hole Mergers as the Fastest Photon Ring Scramblers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08643)
*D. Giataganas,G. F. Giudice,A. Ianniccari,A. J. Iovino,A. Kehagias,F. Quevedo,D. Perrone,A. Riotto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper shows that the remnant of a binary black hole merger can be accurately modeled as an effective Kerr black hole whose parameters maximize the instability rate of null geodesics, revealing a profound link between merger dynamics and unstable photon orbits.
\n\n
本文表明，双黑洞并合的残余物可以被精确地建模为一个有效Kerr黑洞，其参数使零测地线的不稳定性增长率最大化，揭示了并合动力学与不稳定光子轨道之间的深刻联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the conjecture that black holes are nature’s fastest scramblers, implying that their dynamics should saturate chaos bounds linked to the instability of null geodesics. The authors aim to test whether binary black hole mergers naturally produce remnants that maximize this instability rate, thereby connecting gravitational wave observations with fundamental aspects of black hole physics.
\n\n
动机源于“黑洞是自然界最高效的scrambler”这一猜想，意味着其动力学应饱和与零测地线不稳定性相关的混沌界限。作者旨在检验双黑洞并合是否自然产生使该不稳定性增长率最大化的残余黑洞，从而将引力波观测与黑洞物理的基本性质联系起来。

Method: The authors map the instantaneous mass $M(t)$ and angular momentum $J(t)$ of two non-spinning black holes in a quasi-circular inspiral onto the mass and spin of an effective Kerr black hole. They then compute the Lyapunov exponent associated with unstable null geodesics (photon orbits) around this effective geometry and show that the merger remnant corresponds to the configuration that maximizes this exponent.
\n\n
作者将准圆轨道上两个无自旋黑洞的瞬时质量$M(t)$和角动量$J(t)$映射到一个有效Kerr黑洞的质量和自旋上。然后计算该有效几何中不稳定零测地线（光子轨道）对应的Lyapunov指数，并证明并合残余物恰好对应于使该指数最大化的构型。

Result: The final state of the binary black hole merger aligns with extraordinary precision to the effective Kerr black hole configuration that maximizes the Lyapunov exponent governing the instability of null geodesics. This agreement holds across different mass ratios and suggests universality in the remnant properties dictated by chaotic scattering dynamics.
\n\n
双黑洞并合的终态以极高的精度对应于使控制零测地线不稳定性增长的Lyapunov指数最大化的有效Kerr黑洞构型。该一致性在不同质量比下均成立，表明残余黑洞的性质由混沌散射动力学所决定，并具有普适性。

Conclusion: The results support a deep connection between black hole scrambling, chaotic dynamics of null geodesics, and the outcome of binary mergers. This implies that the endpoint of black hole coalescence is not arbitrary but is instead selected by extremizing a fundamental property—namely, the instability rate of photon orbits—linking general relativity, quantum information, and nonlinear dynamics.
\n\n
结果支持黑洞scrambling、零测地线的混沌动力学与双黑洞并合结果之间存在深刻联系。这表明黑洞并合的终点并非任意，而是通过极值化一个基本性质——即光子轨道的不稳定性增长率——所选定，从而将广义相对论、量子信息与非线性动力学联系起来。

Abstract: Black holes are the most efficient scramblers in nature. By mapping the instantaneous mass and angular momentum of two spinless black holes in a quasi-circular binary onto those of an effective Kerr black hole, we demonstrate that the final state of the merger remnant corresponds with remarkable accuracy to the configuration that renders null geodesics unstable at the highest possible rate. This suggests a deep connection between the properties of black holes resulting from binary mergers and their unstable null orbits.

</details>


### [34] [Flat subspaces of the $SL(n,\mathbb{R})$ chiral equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07385)
*I. A. Sarmiento-Alvarado,P. Wiederhold,T. Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a method to generate exact higher-dimensional vacuum solutions to Einstein's equations by reducing them to a chiral equation under the presence of $n$ commuting Killing vectors. The spacetime metric is block-diagonal, and the problem reduces to solving a matrix-valued chiral model coupled with constraints on an auxiliary function $f$. An ansatz based on generalized harmonic parameters $\xi^a$ satisfying a Laplace-type equation is introduced, and commuting matrices $A_a = g_{,\xi^a} g^{-1}$ are used to satisfy the associated Killing equation.
\n\n
本文提出了一种在存在 $n$ 个对易 Killing 矢量的情况下，通过将真空 Einstein 场方程约化为一个 chiral 方程来构造高维精确解的方法。时空度规呈块对角形式，问题简化为求解一个矩阵值的 chiral 模型，并辅以关于辅助函数 $f$ 的约束条件。作者引入了一个基于广义调和参数 $\xi^a$（满足 Laplace 型方程）的 ansatz，并利用彼此对易的矩阵 $A_a = g_{,\xi^a} g^{-1}$ 来满足相应的 Killing 方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the difficulty of finding exact solutions to the vacuum Einstein field equations in higher dimensions, which are crucial for exploring black hole physics, string theory compactifications, and gravitational dualities. By exploiting spacetimes with $n$ commuting Killing vectors, the authors aim to reduce the complexity of Einstein’s equations to a more tractable integrable system—the chiral equation—thereby enabling systematic construction of new exact solutions.
\n\n
该工作的动机源于在高维中寻找真空 Einstein 场方程精确解的困难，而这些解对于研究黑洞物理、弦论紧化以及引力对偶性至关重要。通过利用具有 $n$ 个对易 Killing 矢量的时空，作者旨在将 Einstein 方程的复杂性降低为一个更易处理的可积系统——chiral 方程，从而系统性地构造新的精确解。

Method: The authors consider an $(n+2)$-dimensional vacuum spacetime with $n$ commuting Killing vectors, leading to a metric ansatz $\hat{g} = f(\rho, \zeta)(d\rho^2 + d\zeta^2) + g_{\mu\nu}(\rho, \zeta) dx^\mu dx^\nu$, where $g_{\mu\nu}$ is an $SL(n, \mathbb{R})$-valued matrix. The vacuum Einstein equations reduce to a chiral equation: $(\rho g_{,z} g^{-1})_{,\bar{z}} + (\rho g_{,\bar{z}} g^{-1})_{,z} = 0$, with $z = \rho + i\zeta$, and two additional equations for $f$. They introduce parameters $\xi^a(z, \bar{z})$ satisfying a generalized Laplace equation $(\rho \xi^a_{,z})_{,\bar{z}} + (\rho \xi^a_{,\bar{z}})_{,z} = 0$, and assume $g = g(\xi^a)$. This leads to $A_a = g_{,\xi^a} g^{-1}$ obeying the Killing-type condition $A_{a,\xi^b} + A_{b,\xi^a} = 0$. Crucially, they impose that the matrices $A_a$ commute, which ensures integrability and satisfaction of the chiral equation.
\n\n
作者考虑一个具有 $n$ 个对易 Killing 矢量的 $(n+2)$ 维真空时空，导出度规 ansatz：$\hat{g} = f(\rho, \zeta)(d\rho^2 + d\zeta^2) + g_{\mu\nu}(\rho, \zeta) dx^\mu dx^\nu$，其中 $g_{\mu\nu}$ 是取值于 $SL(n, \mathbb{R})$ 的矩阵。真空 Einstein 方程约化为 chiral 方程：$(\rho g_{,z} g^{-1})_{,\bar{z}} + (\rho g_{,\bar{z}} g^{-1})_{,z} = 0$（其中 $z = \rho + i\zeta$），以及关于 $f$ 的两个附加方程。他们引入满足广义 Laplace 方程 $(\rho \xi^a_{,z})_{,\bar{z}} + (\rho \xi^a_{,\bar{z}})_{,z} = 0$ 的参数 $\xi^a(z, \bar{z})$，并假设 $g = g(\xi^a)$。这导致 $A_a = g_{,\xi^a} g^{-1}$ 满足 Killing 型条件 $A_{a,\xi^b} + A_{b,\xi^a} = 0$。关键在于，他们施加了矩阵 $A_a$ 彼此对易的条件，从而保证可积性并满足 chiral 方程。

Result: The method successfully reduces the vacuum Einstein equations in $(n+2)$ dimensions with $n$ commuting Killing vectors to a solvable system: a chiral model for $g \in SL(n, \mathbb{R})$ and scalar equations for $f$. By introducing generalized harmonic coordinates $\xi^a$ and assuming commutativity of the connection-like matrices $A_a$, the authors ensure that the chiral equation and associated constraints are satisfied. This provides a constructive framework for generating new families of exact higher-dimensional vacuum solutions.
\n\n
该方法成功地将具有 $n$ 个对易 Killing 矢量的 $(n+2)$ 维真空 Einstein 方程约化为一个可解系统：一个关于 $g \in SL(n, \mathbb{R})$ 的 chiral 模型和关于 $f$ 的标量方程。通过引入广义调和坐标 $\xi^a$ 并假设类联络矩阵 $A_a$ 的对易性，作者确保了 chiral 方程及相关约束条件的满足。这为生成新的高维真空精确解族提供了一个构造性框架。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a systematic procedure to construct exact vacuum solutions in higher-dimensional gravity by leveraging integrable structures arising from spacetime symmetries. The reduction to a chiral model, combined with the ansatz involving generalized harmonic parameters and commuting $A_a$ matrices, offers a powerful tool for exploring the solution space of Einstein’s equations beyond four dimensions.
\n\n
本文建立了一种系统性的程序，通过利用由时空对称性产生的可积结构来构造高维引力中的真空精确解。通过将问题约化为 chiral 模型，并结合基于广义调和参数和对易 $A_a$ 矩阵的 ansatz，为探索四维以外 Einstein 方程的解空间提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a method for finding exact solutions to the vacuum Einstein field equations in higher dimensions from a given solution to the chiral equation. When considering a $n + 2$-dimensional spacetime with $n$ commutative Killing vectors, the metric tensor can take the form $\hat g = f ( ρ, ζ) ( d ρ^2 + d ζ^2 ) + g_{μν} ( ρ, ζ) d x^μd x^ν$. Then, the Einstein field equations in vacuum reduce to a chiral equation, $( ρg_{, z} g ^{-1} )_{, \bar z} + ( ρg_{, \bar z} g ^{-1} )_{, z} = 0$, and two differential equations, $( \ln f ρ^{1-1/n} )_{, Z} = \fracρ{2} \operatorname{tr} ( g_{, _Z} g^{-1} )^2$, where $g \in SL( n, \mathbb{R} )$ is the normalized matrix representation of $g_{μν}$, $z = ρ+ i ζ$ and $Z = z, \bar z$. We use the ansatz $g = g ( ξ^a )$, where the parameters $ξ^a$ depend on $z$ and $\bar z$ and satisfy a generalized Laplace equation, $( ρξ^a _{, z} )_{, \bar z} + ( ρξ^a _{, \bar z} )_{, z} = 0$. The chiral equation to the Killing equation, $A_{a , ξ^b} + A_{b , ξ^a} = 0$, where $A_a = g_{, ξ^a} g^{-1}$. Furthermore, we assume that the matrices $A_a$ commute with each other; in this way, they fulfill the Killing equation.

</details>


### [35] [Can Oscillatory and Persistent Nonlinearities Be Bridged in Black Hole Ringdown?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07469)
*Jun-Xi Shi,Zhen-Tao He,Jiageng Jiao,Jing-Qi Lai,Caiying Shao,Yu Tian,Hongbao Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper establishes a quantitative link between quadratic quasinormal modes (QQNMs)—nonlinear near-zone black hole ringdown excitations—and the Christodoulou memory effect—a permanent displacement in gravitational wave strain at null infinity—via bridge coefficients determined by the remnant black hole’s parameters. This connection offers a new observational test of nonlinear general relativity with future space-based detectors.
\n\n
本文建立了二次准正规模（Quadratic Quasinormal Modes, QQNMs）——黑洞近区非线性铃宕激发态——与Christodoulou记忆效应——在类光无穷远处引力波应变的永久位移——之间的定量联系，该联系通过由残余黑洞参数决定的“桥接系数”（bridge coefficients）实现。这一关联为利用未来空间引力波探测器检验广义相对论的非线性机制提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the apparent disconnect between two fundamental nonlinear phenomena in gravitational wave physics: the near-horizon dynamics encoded in QQNMs and the asymptotic memory effect at null infinity. Understanding whether these seemingly distinct manifestations of nonlinearity in general relativity are physically connected addresses a foundational question about the global structure of nonlinear perturbations around black holes and provides a novel consistency check for strong-field gravity.
\n\n
动机源于引力波物理中两个基本非线性现象之间表面上的脱节：由QQNMs编码的近视界动力学与在类光无穷远处的渐近记忆效应。探究这些看似不同的广义相对论非线性表现是否在物理上相互关联，有助于回答关于黑洞周围非线性微扰全局结构的基础性问题，并为强场引力提供一种新的自洽性检验。

Method: The authors introduce “bridge coefficients” that analytically relate the amplitudes of quadratic quasinormal modes in the near zone to the magnitude of the Christodoulou memory effect measured at null infinity. These coefficients are derived using black hole perturbation theory and depend primarily on the mass $M$ and spin $a$ of the remnant black hole formed after merger. The method leverages the causal structure of spacetime and conservation laws to connect near-horizon nonlinear mode coupling to asymptotic waveform memory.
\n\n
作者引入“桥接系数”（bridge coefficients），通过解析方式将近区二次准正规模的振幅与在类光无穷远处测得的Christodoulou记忆效应幅度联系起来。这些系数利用黑洞微扰理论推导得出，主要依赖于并合后形成的残余黑洞的质量 $M$ 和自旋 $a$。该方法利用时空的因果结构和守恒律，将近视界处的非线性模耦合与渐近波形记忆效应关联起来。

Result: The paper demonstrates that QQNMs and the Christodoulou memory effect are not independent but are quantitatively linked through bridge coefficients that are functions of the remnant black hole’s mass and spin. This relation implies that measuring either the memory effect or the QQNM content in ringdown signals can constrain the other, enabling cross-validation of nonlinear GR predictions. The effect is potentially detectable by future space-based interferometers like LISA.
\n\n
论文表明，QQNMs 与 Christodoulou 记忆效应并非独立，而是通过依赖于残余黑洞质量与自旋的桥接系数定量关联。这一关系意味着，通过测量铃宕信号中的记忆效应或 QQNM 成分，可相互约束对方，从而实现对广义相对论非线性预言的交叉验证。该效应有望被 LISA 等未来空间干涉仪探测到。

Conclusion: The established bridge between near-zone nonlinear dynamics (QQNMs) and asymptotic memory provides a unified view of nonlinear gravitational radiation in general relativity. It opens a new observational window into the nonlinear regime of black hole spacetimes and offers a robust test of GR’s self-consistency across different regions of spacetime—near horizon and null infinity—using gravitational-wave data.
\n\n
所建立的近区非线性动力学（QQNMs）与渐近记忆效应之间的桥梁，为广义相对论中非线性引力辐射提供了统一视角。它开辟了观测黑洞时空非线性机制的新窗口，并利用引力波数据，在时空不同区域（近视界与类光无穷远）对广义相对论的自洽性提供了稳健检验。

Abstract: Quadratic quasinormal modes (QQNMs) and Christodoulou memory effect are key nonlinear phenomena in gravitational wave physics. QQNMs characterize the near zone nonlinear response of a perturbed black hole, whereas the memory effect is a nonlinear remnant imprinted at null infinity by outgoing radiation. This naturally raises the question of whether and in what sense the two can be bridged. We show that they are related through bridge coefficients which depend primarily on remnant black hole parameters during ringdown. Future space-based gravitational-wave detectors can probe this relation. These results provide a new avenue for testing gravity and a fresh perspective on the nonlinear regime of general relativity.

*Joon-Hwi Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: An all-orders worldline effective action for the Kerr-Newman black hole is constructed within twistor particle theory, revealing exact hidden symmetries in self-dual backgrounds.
\n\n
在扭量粒子理论中构建了Kerr-Newman黑洞的全阶世界线有效作用量，揭示了自对偶背景中的精确隐藏对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to uncover a unified and exact description of the dynamics of charged rotating black holes by leveraging the geometric structure of twistor theory, which naturally encodes spin and electromagnetic coupling. This approach seeks to expose hidden symmetries that are not manifest in conventional spacetime formulations, especially in self-dual gravitational-electromagnetic backgrounds.
\n\n
本文旨在利用扭量理论的几何结构（自然编码自旋与电磁耦合）来获得带电旋转黑洞动力学的统一且精确描述。该方法试图揭示在常规时空表述中不明显的隐藏对称性，尤其是在自对偶引力-电磁背景中。

Method: The authors employ twistor particle theory to construct a worldline effective action valid to all orders in the black hole's spin and charge. By reformulating the Kerr-Newman solution in terms of twistors, they exploit the integrability properties of self-dual backgrounds to identify conserved charges and symmetry generators. The method combines first-quantized worldline formalism with twistorial phase space techniques to achieve an exact effective action.

作者采用扭量粒子理论构建一个对黑洞自旋和电荷全阶有效的世界线有效作用量。通过将Kerr-Newman解用扭量重新表述，他们利用自对偶背景的可积性来识别守恒荷与对称性生成元。该方法结合了一阶量子化世界线形式与扭量相空间技术，以获得精确的有效作用量。

Result: The paper successfully derives an all-orders worldline effective action for the Kerr-Newman black hole, fully incorporating spin and charge effects. Moreover, it identifies exact hidden symmetries—such as infinite-dimensional algebras or higher-spin extensions—associated with self-dual sectors of the background geometry, which constrain scattering amplitudes and classical observables.

Conclusion: The construction demonstrates that twistor particle theory provides a powerful framework for capturing the full nonlinear dynamics of Kerr-Newman black holes and reveals deep algebraic structures underlying self-dual gravity coupled to electromagnetism. These hidden symmetries may have implications for the Cosmological Bootstrap, amplitude techniques, and integrable systems in curved spacetime.

该构造表明，扭量粒子理论为捕捉Kerr-Newman黑洞的完整非线性动力学提供了一个强大框架，并揭示了自对偶引力与电磁场耦合背后深刻的代数结构。这些隐藏对称性可能对Cosmological Bootstrap、振幅方法以及弯曲时空中的可积系统具有重要意义。

Abstract: An all-orders worldline effective action for Kerr-Newman black hole is achieved in twistor particle theory. Exact hidden symmetries are identified in self-dual backgrounds.

### [37] [Josephson Effects in Slowly Rotating Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07553)
*Nurmukhammed Aytimbetov,Reggie C. Pantig,Ali Övgün,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Javlon Rayimbaev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper analyzes Josephson effects in slowly rotating stationary spacetimes, distinguishing gravitational redshift (lapse function) from frame-dragging (shift vector) contributions. At linear order in rotation parameter $a$, redshift governs AC/DC Josephson responses while rotational effects only appear in interferometric or phase-transport-sensitive setups via Sagnac-type shifts.
\n\n
本文分析了慢速旋转稳态时空中的Josephson效应，区分了引力红移（lapse函数）与参考系拖曳（shift矢量）的贡献。在旋转参数$a$的一阶近似下，红移主导AC/DC Josephson响应，而旋转效应仅在干涉或相位输运敏感的构型中通过Sagnac型相移显现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to disentangle gravitational redshift and rotational frame dragging in quantum coherent phenomena like the Josephson effect in curved spacetime, especially in light of recent work [10.1007/JHEP02(2026)006]. Understanding how general relativistic effects modify superconducting circuits is crucial for both fundamental physics and potential applications in relativistic quantum sensing.
\n\n
动机源于需要在弯曲时空中的量子相干现象（如Josephson效应）中解耦引力红移与旋转参考系拖曳效应，特别是受近期工作[10.1007/JHEP02(2026)006]启发。理解广义相对论效应对超导电路的修正，对基础物理和相对论性量子传感应用至关重要。

Method: The authors employ a covariant $3+1$ spacetime decomposition in the Eulerian/ZAMO (Zero Angular Momentum Observer) frame, using gauge-invariant phase dynamics and conserved supercurrents. They expand all quantities to linear order in the Kerr rotation parameter $a$, treating the lapse function as static up to $\mathcal{O}(a^2)$ and isolating rotational effects through the shift vector. Josephson relations are expressed both in terms of proper local observables and asymptotic Killing-time quantities.
\n\n
作者采用协变的$3+1$时空分解，在Eulerian/ZAMO（零角动量观测者）框架下，利用规范不变的相位动力学与守恒超流。他们将所有量展开至Kerr旋转参数$a$的一阶，将lapse函数视为静态形式（误差为$\mathcal{O}(a^2)$），并通过shift矢量分离旋转效应。Josephson关系既用局域固有观测量表达，也用渐近Killing时间观测量表达。

Result: At $\mathcal{O}(a)$, gravitational redshift—encoded in the lapse function—fully determines the AC Josephson frequency shift and the DC critical current scaling, which remain identical to the static case. Rotational frame dragging, encoded in the shift vector, does not affect these quantities unless there is azimuthal condensate momentum or spatial phase transport. However, in RF-driven interferometers, frame dragging induces Sagnac-type phase offsets, while the DC fluxoid quantization condition remains unshifted at linear order.
\n\n
在$\mathcal{O}(a)$阶，引力红移（由lapse函数编码）完全决定了AC Josephson频率偏移和DC临界电流的标度，其结果与静态情形相同。参考系拖曳（由shift矢量编码）仅在存在方位角凝聚体动量或空间相位输运时才影响这些量。然而，在射频驱动的干涉仪中，参考系拖曳会引入Sagnac型相位偏移，而DC fluxoid量子化条件在当前一阶近似下保持不变。

Conclusion: The study establishes a clear separation between lapse-driven redshift effects and shift-driven rotational contributions in Josephson physics within stationary spacetimes. It provides a consistent theoretical framework for analyzing superconducting quantum interference devices (SQUIDs) and related circuits in general relativistic settings, highlighting that rotation only modifies Josephson responses in configurations sensitive to global time synchronization or spatial phase gradients.
\n\n
本研究在稳态时空中为Josephson物理建立了清晰的lapse驱动红移效应与shift驱动旋转贡献的分离。它为在广义相对论背景下分析超导量子干涉器件（SQUIDs）及相关电路提供了自洽的理论框架，并指出旋转仅在对全局时间同步或空间相位梯度敏感的构型中修正Josephson响应。

Abstract: We investigate Josephson phenomena in a slowly rotating stationary spacetime, emphasizing the distinct roles of gravitational redshift and rotational frame dragging motivated by [10.1007/JHEP02(2026)006]. Using a covariant formulation based on gauge-invariant phase dynamics and conserved currents within a $3+1$ decomposition, we analyze both AC and DC Josephson effects and interferometric configurations. Restricting attention to linear order in the rotation parameter $a$, and working in the Eulerian/ZAMO frame, we show that in the slow-rotation slicing adopted here the lapse function agrees with its static (Schwarzschild-type) form up to $\mathcal{O}(a^2)$, while rotational effects enter through the shift vector. Consequently, redshift effects on Josephson frequencies and DC critical currents remain unchanged relative to the non-rotating case at $\mathcal{O}(a)$. The AC Josephson relation retains its redshifted structure when expressed in terms of proper voltages and reduces to the standard flat-spacetime form when formulated in terms of asymptotic (Killing-time) observables. Likewise, the DC critical current measured at infinity scales with a single power of the lapse function and is unaffected by rotation at linear order in the absence of azimuthal condensate momentum. Rotational effects become relevant only in configurations sensitive to spatial phase transport or to synchronization with respect to the global time coordinate. In particular, RF-driven interferometric setups can acquire Sagnac-type phase offsets associated with frame dragging, whereas the DC fluxoid constraint remains unshifted at linear order in the present approximation. Our results provide a clean separation between lapse-driven redshift effects and shift-driven rotational contributions in Josephson physics and furnish a consistent framework for superconducting circuits in stationary spacetimes.

</details>


### [38] [Black Hole Topologies and Geodesic Structures in Symmetric Teleparallel f(Q) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07576)
*G. G. L. Nashed,A. Eid*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates static, circularly symmetric black hole solutions in $(2+1)$-dimensional symmetric teleparallel gravity using a power-law $f(Q)$ model. It derives exact solutions for both charged and uncharged cases, revealing stronger central singularities than in general relativity, horizon modifications due to charge and non-metricity parameters, and geodesic-dependent singularity accessibility. Thermodynamic stability is confirmed, and topological features are analyzed via the Euler characteristic.
\n\n
本文在$(2+1)$维对称teleparallel引力框架下，采用幂律形式的$f(Q)$模型，研究静态、圆对称黑洞解。推导了带电与不带电情形的精确解，发现其中心奇点比广义相对论中更强；电荷和非度规性参数会改变视界结构；奇点是否可被测地线到达取决于电荷存在与否。通过温度、熵和热容验证了热力学稳定性，并利用欧拉示性数分析了拓扑性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring how modified gravity theories—specifically symmetric teleparallel gravity based on non-metricity—alter black hole physics in lower dimensions. Unlike general relativity, where $(2+1)$-dimensional black holes require a cosmological constant (e.g., BTZ), $f(Q)$ gravity may yield richer structures even without it. The authors aim to understand the interplay between non-metricity, electric charge, and topology in shaping black hole geometry, singularities, and thermodynamics.
\n\n
该研究的动机在于探索修改引力理论——特别是基于非度规性（non-metricity）的对称teleparallel引力——如何在低维情形下改变黑洞物理。不同于广义相对论中$(2+1)$维黑洞需依赖宇宙学常数（如BTZ黑洞），$f(Q)$引力即使在无宇宙学常数时也可能产生更丰富的结构。作者旨在理解非度规性、电荷与拓扑之间的相互作用如何影响黑洞几何、奇点性质及热力学行为。

Method: The authors adopt a power-law ansatz $f(Q) = c_1 Q + c_4 Q^n$ in $(2+1)$-dimensional symmetric teleparallel gravity, where $Q$ is the non-metricity scalar. They assume static, circular symmetry and solve the field equations for both charged (with Maxwell field) and uncharged cases. Geometric properties are probed via curvature and non-metricity scalars. Horizon structure is analyzed by studying metric functions. Topology is assessed using the Euler characteristic, while geodesic completeness determines singularity accessibility. Thermodynamic quantities—temperature, entropy, and heat capacity—are computed to evaluate stability.
\n\n
作者在$(2+1)$维对称teleparallel引力中采用幂律形式的$f(Q) = c_1 Q + c_4 Q^n$，其中$Q$为非度规性标量。假设静态、圆对称时空，求解带Maxwell场（带电）与不带电情形下的场方程。通过曲率标量与非度规性标量探测几何性质；通过度规函数分析视界结构；利用欧拉示性数评估拓扑；通过测地线完备性判断奇点是否可达；并计算温度、熵和热容以评估热力学稳定性。

Result: Exact black hole solutions are obtained with central singularities stronger than in general relativity. The horizon radii increase with electric charge, while larger $c_4$ or $\\Lambda$ can merge or eliminate horizons. The Euler characteristic indicates nontrivial topology. Geodesic analysis shows that singularities are timelike and may be avoidable in the charged case but unavoidable in the uncharged case. Thermodynamic calculations confirm local stability via positive heat capacity in certain parameter regimes.
\n\n
获得了具有比广义相对论更强中心奇点的精确黑洞解。视界半径随电荷增大而增大，而较大的$c_4$或$\\Lambda$会导致视界合并或消失。欧拉示性数表明存在非平凡拓扑。测地线分析显示奇点为类时奇点：在带电情形下可能不可达，而在不带电情形下则不可避免。热力学计算表明在某些参数范围内热容为正，确认了局域热力学稳定性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that $f(Q)$ gravity in $(2+1)$ dimensions supports black hole solutions with distinct geometric, topological, and thermodynamic features compared to general relativity. Non-metricity significantly influences horizon structure, singularity strength, and geodesic completeness. These results underscore the potential of symmetric teleparallel gravity to provide new insights into low-dimensional black holes and the role of non-Riemannian geometry in gravitational physics.
\n\n
研究表明，$(2+1)$维$f(Q)$引力支持具有区别于广义相对论的几何、拓扑与热力学特性的黑洞解。非度规性显著影响视界结构、奇点强度及测地线完备性。这些结果凸显了对称teleparallel引力在揭示低维黑洞性质及非黎曼几何在引力物理中作用方面的潜力。

Abstract: Black hole solutions are studied here within the symmetric teleparallel formulation of gravity, employing the $f(Q)$ model in which the gravitational dynamics are governed by the non-metricity scalar $Q$. We focus on static, circularly symmetric spacetimes in $(2+1)$-dimensions, analyzing both charged and uncharged cases. By adopting a power-law form for $f(Q)$, we derive exact black hole solutions and explore their thermodynamic and geometric properties. Curvature and non-metricity scalars reveal central singularities stronger than those in general relativity. we find that the horizon radii increase with the charge parameter while higher values of the non-metricity coefficient, $c_{4}$, or the cosmological constant $Λ$ tend to merge or eliminate horizons, reducing their total number and altering the near-origin structure of the spacetime. We perform a detailed topological analysis based on the Euler characteristic and examine the geodesic completeness of the spacetime. Our findings show that, depending on the presence of electric charge, the singularity may or may not be reachable by geodesics. The thermodynamic stability is confirmed via temperature, entropy, and heat capacity calculations. This study highlights the rich structure of $f(Q)$ gravity in lower-dimensional settings and offers new insights into the nature of singularities and black hole topologies in modified gravity theories.

### [39] [Non-minimally coupled Einstein-Yang-Mills black holes: periodic orbits and gravitational wave radiation in extreme mass ratio systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07610)
*Xiuqin He,Zhaoyi Xu,Meirong Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates orbital dynamics and gravitational wave signatures of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) around a non-minimally coupled Einstein-Yang-Mills (EYM) black hole, showing that increasing magnetic charge $Q$ and coupling constant $ξ$ shrink the marginally bound and innermost stable circular orbits, shift the allowed $E$-$L$ parameter space, suppress orbital contraction, and induce distinctive waveform features—offering observational discriminators for black hole models.
\n\n
本文研究了极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）在非最小耦合Einstein-Yang-Mills（EYM）黑洞时空中的轨道动力学和引力波特征，发现随着磁荷参数 $Q$ 和非最小耦合常数 $ξ$ 的增大，边际束缚轨道（$r_{\text{MBO}}$）和最内稳定圆轨道（$r_{\text{ISCO}}$）半径显著减小，允许的 $E$-$L$ 参数空间左移，非最小耦合效应抑制了磁荷引起的轨道收缩，并导致引力波形出现相移、振幅增强和周期缩短——为未来通过引力波观测区分不同黑洞模型提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EMRIs are key probes for strong-field gravity with future space-based detectors like LISA. To interpret such data, one must understand how deviations from Kerr geometry—such as those in non-minimally coupled EYM black holes—affect orbital structure and gravitational waveforms. This motivates a systematic study of periodic orbits and radiation properties in this specific modified black hole spacetime.
\n\n
极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）是未来LISA等空间引力波探测器探测强场引力的关键探针。为解读此类数据，必须理解偏离Kerr几何的黑洞解（如非最小耦合Einstein-Yang-Mills黑洞）如何影响轨道结构和引力波形。这促使作者系统研究该特定修正黑洞时空中的周期轨道与辐射特性。

Method: The authors analyze geodesic motion in the static, spherically symmetric spacetime of a non-minimally coupled EYM black hole, characterized by magnetic charge $Q$ and coupling constant $ξ$. They compute the radii of the marginally bound orbit ($r_{\text{MBO}}$) and innermost stable circular orbit ($r_{\text{ISCO}}$) by solving effective potential conditions. The allowed $(E, L)$ parameter space for bound orbits is mapped. Periodic orbits are classified using the taxonomy based on radial and angular frequencies, and corresponding gravitational waveforms are generated via quadrupole approximation or geodesic-based radiation modeling.
\n\n
作者分析了由磁荷 $Q$ 和耦合常数 $ξ$ 表征的非最小耦合EYM黑洞的静态球对称时空中的测地线运动。通过求解有效势条件，计算边际束缚轨道（$r_{\text{MBO}}$）和最内稳定圆轨道（$r_{\text{ISCO}}$）的半径，并绘制束缚轨道的 $(E, L)$ 允许参数空间。利用基于径向与角频率的分类法对周期轨道进行分类，并通过四极矩近似或基于测地线的辐射模型生成相应的引力波形。

Result: Increasing $Q$ and $ξ$ reduces $r_{\text{MBO}}$ and $r_{\text{ISCO}}$, lowers orbital energy $E$ and angular momentum $L$, and shifts the allowed $E$-$L$ region leftward. The non-minimal coupling $ξ$ counteracts the orbital contraction caused by $Q$, causing orbits with different $Q$ to degenerate toward the Schwarzschild limit. Gravitational waveforms exhibit phase shifts, increased amplitude, and shortened period as $Q$ and $ξ$ grow.
\n\n
随着 $Q$ 和 $ξ$ 增大，$r_{\text{MBO}}$ 与 $r_{\text{ISCO}}$ 减小，轨道能量 $E$ 和角动量 $L$ 降低，且允许的 $E$-$L$ 区域向左移动。非最小耦合常数 $ξ$ 抑制了磁荷 $Q$ 引起的轨道收缩，使不同 $Q$ 值的轨道退化趋近于Schwarzschild情形。引力波形随 $Q$ 和 $ξ$ 增大而出现相移、振幅增强和周期缩短。

Conclusion: The distinct imprints of $Q$ and $ξ$ on EMRI orbital structure and gravitational waveforms provide observable signatures that could be used by future space-based detectors to test the nature of compact objects and distinguish non-minimally coupled EYM black holes from Kerr or Schwarzschild black holes.
\n\n
$Q$ 和 $ξ$ 对EMRI轨道结构和引力波形的独特印记，为未来空间引力波探测器提供了可观测信号，可用于检验致密天体的本质，并区分非最小耦合EYM黑洞与Kerr或Schwarzschild黑洞。

Abstract: Extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs), as a core target for future space-based gravitational wave detection, offer crucial observational grounds for testing strong-field gravitational theories and classifying black holes through their orbital dynamics and gravitational wave radiation characteristics. This study systematically investigates the periodic orbit characteristics and gravitational wave radiation properties of EMRIs in the spacetime of a non-minimally coupled Einstein-Yang-Mills (EYM) black hole. The results show that as the magnetic charge parameter \(Q\) and the non-minimal coupling constant \(ξ\) increase, the radii of the marginally bound orbit (\(r_{\text{MBO}}\)) and the innermost stable circular orbit (\(r_{\text{ISCO}}\)) decrease significantly, with corresponding reductions in the orbital energy \(E\) and angular momentum \(L\). Furthermore, the allowable parameter space of energy and angular momentum (\(E\)-\(L\)) for bound orbits shifts towards the left. We then plot typical periodic orbits through orbit classification, finding that the non-minimal coupling effect suppresses the orbital contraction induced by the magnetic charge, leading to degeneracy of orbits with different \(Q\) values towards the Schwarzschild case, as well as phase shifts, amplitude enhancement, and period shortening in the gravitational waveforms with increasing \(Q\) and \(ξ\). These results provide theoretical predictions for distinguishing different black hole models through future gravitational wave observations.

### [40] [Scattering from compact objects: Debye series and Regge-Debye poles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07714)
*Mohamed Ould El Hadj*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies elastic scattering of massless scalar waves by a compact, horizonless star with a Schwarzschild exterior, introducing an exact Debye-series decomposition of the scattering matrix that separates surface reflection from interior propagation. The authors compute the Regge-Debye pole spectrum in the complex angular-momentum plane, identifying distinct pole families for neutron-star-like ($R>3M$) and ultracompact ($R<3M$) objects, and reconstruct the scattering amplitude via partial-wave and complex angular-momentum methods, revealing how different pole branches contribute to scattering features like rainbow enhancements.
\n\n
本文研究了具有Schwarzschild外部时空的无视界致密星体对无质量标量波的弹性散射，引入了散射矩阵的精确Debye级数分解，将表面反射与内部传播贡献分离。作者计算了复角动量平面上的Regge-Debye极点谱，识别出中子星类（$R>3M$）和超致密（$R<3M$）物体的不同极点族，并通过分波和复角动量方法重构散射振幅，揭示了不同极点分支如何贡献于彩虹增强等散射特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand wave scattering by compact astrophysical objects without horizons—such as exotic stars or boson stars—by extending classical scattering theory (e.g., Mie scattering) to curved spacetime. Traditional black hole scattering analyses rely on horizon boundary conditions; here, the absence of a horizon necessitates a new framework that accounts for internal structure and surface matching, enabling a trajectory-based interpretation and precise identification of resonance mechanisms through complex angular momentum techniques.
\n\n
动机在于理解无视界致密天体（如奇异星或玻色星）的波散射行为，将经典散射理论（如Mie散射）推广至弯曲时空。传统黑洞散射分析依赖于视界边界条件；而此处无视界情形要求新框架，需考虑内部结构与表面匹配条件，从而实现基于轨迹的物理解释，并通过复角动量方法精确识别共振机制。

Method: The authors employ an exact Debye-series expansion of the scattering matrix $S_\ell$, decomposing it into terms corresponding to successive internal reflections and transmissions. Each Debye term is associated with a specific physical path: direct reflection, single transmission-reflection, etc. They analytically continue the partial-wave index $\ell$ to complex values to locate Regge poles (complex angular-momentum singularities) and perform a Regge-Debye pole analysis. Scattering amplitudes are reconstructed both via direct partial-wave summation and via complex angular-momentum contour deformation, isolating contributions from pole families and branch cuts order by order in the Debye series.
\n\n
作者采用散射矩阵 $S_\ell$ 的精确Debye级数展开，将其分解为对应于多次内部反射与透射的项。每一Debye项对应特定物理路径：直接反射、单次透射-反射等。他们将分波指标 $\ell$ 解析延拓至复平面以定位Regge极点（复角动量奇点），并进行Regge-Debye极点分析。散射振幅通过直接分波求和与复角动量围道形变两种方式重构，逐阶分离Debye级数中各极点族与分支切割的贡献。

Result: For $R > 3M$ (neutron-star-like), two Regge-Debye pole families emerge: a surface-wave branch from the exterior–interior matching condition and a broad-resonance branch from interior regularity. For $R < 3M$ (ultracompact), the interior branch splits into broad and narrow resonances. The reconstructed scattering amplitude from Debye partial waves matches direct computations. In the $R > 3M$ regime, high-frequency rainbow-like scattering arises already at first interior-transmission order and is dominated by interior-resonance poles, yet competes with non-pole (branch-cut) contributions. In contrast, for $R < 3M$, Debye amplitudes are overwhelmingly dominated by poles, with negligible branch-cut effects.
\n\n
对于 $R > 3M$（中子星类），出现两个Regge-Debye极点族：一个源于外-内匹配条件的表面波分支，另一个源于内部正则性条件的宽共振分支。对于 $R < 3M$（超致密），内部分支分裂为宽共振与窄共振。由Debye分波重构的散射振幅与直接计算高度一致。在 $R > 3M$ 情形下，高频彩虹状散射在首次内部透射阶即已出现，由内部共振极点主导，但与非极点（分支切割）贡献存在显著竞争；而在 $R < 3M$ 情形下，Debye振幅几乎完全由极点主导，分支切割效应可忽略。

Conclusion: The Debye-series decomposition provides a physically transparent and mathematically exact framework for scattering by horizonless compact objects in general relativity. It enables a clear separation of surface and interior dynamics, reveals the structure of the Regge-Debye pole spectrum across different compactness regimes, and demonstrates how complex angular-momentum techniques can be systematically applied order by order in a semiclassical trajectory picture. This approach bridges geometric optics, resonance physics, and full wave scattering in strong-field gravity.
\n\n
Debye级数分解为广义相对论中无视界致密天体的散射问题提供了物理清晰且数学精确的框架。它实现了表面与内部动力学的明确分离，揭示了不同致密度下Regge-Debye极点谱的结构，并展示了如何在半经典轨迹图像中逐阶系统应用复角动量技术。该方法架起了几何光学、共振物理与强场引力中全波散射之间的桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate elastic scattering by a compact, horizonless body in curved spacetime, considering a massless scalar wave incident on a static, spherically symmetric, uniform-density star of radius $R$ and mass $M$ with a Schwarzschild exterior. We introduce an exact Debye-series decomposition of the scattering matrix, in the spirit of Debye expansions in Mie scattering. This decomposition separates direct surface reflection from contributions involving transmission into the interior and subsequent propagation, and admits a natural trajectory interpretation. We then determine the associated Regge-Debye pole spectrum in the complex angular-momentum plane. For neutron-star-like tenuities ($R>3M$), the spectrum exhibits two pole families: a surface-wave branch associated with the surface matching condition and a broad-resonance branch associated with the interior regularity condition. For ultracompact objects ($R<3M$), the surface-wave branch persists, while the interior-resonance sector splits into broad- and narrow-resonance branches.
  We next reconstruct the scattering amplitude from the Debye partial-wave contributions and find excellent agreement with direct partial-wave calculations. Finally, we develop complex angular-momentum representations order by order in the Debye series, making explicit how the pole families and non-pole sectors contribute to each Debye term. In the neutron-star-like regime, we find a genuine competition between Regge-Debye pole sums and branch-cut contributions, and show that, at high frequency, the rainbow-like enhancement already arises from the first interior-transmission contribution and is dominated by the interior-resonance Regge-Debye poles. By contrast, in the ultracompact regime, the Debye amplitudes are overwhelmingly pole dominated.

</details>


### [41] [Green functions of the Regge-Wheeler and Teukolsky equations in Schwarzschild spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07747)
*David Q. Aruquipa,Marc Casals*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper computes the full retarded Green functions for gravitational perturbations (Regge-Wheeler and Teukolsky equations) in Schwarzschild spacetime along two types of worldlines: timelike circular geodesics and static observers. It reveals a 4-fold singularity structure away from caustics and a 2-fold structure at caustics, with new physical oscillations near singularities absent in scalar field cases.
\n\n
本文计算了Schwarzschild时空中引力扰动（Regge-Wheeler和Teukolsky方程）的完整推迟Green函数，沿两类世界线：类时圆轨道测地线和静态观测者。结果揭示了在非焦散点处具有四重奇异性结构，在焦散点处为二重结构，并且在引力情形中奇异性附近出现了标量场情形中所没有的物理振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the causal structure and propagation of gravitational perturbations in black hole spacetimes is essential for modeling gravitational wave emission, self-force effects, and quantum field theory in curved spacetime. The Green function encodes this information, but its explicit construction—especially near singularities and caustics—is highly nontrivial for tensor fields like gravity, unlike simpler scalar cases.
\n\n
理解黑洞时空中引力扰动的因果结构与传播对于建模引力波辐射、自力效应（self-force effects）以及弯曲时空中的量子场论至关重要。Green函数编码了这些信息，但其显式构造——特别是在奇点和焦散点附近——对于引力这样的张量场而言极为复杂，远比标量场情形困难。

Method: The authors develop a combination of numerical and analytical techniques to compute the retarded Green functions for the Regge-Wheeler (axial) and Teukolsky (spin-weighted) equations in Schwarzschild spacetime. They evaluate the Green functions along two specific worldlines: (i) a timelike circular geodesic (non-caustic null-separated points), and (ii) a static worldline (caustic null-separated points). Mode-sum regularization and careful treatment of high-frequency asymptotics are employed to resolve the singular structure.
\n\n
作者发展了一套结合数值与解析方法的技术，用于计算Schwarzschild时空中Regge-Wheeler（轴向）和Teukolsky（自旋加权）方程的推迟Green函数。他们在两类特定世界线上进行计算：(i) 类时圆轨道测地线（非焦散的类光分离点），(ii) 静态世界线（焦散的类光分离点）。通过模求和正则化（mode-sum regularization）和对高频渐近行为的精细处理，解析出奇异性结构。

Result: The gravitational Green functions exhibit a 4-fold singularity structure (Dirac-delta, its derivative, and step-function discontinuities) away from caustics, reducing to a 2-fold structure at caustics—mirroring the scalar field behavior. Crucially, new physical oscillatory features appear near the singular support in the gravitational case, which are absent for scalar fields. These oscillations encode spin-dependent propagation effects of gravitational waves.
\n\n
引力Green函数在非焦散区域展现出四重奇异性结构（Dirac-delta函数、其导数及阶跃不连续性），在焦散点处退化为二重结构——与标量场行为类似。关键的是，引力情形在奇异支集附近出现了新的物理振荡特征，这在标量场中并不存在。这些振荡编码了引力波传播中的自旋依赖效应。

Conclusion: This work provides the first complete characterization of the retarded Green functions for gravitational perturbations in Schwarzschild spacetime along physically relevant worldlines, revealing richer singularity structures and novel oscillatory phenomena due to the tensor nature of gravity. The methods developed pave the way for accurate self-force calculations and improved effective models of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals.
\n\n
本工作首次完整刻画了Schwarzschild时空中沿物理相关世界线的引力扰动推迟Green函数，揭示了由于引力的张量本质而产生的更丰富的奇异性结构和新颖振荡现象。所发展的方法为精确计算自力效应和改进极端质量比旋进（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals）的有效模型铺平了道路。

Abstract: We present a calculation of the full retarded Green functions of the Regge-Wheeler and Teukolsky equations obeyed by gravitational field perturbations of Schwarzschild spacetime. We perform the calculations for spacetime points along: (i) a timelike circular geodesic (where null-separated points are not at caustics); and (ii) a static worldline (where null-separated points are at caustics). These Green functions show a 4-fold singularity structure away from caustics, and 2-fold at caustics (similarly to the case of scalar field perturbations, which we also reproduce). Physical oscillations near the singularities appear in the gravitational case, which were not present in the scalar case. We obtain our results by developing various numerical and analytical methods.

</details>


### [42] [Evolution of density perturbations in fractional Newtonian cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07781)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates density perturbations in a fractional Newtonian cosmology during the matter-dominated era, deriving and solving an analytical growth equation that depends explicitly on the fractional parameter $α$. The model avoids dynamical instabilities, recovers standard Newtonian/relativistic results when $α = 1$, and yields a tighter observational upper bound on $α$ via the Sachs–Wolfe effect than background or theoretical constraints alone. This suggests that fractional modifications imprint detectable signatures in structure formation distinct from $Λ$CDM.
\n\n
本文研究了物质主导时期分数阶牛顿宇宙学中的密度扰动，推导并解析求解了一个显式依赖于分数阶参数 $α$ 的增长方程。该模型在物理相关参数空间中无动力学不稳定性，当 $α = 1$ 时可还原为标准牛顿/相对论结果，并通过Sachs–Wolfe效应给出了比背景演化或理论扰动分析更严格的 $α$ 上限。这表明分数阶修正会在结构形成中留下可观测的、区别于 $Λ$CDM 的独特印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore whether fractional calculus—specifically a fractional generalization of Newtonian gravity—can provide a viable alternative or extension to standard cosmological models. While background dynamics may mimic $Λ$CDM, the authors aim to test whether linear density perturbations encode unique signatures of the fractional parameter $α$, which could be constrained or detected through cosmological observations such as the Sachs–Wolfe effect.
\n\n
动机在于探索分数阶微积分（特别是牛顿引力的分数阶推广）是否能构成标准宇宙学模型的有效替代或扩展。尽管背景演化可能模拟 $Λ$CDM，作者旨在检验线性密度扰动是否编码了分数阶参数 $α$ 的独特信号，并可通过Sachs–Wolfe效应等宇宙学观测加以约束或探测。

Method: The authors employ a fluid-flow approach within fractional Newtonian cosmology to derive a linearized growth equation for density perturbations during the matter-dominated era. They solve this equation analytically, identifying both growing and decaying modes. Focusing on the growing mode consistent with observations, they connect the perturbation amplitude to the cosmic microwave background (CMB) via the Sachs–Wolfe relation to place an observational constraint on the fractional parameter $α$. This constraint is then combined with existing bounds from background cosmology.
\n\n
作者在分数阶牛顿宇宙学框架下采用流体流动方法，推导出物质主导时期密度扰动的线性增长方程，并对其进行解析求解，识别出增长模和衰减模。聚焦于与观测一致的增长模，他们通过Sachs–Wolfe关系将扰动振幅与宇宙微波背景（CMB）联系起来，从而对分数阶参数 $α$ 施加观测约束，并将其与来自背景宇宙学的已有约束相结合。

Result: The growth equation for density perturbations explicitly depends on the fractional parameter $α$, with no dynamical instabilities in the physical regime. The solutions reduce to standard results when $α = 1$. Using the Sachs–Wolfe equation, the authors obtain an upper bound on $α$ that is tighter than constraints from background expansion or theoretical stability. Combined with background constraints, $α$ is confined to a narrow viable range, indicating that perturbations carry a distinct fractional signature even if the background mimics $Λ$CDM.
\n\n
密度扰动的增长方程显式依赖于分数阶参数 $α$，且在物理参数范围内无动力学不稳定性；当 $α = 1$ 时，解还原为标准结果。利用Sachs–Wolfe方程，作者获得了比背景膨胀或理论稳定性约束更严格的 $α$ 上限。结合背景约束后，$α$ 被限制在一个狭窄的可行区间内，表明即使背景演化模拟 $Λ$CDM，扰动仍携带独特的分数阶印记。

Conclusion: Fractional Newtonian cosmology introduces a physically consistent framework for structure formation where density perturbations depend nontrivially on the fractional parameter $α$. Although the background can closely resemble $Λ$CDM, perturbative observables—particularly through CMB anisotropies—provide a more sensitive probe of fractional effects. This demonstrates that testing deviations from standard gravity requires going beyond background dynamics to include perturbation theory.
\n\n
分数阶牛顿宇宙学为结构形成提供了一个物理自洽的框架，其中密度扰动非平凡地依赖于分数阶参数 $α$。尽管背景演化可高度模拟 $Λ$CDM，但扰动观测量（尤其是通过CMB各向异性）能更灵敏地探测分数阶效应。这表明，检验对标准引力的偏离必须超越背景动力学，纳入微扰理论。

Abstract: In this work, density perturbations are investigated within the framework of a fractional Newtonian cosmology. Focusing on the matter-dominated era and employing the fluid-flow approach, the growth equation for density perturbations is derived and solved analytically. No dynamical instability arises in the physically relevant parameter space. It is shown that both the growth equation and its solutions depend explicitly on the fractional parameter $α$, and reduce to their standard Newtonian and relativistic counterparts in the special limit $α= 1$. The existence of both growing and decaying perturbative modes is confirmed, and, in accordance with current cosmological observations, the analysis is restricted to the growing mode. Using observational relations, in particular the Sachs--Wolfe equation, an observational upper bound on the parameter $α$ is obtained, which is more restrictive than the bounds inferred from background dynamics and theoretical perturbative considerations. When combined with the independent constraints arising from the background analysis, these results confine the fractional parameter $α$ to a narrow and physically viable region of parameter space. Overall, the present study indicates that, although the background evolution of the fractional model may closely mimic that of $Λ$CDM, the associated density perturbations generically carry a distinct fractional signature that can, in principle, be tested observationally.

</details>


### [43] [Gravitational waves in metric-affine bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08310)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates gravitational wave propagation and emission in the metric-affine bumblebee model, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking occurs via a vector field vacuum expectation value. The authors derive modified dispersion relations dependent on the graviton's direction relative to the background vector, analyze polarization modes for timelike and spacelike Lorentz-violating backgrounds, construct the retarded Green function, and compute radiation from localized sources—finding distinct Lorentz-violating signatures in timelike (speed shift and amplitude renormalization) versus spacelike (anisotropic quadrupole corrections and octupole-like terms) cases. Observational constraints on the parameter $\\xi b^2$ are derived using GW170817/GRB~170817A multimessenger data.
\n\n
本文研究了度规-仿射（metric-affine）bumblebee模型中的引力波传播与辐射，其中Lorentz对称性自发破缺源于矢量场获得非零真空期望值。作者在几何光学近似下推导出依赖于引力子波矢与背景矢量相对取向的修正色散关系，分析了类时和类空Lorentz破缺真空下的偏振模式，构建了修正波动算符的推迟Green函数，并计算了局域源产生的辐射区场。在类时情形下，Lorentz破缺效应表现为传播速度改变和整体振幅重整化，导致推迟时间偏移但保留四极矩波形结构；而在类空情形下，则引入各向异性的四极矩振幅修正以及正比于四极矩三阶时间导数的额外贡献。利用GW170817/GRB~170817A多信使观测数据，对参数 $\\xi b^2$ 给出了观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the phenomenological consequences of spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in gravity, specifically within the metric-affine bumblebee model—a well-motivated effective field theory framework for Lorentz violation. Understanding how gravitational waves propagate and are emitted in such scenarios is crucial for testing fundamental symmetries with current and future gravitational-wave observatories, especially in light of stringent multimessenger constraints like those from GW170817.
\n\n
动机在于探索引力理论中自发Lorentz对称性破缺的现象学后果，特别是度规-仿射bumblebee模型——这是一个研究Lorentz破缺的、具有良好理论动机的有效场论框架。理解在此类理论中引力波如何传播与辐射，对于利用当前及未来的引力波天文台检验基本对称性至关重要，尤其是在GW170817等多信使观测给出严格限制的背景下。

Method: The authors work in the linearized gravity regime under the geometric-optics approximation. They derive the modified wave equation for the metric perturbation by expanding the field equations of the metric-affine bumblebee model around a flat background with a fixed vector vacuum expectation value $b_\\mu$. The dispersion relation is obtained by analyzing the principal symbol of the wave operator. Polarization content is determined by examining the kernel of this operator for timelike ($b_\\mu b^\\mu > 0$) and spacelike ($b_\\mu b^\\mu < 0$) backgrounds. The retarded Green function is constructed via Fourier transform of the inverse wave operator, enabling calculation of the radiation-zone metric perturbation from compact sources. The formalism is applied to a circular binary black hole system to compute observable waveform modifications.
\n\n
作者在几何光学近似下采用线性化引力方法。他们将度规-仿射bumblebee模型的场方程在具有固定矢量真空期望值 $b_\\mu$ 的平直背景上展开，得到度规微扰的修正波动方程。通过分析波动算符的主符号（principal symbol）获得色散关系。通过考察该算符在类时（$b_\\mu b^\\mu > 0$）和类空（$b_\\mu b^\\mu < 0$）背景下的核空间（kernel）来确定偏振自由度。通过傅里叶变换对波动算符的逆进行积分，构造推迟Green函数，从而计算紧致源产生的辐射区度规微扰。该形式体系被应用于圆轨道双黑洞系统，以计算可观测的波形修正。

Result: The study finds that only two propagating tensor modes exist in both timelike and spacelike Lorentz-violating vacua, but their propagation characteristics differ. In the timelike case, Lorentz violation manifests as an isotropic modification: a rescaled propagation speed $c_g = 1 - \\xi b^2$ and an overall amplitude renormalization, shifting the retarded time while preserving the standard quadrupole structure. In the spacelike case, the waveform acquires anisotropic angular dependence in the quadrupole amplitude and an additional term proportional to $\\dddot{I}_{ij}$ (the third time derivative of the quadrupole moment), resembling an octupole contribution. Using GW170817’s near-simultaneous gamma-ray and gravitational-wave arrival, the combination $|\\xi b^2| \\lesssim 10^{-15}$ is constrained.
\n\n
研究发现，在类时和类空Lorentz破缺真空中均仅有两个传播的张量模式，但其传播特性不同。在类时情形下，Lorentz破缺表现为各向同性的修正：引力波传播速度被重标度为 $c_g = 1 - \\xi b^2$，并伴随整体振幅重整化，导致推迟时间偏移但仍保留标准四极矩结构。在类空情形下，波形在四极矩振幅中出现各向异性角依赖，并附加一项正比于 $\\dddot{I}_{ij}$（四极矩的三阶时间导数）的贡献，类似于八极矩项。利用GW170817引力波与伽马暴信号的近乎同时到达，对组合参数给出约束 $|\\xi b^2| \\lesssim 10^{-15}$。

Conclusion: The metric-affine bumblebee model predicts distinct, testable signatures in gravitational-wave signals depending on the nature (timelike vs. spacelike) of the Lorentz-violating background. These include isotropic speed shifts, amplitude renormalizations, anisotropic angular modulations, and higher-derivative radiation terms. Current multimessenger observations already place extremely tight bounds on the Lorentz-violating parameter $\\xi b^2$, demonstrating the power of gravitational-wave astronomy as a probe of fundamental spacetime symmetries.
\n\n
度规-仿射bumblebee模型预言了依赖于Lorentz破缺背景性质（类时或类空）的、可检验的引力波信号特征，包括各向同性的速度偏移、振幅重整化、各向异性角调制以及高阶导数辐射项。当前的多信使观测已对Lorentz破缺参数 $\\xi b^2$ 给出了极其严格的限制，彰显了引力波天文学作为探测时空基本对称性工具的强大能力。

Abstract: We study the propagation and emission of gravitational waves in the metric-affine formulation of the bumblebee model, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking arises from a vector field acquiring a nonvanishing vacuum expectation value. Working in the geometric-optics limit of the linearized theory, we derive the modified dispersion relation governing the graviton modes and show that it depends on the orientation of the wave vector relative to the background vector. The polarization sector is examined for timelike and spacelike configurations of the Lorentz-violating vacuum. In both cases only two independent tensor modes propagate, although their propagation properties and tensor structure depend on the orientation of the background field. We then construct the retarded Green function associated with the modified wave operator and determine the radiation-zone produced by localized sources. In the timelike configuration the Lorentz-violating effects appear through a modified propagation speed and an overall amplitude renormalization, leading to a shifted retarded time while preserving the quadrupole structure of the waveform. In contrast, the spacelike sector introduces anisotropic corrections to the quadrupole amplitude together with an additional contribution proportional to the third time derivative of the quadrupole moment. As an astrophysical application, the gravitational radiation emitted by a circular binary black hole system is evaluated, allowing observational constraints on the Lorentz-violating combination $ξb^{2}$ to be estimated using multimessenger bounds from GW170817/GRB~170817A and waveform consistency requirements from gravitational wave observations.

</details>


### [44] [Threshold Temperature for Neutron-Star Emergence in a Gravitational Thermodynamic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07951)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reformulates neutron star formation as a gravitational-thermodynamic threshold problem by integrating the entropy-functional emergent gravity paradigm with Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) hydrostatic equilibrium, Tolman redshift, and energy balance between bulk binding and thermal energies, yielding four distinct temperature scales characterizing static compact objects.
\n\n
本文将中子星的形成重新表述为一个引力-热力学阈值问题，通过将熵泛函形式的涌现引力（emergent gravity）范式与Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）流体静力学平衡、Tolman红移以及体束缚能与热能之间的能量平衡相结合，导出了刻画静态致密天体的四个特征温度标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The work is motivated by the entropy-functional formulation of emergent gravity—where spacetime thermodynamics yields Einstein’s equations via entropy extremization—and seeks to apply this thermodynamic-gravitational correspondence to compact object physics, specifically to understand neutron star onset through thermodynamic thresholds rather than purely mechanical stability criteria.
\n\n
本研究受涌现引力的熵泛函表述所驱动——在该框架中，时空热力学通过对熵的极值化导出爱因斯坦场方程——并试图将这种热力学-引力对应关系应用于致密天体物理，特别是通过热力学阈值（而非纯力学稳定性判据）来理解中子星的形成条件。

Method: The authors combine the Jacobson-Padmanabhan interpretation of gravity as an equation of state with general relativistic hydrostatics (TOV equations), Tolman redshift for thermal equilibrium in curved spacetime, and a bulk energy balance condition comparing gravitational binding energy $|E_{\\text{bind}}|$ and thermal energy $E_{\\text{th}}$. They explicitly solve the TOV system for degenerate Fermi gas matter and derive thermodynamic consistency relations linking temperature, pressure, and metric potentials.
\n\n
作者结合Jacobson-Padmanabhan关于引力作为物态方程的诠释、广义相对论流体静力学（TOV方程）、弯曲时空中热平衡所需的Tolman红移，以及比较引力束缚能 $|E_{\\text{bind}}|$ 与热能 $E_{\\text{th}}$ 的体能量平衡条件。他们对简并Fermi气体物质显式求解TOV系统，并导出联系温度、压强与度规势的热力学自洽关系。

Result: Four characteristic temperature scales are derived: (1) the Newtonian virial temperature $T_{\\text{vir}} \\sim |E_{\\text{bind}}|/N$, (2) its redshifted counterpart $T_{\\infty} = T_{\\text{vir}} / \\sqrt{g_{00}}$ as measured at infinity, (3) the degenerate-matter temperature scale set by Fermi energy $T_{\\text{deg}} \\sim E_F/k_B$, and (4) the surface screen temperature associated with the holographic screen at the stellar boundary. Explicit analytic expressions for TOV solutions and Fermi-gas thermodynamics are provided, along with consistency checks from thermodynamic identities.
\n\n
导出了四个特征温度标度：(1) 牛顿维里温度 $T_{\\text{vir}} \\sim |E_{\\text{bind}}|/N$；(2) 在无穷远处观测到的红移版本 $T_{\\infty} = T_{\\text{vir}} / \\sqrt{g_{00}}$；(3) 由Fermi能决定的简并物质温度标度 $T_{\\text{deg}} \\sim E_F/k_B$；(4) 与恒星边界全息屏相关的表面屏温度。文中给出了TOV解和Fermi气体热力学的显式解析表达式，并通过热力学恒等式进行了自洽性检验。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that neutron star formation can be consistently described within an emergent gravity framework as a thermodynamic phase transition governed by competing energy scales, reinforcing the deep connection between gravity, thermodynamics, and quantum degeneracy in compact objects.
\n\n
研究表明，中子星的形成可在涌现引力框架内被一致地描述为由竞争性能量标度主导的热力学相变，从而强化了引力、热力学与致密天体中量子简并在深层上的联系。

Abstract: Motivated by the entropy-functional formulation of emergent gravity, in which spacetime is endowed with a thermodynamic entropy that, upon extremization, yields the Einstein field equations, we reformulate the onset of a neutron star as a bulk gravitational-thermodynamic threshold problem. By combining the Jacobson-Padmanabhan perspective of gravity as an equation of state with Tolman redshift, Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff hydrostatics, and a bulk binding versus thermal energy balance, we derive four characteristic temperature scales for a static compact object: the Newtonian virial threshold, the redshifted threshold as observed at infinity, the degenerate-matter threshold, and the surface screen temperature.The paper supplies a mathematically expanded derivation, explicit TOV and Fermi-gas formulae, and thermodynamic consistency relations.

### [45] [The Interior of the Scalar Hairy Black Hole with Inverted Higgs Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08067)
*Xiao Yan Chew,Kok-Geng Lim,Dong-han Yeom*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper numerically studies the interior geometry of asymptotically flat hairy black holes (HBHs) in Einstein-Klein-Gordon theory with nonpositive-definite scalar potentials. It finds a spacelike curvature singularity at $r=0$, no Cauchy horizon, and persistent violation of the weak energy condition inside the event horizon.
\n\n
本文通过数值方法研究了Einstein-Klein-Gordon理论中具有非正定标量势的渐近平坦hairy black holes（HBHs）的内部几何结构。研究发现，在$r=0$处存在类空曲率奇点，不存在Cauchy horizon，并且在事件视界内部始终违反weak energy condition。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the incomplete understanding of the interior structure of hairy black holes (HBHs), especially given that their exterior properties—such as shadow imaging for those supported by an inverted Higgs-like potential—have been well studied. Additionally, the instability of the Cauchy horizon due to mass inflation and its implications for the Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture necessitate a detailed investigation into whether such horizons persist in HBHs with nontrivial scalar hair.
\n\n
研究动机源于对hairy black holes（HBHs）内部结构理解的不足，尤其是其外部性质（如由倒置Higgs-like势支撑的HBHs的阴影成像）已被充分研究。此外，由于mass inflation效应导致Cauchy horizon高度不稳定，这对Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture提出了挑战，因此有必要深入探究具有非平凡标量hair的HBHs中是否仍存在此类horizon。

Method: The authors numerically integrate the coupled Einstein-Klein-Gordon field equations inward from the event horizon toward $r = 0$, using boundary conditions that encode nontrivial scalar hair at the horizon. The scalar potential is assumed to be nonpositive-definite, allowing for solutions with scalar condensates at the horizon. The analysis focuses on electrically neutral configurations and examines the behavior of metric functions, curvature invariants (Ricci and Kretschmann scalars), and energy conditions in the black hole interior.
\n\n
作者从事件视界向$r = 0$方向数值积分耦合的Einstein-Klein-Gordon场方程，使用在视界处编码非平凡标量hair的边界条件。假设标量势为非正定，从而允许在视界处存在标量凝聚态。分析聚焦于电中性构型，并考察黑洞内部度规函数、曲率不变量（Ricci标量和Kretschmann标量）以及能量条件的行为。

Result: Inside the event horizon, the scalar field and metric functions increase monotonically and diverge as $r \rightarrow 0$. Both the Ricci scalar and Kretschmann scalar diverge at the origin, confirming a genuine curvature singularity. No inner horizon (Cauchy horizon) is found, as the metric function exhibits no additional root. Moreover, the weak energy condition is violated throughout the interior, with the magnitude of violation growing with the scalar field value at the horizon.
\n\n
在事件视界内部，标量场和度规函数单调递增，并在$r \rightarrow 0$时发散。Ricci标量和Kretschmann标量均在原点发散，证实存在真实的曲率奇点。未发现内视界（Cauchy horizon），因为度规函数没有额外的根。此外，weak energy condition在整个内部区域被违反，且违反程度随视界处标量场值的增大而加剧。

Conclusion: The absence of a Cauchy horizon and the presence of a spacelike curvature singularity support the validity of the Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture for the class of electrically neutral hairy black holes considered. The persistent violation of the weak energy condition underscores the role of exotic matter in shaping the interior geometry of these black holes, offering new insights into their global causal structure and stability.
\n\n
所研究的电中性hairy black holes不存在Cauchy horizon并存在类空曲率奇点，这支持了Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture在此类黑洞中的有效性。weak energy condition的持续违反突显了奇异物质在塑造这些黑洞内部几何结构中的作用，为其整体因果结构和稳定性提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the interior structure of asymptotically flat hairy black holes (HBHs) arising in the Einstein-Klein-Gordon theory with nonpositive-definite scalar potentials, where nontrivial scalar hair exists at the event horizon. While exterior properties, including shadow imaging for HBHs supported by an inverted Higgs-like potential have been extensively investigated, their interior structure remains largely unexplored. In many gravitational theories, backreaction of classical fields can significantly eliminate the Cauchy horizon, which is known to be highly unstable due to the mass inflation effect, raising important questions regarding the validity of the Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture. These considerations motivate us to examine the interior structure of HBHs by numerically integrating the field equations inward from the outer horizon. We find that the scalar field and the metric functions increase monotonically inside the horizon and diverge as $r \rightarrow 0$. The Ricci and Kretschmann scalars also diverge at $r=0$, confirming the presence of a genuine curvature singularity. No additional root of the metric function is observed, indicating the absence of a Cauchy horizon in the electrically neutral HBHs considered here. Furthermore, the weak energy condition is violated throughout the interior region, and the degree of violation becomes more pronounced as the scalar field at the horizon increases. These results provide new insight into the global structure of HBHs and their implications for cosmic censorship.

</details>


### [46] [Circular stable orbits in $f(R)$ realistic static and spherically-symmetric spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08637)
*Néstor Rivero González,Álvaro de la Cruz Dombriz,Gonzalo J. Olmo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies geodesic motion around neutron stars in metric $f(R)$ gravity with the Starobinsky model $f(R) = aR^2$ ($a < 0$). Stable circular timelike orbits exist only in discrete radial bands, influenced by the equation of state, central pressure, and $|a|$. No photon spheres are found for null geodesics outside the star.
\n\n
本文研究了在度规$f(R)$引力中采用Starobinsky模型$f(R) = aR^2$（$a < 0$）时中子星周围的测地线结构。类时稳定圆轨道仅存在于离散的径向带中，其位置敏感依赖于物态方程、中心压强和参数$|a|$。在所研究的参数范围内，未发现中子星外部存在光子球。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how modifications to General Relativity—specifically metric $f(R)$ gravity with a quadratic correction—affect orbital dynamics around compact objects like neutron stars. Unlike black holes, neutron stars have material interiors, requiring careful matching between interior and exterior geometries via junction conditions unique to $f(R)$ theories. This setup allows probing deviations from GR in strong-field regimes relevant for astrophysical observations.
\n\n
动机在于理解对广义相对论的修改——特别是具有二次修正项的度规$f(R)$引力——如何影响中子星等致密天体周围的轨道动力学。与黑洞不同，中子星具有物质内部结构，需通过$f(R)$理论特有的连接条件将内部解与外部真空几何严格匹配。该设置可用于探测强场区域中与观测相关的GR偏离效应。

Method: The authors numerically solve the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for realistic neutron-star equations of state in the Starobinsky $f(R)=aR^2$ model with $a<0$. They match the interior solution to the exterior vacuum spacetime using the full set of Israel-like junction conditions required in metric $f(R)$ gravity. Geodesic motion is then analyzed via an effective potential formalism for both massive (timelike) and massless (null) particles.
\n\n
作者在Starobinsky模型$f(R)=aR^2$（$a<0$）下，针对多种真实物态方程数值求解修正的Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程，获得中子星内部解。随后利用度规$f(R)$引力中所需的完整Israel型连接条件，将内部解与外部真空时空严格匹配。接着通过有效势方法分析大质量粒子（类时）和无质量粒子（类光）的测地线运动。

Result: Stable circular timelike geodesics occur only in discrete radial bands, separated by forbidden regions where no stable orbits exist. The innermost (principal) band’s location strongly depends on the stellar central pressure, the equation of state, and $|a|$. Outside these bands, bound but unstable precessing orbits and unbound trajectories are possible. For null geodesics, no photon spheres are found outside the neutron star surface within the explored parameter space.
\n\n
类时稳定圆轨道仅出现在离散的径向带中，各带之间被禁止区域隔开。最内侧（主）稳定带的位置强烈依赖于恒星中心压强、物态方程及参数$|a|$。在这些带之外，可能存在束缚但不稳定的进动轨道以及非束缚轨道。对于类光测地线，在所探索的参数范围内，中子星表面外未发现光子球。

Conclusion: Metric $f(R)$ gravity with $f(R)=aR^2$ ($a<0$) leads to qualitatively distinct orbital structures around neutron stars compared to General Relativity, featuring fragmented stability zones for massive particles and absence of photon spheres. These features could serve as observational signatures to test modified gravity theories using future high-precision astrophysical data.
\n\n
在$f(R)=aR^2$（$a<0$）的度规$f(R)$引力中，中子星周围的轨道结构与广义相对论相比呈现出定性差异：大质量粒子的稳定轨道呈碎片化分布，且不存在光子球。这些特征可作为修改引力理论的观测判据，有望通过未来的高精度天体物理数据进行检验。

Abstract: We investigate the geodesic structure of realistic static and spherically symmetric spacetimes embedding neutron stars in metric $f(R)$ gravity, focusing on the quadratic Starobinsky model $f(R)=aR^2$ with $a<0$. Neutron-star solutions are obtained by numerically solving the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff system for several realistic equations of state. Such solutions are then matched consistently to the exterior vacuum geometry by enforcing the full set of junction conditions required in metric $f(R)$ theories. Using an effective potential approach, we show that stable circular orbits appear in discrete radial bands separated by forbidden regions, with a dominant principal band of stability that depends sensitively on the stellar central pressure, the equation of state, and the magnitude of the parameter $|a|$. Outside the stable bands, massive particles can have bound but unstable precessing trajectories as well as unbounded motions. On the other hand, for null geodesics, we find no evidence for photon spheres outside the neutron star within the parameter range studied.

</details>


### [47] [Phase Transitions, Geodesic Structure, and Thermodynamic Properties Measurement of Einstein-Maxwell-Power Yang-Mills Black Hole Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08222)
*Abdelmalek Bouzenada,Allan. R. P. Moreira,Shi-Hai Dong,Guo-Hua Sun,Muhammad Sharif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the geometry, particle dynamics, and thermodynamics of Einstein-Maxwell-Power-Yang-Mills black holes, showing that the nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter significantly alters horizon structure, photon orbits, ISCO, and induces both first- and second-order phase transitions.
\n\n
本文研究了Einstein-Maxwell-Power-Yang-Mills黑洞的几何结构、粒子动力学和热力学性质，表明非线性Yang-Mills参数显著改变了视界结构、光子轨道、ISCO，并诱导出一阶和二阶相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from extending the standard Einstein-Yang-Mills theory to include nonlinear Yang-Mills fields via a power-law invariant, which may better model strong-field regimes or provide insights into quantum gravity effects. Understanding how such nonlinearities affect spacetime geometry, observable features like BH shadow, and thermodynamic stability is crucial for both theoretical and phenomenological studies of black holes.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于通过幂律不变量将标准Einstein-Yang-Mills理论推广至包含非线性Yang-Mills场的情形，这可能更准确地描述强场区域或为量子引力效应提供线索。理解此类非线性项如何影响时空几何、黑洞阴影等可观测量以及热力学稳定性，对黑洞的理论与现象学研究至关重要。

Method: The authors analyze the metric function $f(r)$ to study horizon and causal structures. They solve null and timelike geodesic equations to obtain effective potentials, photon sphere radius, Lyapunov exponent for photon orbit stability, and ISCO for massive particles. Thermodynamically, they compute mass, Hawking temperature $T_H$, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S$, heat capacity $C$, and Gibbs free energy $G$, using divergences in $C$ to identify second-order phase transitions and comparing $G$ across branches to detect first-order transitions.
\n\n
作者通过分析度规函数$f(r)$研究视界与因果结构；求解零测地线与类时测地线方程，得到有效势、光子球半径、用于刻画光子轨道稳定性的Lyapunov指数，以及大质量粒子的ISCO。在热力学方面，计算黑洞质量、Hawking温度$T_H$、Bekenstein-Hawking熵$S$、热容$C$和Gibbs自由能$G$，利用$C$的发散点识别二阶相变，并通过比较不同分支的$G$来探测一阶相变。

Result: The nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter modifies the number and location of horizons, shifts the photon sphere and ISCO radii, and alters the effective potential for both photons and massive particles. The Lyapunov exponent reveals changes in orbital instability timescales. Thermodynamically, the system exhibits second-order phase transitions at heat capacity divergences and first-order transitions via Gibbs free energy crossings, with critical points and stability regions strongly dependent on the Yang-Mills nonlinearity.
\n\n
非线性Yang-Mills参数改变了视界的数量与位置，移动了光子球和ISCO半径，并修正了光子与大质量粒子的有效势。Lyapunov指数揭示了轨道不稳定性时标的改变。在热力学上，系统在热容发散处表现出二阶相变，并通过Gibbs自由能交叉点展现出一阶相变，其临界点与稳定区域强烈依赖于Yang-Mills非线性参数。

Conclusion: The inclusion of a power-law Yang-Mills term enriches the physical structure of black holes, yielding distinct geometric, dynamical, and thermodynamic signatures. These findings suggest that nonlinear gauge fields can significantly influence both observable phenomena (e.g., BH shadow, accretion disk properties) and phase behavior, offering new avenues to test extensions of general relativity and Yang-Mills theory in strong-gravity regimes.
\n\n
引入幂律Yang-Mills项丰富了黑洞的物理结构，产生独特的几何、动力学和热力学特征。这些结果表明，非线性规范场可显著影响可观测现象（如黑洞阴影、吸积盘特性）及相变行为，为在强引力区域检验广义相对论与Yang-Mills理论的扩展提供了新途径。

Abstract: In this work, we test the geometrical structure and thermodynamic properties of the Einstein-Maxwell-Power-Yang-Mills black hole (BH) models, which constitute a nonlinear generalization of the standard Einstein-Yang-Mills theory through the inclusion of a power-law Yang-Mills invariant. Also, we begin by analyzing the spacetime geometry via the metric function $f(r)$ and examine the modifications induced by the electromagnetic charge and nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter on the horizon structure, causal structure, and gravitational potential. Subsequently, the dynamics of photons and massive particles are explored through the study of null and timelike geodesics, allowing the determination of the effective potential, photon sphere radius, and associated BH shadow. Also, the stability of circular photon orbits is quantified using the Lyapunov exponent, which characterizes the timescale of orbital instability and provides a direct link to observable photon ring features. For massive particles, the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) is calculated, illustrating the influence of BH parameters on the dynamics of accretion disks. From the thermodynamic viewpoint, we compute the principal thermodynamic quantities, including the BH mass, Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy, to assess both local and global stability of the system. The divergence of the heat capacity signals the occurrence of second-order phase transitions, whereas the Gibbs free energy analysis identifies possible first-order phase transitions between distinct thermodynamic configurations. In this context, our results demonstrate that the nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter strongly affects the spacetime geometry, particle dynamics, and thermodynamic phase structure, shifting the location of stability regions and critical points associated with phase transitions.
