### [48] [Disformal transformations in a Palatini extension of Horndeski's gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08401)
*Aleksander Kozak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper extends Horndeski's theory into the Palatini formalism by treating the metric and symmetric connection as independent, introducing a new connection transformation that—combined with metric disformal transformations—leaves the action form-invariant. The resulting theory reduces on-shell to kinetic gravity braiding, a metric subclass of Horndeski gravity. Using invariant metric and connection constructs, the authors recover a purely metric description. A cosmological application demonstrates late-time cosmic acceleration asymptoting to de Sitter, with connections to $k$-essence theories featuring non-minimal scalar-matter coupling in the Einstein frame.
\n\n
本文将Horndeski理论推广至Palatini形式，将度规张量与（对称）联络视为先验独立的几何对象，并引入一种新的联络变换，使得作用量在度规的disformal变换与该新联络变换下保持形式不变。所构造的理论在壳（on-shell）约化为Horndeski引力的一个度规子类——kinetic gravity braiding。作者进一步引入了不变的度规与联络，并证明由此定义的物理量可导出一个纯度规理论。在宇宙学应用中，该理论通过Einstein框架下标量场与物质项的非平凡耦合，展现出通向de Sitter相的晚期宇宙加速膨胀行为，与$k$-essence型理论存在潜在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring gravitational theories beyond General Relativity that maintain second-order field equations and avoid Ostrogradsky instabilities. Horndeski's theory is the most general scalar-tensor theory with this property in the metric formalism. Extending it to the Palatini framework—where metric and connection are independent—offers a new avenue to construct viable modified gravity models, especially for cosmology. The authors aim to preserve symmetry under generalized transformations (disformal for the metric and a novel one for the connection) while ensuring theoretical consistency and phenomenological relevance, such as explaining cosmic acceleration.
\n\n
动机源于探索超越广义相对论的引力理论，这些理论需保持场方程为二阶以避免Ostrogradsky不稳定性。Horndeski理论是度规形式下满足此条件的最一般的标量-张量理论。将其推广至Palatini框架（其中度规与联络独立）为构建可行的修改引力模型提供了新途径，尤其适用于宇宙学研究。作者旨在保持作用量在广义变换下的对称性（度规的disformal变换与联络的新变换），同时确保理论自洽性及现象学相关性，例如解释宇宙加速膨胀。

Method: The authors employ the Palatini variational principle, treating the metric $g_{\mu\nu}$ and symmetric affine connection $\Gamma^\lambda_{\mu\nu}$ as independent variables. They define a joint transformation: a disformal transformation of the metric, $g_{\mu\nu} \to A(\phi,X)g_{\mu\nu} + B(\phi,X)\partial_\mu\phi\partial_\nu\phi$, and a new transformation of the connection involving derivatives of the scalar field $\phi$ and its kinetic term $X = -\\frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\partial_\mu\phi\partial_\nu\phi$. They construct an action functional invariant under this combined transformation. By solving the connection equation of motion algebraically (on-shell), they reduce the theory to a metric formulation. They also define invariant metric $\hat{g}_{\mu\nu}$ and invariant connection $\hat{\Gamma}^\lambda_{\mu\nu}$, showing that the theory can be recast entirely in terms of these invariant objects, yielding a standard metric theory. Finally, they apply the framework to a Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker (FLRW) cosmology with matter minimally coupled in the Einstein frame, analyzing the background dynamics.
\n\n
作者采用Palatini变分原理，将度规$g_{\mu\nu}$与对称仿射联络$\Gamma^\lambda_{\mu\nu}$视为独立变量。他们定义了一种联合变换：度规的disformal变换$g_{\mu\nu} \to A(\phi,X)g_{\mu\nu} + B(\phi,X)\partial_\mu\phi\partial_\nu\phi$，以及一种涉及标量场$\phi$及其动能项$X = -\\frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\partial_\mu\phi\partial_\nu\phi$导数的新联络变换。他们构建了一个在此联合变换下形式不变的作用量。通过代数求解联络的运动方程（on-shell），将理论约化为度规形式。此外，他们定义了不变度规$\hat{g}_{\mu\nu}$与不变联络$\hat{\Gamma}^\lambda_{\mu\nu}$，并证明该理论可完全用这些不变量重写，从而得到一个标准的度规理论。最后，他们将该框架应用于Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker（FLRW）宇宙学模型，其中物质在Einstein框架下最小耦合，并分析了背景动力学。

Result: The main results are: (1) A consistent Palatini extension of Horndeski theory is constructed, invariant under combined disformal (metric) and new (connection) transformations. (2) On-shell, this theory is equivalent to the metric Horndeski subclass known as kinetic gravity braiding. (3) The introduction of invariant metric and connection allows reformulation as a purely metric theory, clarifying its physical content. (4) In a cosmological setting with non-minimal scalar-matter coupling in the Einstein frame, a specific model yields late-time cosmic acceleration that asymptotically approaches a de Sitter solution, demonstrating phenomenological viability.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 构建了一个自洽的Horndeski理论的Palatini推广，其作用量在联合的disformal（度规）与新（联络）变换下保持形式不变；(2) 在壳条件下，该理论等价于度规Horndeski理论的一个子类——kinetic gravity braiding；(3) 通过引入不变度规与不变联络，可将理论重写为纯度规形式，从而澄清其物理内涵；(4) 在Einstein框架下具有非最小标量-物质耦合的宇宙学模型中，特定模型能产生晚期宇宙加速膨胀，并渐近趋于de Sitter解，展现出良好的现象学可行性。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that extending Horndeski gravity to the Palatini formalism with appropriate symmetry principles leads to a theoretically consistent framework that, despite its apparent bimetric nature, reduces to a known healthy metric theory on-shell. The use of invariant geometric objects provides a powerful tool to map the Palatini theory to its metric counterpart. The successful reproduction of late-time cosmic acceleration suggests that such Palatini-disformal theories are promising candidates for dark energy models and warrant further investigation, particularly regarding their perturbative stability and observational signatures.
\n\n
本文表明，将Horndeski引力在适当对称性原则下推广至Palatini形式，可得到一个理论自洽的框架，尽管其表观上具有双度规特征，但在壳条件下约化为已知的健康度规理论。利用不变几何对象为将Palatini理论映射到其度规对应物提供了有力工具。该理论成功复现晚期宇宙加速膨胀，表明此类Palatini-disformal理论是暗能量模型的有力候选者，值得进一步研究，尤其是在微扰稳定性与观测信号方面。

Abstract: In this paper, we extend Horndeski's theory into the Palatini approach, assuming that the metric tensor and the (symmetric) connection are a priori independent objects. We introduce an additional transformation of the connection and write down the action functional being form-invariant under both the disformal transformation of the metric and the new transformation of the connection. We show that such a theory reduces on-shell to a metric subclass of Horndeski's gravity called kinetic gravity braiding. We also introduce an invariant metric and connection, and demonstrate that quantities defined in such a way lead to a metric theory. In the second part of the paper, we consider a simple cosmological model within the theory and explore its potential links with $ k$-essence-type theories, with a non-trivial coupling between the scalar field and the matter part of the action in the Einstein frame. We show that there exists a model that reproduces late-time cosmic acceleration, approaching asymptotically the de Sitter phase, motivating further study of the theories.

</details>


### [49] [Local Origin of Hidden Symmetry in Rotating Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08408)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that the hallmark features of Kerr geometry—hidden symmetry, separability, and Petrov type D structure—emerge locally from the Einstein equations under minimal physical assumptions (stationarity, axisymmetry, and local equilibrium), without imposing global conditions or vacuum. The mixed Einstein equations enforce a rigid alignment between radial and angular sectors, leading to a classification of local solutions via Schwarzian derivatives into Möbius, exponential, and trigonometric branches, with only the first two compatible with global regularity, thereby singling out Kerr-type geometries.
\n\n
本文证明了Kerr几何的标志性特征——隐藏对称性、可分离性（separability）和Petrov type D结构——在最小物理假设（定常性、轴对称性和局部平衡条件）下，作为Einstein方程的局部结果自然出现，无需施加全局边界条件或真空假设。混合Einstein方程强制径向与角向部分之间存在刚性射影对齐（rigid projective alignment），通过Schwarzian导数将局部解分类为Möbius、指数和三角函数分支；其中仅前两类与全局正则性相容，从而唯一地选出Kerr-type几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand why the Kerr solution exhibits such special mathematical properties—like separability of the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, existence of a Killing-Yano tensor, and algebraic speciality (Petrov type D)—and whether these are contingent on global or vacuum assumptions, or instead reflect a deeper local structure encoded in the Einstein equations themselves. The authors aim to show that these features are not accidental but arise inevitably from local physics under mild symmetry and equilibrium conditions.
\n\n
动机在于理解为何Kerr解具有如此特殊的数学性质——如Hamilton-Jacobi方程的可分离性、Killing-Yano张量的存在性以及代数特殊性（Petrov type D）——并探究这些性质是否依赖于全局或真空假设，抑或反映了Einstein方程本身所蕴含的更深层局部结构。作者旨在证明：在温和的对称性与平衡条件下，这些特征并非偶然，而是由局部物理必然导出。

Method: The authors work in a locally non-rotating orthonormal frame adapted to stationary and axisymmetric spacetimes. They impose only stationarity, axisymmetry, and a minimal "local equilibrium condition" (requiring no torque between fluid elements in the comoving frame). They analyze the mixed components of the Einstein equations (those coupling radial and angular directions) without assuming vacuum, algebraic speciality, or separability. Using the structure of these equations, they derive a constraint that enforces projective alignment between the radial and angular metric functions. This leads to an equality of Schwarzian derivatives $\\{R, r\\} = \\{\\Theta, \\theta\\}$, which classifies local solutions into three types based on the value of the common Schwarzian invariant.
\n\n
作者采用一个适用于定常、轴对称时空的局部非旋转正交标架（locally non-rotating orthonormal frame）。仅施加定常性、轴对称性及一个最小“局部平衡条件”（要求共动系中流体元之间无扭矩）。他们分析Einstein方程的混合分量（耦合径向与角向的分量），而不预设真空、代数特殊性或可分离性。通过这些方程的结构，推导出一个约束，强制径向与角向度规函数之间满足射影对齐。这导致Schwarzian导数等式 $\\{R, r\\} = \\{\\Theta, \\theta\\}$，根据共同的Schwarzian不变量之值，将局部解分为三类。

Result: The mixed Einstein equations imply a universal relation $\\{R(r), r\\} = \\{\\Theta(\\theta), \\theta\\} = c$, where $c$ is a constant. This yields three families of local solutions: (i) Möbius ($c > 0$), (ii) exponential ($c = 0$), and (iii) trigonometric ($c < 0$). Global regularity (e.g., absence of conical singularities or pathological horizons) generically rules out the trigonometric branch. The remaining branches correspond precisely to geometries with Kerr-like structure, including emergent Petrov type D algebraic speciality and hidden symmetries. Crucially, this holds even in the presence of matter, as the mixed equations are insensitive to the detailed form of a comoving stress-energy tensor.
\n\n
混合Einstein方程导出普适关系 $\\{R(r), r\\} = \\{\\Theta(\\theta), \\theta\\} = c$，其中 $c$ 为常数。由此得到三类局部解：(i) Möbius型（$c > 0$），(ii) 指数型（$c = 0$），(iii) 三角函数型（$c < 0$）。全局正则性（如无锥形奇点或病态视界）通常排除三角函数分支。剩余分支恰好对应具有Kerr-like结构的几何，包括涌现的Petrov type D代数特殊性与隐藏对称性。关键的是，即使存在物质，该结论依然成立，因为混合方程对共动应力-能量张量的具体形式不敏感。

Conclusion: The kinematical essence of Kerr geometry—its separability, hidden symmetries, and Petrov type D nature—is not an artifact of global boundary conditions or vacuum, but is locally encoded in the Einstein equations through the interplay of stationarity, axisymmetry, and local equilibrium. This provides a foundational explanation for the uniqueness and universality of the Kerr solution, positioning it as the generic local outcome for rotating relativistic systems in equilibrium, even with matter present.
\n\n
Kerr几何的运动学本质——其可分离性、隐藏对称性及Petrov type D特性——并非全局边界条件或真空假设的人工产物，而是通过定常性、轴对称性与局部平衡条件的相互作用，被局部编码于Einstein方程之中。这为Kerr解的唯一性与普适性提供了基础性解释，表明即使存在物质，Kerr解也是处于平衡态的旋转相对论系统的典型局部结果。

Abstract: We show that the hidden symmetry and separability characteristic of Kerr geometry arise as an inevitable \emph{local} consequence of the Einstein equations for rotating spacetimes. Without assuming separability, algebraic speciality, Killing-Yano symmetry, or global boundary conditions, we analyze general stationary and axisymmetric geometries in a locally non-rotating orthonormal frame. Imposing a minimal physical requirement, the local equilibrium condition, we find that the mixed Einstein equations enforce a rigid projective alignment between the radial and angular sectors. This result does not rely on vacuum: the mixed equations are insensitive to the detailed form of a comoving stress-energy tensor. Consistency then requires equality of Schwarzian derivatives, leading to a universal classification of local solutions into Möbius, exponential, and trigonometric branches. Global regularity generically excludes the trigonometric branch, leaving precisely the Kerr-type sector and the emergence of Petrov type D structure. This provides a structural precursor to Kerr uniqueness, demonstrating that the kinematical core of Kerr geometry is encoded locally within the Einstein equations.

</details>


### [50] [Signature Change in $f(R, T_φ)$ Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08410)
*Serkan Doruk Hazinedar,Yaghoub Heydarzade*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies an $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ gravity model coupled to a scalar field and shows it admits classical degenerate metric solutions that allow a smooth Euclidean-to-Lorentzian signature change, analogous to known solutions in general relativity.
\n\n
本文研究了一个与标量场耦合的 $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ 引力模型，表明该理论允许存在经典的退化度规解，这些解能实现从欧几里得域到洛伦兹域的平滑过渡，类似于广义相对论中已知的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore whether modified gravity theories like $f(R, T_\\varphi)$—which extend general relativity by including non-minimal couplings between geometry and matter—can support classical signature change, a phenomenon of interest in quantum gravity and early-universe cosmology.
\n\n
动机在于探索诸如 $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ 这类修改引力理论——通过引入几何与物质之间的非最小耦合来扩展广义相对论——是否能够支持经典的度规符号改变（signature change），这一现象在量子引力和早期宇宙学中具有重要意义。

Method: The authors analyze the field equations derived from an action of the form $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} f(R, T_\\varphi) + S_\\varphi$, where $T_\\varphi$ is the trace of the energy-momentum tensor of a scalar field $\\varphi$. They search for degenerate metric solutions (where $\\det g_{\\mu\\nu} = 0$ at some hypersurface) that smoothly interpolate between Euclidean ($+++$) and Lorentzian ($-+++$) signatures.
\n\n
作者分析了由作用量 $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} f(R, T_\\varphi) + S_\\varphi$ 导出的场方程，其中 $T_\\varphi$ 是标量场 $\\varphi$ 的能量-动量张量的迹。他们寻找退化度规解（在某些超曲面上满足 $\\det g_{\\mu\\nu} = 0$），这些解可在欧几里得（$+++$）和洛伦兹（$-+++$）符号之间平滑插值。

Result: The paper identifies explicit classical solutions within the $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ framework that exhibit a smooth signature change from Euclidean to Lorentzian geometry, demonstrating that such behavior is not exclusive to general relativity but can also arise in modified gravity theories with matter-geometry coupling.
\n\n
论文在 $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ 框架内找到了显式的经典解，这些解展现出从欧几里得几何到洛伦兹几何的平滑符号改变，表明这种行为并非广义相对论所独有，也可出现在具有物质-几何耦合的修改引力理论中。

Conclusion: The existence of classical signature-changing solutions in $f(R, T_\\varphi)$ gravity suggests that such models may provide viable classical frameworks for studying quantum-gravity-inspired scenarios like the Hartle–Hawking no-boundary proposal or Euclidean quantum gravity, without requiring full quantum treatment.
\n\n
$f(R, T_\\varphi)$ 引力中存在经典符号改变解表明，这类模型可能为研究受量子引力启发的情景（如 Hartle–Hawking 无边界提案或欧几里得量子引力）提供可行的经典框架，而无需完整的量子处理。

Abstract: We investigate a simple $f(R, T_φ)$ gravity model coupled to a scalar field and demonstrate that the theory admits classical degenerate metric solutions, analogous to those known in general relativity. In particular, we identify a class of solutions that exhibits a smooth transition from a Euclidean to a Lorentzian domain, thus yielding a classical dynamical realization of signature change.

</details>


### [51] [Black hole shadows in nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08441)
*Cláudio Gomes,Margarida Lima,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Luís F. D. da Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates black hole shadows in nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity—a metric-affine theory with a non-dynamical Weyl vector inducing non-metricity—deriving modified Schwarzschild- and Reissner–Nordström-like solutions. Using Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) constraints on Sgr A*, the authors place lower bounds on the Weyl integration constant $ω$, demonstrating that current shadow observations can meaningfully constrain spacetime non-metricity.
\n\n
本文研究了非最小耦合Weyl联络引力理论中的黑洞阴影——这是一种具有非动力学Weyl矢量并引入non-metricity的metric-affine理论——推导出修正的Schwarzschild型和Reissner–Nordström型解。利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）对Sgr A*的观测限制，作者对Weyl积分常数$ω$设定了下限，表明当前的阴影观测已能有效约束时空的non-metricity。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test extensions of General Relativity (GR) that incorporate non-Riemannian geometry, specifically spacetime non-metricity via a Weyl vector field, using observational data from black hole shadow imaging. The authors aim to establish whether horizon-scale observations can constrain such metric-affine theories, which remain theoretically viable due to their second-order field equations despite departing from Riemannian geometry.
\n\n
动机在于利用黑洞阴影成像的观测数据，检验包含非黎曼几何（特别是通过Weyl矢量场引入时空non-metricity）的广义相对论（GR）扩展理论。作者旨在确定视界尺度的观测是否能够约束这类metric-affine理论——尽管其偏离了黎曼几何框架，但由于具有二阶场方程，这些理论在理论上仍具可行性。

Method: The authors consider nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity, where spacetime is endowed with both a metric and a non-dynamical Weyl vector field $Q_μ$, leading to non-metricity while preserving second-order field equations. They derive exact black hole solutions analogous to Schwarzschild and Reissner–Nordström, modified by a Weyl integration constant $ω$. The shadow radius for a distant observer at $r_O = 4.1\times 10^{10}M$ is computed using null geodesics in this geometry. These theoretical predictions are then compared with EHT 2σ observational constraints on the shadow size of Sgr A* to infer bounds on $ω$ across three distinct models.
\n\n
作者采用非最小耦合Weyl联络引力理论，其中时空由度规和一个非动力学Weyl矢量场$Q_μ$共同描述，从而引入non-metricity，同时保持场方程为二阶。他们推导出与Schwarzschild和Reissner–Nordström解类似但受Weyl积分常数$ω$修正的精确黑洞解。通过计算该几何中零测地线，得到距离为$r_O = 4.1\times 10^{10}M$的远处观测者所见的阴影半径，并将此理论预测与EHT对Sgr A*阴影尺寸的2σ观测限制进行对比，从而在三种不同模型下推断出对$ω$的约束。

Result: The analysis yields stringent lower bounds on the Weyl parameter: $ω\gtrsim 10^{11.7}M$ (model I), $ω\gtrsim 10^{10.5}M$ (model II), and $ω\sim 10^{12}M$ (model III), assuming consistency with EHT 2σ data for Sgr A*. These results demonstrate that even in the absence of direct detection of non-metricity, current black hole shadow observations already provide meaningful empirical constraints on Weyl-based metric-affine gravity.
\n\n
分析得出对Weyl参数的严格下限：$ω\gtrsim 10^{11.7}M$（模型I）、$ω\gtrsim 10^{10.5}M$（模型II）和$ω\sim 10^{12}M$（模型III），前提是与EHT对Sgr A*的2σ数据一致。这些结果表明，即使尚未直接探测到non-metricity，当前的黑洞阴影观测已能对基于Weyl的metric-affine引力理论提供有意义的经验约束。

Conclusion: Black hole shadow observations serve as a powerful probe of gravitational theories beyond Riemannian geometry. The study establishes that nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity, despite its departure from standard GR, is testable with current EHT data, and that spacetime non-metricity is already constrained at astrophysical scales. This bridges theoretical metric-affine frameworks with real observational data, opening avenues for further tests of non-Riemannian gravity.
\n\n
黑洞阴影观测是检验超越黎曼几何的引力理论的有力工具。本研究表明，尽管非最小耦合Weyl联络引力偏离了标准广义相对论，但仍可通过当前EHT数据进行检验，且时空non-metricity已在天体物理尺度上受到限制。这架起了理论metric-affine框架与实际观测数据之间的桥梁，为未来检验非黎曼引力开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We study black hole shadows in nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity, a metric-affine extension of general relativity in which spacetime is described by a metric and a Weyl vector field encoding non-metricity. Despite going beyond the Riemannian framework, the presence of a non-dynamical Weyl vector ensures second-order field equations. The theory admits Schwarzschild- and Reissner--Nordström-like solutions modified by a Weyl integration constant that parametrizes deviations from General Relativity. By computing the corresponding shadow radii and confronting them with the Event Horizon Telescope constraints on Sgr A*, we place observational bounds on the Weyl parameter. Assuming an observer distance $r_O = 4.1\times 10^{10}M$ and requiring consistency at the $2σ$ level, we obtain $ω\gtrsim 10^{11.7}M$ (model I), $ω\gtrsim 10^{10.5}M$ (model II), and $ω\sim 10^{12}M$ (model III). Our results show that present horizon-scale imaging already sets meaningful limits on spacetime non-metricity. This work highlights the power of black hole shadow observations as probes of extended gravitational dynamics and establishes a direct link between Weyl-based theories and current astrophysical data.

### [52] [A dynamical approach to General Relativity based on proper time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08568)
*Jaume de Haro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reinterprets the spacetime interval $ds^2$ as the differential of proper time with direct physical significance, derives its form in static and moving gravitational fields using Fermat's principle for massive particles and Lorentz invariance, and shows that Einstein's field equations emerge uniquely as the nonlinear completion required by energy-momentum conservation and self-consistency.
\n\n
本文将时空线元 $ds^2$ 重新诠释为具有直接物理意义的固有时微分，利用适用于有质量粒子的费马原理（即自由落体轨迹使固有时取极值）和洛伦兹不变性，推导出静态及运动引力场中 $ds^2$ 的形式，并表明爱因斯坦场方程作为非线性延拓，是能量-动量守恒与引力相互作用自洽性所唯一要求的协变闭包。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to ground General Relativity in a more physically intuitive principle—extremization of proper time for massive particles—rather than starting from abstract geometric postulates. By emphasizing the physical meaning of $ds^2$ as $d\\tau$, the proper time differential, and combining it with the universality of free fall and Lorentz invariance, the authors aim to show that Einstein's equations are not arbitrary geometric axioms but necessary consequences of consistency and conservation laws.
\n\n
动机在于将广义相对论建立在更直观的物理原理之上——即有质量粒子沿固有时取极值的轨迹运动，而非从抽象的几何公设出发。通过强调 $ds^2$ 作为固有时微分 $d\\tau$ 的物理意义，并结合自由落体普适性与洛伦兹不变性，作者旨在表明爱因斯坦方程并非任意的几何公理，而是由自洽性与守恒律所必然导出的结果。

Method: The method begins by applying an extended Fermat’s principle: freely falling massive particles follow timelike geodesics that locally maximize proper time $\\tau = \\int ds$. Using the universality of Galilean free fall, the authors constrain the form of $ds^2$ in a static weak gravitational field. They then invoke Lorentz invariance to generalize this to moving sources, yielding the harmonic-gauge linearized metric. Finally, they analyze the consistency of coupling gravity to its own energy-momentum tensor, showing that closure under diffeomorphism invariance forces the appearance of the Ricci tensor, leading uniquely to Einstein’s field equations.
\n\n
方法始于推广的费马原理：自由下落的有质量粒子沿类时测地线运动，使固有时 $\\tau = \\int ds$ 局部取极大值。利用伽利略自由落体普适性，作者约束了静态弱引力场中 $ds^2$ 的形式；再通过洛伦兹不变性将其推广至运动源情形，得到谐和规范下的线性化度规。最后，通过分析引力与其自身能量-动量张量耦合的自洽性，表明在微分同胚不变性下闭合的唯一可能要求引入 Ricci 张量，从而唯一导出爱因斯坦场方程。

Result: The authors derive the weak-field metric in harmonic gauge directly from physical principles (proper time extremization and Lorentz invariance), without assuming the Einstein-Hilbert action or geometric curvature. Moreover, they demonstrate that demanding local energy-momentum conservation ($\\nabla_\\mu T^{\\mu\
u} = 0$) and self-interaction consistency in the nonlinear regime uniquely selects the Einstein tensor $G_{\\mu\
u} = R_{\\mu\
u} - \\frac{1}{2}R g_{\\mu\
u}$ as the left-hand side of the field equations, thereby recovering General Relativity as the only viable theory.
\n\n
作者仅基于物理原理（固有时极值化与洛伦兹不变性）直接导出了谐和规范下的弱场度规，无需预设爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量或几何曲率概念。此外，他们证明：在非线性区域，若要求局域能量-动量守恒（$\\nabla_\\mu T^{\\mu\
u} = 0$）与自相互作用自洽性，则唯一可选的场方程左侧为爱因斯坦张量 $G_{\\mu\
u} = R_{\\mu\
u} - \\frac{1}{2}R g_{\\mu\
u}$，从而将广义相对论恢复为唯一可行的理论。

Conclusion: Einstein's field equations are not fundamental postulates but emergent from the requirement that the gravitational interaction, initially defined through the physical proper time interval and Lorentz symmetry, remains self-consistent and conserves energy-momentum when extended to strong fields. This provides a physically motivated derivation of General Relativity rooted in variational principles and conservation laws rather than geometric axioms.
\n\n
爱因斯坦场方程并非基本公设，而是源于如下要求：最初通过物理固有时间隔与洛伦兹对称性定义的引力相互作用，在推广至强场时必须保持自洽并满足能量-动量守恒。这为广义相对论提供了一种基于变分原理与守恒律、而非几何公理的物理解释路径。

Abstract: This work places the invariant $ds^2$ at the center of the gravitational interaction, interpreting it not as a purely geometric object but as the differential of proper time, endowed with direct physical meaning. Starting from the extension of Fermat's principle to massive particles--namely, the requirement that freely falling bodies follow trajectories that extremize proper time, which for timelike motion corresponds to a local maximum--and invoking the universality of Galilean free fall, we derive the form of $ds^2$ in a static gravitational field. Lorentz invariance then provides the natural framework to extend this result to systems involving moving matter. The invariant derived through this procedure matches the weak-field limit of General Relativity formulated in the harmonic gauge.
  Within this linearized regime, we show that the structure of the theory already contains the seeds of its non-linear completion: any dynamically consistent extension to strong gravitational fields necessarily involves the Ricci tensor. From this viewpoint, Einstein's field equations appear not as a postulated geometric law, but as the unique covariant closure required to ensure energy momentum conservation and the self consistency of the gravitational interaction.

### [54] [Secondary gravitational waves against a strong gravitational wave in the Bianchi VI universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08628)
*Konstantin E. Osetrin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper introduces a proper-time method to analytically construct secondary gravitational-wave solutions as perturbations around an exact vacuum gravitational wave background in the Bianchi VI universe. Stability of these perturbative solutions is demonstrated for a continuous range of wave parameters.
\n\n
本文提出了一种固有时方法，用于在Bianchi VI宇宙中围绕精确真空引力波背景解析地构建次级引力波解。研究表明，对于连续范围的波参数，这些微扰解是稳定的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop an analytical framework—distinct from numerical relativity—for modeling secondary gravitational waves generated in strong-field regimes, using the exact vacuum solution in Bianchi VI spacetime as a background. This addresses the need for controlled perturbative treatments in anisotropic cosmological settings where standard approximations may fail.
\n\n
动机在于发展一种区别于数值相对论的解析框架，用于在强场区域中建模由Bianchi VI时空中的精确真空解作为背景所产生的次级引力波。这解决了在各向异性宇宙学背景下标准近似可能失效时对可控微扰处理的需求。

Method: The authors employ a proper-time method based on the proper time of test particles in a privileged wave coordinate system adapted to the Bianchi VI exact gravitational wave background. They linearize Einstein’s equations around this background and impose compatibility conditions to derive ordinary differential equations (ODEs) for the metric perturbations. The solutions to these ODEs yield analytical expressions for the secondary gravitational-wave metric components.
\n\n
作者采用一种基于测试粒子固有时的方法，在适配于Bianchi VI精确引力波背景的特权波坐标系中进行操作。他们在此背景上对爱因斯坦方程进行线性化，并施加相容性条件以导出度规微扰的常微分方程（ODEs）。这些ODEs的解给出了次级引力波度规分量的解析表达式。

Result: The paper obtains explicit analytical forms for the metric components of secondary gravitational waves via solutions to derived ODEs. It further demonstrates that for a continuum of gravitational wave parameters (e.g., frequency, amplitude), the perturbative solutions remain stable under the imposed compatibility and field equations.
\n\n
本文通过求解所导出的常微分方程，获得了次级引力波度规分量的显式解析形式。此外，研究表明，对于引力波参数（如频率、振幅）的一个连续集，微扰解在所施加的相容性和场方程下保持稳定。

Conclusion: The proper-time method provides a robust analytical tool for constructing stable secondary gravitational-wave solutions in anisotropic Bianchi VI spacetimes, offering a new avenue for studying nonlinear gravitational dynamics beyond numerical simulations.
\n\n
固有时方法为在各向异性Bianchi VI时空构建稳定的次级引力波解提供了一种稳健的解析工具，为超越数值模拟研究非线性引力动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: A proper-time method for constructing models of dynamic gravitational-wave fields is presented. Using the proper-time method, analytical (not numerical) models of secondary gravitational waves are constructed as perturbative solutions of linearized field equations against the background of the exact wave solution of Einstein's equations for the vacuum in the Bianchi VI universe in a privileged wave coordinate system. Relations for the proper time of test particles against the background of a strong gravitational wave are used. The analytical form of the metric components for secondary gravitational waves is found from compatibility conditions for the field equations. From the field equations, an explicit form of ordinary differential equations and their solutions is obtained for functions included in small corrections to the metric for secondary gravitational waves. It is shown that there exists a continuum of gravitational wave parameters for which the perturbative solutions are stable.

### [55] [A Deep Learning Framework for Amplitude Generation of Generic EMRIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08635)
*Yan-bo Zeng,Jian-dong Zhang,Yi-Ming Hu,Jianwei Mei*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a deep learning-based surrogate model using a convolutional encoder-decoder architecture to rapidly generate Teukolsky amplitudes for generic Kerr EMRI orbits, achieving millisecond inference times and median errors of $\\sim10^{-3}$ by leveraging transfer learning from simpler orbit configurations.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于深度学习的代理模型，采用卷积编码器-解码器架构，通过从较简单的轨道构型迁移学习，快速生成通用Kerr EMRI轨道的Teukolsky振幅，在毫秒级推理时间内达到约$\\sim10^{-3}$的中位模态分布误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Modeling Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) for space-borne gravitational wave detectors demands waveform templates that are both highly accurate and computationally efficient. The bottleneck lies in the rapid evaluation of Teukolsky amplitudes across a four-dimensional parameter space (mass ratio, eccentricity, inclination, and orbital frequency) involving $\\sim10^5$ harmonic modes. Traditional numerical or interpolation-based methods are too slow or memory-intensive for data analysis pipelines, necessitating a new approach.
\n\n
为星载引力波探测器建模Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs)需要既高度精确又计算高效的波形模板。瓶颈在于在四维参数空间（质量比、偏心率、倾角和轨道频率）中快速计算涉及$\\sim10^5$个谐波模态的Teukolsky振幅。传统的数值方法或基于插值的方法对于数据分析流程而言过于缓慢或内存消耗过大，因此需要一种新方法。

Method: The authors develop a convolutional encoder-decoder neural network to perform end-to-end global fitting of the Teukolsky amplitudes. They employ a transfer learning strategy: training begins with the simplest case—Schwarzschild circular orbits—and progressively incorporates more complex physics (eccentricity, inclination, and spin) until the model handles fully generic Kerr orbits. The training data is derived from a semi-analytical Post-Newtonian (PN) approximation dataset, which balances accuracy and computational cost. This staged learning reduces the required training data volume and stabilizes convergence.
\n\n
作者开发了一种卷积编码器-解码器神经网络，对Teukolsky振幅进行端到端的全局拟合。他们采用迁移学习策略：训练从最简单的情形——Schwarzschild圆轨道开始，逐步引入更复杂的物理（偏心率、倾角和自旋），直到模型能够处理完全通用的Kerr轨道。训练数据源自半解析的Post-Newtonian (PN)近似数据集，在精度与计算成本之间取得平衡。这种分阶段学习减少了所需训练数据量并稳定了收敛过程。

Result: The resulting surrogate model generates the full set of $\\sim10^5$ harmonic Teukolsky amplitudes for generic Kerr EMRI orbits in milliseconds. It achieves a median mode-distribution error of approximately $\\sim10^{-3}$, demonstrating high fidelity across the four-dimensional parameter space. The use of transfer learning significantly reduces the size of the required training dataset while maintaining accuracy.
\n\n
所得到的代理模型可在毫秒内生成通用Kerr EMRI轨道的全部$\\sim10^5$个谐波Teukolsky振幅，中位模态分布误差约为$\\sim10^{-3}$，在四维参数空间中展现出高保真度。迁移学习的使用显著减少了所需训练数据集的规模，同时保持了精度。

Conclusion: The proposed deep learning framework with transfer learning provides a viable and efficient pathway to construct fast, accurate waveform models for EMRIs, overcoming the computational bottlenecks of traditional methods. This approach is well-suited for real-time data analysis in future space-based gravitational wave observatories like LISA.
\n\n
所提出的结合迁移学习的深度学习框架为构建快速、精确的EMRI波形模型提供了一条可行且高效的路径，克服了传统方法的计算瓶颈。该方法非常适合用于LISA等未来空间引力波天文台的实时数据分析。

Abstract: One of the main targets for space-borne gravitational wave detectors is the detection of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs). The data analysis of EMRIs requires waveform models that are both accurate and fast. The major challenge for the fast generation of such waveforms is the generation of the Teukolsky amplitudes for generic (eccentric and inclined) Kerr orbits. The requirement for the modeling of $\sim10^5$ harmonic modes across a four-dimensional parameter space makes traditional approaches, including direct computation or dense interpolation, computationally prohibitive. To overcome this issue, we introduce a convolutional encoder-decoder architecture for a fast and end-to-end global fitting of the Teukolsky amplitudes. We also adopt a transfer learning strategy to reduce the size of the training dataset, and the model is trained gradually from the simplest Schwarzschild circular orbits to generic Kerr orbits step by step. Within this framework, we obtain a surrogate model based on a semi-analytical Post-Newtonian dataset, and the full harmonic amplitudes can be generated within milliseconds, while the median mode-distribution error for generic orbits is approximately $\sim10^{-3}$. This result indicates that the framework is viable for constructing efficient waveform models for EMRIs.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

\n\n
动机源于需要理解暗物质晕如何影响黑洞的经典可观测量——如ISCO、光子球、引力透镜和阴影形态——并将理论预测与当前EHT观测进行对比，从而探索广义相对论与暗物质分布之间的相互作用。

Method: The authors analyze the modified Schwarzschild metric incorporating a dark matter halo, compute curvature invariants (Ricci scalar $R$, $R_{\\mu\
u}R^{\\mu\
u}$, and Kretschmann scalar), derive geodesic equations for massive and massless particles to obtain ISCO and photon sphere radii, apply the Gauss–Bonnet theorem to study weak gravitational lensing in both uniform and non-uniform plasma media, and compare synthetic BH shadow models with EHT data to constrain spacetime parameters.
\n\n
作者分析了包含暗物质晕修正的Schwarzschild度规，计算曲率不变量（Ricci标量 $R$、$R_{\\mu\
u}R^{\\mu\
u}$ 和Kretschmann标量），推导有质量与无质量粒子的测地线方程以获得ISCO和光子球半径，应用Gauss–Bonnet定理研究均匀与非均匀等离子体介质中的弱引力透镜，并将合成的黑洞阴影模型与EHT数据对比以约束时空参数。

Result: The presence of a dark matter halo increases the ISCO radius compared to the standard Schwarzschild case; the photon sphere is similarly affected. Weak lensing deflection angles are modified by both the DM distribution and plasma properties. The BH shadow size and shape depend on plasma density profiles, and EHT data place upper bounds on the dark matter-induced deviations from vacuum Schwarzschild geometry.
\n\n
暗物质晕的存在使得ISCO半径相较于标准Schwarzschild情形增大；光子球也受到类似影响。弱透镜偏转角受暗物质分布和等离子体性质共同修正。黑洞阴影的大小和形状依赖于等离子体密度分布，而EHT数据对暗物质引起的偏离真空Schwarzschild几何的参数设定了上限。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that dark matter halos leave potentially detectable imprints on black hole observables, particularly through ISCO shifts, lensing corrections, and shadow deformation in plasma. Combining EHT observations with plasma-aware modeling provides a viable pathway to constrain dark matter profiles near supermassive black holes.
\n\n
本文表明，暗物质晕会在黑洞可观测量上留下潜在可探测的印记，尤其体现在ISCO偏移、透镜修正以及等离子体中的阴影形变。结合EHT观测与考虑等离子体效应的建模，为约束超大质量黑洞附近的暗物质分布提供了可行途径。

Abstract: This article is devoted to the investigation of the observational properties of the Schwarzschild black hole (BH) surrounded by a dark matter (DM) halo. Our study commences with a brief review of spacetime, including the horizon structure and curvature invariants, which are the Ricci scalar, the square of the Ricci tensor, and the Kretschmann scalar. Subsequently, we explore the massive and massless particle dynamics around the Schwarzschild BH surrounded by a dark matter halo, including the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) and photon sphere radii. It was found that the radius of the ISCO increases under the influence of the spacetime parameters. Additionally, we investigate the weak gravitational lensing with the assumption that the BH is surrounded by a uniform and non-uniform plasma. Finally, we examine the impact of a plasma on the BH shadow and employ Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observational data to constrain the BH's parameters.

</details>

### [57] [Mass Without Mass from a Berry--Shifted SU(3) Holonomy Rotor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06770)
*Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates a mechanism in pure SU(3) Yang–Mills theory on a punctured three-ball that generates a finite energy scale (nonzero level spacing) without introducing explicit mass terms or Higgs fields. This “mass without mass” arises from gauge invariance, topology, and fixing a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ center sector, leading to a quantum rotor description with controlled adiabatic dynamics and a variational upper bound on the first positive Yang–Mills eigenvalue at the hadronic scale (~1 GeV).
\n\n
本文在穿孔三维球上的纯SU(3) Yang–Mills理论中展示了一种机制，该机制在不引入显式质量项或Higgs场的情况下生成有限能量标度（非零能级间距）。这种“无质量的质量”（mass without mass）源于规范不变性、拓扑结构以及固定$\mathbb{Z}_3$中心扇区，从而导出一个具有受控绝热动力学的量子转子描述，并对首个正Yang–Mills本征值给出了在强子标度（~1 GeV）上的变分上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how a physical mass scale can emerge in pure Yang–Mills theory—devoid of matter fields or explicit mass terms—through nonperturbative, topological, and gauge-invariant mechanisms. This addresses the conceptual puzzle of confinement and mass gap generation in QCD-like theories, particularly in finite spatial domains relevant to local physics or lattice simulations.
\n\n
动机在于理解在不含物质场或显式质量项的纯Yang–Mills理论中，物理质量标度如何通过非微扰、拓扑及规范不变机制产生。这解决了QCD类理论中禁闭与质量间隙生成的概念性难题，尤其适用于与局域物理或格点模拟相关的有限空间区域。

Method: The authors work on a punctured three-ball with relative boundary conditions and fix a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ center symmetry sector to isolate a single gauge-invariant holonomy angle. They enforce Gauss’s law via a covariant Dirichlet Helmholtz projector constructed from the Dirichlet inverse of the covariant scalar Laplacian. The slow holonomy mode is selected variationally by minimizing transverse electric energy under a fixed holonomy constraint, yielding a gauge-invariant inertia. Adiabatic separation is justified by the transverse vector gap of the covariant Laplacian on divergence-free one-forms, enabling a quantum rotor effective description. A variational upper bound on the first positive eigenvalue of the Yang–Mills Hamiltonian is derived using this framework.
\n\n
作者在具有相对边界条件的穿孔三维球上工作，并固定$\mathbb{Z}_3$中心对称扇区以分离出单个规范不变的和乐角。他们通过由协变标量Laplacian的Dirichlet逆构造的协变Dirichlet Helmholtz投影算子来实施Gauss定律。慢和乐模通过在固定和乐约束下最小化横向电场能量而被变分地选定，从而得到一个与规范代表无关的转动惯量。协变Laplacian在无散一度形式上的横向矢量能隙保证了绝热分离的合理性，使得系统可有效描述为量子转子。在此框架下，作者推导出Yang–Mills哈密顿量首个正本征值的变分上界。

Result: The key results include: (1) a gauge-invariant, linearly scaling inertia for the holonomy rotor; (2) proof of stability of the covariant Helmholtz projector; (3) an adiabatic variational upper bound on the first positive Yang–Mills eigenvalue, with error controlled by the transverse vector gap; and (4) a numerical benchmark yielding an upper bound at ~1 GeV for a femtometer-scale domain at realistic coupling. The nonzero level spacing arises purely from gauge invariance, topology, and center symmetry, realizing “mass without mass” in Wilczek’s sense.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 和乐转子具有规范不变且随区域尺寸线性增长的转动惯量；(2) 协变Helmholtz投影算子的稳定性证明；(3) 对首个正Yang–Mills本征值的绝热变分上界，其误差由横向矢量能隙控制；(4) 在飞米尺度区域和真实耦合下的数值基准给出约1 GeV的上界。非零能级间距纯粹源于规范不变性、拓扑结构和中心对称性，实现了Wilczek意义上的“无质量的质量”。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that a finite spectral scale can emerge in pure Yang–Mills theory on a finite domain through a topological and gauge-invariant mechanism tied to center symmetry and holonomy. This provides a concrete realization of “mass without mass,” where the mass gap is not input but derived from first principles. However, interpreting the domain size $R$ as a physical length in Minkowski spacetime requires additional physical assumptions, such as identifying $R$ with a local confinement scale.
\n\n
本文确立了在有限区域上的纯Yang–Mills理论中，通过与中心对称性和和乐相关的拓扑及规范不变机制，可以涌现出有限谱标度。这为“无质量的质量”提供了具体实现——质量间隙并非人为输入，而是从第一性原理导出。然而，将区域尺寸$R$解释为闵氏时空中的物理长度需要额外的物理解释，例如将$R$视为局域禁闭长度。

Abstract: We identify a local, gauge-invariant mechanism that generates a finite spectral scale in pure SU(3) Yang--Mills theory on a punctured three-ball. Fixing a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ center sector isolates a single gauge-invariant holonomy angle whose Berry shift produces a quantum rotor with strictly nonzero level spacing. Gauss law is enforced by a covariant Dirichlet Helmholtz projector built from the Dirichlet inverse of the covariant scalar Laplacian with relative boundary conditions. The slow holonomy mode is chosen variationally as the minimizer of transverse electric energy under the holonomy constraint, yielding an inertia \emph{independent of the gauge representative} with linear domain-size scaling and a controlled commutator-dominated regime. We prove projector stability and derive an adiabatic variational upper bound on the first positive Yang--Mills eigenvalue, with error controlled by the transverse vector gap of the covariant Laplacian on divergence-free one-forms. A femtometer-scale benchmark at realistic coupling gives an upper bound at a hadronic ($\sim 1\,$GeV) scale. In Wilczek's sense this realizes ``mass without mass'': no explicit mass term or Higgs field is introduced, and the nonzero level spacing is fixed by gauge invariance, topology, and the chosen center sector. The present results are derived on a finite domain; interpreting the length $R$ in Minkowski space requires an additional physical input (e.g.\ as a local confinement length), which we make explicit.

</details>


### [58] [All $2D$ generalised dilaton theories from $d\geq 4$ gravities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06786)
*Johanna Borissova*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: All 2D Horndeski theories can be obtained via dimensional reduction of pure gravity in $d \geq 4$ dimensions, implying their on-shell solutions correspond to genuine higher-dimensional vacuum spacetimes. A subclass—called quasi-topological gravities—yields integrable 2D Horndeski theories and satisfies a Birkhoff theorem with $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$. This allows explicit reconstruction of certain static spherically symmetric black holes (e.g., Bardeen) as vacuum solutions of higher-dimensional gravitational theories.
\n\n
所有二维 Horndeski 理论均可通过 $d \\geq 4$ 维纯引力理论的维度约化得到，这意味着其在壳解对应于真实的高维真空时空。其中一类被称为“准拓扑引力”（quasi-topological gravities）的子类会产生可积的二维 Horndeski 理论，并满足 Birkhoff 定理，即 $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$。这使得某些静态球对称黑洞（如 Bardeen 黑洞）可被显式重构为高维引力理论的真空解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to clarify the origin and physical meaning of two-dimensional Horndeski theories by showing they are not ad hoc constructions but arise naturally from higher-dimensional pure gravity via dimensional reduction. This provides a geometric interpretation for 2D scalar-tensor solutions and connects them to genuine vacuum solutions in $d \geq 4$ dimensions. Additionally, it seeks to characterize which higher-dimensional gravitational actions yield integrable 2D reductions and to establish conditions under which static spherically symmetric solutions obey a generalized Birkhoff theorem.
\n\n
本文旨在阐明二维 Horndeski 理论的起源和物理意义，表明它们并非人为构造，而是通过高维纯引力的维度约化自然产生。这为二维标量-张量解提供了几何诠释，并将其与 $d \\geq 4$ 维的真实真空解联系起来。此外，文章试图刻画哪些高维引力作用量能产生可积的二维约化，并建立静态球对称解满足广义 Birkhoff 定理的条件。

Method: The authors perform a Kaluza–Klein-type dimensional reduction of general $d$-dimensional gravitational actions on $2 + (d-2)$ warped-product backgrounds, assuming the internal space is maximally symmetric. They first consider actions built solely from curvature invariants without covariant derivatives (e.g., Lovelock or quasi-topological gravities), then extend to more general actions that still yield second-order equations of motion. By analyzing the reduced 2D theory, they identify when it belongs to the Horndeski class and when it is integrable. For integrable cases, they derive a Birkhoff-type theorem leading to the condition $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ in Schwarzschild gauge, with $f = -g_{tt}$ determined algebraically. The inverse problem—reconstructing the $d$-dimensional action from a given 2D solution—is also addressed.
\n\n
作者在 $2 + (d-2)$ 维翘曲积背景上对一般的 $d$ 维引力作用量进行类似 Kaluza–Klein 的维度约化，假设内空间是极大对称的。他们首先考虑仅由曲率不变量（不含协变导数）构成的作用量（如 Lovelock 或准拓扑引力），随后推广到更一般但仍保持二阶运动方程的作用量。通过分析约化后的二维理论，他们判断其何时属于 Horndeski 类，以及何时可积。对于可积情形，推导出 Birkhoff 型定理，得到 Schwarzschild 规范下 $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ 的条件，且 $f = -g_{tt}$ 由代数方程确定。文章还处理了逆问题——从给定的二维解重构 $d$ 维作用量。

Result: The main results are: (1) All 2D Horndeski theories arise from dimensional reduction of pure gravity in $d \geq 4$; (2) When the parent $d$-dimensional theory yields an integrable 2D Horndeski reduction, a Birkhoff theorem holds: static spherically symmetric vacuum solutions satisfy $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ with $f = -g_{tt}$ given by an algebraic relation involving the ADM mass; (3) Such parent theories are dubbed “quasi-topological gravities”; (4) Conversely, any $d$-dimensional static, asymptotically flat, spherically symmetric spacetime with $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ and invertible $f(M)$ can be explicitly reconstructed as a vacuum solution of some $d$-dimensional gravity theory; (5) Regular black holes like the Bardeen metric cannot be obtained from polynomial or non-polynomial quasi-topological gravities built only from curvature invariants without derivatives.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 所有二维 Horndeski 理论均可由 $d \\geq 4$ 维纯引力维度约化得到；(2) 当母理论产生可积的二维 Horndeski 约化时，Birkhoff 定理成立：静态球对称真空解满足 $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$，且 $f = -g_{tt}$ 由涉及 ADM 质量的代数关系给出；(3) 此类母理论被称为“准拓扑引力”（quasi-topological gravities）；(4) 反之，任何满足 $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ 且 $f(M)$ 可逆的 $d$ 维静态、渐近平直、球对称时空，均可显式重构为某 $d$ 维引力理论的真空解；(5) Bardeen 等正则黑洞无法由仅含曲率不变量（不含协变导数）的多项式或非多项式准拓扑引力得到。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a deep correspondence between two-dimensional Horndeski scalar-tensor theories and higher-dimensional pure gravity, revealing that 2D solutions are shadows of genuine $d$-dimensional vacuum geometries. The subclass of “quasi-topological gravities” is identified as those yielding integrable 2D reductions with a Birkhoff theorem, enabling exact reconstruction of black hole spacetimes. This framework not only demystifies 2D Horndeski models but also provides a constructive method to embed known 4D black hole solutions into consistent higher-dimensional gravitational theories.
\n\n
本文建立了二维 Horndeski 标量-张量理论与高维纯引力之间的深刻对应关系，揭示了二维解实为真实 $d$ 维真空几何的“投影”。其中，“准拓扑引力”子类被识别为能产生可积二维约化并满足 Birkhoff 定理的理论，从而可精确重构黑洞时空。这一框架不仅澄清了二维 Horndeski 模型的物理本质，还提供了一种构造性方法，将已知的四维黑洞解嵌入自洽的高维引力理论中。

Abstract: We show that all two-dimensional Horndeski theories can arise from the reduction of pure gravities in $d \geq 4$ dimensions and therefore all onshell configurations for the two-dimensional metric and scalar field correspond to genuine $d$-dimensional gravitational vacuum solutions. We discuss separately the two-dimensional Horndeski theories which can arise from the reduction of $d$-dimensional generally covariant gravitational actions built only from curvature invariants without covariant derivatives and possessing second-order equations of motion on $2 + (d-2)$ warped-product backgrounds. The discussion is subsequently extended to generic $d$-dimensional gravitational actions with this latter property. We establish a Birkhoff theorem for all gravitational theories whose reduction yields an integrable two-dimensional Horndeski theory, in which case static spherically symmetric solutions satisfy $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ in Schwarzschild gauge whereby the metric function $g_{tt} = -f$ is determined by an algebraic equation. We therefore propose to call all such theories quasi-topological gravities. These results can be used to show in reverse that any $d$-dimensional static spherically symmetric and asymptotically flat spacetime satisfying $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ in Schwarzschild gauge with an invertible dependence of $f$ on the ADM mass can be reconstructed explicitly as a vacuum solution to a $d$-dimensional gravitational theory. We discuss examples of regular black holes such as the Bardeen spacetime, which could not be obtained from polynomial and non-polynomial quasi-topological gravities involving only curvature invariants without covariant derivatives.

</details>


### [59] [Flat holography for spinor fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06794)
*Dmitry S. Ageev,Anna S. Bernakevich*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper constructs a flat-space holographic dictionary for a free massive spinor field in 4D Minkowski spacetime by slicing it into hyperbolic (Milne) slices isomorphic to $\mathbb H^3$ (Euclidean $\mathrm{AdS}_3$). The on-shell action is expressed as a functional of boundary data on the celestial sphere, yielding two-point correlators of dual spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ operators that obey 2D conformal symmetry. The Dirac equation in 4D is thus recast as a family of effective $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ problems, and the near-boundary asymptotics fix the conformal dimensions and sources. Spinor conformal primary wavefunctions are also derived and linked to the bulk-to-boundary map.
\n\n
本文通过将四维闵可夫斯基时空切片为双曲（Milne）片——同构于$\mathbb H^3$（欧几里得$\mathrm{AdS}_3$）——构建了自由大质量旋量场的平直时空全息字典。在天球边界上，壳上作用量被表示为边界数据的泛函，从而导出满足二维共形对称性的对偶自旋-$\frac{1}{2}$算符的两点关联函数。由此，四维Dirac方程被重构为一族有效的$\mathrm{AdS}_3$问题，其近边界渐进行为确定了共形维数与源项。文章还构造了相应的旋量共形主波函数，并阐明了其与平直时空体到边界的映射关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the Celestial Holography program, which aims to reformulate four-dimensional scattering amplitudes in asymptotically flat spacetimes as correlation functions of a conjectural two-dimensional CFT living on the celestial sphere. A key challenge is to establish a precise holographic dictionary for spinning fields, especially fermions, in flat space. This work addresses this gap by leveraging the hyperbolic slicing of Minkowski space to connect bulk spinor dynamics with boundary CFT data, thereby extending AdS/CFT intuition to flat space.
\n\n
动机源于Celestial Holography纲领，该纲领旨在将渐近平直时空中的四维散射振幅重新表述为天球上某个猜想的二维CFT的关联函数。关键挑战之一是在平直时空中为带自旋场（尤其是费米子）建立精确的全息字典。本文通过利用闵可夫斯基时空的双曲切片，将体旋量动力学与边界CFT数据联系起来，从而将AdS/CFT的逻辑推广至平直时空，填补了这一空白。

Method: The authors employ the Milne (hyperbolic) slicing of four-dimensional Minkowski spacetime, which foliates the bulk into copies of three-dimensional hyperbolic space $\mathbb H^3$, identified with Euclidean $\mathrm{AdS}_3$. They decompose the free massive Dirac field into $\mathbb H^3$ scalar and spinor harmonics labeled by a continuous spectral parameter. By solving the Dirac equation in this slicing and analyzing the near-boundary ($\rho \to \infty$) behavior, they identify the leading and subleading asymptotic modes as sources and responses for dual CFT operators. The renormalized on-shell action is then computed as a functional of the boundary source, from which the two-point function of spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ primaries is extracted using standard holographic prescription. The method closely parallels the AdS/CFT procedure but adapted to flat space via the $\mathbb H^3$ reduction.
\n\n
作者采用四维闵可夫斯基时空的Milne（双曲）切片，将体空间叶状分解为三维双曲空间$\mathbb H^3$（即欧几里得$\mathrm{AdS}_3$）的拷贝。他们将自由大质量Dirac场按$\mathbb H^3$的标量与旋量调和函数展开，后者由连续谱参数标记。通过在此切片下求解Dirac方程并分析近边界（$\rho \to \infty$）行为，识别出主导与次主导渐近模分别对应于对偶CFT算符的源与响应。随后，计算以边界源为变量的重整化壳上作用量，并依据标准全息处方提取出自旋-$\frac{1}{2}$主算符的两点函数。该方法紧密类比AdS/CFT程序，但通过$\mathbb H^3$约化适配于平直时空。

Result: The paper successfully derives the two-point correlation functions for dual spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ operators on the celestial sphere, which take the universal form fixed by two-dimensional conformal symmetry: $\langle \mathcal{O}_{\Delta}^{+}(z,\bar{z}) \mathcal{O}_{\Delta}^{-}(w,\bar{w}) \rangle \propto \frac{1}{(z-w)^{2\Delta}} \delta(\bar{z}-\bar{w})$ (up to gamma matrices and normalization), with conformal dimension $\Delta = \frac{1}{2} \pm i m$, where $m$ is the bulk mass. The near-boundary expansion of the bulk spinor unambiguously selects the appropriate boundary conditions and fixes $\Delta$. Additionally, explicit expressions for spinor conformal primary wavefunctions are obtained and shown to coincide with the bulk-to-boundary propagator derived from the on-shell action.
\n\n
本文成功导出了天球上对偶自旋-$\frac{1}{2}$算符的两点关联函数，其形式由二维共形对称性唯一确定：$\langle \mathcal{O}_{\Delta}^{+}(z,\bar{z}) \mathcal{O}_{\Delta}^{-}(w,\bar{w}) \rangle \propto \frac{1}{(z-w)^{2\Delta}} \delta(\bar{z}-\bar{w})$（忽略伽马矩阵与归一化因子），其中共形维数为$\Delta = \frac{1}{2} \pm i m$，$m$为体质量。体旋量的近边界展开明确选定了合适的边界条件并固定了$\Delta$。此外，文章还得到了旋量共形主波函数的显式表达式，并证明其与由壳上作用量导出的体到边界传播子一致。

Conclusion: This work establishes a concrete holographic dictionary for massive spinor fields in flat space by reducing the four-dimensional Dirac problem to an effective $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ framework via hyperbolic slicing. It demonstrates that the standard AdS/CFT logic—relating bulk solutions to boundary CFT data through asymptotic analysis and on-shell actions—can be systematically extended to Minkowski space. The results provide a foundational step toward understanding fermionic sectors in Celestial Holography and offer a clear prescription for computing spinning correlators from flat-space bulk dynamics.
\n\n
本文通过双曲切片将四维Dirac问题约化为有效的$\mathrm{AdS}_3$框架，为平直时空中的大质量旋量场建立了具体的全息字典。研究表明，标准AdS/CFT逻辑——即通过渐近分析与壳上作用量将体解与边界CFT数据关联——可系统地推广至闵可夫斯基时空。该成果为理解Celestial Holography中的费米子部分奠定了基础，并为从平直时空体动力学计算带自旋关联函数提供了清晰的方案。

Abstract: We develop a flat-space holographic dictionary for a free massive spinor field in four-dimensional Minkowski spacetime, using the hyperbolic (Milne) slicing into $\mathbb H^3$ (Euclidean $\mathrm{AdS}_3$). Decomposing bulk fields into $\mathbb H^3$ harmonics labeled by a continuous parameter, we obtain the renormalized on-shell action as a functional of boundary data and extract the corresponding two-point correlation functions of dual spinning operators on the celestial sphere. The resulting correlators take the universal form dictated by two-dimensional conformal symmetry for spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ primaries. In this way, the four-dimensional Dirac problem is reduced to a family of effective $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ problems, closely following the logic of standard AdS/CFT. We show how the near-boundary behavior of the bulk spinor selects the appropriate celestial sources and determines the conformal dimension of the dual operators. As a further application, we construct the associated spinor conformal primary wavefunctions and clarify their relation to the flat-space bulk-to-boundary map.

</details>


### [60] [Moduli Space Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06795)
*Luis Anchordoqui,Muldrow Etheredge,Dieter Lust*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper extends Species Quantum Mechanics by treating moduli-dependent functions as quantum operators in a mini-superspace framework, using the Emergent String Conjecture to constrain their non-commutativity. It shows that moduli space geometry induces bulk-localized, positive-energy excited wave functions, and in the presence of potentials, leads to moduli stabilization away from classical minima.
\n\n
本文通过在迷你超空间（mini-superspace）框架下将模依赖函数视为量子算符，拓展了Species Quantum Mechanics的研究，并利用Emergent String Conjecture约束这些算符之间的非对易性。研究表明，模空间几何会诱导出定域于模空间体区域（bulks）的激发态波函数，且具有正能量本征值；当存在势能时，该效应导致模被定域在远离经典极小值的位置，并通常形成激发的正能量态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding quantum mechanical aspects of moduli spaces in quantum gravity, particularly within the framework of Species Quantum Mechanics. The authors aim to explore how swampland constraints—specifically taxonomic relations from the Emergent String Conjecture—can inform or restrict quantum operator algebras on moduli space, and how geometric features of moduli space influence quantum states.
\n\n
动机源于理解量子引力中模空间的量子力学特性，特别是在Species Quantum Mechanics框架下。作者旨在探究沼泽地约束（尤其是来自Emergent String Conjecture的分类关系）如何影响或限制模空间上的量子算符代数，以及模空间的几何特征如何影响量子态。

Method: The authors adopt a mini-superspace approach to quantize moduli-dependent functions as operators acting on wave functions over moduli space. They impose constraints derived from the taxonomic relations of the Emergent String Conjecture to restrict the non-commutativity of these operators. The resulting Schrödinger-like equation incorporates the metric of the moduli space, and solutions are analyzed both in the absence and presence of scalar potentials.
\n\n
作者采用迷你超空间方法，将模依赖函数量子化为作用于模空间上波函数的算符。他们利用Emergent String Conjecture中的分类关系导出的约束来限制这些算符的非对易性。所得的类薛定谔方程包含模空间的度规，并在有无标量势的情形下分别分析其解。

Result: The analysis reveals that the intrinsic geometry of moduli space generates effective potentials leading to normalizable, bulk-localized excited wave functions with positive energy eigenvalues $E > 0$. When explicit scalar potentials are included, the combined geometric and potential effects stabilize moduli at positions displaced from classical minima, typically yielding excited quantum states rather than ground states.
\n\n
分析表明，模空间的内禀几何会产生有效势，从而导致可归一化的、定域于体区域的激发态波函数，其能量本征值满足 $E > 0$。当引入显式的标量势时，几何效应与势能共同作用，使模稳定在偏离经典极小值的位置，通常产生的是激发量子态而非基态。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that quantum mechanics on moduli space—guided by swampland conjectures like the Emergent String Conjecture—naturally gives rise to localized, positive-energy quantum states due to geometric effects. This suggests a deep interplay between quantum gravity constraints, moduli space geometry, and the structure of the quantum Hilbert space, with implications for moduli stabilization beyond classical expectations.
\n\n
本文表明，在Emergent String Conjecture等沼泽地猜想指导下，模空间上的量子力学会因几何效应自然产生定域的正能量量子态。这揭示了量子引力约束、模空间几何与量子希尔伯特空间结构之间的深刻联系，并对超越经典预期的模稳定机制具有启示意义。

Abstract: In this paper, continuing the discussion about Species Quantum Mechanics, we investigate quantum mechanics in moduli spaces using a mini-superspace approach. From this perspective, moduli-dependent functions can be viewed as operators, and we explore how the taxonomic relations from the Emergent String Conjecture can constrain the non-commutativity between these operators. Next, we study wave functions on moduli spaces, and we find that the geometry of moduli space plays an important role and leads to excited wave functions localised in the bulks of moduli spaces, and with positive energy eigenvalues. For cases when potentials are present, these effects result in moduli localised away from classical minima, and often result in excited, positive energy states.

### [61] [Quantum (quadratic) gravity: replacing the massive tensor ghost with an inverted harmonic oscillator-like instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07150)
*K. Sravan Kumar,João Marto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Quadratic gravity, though traditionally plagued by a massive spin-2 ghost, is reinterpreted in this work as hosting an inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO)-like instability that can be consistently quantized using direct-sum quantum field theory (DQFT). This mode lacks a particle interpretation, remains off-shell, and decouples from matter, thereby preserving unitarity. The framework yields testable predictions for primordial gravitational waves, including new bounds on the tensor-to-scalar ratio and parity asymmetry at large angular scales.
\n\n
二次引力理论传统上因存在一个大质量自旋-2鬼粒子而备受质疑，本文将其重新诠释为一种倒置谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator, IHO）型不稳定性，并利用直和量子场论（direct-sum quantum field theory, DQFT）对其进行一致的量子化。该模式缺乏粒子诠释，保持在壳外（off-shell），并与物质场解耦，从而保持幺正性。该框架对原初引力波给出了可观测预言，包括张量-标量比的新上限以及大角尺度上的宇称不对称特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the long-standing problem of the massive spin--2 ghost in quadratic gravity, which threatens unitarity despite the theory’s renormalizability. Previous attempts to resolve this issue via alternative quantization schemes have been inconclusive. The authors aim to provide a consistent quantum description that preserves unitarity while retaining the renormalizable structure of quadratic gravity, and to connect this theoretical resolution to observable cosmological signatures.
\n\n
动机源于二次引力中长期存在的大质量自旋-2鬼粒子问题——尽管该理论具有可重整性，但鬼粒子威胁幺正性。以往通过替代量子化方案解决此问题的尝试均未得出明确结论。作者旨在提供一种既能保持幺正性又能保留二次引力可重整结构的一致量子描述，并将这一理论突破与可观测的宇宙学信号联系起来。

Method: The authors reinterpret the massive spin--2 degree of freedom in quadratic gravity as an inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO) instability. They employ direct-sum quantum field theory (DQFT), which incorporates geometric superselection sectors, to quantize such modes. This formalism allows for a well-defined Hilbert space structure despite the hyperbolic time evolution and spacelike momentum support. The analysis connects this quantization scheme to the absence of asymptotic particle states for the extra mode, ensuring its decoupling from physical observables. Cosmological implications are derived by applying this framework to early-universe dynamics, particularly inflationary tensor perturbations.
\n\n
作者将二次引力中的大质量自旋-2自由度重新诠释为倒置谐振子（IHO）型不稳定性，并采用包含几何超选择（geometric superselection sectors）的直和量子场论（DQFT）对该模式进行量子化。该形式体系允许在双曲时间演化和类空动量支撑下仍具有良定义的希尔伯特空间结构。分析表明，该量子化方案导致额外模式不存在渐近粒子态，从而确保其与物理可观测量解耦。通过将该框架应用于早期宇宙动力学（特别是暴胀时期的张量扰动），推导出宇宙学预言。

Result: The paper demonstrates that the massive spin--2 mode in quadratic gravity can be consistently quantized as an IHO-like instability within DQFT, avoiding unitarity violation. This mode is off-shell, lacks a particle interpretation, and decouples from ordinary matter. The framework predicts suppressed primordial gravitational waves with a tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ below current observational limits, and introduces parity-asymmetric correlations in the cosmic microwave background (CMB) at large angular scales due to the chiral nature of the instability.
\n\n
论文证明，二次引力中的大质量自旋-2模式可在DQFT框架内作为IHO型不稳定性被一致地量子化，从而避免幺正性破坏。该模式处于壳外、无粒子诠释，并与普通物质解耦。该框架预言原初引力波被压低，张量-标量比 $r$ 低于当前观测上限，并由于该不稳定性的手征特性，在宇宙微波背景（CMB）大角尺度上引入宇称不对称关联。

Conclusion: The authors conclude that quadratic gravity, when properly quantized via DQFT, provides a viable and unitary theory of quantum gravity in four dimensions. The IHO instability is not a pathology but a fundamental feature shared across quantum field theory on curved spacetimes and even the Standard Model (e.g., Higgs $\mathbb{Z}_2$ breaking). This reframing resolves the ghost problem and offers a self-consistent beginning for the Universe, with falsifiable predictions for future CMB and gravitational-wave observations.
\n\n
作者得出结论：当通过DQFT正确量子化时，二次引力在四维中构成一个可行且幺正的量子引力理论。IHO不稳定性并非病态，而是贯穿弯曲时空量子场论乃至标准模型（如Higgs $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 对称性破缺）的基本特征。这一重新诠释解决了鬼粒子问题，为宇宙提供了一个自洽的开端，并对未来的CMB和引力波观测给出可证伪的预言。

Abstract: The quadratic theory of gravity is the unique renormalizable theory of quantum gravity in 4 dimensions, as proved by K. S. Stelle in 1977. Over the decades, the theory has been understood to contain a massive tensor ghost, and several attempts have been made to evade its adverse effects by proposing new quantization prescriptions and interpretations. In this paper, we show that the additional spin--2 of quadratic gravity can be turned into a healthy inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO)-like instability, which can be quantized consistently with direct-sum quantum field theory (DQFT), which incorporates geometric superselection sectors. Such modes possess a well-defined quantum description yet do not admit a particle interpretation and are not part of the asymptotic spectrum, being characterized by hyperbolic evolution and spacelike momentum support. We argue that, as a consequence, the extra spin--2 degree of freedom remains off-shell and effectively decoupled from ordinary matter fields, avoiding unitarity violations in observable processes. We argue that this IHO instability is a prevalent feature of fundamental physics, whether it concerns quantum fields on curved spacetimes or the Higgs $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry breaking in the Standard Model of particle physics. Thus, we demonstrate that our new understanding of quadratic gravity offers a fundamental pathway to quantum gravity and a safe beginning for the Universe. Furthermore, we derive key observational predictions of this construction in the view of primordial gravitational waves with new bounds on the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the parity asymmetric features on the large angular scales.

</details>


### [62] [Time Dependent String Compactification: Towards Bouncing Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07298)
*Mir Mehedi Faruk*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates how the Null Energy Condition (NEC) arises from Virasoro constraints on the string worldsheet and demonstrates that, under specific time-dependent compactifications, the lower-dimensional effective spacetime can violate the NEC—enabling bouncing cosmologies—while the full higher-dimensional theory preserves the NEC due to worldsheet symmetry.
\n\n
本文研究了由弦世界面（string worldsheet）上的Virasoro约束所导出的零能量条件（Null Energy Condition, NEC），并展示了在特定的时间依赖紧致化（time-dependent compactifications）下，低维有效时空可以违反NEC（从而实现反弹宇宙学），而高维完整理论由于世界面对称性仍满足NEC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the tension between the apparent violation of the Null Energy Condition in effective lower-dimensional cosmological models—such as those describing bouncing universes—and the fundamental requirement in string theory that the NEC be preserved due to consistency conditions like the Virasoro constraint on the worldsheet. The authors aim to reconcile these by showing how NEC violation can be an artifact of dimensional reduction while the full higher-dimensional theory remains consistent.
\n\n
动机源于低维有效宇宙学模型（如描述反弹宇宙的模型）中NEC的明显违反与弦理论中因世界面Virasoro约束等一致性条件而要求NEC必须保持之间的张力。作者旨在通过展示NEC违反仅是维度约化（dimensional reduction）的产物，而完整的高维理论仍保持一致，来调和这一矛盾。

Method: The authors start from the Virasoro constraints on the string worldsheet, which encode worldsheet conformal invariance and lead to energy conditions in spacetime. They then consider general time-dependent compactifications of string theory, analyzing how the NEC in external spacetime directions is inherited from the worldsheet. Using the Einstein-frame formulation, they examine averaged energy conditions in the lower-dimensional effective theory and construct explicit compactification scenarios where the reduced theory violates the NEC while the higher-dimensional theory satisfies it.
\n\n
作者从弦世界面上的Virasoro约束出发，该约束编码了世界面共形不变性，并导出时空中的能量条件。随后，他们考虑弦理论中一般的时间依赖紧致化，分析外部时空方向上的NEC如何从世界面继承而来。利用爱因斯坦标架（Einstein-frame）表述，他们考察低维有效理论中的平均能量条件，并构造出具体的紧致化情形，其中约化理论违反NEC，而高维理论仍满足NEC。

Result: The key result is that while the higher-dimensional string theory respects the NEC as required by worldsheet conformal symmetry, certain time-dependent compactifications can lead to an effective lower-dimensional spacetime that violates the averaged NEC in the Einstein frame. This violation permits cosmological solutions such as a bounce, without contradicting the fundamental consistency of the UV-complete string theory.
\n\n
核心结果是：尽管高维弦理论因世界面共形对称性而必须满足NEC，但某些时间依赖的紧致化可导致爱因斯坦标架下低维有效时空违反平均NEC。这种违反允许反弹等宇宙学解的存在，同时不违背紫外完备（UV-complete）弦理论的基本一致性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that apparent violations of the Null Energy Condition in low-energy effective descriptions of gravity do not necessarily signal inconsistencies in the underlying quantum gravity theory. Instead, they can arise from the process of dimensional reduction, with the full higher-dimensional string theory preserving the NEC through worldsheet symmetries. This provides a consistent embedding of bouncing cosmologies within string theory.
\n\n
本研究表明，引力低能有效描述中NEC的表观违反并不必然意味着底层量子引力理论存在不一致性；相反，它可能源于维度约化过程，而完整的高维弦理论通过世界面对称性保持NEC。这为反弹宇宙学在弦理论中的自洽嵌入提供了途径。

Abstract: We study the Null Energy Condition (NEC) arising from the Virasoro constraint on the string worldsheet. We then analyze how the NEC in the external spacetime directions emerges under general time-dependent string compactifications. Finally, we exhibit compactifications in which the averaged Einstein-frame condition allows the lowerdimensional description of the external spacetime to violate the NEC, thereby realizing a bouncing cosmology, while the higher-dimensional NEC remains satisfied, as dictated by worldsheet symmetry.

### [63] [Gauss-Bonnet corrected string/black hole transition in large dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07451)
*Bum-Hoon Lee,Hocheol Lee,Somyadip Thakur*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper presents a unified analytic framework for the Horowitz--Polchinski (HP) string/black hole correspondence by incorporating higher-derivative (Gauss--Bonnet) corrections using the large-$D$ expansion. It solves the thermal scalar sector as a Schrödinger problem in the near-zone and constructs explicit Euclidean black hole solutions in the far-zone, then matches them to determine corrected thermodynamic quantities and locate the HP transition point with $α'$ corrections.
\n\n
本文通过引入高阶导数（Gauss--Bonnet）修正，利用大$D$展开方法，构建了Horowitz--Polchinski（HP）弦/黑洞对应关系的统一解析框架。在近区将热标量部分简化为可解的Schrödinger问题，在远区构造了Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet理论的欧几里得黑洞解，并通过区域匹配确定了包含$α'$修正的热力学量和HP相变点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Horowitz--Polchinski correspondence between highly excited strings and small black holes lacks a systematic treatment of higher-curvature ($α'$) corrections, especially in a regime where both the thermal scalar and Euclidean black hole describe competing phases of the same finite-temperature ensemble. A controlled analytic approach that incorporates such UV-sensitive corrections is needed to precisely locate the HP transition and understand its dependence on quantum gravity effects.
\n\n
Horowitz--Polchinski关于高激发弦与小黑洞之间的对应关系缺乏对高曲率（$α'$）修正的系统性处理，尤其是在热标量与欧几里得黑洞作为同一有限温度系综中竞争相的区域。需要一种受控的解析方法来纳入这些紫外敏感的修正，以精确确定HP相变点并理解其对量子引力效应的依赖。

Method: The authors employ the large-$D$ expansion of general relativity, which cleanly separates spacetime into a universal near-zone (where stringy effects dominate) and an asymptotic far-zone (governed by classical gravity). In the near-zone, they reduce the thermal scalar dynamics coupled to gravity to an exactly solvable Schrödinger equation, yielding $α'$-corrected decay exponents and Hagedorn temperature shifts. In the far-zone, they construct closed-form Euclidean black hole solutions in Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet gravity at leading order in both $1/D$ and $α'$. The two zones are matched to obtain the full corrected saddle, including its temperature, horizon data, and on-shell action, enabling analytic comparison of free energies.
\n\n
作者采用广义相对论的大$D$展开方法，将时空清晰划分为近区（弦效应主导）和远区（经典引力主导）。在近区，他们将热标量与引力的耦合动力学简化为一个可精确求解的Schrödinger方程，从而获得$α'$修正的衰减指数和Hagedorn温度移动。在远区，他们在Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet引力中构造了欧几里得黑洞解（在$1/D$和$α'$的最低阶）。通过匹配两个区域，得到完整的修正鞍点，包括其温度、视界数据和on-shell作用量，从而实现自由能的解析比较。

Result: The paper derives explicit $α'$-corrected expressions for the decay exponent of the thermal scalar, the shift in the Hagedorn temperature, and the on-shell action of the Euclidean black hole saddle. By matching near- and far-zone solutions, it provides a fully analytic determination of the corrected HP correspondence point, demonstrating how higher-curvature terms modify the phase transition between the string and black hole phases.
\n\n
本文推导出热标量衰减指数、Hagedorn温度移动以及欧几里得黑洞鞍点on-shell作用量的显式$α'$修正表达式。通过匹配近区与远区解，实现了对修正后HP对应点的完全解析确定，展示了高曲率项如何改变弦相与黑洞相之间的相变。

Conclusion: This work establishes a controlled, analytic framework for incorporating higher-derivative corrections into the Horowitz--Polchinski correspondence using the large-$D$ expansion. It demonstrates that the interplay between string-scale physics (thermal scalar) and classical gravity with $α'$ corrections can be systematically treated, yielding precise predictions for the HP transition point beyond leading order in $α'$.
\n\n
本工作利用大$D$展开建立了在Horowitz--Polchinski对应中纳入高阶导数修正的受控解析框架。研究表明，弦尺度物理（热标量）与含$α'$修正的经典引力之间的相互作用可以被系统处理，从而在$α'$展开的超越领头阶上对HP相变点做出精确预言。

Abstract: We develop a unified analytic treatment of the Horowitz--Polchinski string/black hole correspondence that systematically incorporates higher-derivative corrections to gravity. Working in Euclidean signature -- where the Euclidean black hole and the thermal scalar arise as competing saddles of the same finite-temperature ensemble -- we include the Gauss--Bonnet term. The analysis is rendered tractable in this UV--sensitive regime by the large-\(D\) expansion, which sharply separates the geometry into a universal near-zone and an asymptotic far-zone. In the near-zone, the coupled large-\(D\) equations reduce the thermal-scalar sector to an exactly solvable Schrödinger problem, from which we extract the \(α'\)-corrected decay exponent and the corresponding shift of the Hagedorn temperature. In the far-zone, we construct closed-form Euclidean solutions of Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet theory at leading order in both \(1/D\) and \(α'\). Matching the two regions yields the complete corrected saddle -- fixing its temperature, horizon data, and on--shell action -- and permits a fully analytic comparison of free energies between the thermal-scalar and black hole phases. This provides a controlled derivation of the HP correspondence point with explicit higher-curvature corrections.
