### [64] [Thermal and chemical response from entanglement entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07635)
*Niko Jokela,Aatu Rajala,Tobias Rindlisbacher*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a universal connection between entanglement entropy (EE) in interacting quantum field theories (QFTs) at finite density and thermodynamic entropy. In the limit of large entangling regions (specifically slabs), the derivative of EE with respect to region size approaches the thermal entropy density, independent of microscopic details. Moreover, EE obeys thermodynamic response relations—including a generalized Maxwell relation—linking chemical potential and charge density. Nonperturbative evidence from the 3D $\operatorname{O}(4)$ model supports these claims, suggesting they hold generically for continuum QFTs, thereby enabling extraction of equation-of-state data from entanglement measurements.
\n\n
本文建立了有限密度下相互作用量子场论（QFT）中纠缠熵（EE）与热力学熵之间的普适联系。在大纠缠区域（特别是平板形区域）极限下，EE 对区域尺寸的导数趋近于热熵密度，且与微观细节无关。此外，EE 满足热力学响应关系——包括一个将化学势与电荷密度联系起来的广义麦克斯韦关系。三维 $\operatorname{O}(4)$ 模型的非微扰证据支持这些结论，表明其对连续 QFT 具有普适性，从而为从纠缠数据中提取物态方程信息开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to understand how quantum entanglement in many-body systems encodes thermodynamic information, especially in strongly interacting QFTs where traditional perturbative methods fail. At finite density—relevant for condensed matter and high-energy physics—it is unclear whether entanglement entropy can universally reflect thermodynamic properties. The authors aim to bridge entanglement and thermodynamics by identifying universal, nonperturbative relations that hold irrespective of microscopic details, potentially enabling entanglement-based probes of the equation of state.
\n\n
动机源于理解多体系统中的量子纠缠如何编码热力学信息，尤其是在强相互作用 QFT 中（传统微扰方法失效）。在有限密度条件下（与凝聚态和高能物理相关），纠缠熵是否能普适地反映热力学性质尚不明确。作者旨在通过识别与微观细节无关的普适、非微扰关系，架起纠缠与热力学之间的桥梁，从而可能实现基于纠缠的物态方程探测。

Method: The authors consider slab-shaped entangling regions in $d$-dimensional QFTs at finite chemical potential $\mu$. They analyze the behavior of entanglement entropy $S_{\text{EE}}(L)$ as a function of slab width $L$, focusing on the asymptotic regime $L \to \infty$. Using symmetry and scaling arguments, they show that $\frac{dS_{\text{EE}}}{dL} \to s_{\text{th}}$, where $s_{\text{th}}$ is the thermal entropy density of the system at temperature $T$ and chemical potential $\mu$. They further derive thermodynamic response identities by treating $S_{\text{EE}}$ as a thermodynamic potential, leading to a generalized Maxwell relation: $\frac{\partial^2 S_{\text{EE}}}{\partial \mu \partial L} = \frac{\partial \langle Q \rangle}{\partial L}$, where $\langle Q \rangle$ is the total charge in the slab. These predictions are tested nonperturbatively using lattice simulations of the 3D $\operatorname{O}(4)$ model at finite density.
\n\n
作者考虑在有限化学势 $\mu$ 下 $d$ 维 QFT 中的平板形纠缠区域。他们分析纠缠熵 $S_{\text{EE}}(L)$ 随平板宽度 $L$ 的变化，聚焦于 $L \to \infty$ 的渐近区域。利用对称性和标度论证，证明 $\frac{dS_{\text{EE}}}{dL} \to s_{\text{th}}$，其中 $s_{\text{th}}$ 是系统在温度 $T$ 和化学势 $\mu$ 下的热熵密度。进一步将 $S_{\text{EE}}$ 视为热力学势，推导出热力学响应恒等式，得到一个广义麦克斯韦关系：$\frac{\partial^2 S_{\text{EE}}}{\partial \mu \partial L} = \frac{\partial \langle Q \rangle}{\partial L}$，其中 $\langle Q \rangle$ 是平板内的总电荷。这些预言通过三维 $\operator擎{O}(4)$ 模型在有限密度下的格点模拟进行了非微扰检验。

Result: The analysis confirms that for large slab widths, $\frac{dS_{\text{EE}}}{dL}$ converges to the thermal entropy density $s_{\text{th}}(T, \mu)$, with corrections suppressed by $1/L$. The generalized Maxwell relation derived from entanglement thermodynamics holds numerically in the 3D $\operatorname{O}(4)$ model, even in the nonperturbative regime near criticality. This demonstrates that entanglement entropy encodes not only equilibrium thermodynamic quantities but also their response functions, such as charge susceptibility. The results are robust across different values of $T$ and $\mu$, supporting the conjecture of universality in continuum QFTs.
\n\n
分析证实，对于大平板宽度，$\frac{dS_{\text{EE}}}{dL}$ 收敛到热熵密度 $s_{\text{th}}(T, \mu)$，修正项被 $1/L$ 压制。从纠缠热力学导出的广义麦克斯韦关系在三维 $\operatorname{O}(4)$ 模型中数值成立，即使在临界点附近的非微扰区域也是如此。这表明纠缠熵不仅编码平衡热力学量，还编码其响应函数（如电荷磁化率）。结果在不同 $T$ 和 $\mu$ 值下均稳健，支持其在连续 QFT 中具有普适性的猜想。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a two-way correspondence between entanglement and thermodynamics in finite-density QFTs: thermodynamic quantities determine the extensive part of entanglement entropy, while entanglement data can be used to reconstruct the equation of state and response functions. This universality—verified nonperturbatively in the $\operatorname{O}(4)$ model—suggests that entanglement entropy serves as a fundamental probe of quantum many-body thermodynamics, with potential applications in lattice QFT, holography, and quantum simulation.
\n\n
本文在有限密度 QFT 中建立了纠缠与热力学之间的双向对应关系：热力学量决定纠缠熵的广延部分，而纠缠数据可用于重构物态方程和响应函数。这种普适性已在 $\operatorname{O}(4)$ 模型中通过非微扰方法验证，表明纠缠熵可作为量子多体热力学的基本探针，在格点 QFT、全息对偶和量子模拟中具有潜在应用。

Abstract: We study entanglement entropy (EE) in interacting quantum field theories (QFTs) at finite density. We argue that, in the limit of large subregions, the derivative of EE with respect to the size of the entangling region approaches the thermal entropy density, independently of microscopic details. We make this relation explicit using slab-shaped subregions, where the limiting behavior can be directly identified. At finite chemical potential, we show that EE satisfies thermodynamic response relations, including a generalized Maxwell relation linking chemical potential and charge density. We provide strong nonperturbative evidence for these statements in the three-dimensional $\operatorname{O}\left(4\right)$ model, and conjecture that they are generic features of continuum QFTs, establishing a two-way link between entanglement and thermodynamics that opens a route toward extracting the equation-of-state information from entanglement data.

</details>


### [65] [Boundary critical behavior of the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07637)
*Andrei A. Fedorenko,Ilya A. Gruzberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates the boundary critical behavior of the semi-infinite Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model with Dirac fermions and bosonic fields under Neumann/Dirichlet boundary conditions for bosons and symmetry-preserving boundary conditions for fermions. One-loop boundary critical exponents are computed, revealing distinct fixed points and universality classes.
\n\n
本文研究了半无限Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型在玻色场满足Neumann/Dirichlet边界条件、费米子满足保持幺正性、共形不变性和电荷共轭对称性的最一般边界条件下的边界临界行为。通过一阶圈图计算得到了边界临界指数，揭示了不同的不动点和普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding boundary critical phenomena in quantum field theories with fermionic degrees of freedom is essential for characterizing surface phase transitions in strongly correlated systems. The Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model provides a tractable framework to explore how boundary conditions affect renormalization group (RG) flows and conformal symmetry, especially when both bosonic and fermionic fields are present.
\n\n
理解具有费米自由度的量子场论中的边界临界现象对于刻画强关联体系中的表面相变至关重要。Gross-Neveu-Yukawa模型为探索边界条件如何影响重整化群（RG）流和共形对称性提供了一个可处理的框架，尤其适用于同时存在玻色场和费米场的情形。

Method: The authors employ perturbative renormalization group techniques within the $\\epsilon$-expansion framework ($d = 4 - \\epsilon$ dimensions). They impose Neumann or Dirichlet boundary conditions on the bosonic fields and the most general unitary, conformally invariant, and charge conjugation symmetric boundary conditions on the Dirac fermions. Fixed points of the boundary RG flow are identified by solving beta functions at one-loop order, and boundary critical exponents (e.g., $\\eta_\\parallel$, $\\beta_1$) are extracted from anomalous dimensions of boundary operators.
\n\n
作者采用$\\epsilon$展开框架（$d = 4 - \\epsilon$维）下的微扰重整化群技术。对玻色场施加Neumann或Dirichlet边界条件，对Dirac费米子施加保持幺正性、共形不变性和电荷共轭对称性的最一般边界条件。通过求解一阶圈图的beta函数确定边界RG流的不动点，并从边界算符的反常维度中提取边界临界指数（如$\\eta_\\parallel$、$\\beta_1$）。

Result: Distinct boundary fixed points are found for different combinations of bosonic and fermionic boundary conditions, corresponding to separate universality classes. The one-loop boundary critical exponents differ between Neumann and Dirichlet cases, reflecting the influence of boundary conditions on scaling behavior. The analysis also extends to the semi-infinite pseudoscalar Yukawa model, suggesting analogous critical behavior.
\n\n
针对玻色场与费米场边界条件的不同组合，发现了不同的边界不动点，对应于不同的普适类。Neumann与Dirichlet情形下的一阶圈图边界临界指数不同，反映了边界条件对标度行为的影响。该分析还推广至半无限赝标量Yukawa模型，表明其具有类似的临界行为。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that boundary conditions crucially determine the nature of boundary criticality in fermionic quantum field theories. The computed exponents provide quantitative predictions for surface critical phenomena in systems described by Gross-Neveu-Yukawa-type models, such as certain topological or strongly correlated materials.
\n\n
研究表明，边界条件对费米型量子场论中的边界临界性质起决定性作用。所计算的指数为Gross-Neveu-Yukawa型模型所描述体系（如某些拓扑或强关联材料）中的表面临界现象提供了定量预言。

Abstract: We study the critical behavior of the semi-infinite Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model, a quantum field theory describing Dirac fermions interacting with bosonic fields via a Yukawa coupling. We consider Neumann and Dirichlet boundary conditions for the bosonic fields, and the most general boundary conditions for the fermions that preserve unitarity, conformal invariance, and charge conjugation symmetry. We analyze the phase diagram and identify distinct fixed points corresponding to different universality classes of boundary critical behavior. The associated boundary critical exponents, which govern the scaling behavior and crossover phenomena, are computed to one-loop order. We also discuss the relevance of our results to the semi-infinite pseudoscalar Yukawa model.

### [66] [Emergent fracton strings from covariant bi-form gauge field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07661)
*Erica Bertolini,Hyungrok Kim,Giandomenico Palumbo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper constructs a covariant rank-4 tensor gauge field theory that naturally yields fractonic string-like excitations governed by Gauss-like constraints derived from symmetry, including a new generalized dipole conservation law for closed strings, and reveals a connection to linearised area-metric gravity in a suitable limit.
\n\n
本文构建了一个协变的四阶张量规范场理论，该理论自然地产生了由对称性导出的高斯型约束所支配的分形子（fracton）弦状激发态，包括一种针对闭合弦的新广义偶极守恒律，并在适当极限下揭示了其与线性化面积度规引力（linearised area-metric gravity）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a fundamental, symmetry-based field-theoretic description of fractonic phases—particularly those involving extended (string-like) excitations—without imposing mobility restrictions by hand, and to explore potential deep connections between higher-rank gauge theories and gravitational physics.
\n\n
动机是建立一个基于对称性的基本场论框架来描述分形子相（尤其是涉及延展弦状激发的情形），避免人为施加运动限制，并探索高阶秩规范理论与引力物理之间可能存在的深刻联系。

Method: The authors construct the most general quadratic, parity-preserving, Lorentz-covariant action for a rank-4 gauge potential $A_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$. They derive the associated field equations, identify conserved currents and charges via Noether’s theorem, define tensorial electric and magnetic fields, and analyze the resulting Gauss-like constraints. They also examine the theory’s reduction to known rank-2 covariant fracton models and its relation to linearised area-metric gravity.
\n\n
作者构造了关于四阶规范势 $A_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$ 的最一般的二次、宇称守恒且洛伦兹协变的作用量。他们推导了相应的场方程，通过诺特定理识别守恒流与荷，定义了张量型电场和磁场，并分析由此产生的高斯型约束。此外，他们还考察了该理论如何约化为已知的二阶秩协变分形子模型及其与线性化面积度规引力的关系。

Result: The theory yields Maxwell-like equations for tensorial fields, a conserved energy-momentum tensor, and a Lorentz-like force law. Crucially, Gauss-like constraints emerge as Bianchi identities or equations of motion, enforcing restricted mobility: one novel constraint enforces generalized dipole conservation for closed strings, defining a new class of fractonic string excitations. In a specific limit, the model reduces to covariant rank-2 fracton theories and matches linearised area-metric gravity.
\n\n
该理论导出了张量场的类麦克斯韦方程、守恒的能量-动量张量以及类洛伦兹力定律。关键的是，高斯型约束作为比安基恒等式或运动方程自然出现，强制限制运动性：其中一种新约束实现了闭合弦的广义偶极守恒，定义了一类新的分形子弦激发态。在特定极限下，该模型可约化为协变的二阶秩分形子理论，并与线性化面积度规引力一致。

Conclusion: This work establishes a unified, symmetry-driven framework linking higher-rank gauge theories, fractonic extended objects, and emergent gravitational structures, demonstrating that fractonic behavior—including exotic conservation laws—can arise intrinsically from covariant field theory without ad hoc assumptions.
\n\n
本工作建立了一个统一的、由对称性驱动的框架，将高阶秩规范理论、分形子延展激发与涌现的引力结构联系起来，表明分形子行为（包括奇异守恒律）可内生于协变场论中，无需人为假设。

Abstract: We present a covariant field-theoretical framework for a rank-4 tensor gauge field theory describing fractonic string-like objects. We show that the most general quadratic, parity-preserving action naturally leads to a Maxwell-like sector, with tensorial analogues of electric and magnetic fields, Maxwell-like equations, a conserved energy-momentum tensor, and a Lorentz-like force. Remarkably, the theory gives rise to fracton-like string excitations purely from symmetry principles: constraints on the motion of these extended objects appear as Gauss-like laws, without being imposed by hand. One of these laws is new and corresponds to a generalised dipole conservation for closed strings, restricting their mobility and defining a novel class of fractonic string-like excitations. Finally, we uncover a connection to linearised area-metric gravity: in a suitable limit, the theory reduces to known covariant fracton models with rank-2 gauge fields, highlighting a deep link between fractonic matter and gravity-like structures. This provides a unified perspective on higher-rank gauge fields, extended excitations, and emergent gravitational features.

</details>


### [67] [On Type II$_0$ Loci in Moduli Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07746)
*Jarod Hattab,Eran Palti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates type II$_0$ infinite-distance singularities in the moduli space of type IIB string theory compactified on Calabi-Yau manifolds, showing that the leading behavior of the gauge kinetic matrix and prepotential can be interpreted as a threshold correction from integrating out a BPS state with an effectively complex charge. A two-parameter Calabi-Yau example reveals a strongly-coupled matter sector with both light electric and magnetic states, which admits a weakly-coupled IR description via this complex-charged state. The Heterotic dual identifies the light magnetic state as a Kaluza-Klein monopole, suggesting emergent infinite-distance loci in quantum gravity moduli spaces.
\n\n
本文研究了IIB型弦理论在Calabi-Yau流形上紧致化后模空间中的type II$_0$无限距离奇点，表明规范动能矩阵和预势的主导行为可被解释为由一个具有有效复电荷的BPS态积分产生的阈值修正。通过一个双参数Calabi-Yau例子，作者揭示了一个同时包含轻电态和轻磁态的强耦合物质扇区，该扇区在红外下具有以该复电荷态为自由度的弱耦合描述。其杂化弦对偶图像中，轻磁态对应Kaluza-Klein单极子，其质量低于基本杂化弦，从而形成非微扰扇区。该图像暗示量子引力模空间中存在红外涌现的无限距离奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the physical origin of the universal leading-order behavior near type II$_0$ infinite-distance singularities in the moduli space of type IIB Calabi-Yau compactifications. Specifically, the authors aim to interpret the appearance of an effectively complex charge in the threshold correction formula for the gauge kinetic function and prepotential, and to identify the underlying non-perturbative sector responsible for this behavior.
\n\n
动机在于理解IIB型Calabi-Yau紧致化模空间中type II$_0$无限距离奇点附近普适主导行为的物理起源。具体而言，作者旨在解释规范动能函数和预势的阈值修正公式中出现的有效复电荷的物理含义，并识别导致该行为的底层非微扰扇区。

Method: The authors analyze the asymptotic form of the gauge kinetic matrix $\\mathcal{N}_{IJ}$ and the prepotential $\\mathcal{F}$ near type II$_0$ loci using the mathematical structure of limiting mixed Hodge structures. They decompose the vector multiplets into the graviphoton and matter sectors based on the asymptotic Hodge decomposition. In a concrete two-modulus Calabi-Yau example, they explicitly compute the spectrum and identify light electric and magnetic states. They then compare this to the Heterotic string dual, where the magnetic state is identified as a Kaluza-Klein monopole, to provide a microscopic interpretation.
\n\n
作者利用极限混合Hodge结构（limiting mixed Hodge structures）的数学框架，分析type II$_0$奇点附近规范动能矩阵$\\mathcal{N}_{IJ}$和预势$\\mathcal{F}$的渐近形式。他们基于渐近Hodge分解，将矢量多重态分解为graviphoton方向与物质扇区。在一个具体的双模Calabi-Yau例子中，他们显式计算能谱并识别出轻电态与轻磁态。随后，他们将其与杂化弦对偶进行比较，在该对偶中磁态被识别为Kaluza-Klein单极子，从而提供微观解释。

Result: The key result is that the leading asymptotic behavior of $\\mathcal{N}_{IJ}$ and $\\mathcal{F}$ near a type II$_0$ locus is universally given by a one-loop threshold correction formula involving a BPS state with an effective complex charge $q_{\\text{eff}}$. In the explicit example, this is shown to arise from a strongly-coupled sector containing both light electric and light magnetic BPS states. The Heterotic dual description confirms that the light magnetic state is a Kaluza-Klein monopole, which becomes lighter than the fundamental string scale, thereby dominating the physics and leading to the observed effective description.
\n\n
核心结果是：在type II$_0$奇点附近，$\\mathcal{N}_{IJ}$和$\\mathcal{F}$的主导渐近行为普适地由一个涉及具有有效复电荷$q_{\\text{eff}}$的BPS态的一圈阈值修正公式给出。在具体例子中，该行为源于一个同时包含轻电BPS态和轻磁BPS态的强耦合扇区。杂化弦对偶描述证实，该轻磁态为Kaluza-Klein单极子，其质量低于基本弦尺度，从而主导物理并导出所观测到的有效描述。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the effective complex charge is a signature of a non-perturbative sector that becomes light at the infinite-distance limit. This sector, comprising both electric and magnetic degrees of freedom, has a weakly-coupled IR description in terms of the complex-charged state. The existence of such a sector in the Heterotic dual, driven by a light Kaluza-Klein monopole, provides strong evidence for the proposal and suggests a general mechanism for emergent infinite-distance loci in quantum gravity moduli spaces.
\n\n
本文结论认为，有效复电荷是非微扰扇区在无限距离极限下变轻的标志。该扇区包含电与磁自由度，并在红外下具有以复电荷态为自由度的弱耦合描述。在杂化弦对偶中，由轻Kaluza-Klein单极子驱动的此类扇区的存在，为该提议提供了有力证据，并暗示了量子引力模空间中涌现无限距离奇点的普适机制。

Abstract: We study type II$_0$ loci in the moduli space of type IIB string theory compactified on Calabi-Yau manifolds. We show that around these infinite distance singular loci the leading order behaviour of the gauge kinetic matrix, and of the prepotential, can always be written in the form of a threshold correction from integrating out a BPS state, but one with an effectively complex charge. In order to understand the physical meaning of this, we carefully identify the splitting in the effective supergravity between the graviphoton direction and matter vector multiplets. Within a specific two-parameter example of a Calabi-Yau, we use this to identify a strongly-coupled matter sector involving both light electric and light magnetic states. We propose that the leading gauge kinetic matrix arises as a threshold correction from integrating out this non-perturbative sector, and that the sector has an effective weakly-coupled infrared description in terms of the complex-charged state. The region in moduli space has a Heterotic string dual microscopic description. The light magnetic state in this description corresponds to a Kaluza-Klein monopole, which becomes lighter than the fundamental Heterotic string, leading to the non-perturbative sector. Assuming this picture is correct, it implies the existence of infrared emergent infinite distance loci in moduli spaces of quantum gravity.

</details>


### [68] [BPS vortex from nonpolynomial scalar QED in a $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-Maxwell theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07803)
*F. C. E. Lima*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper constructs a generalized gauged $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-Maxwell theory in $(2+1)$D where the magnetic permeability becomes field-dependent due to one-loop fermionic vacuum polarization. The resulting effective action supports Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) vortex solutions with quantized magnetic flux, and reveals a nontrivial interplay between the Fubini-Study geometry of the $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$ target space and the induced logarithmic magnetic permeability.
\n\n
本文构建了一个在$(2+1)$维中推广的规范$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-Maxwell理论，其中由于单圈费米子真空极化效应，磁导率变为场依赖的。所得有效作用量支持Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS)涡旋解，其磁通量量子化，并揭示了$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$目标空间的Fubini-Study几何与诱导的对数型磁导率之间的非平凡相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how quantum corrections—specifically fermionic vacuum polarization—affect topological solitons in nonlinear sigma models coupled to gauge fields. The authors aim to explore whether integrating out massive Dirac fermions can dynamically generate a nontrivial, field-dependent magnetic permeability that preserves BPS properties, thereby enriching the structure of vortex solutions in gauged $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$ models beyond standard Maxwell electrodynamics.
\n\n
动机源于理解量子修正（特别是费米子真空极化）如何影响与规范场耦合的非线性sigma模型中的拓扑孤子。作者旨在探索：通过积分掉具有有效质量的Dirac费米子，是否能动态生成一个非平凡的、场依赖的磁导率，同时保持BPS性质，从而在规范$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$模型中超越标准Maxwell电动力学，丰富涡旋解的结构。

Method: Starting from the gauged $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-sigma model on a curved target space equipped with the Fubini-Study metric, the authors couple it to a Dirac fermion with an effective mass proportional to the sigma-model field. They perform a one-loop integration of the fermion to compute the induced effective action for the gauge field. After dimensional reduction to $(2+1)$ dimensions, they obtain a non-polynomial correction to the Maxwell term, which simplifies to a logarithmic magnetic permeability $\\mu(|n|^2) \\propto \\log(1 + |n|^2)$, where $n$ is the $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$ field. They then derive the self-dual (BPS) equations by saturating a Bogomol'nyi bound and solve them analytically or numerically to find vortex configurations with quantized magnetic flux $\\Phi = 2\\pi k/e$ ($k \\in \\mathbb{Z}$).
\n\n
作者从具有Fubini-Study度规的弯曲目标空间上的规范$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-sigma模型出发，将其与一个有效质量正比于sigma模型场的Dirac费米子耦合。通过单圈积分该费米子，计算规范场的诱导有效作用量。在降至$(2+1)$维后，得到对Maxwell项的非多项式修正，简化为对数型磁导率$\\mu(|n|^2) \\propto \\log(1 + |n|^2)$，其中$n$为$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$场。随后，他们通过饱和Bogomol'nyi界导出自对偶（BPS）方程，并解析或数值求解以获得磁通量量子化为$\\Phi = 2\\pi k/e$（$k \\in \\mathbb{Z}$）的涡旋构型。

Result: The key result is the derivation of a dynamically generated, logarithmic magnetic permeability in $(2+1)$D from fermionic loop effects, leading to a modified Maxwell term $\\mathcal{L}_{\\text{eff}} \\supset -\\frac{1}{4e^2} \\log(1 + |n|^2) F_{\\mu\
u}F^{\\mu\
u}$. This modification preserves the BPS property, allowing exact vortex solutions with quantized magnetic flux. The analysis also shows that the curvature of the $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$ target space (via the Fubini-Study metric) directly influences the functional form of the induced permeability, establishing a geometric origin for the nonlinearity in the gauge sector.
\n\n
核心结果是从费米子圈效应中导出了$(2+1)$维中动态生成的对数型磁导率，导致修正的Maxwell项$\\mathcal{L}_{\\text{eff}} \\supset -\\frac{1}{4e^2} \\log(1 + |n|^2) F_{\\mu\
u}F^{\\mu\
u}$。该修正保持了BPS性质，允许存在磁通量量子化的精确涡旋解。分析还表明，$\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$目标空间的曲率（通过Fubini-Study度规）直接影响诱导磁导率的函数形式，从而为规范场部分的非线性提供了几何起源。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that quantum effects from fermionic degrees of freedom can induce nontrivial, geometry-dependent modifications to the gauge sector in topological field theories, while preserving integrability through BPS bounds. This establishes a novel link between target-space geometry, quantum vacuum polarization, and classical soliton structure in $(2+1)$-dimensional gauge theories, opening avenues for exploring emergent electromagnetic responses in systems with internal curved manifolds.
\n\n
本文表明，在拓扑场论中，费米子自由度的量子效应可诱导出规范场部分的非平凡、几何依赖的修正，同时通过BPS界保持可积性。这在$(2+1)$维规范理论中建立了目标空间几何、量子真空极化与经典孤子结构之间的新联系，为探索具有内禀弯曲流形系统的涌现电磁响应开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate a generalized gauged $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-Maxwell theory in which the electromagnetic sector acquires a field-dependent magnetic permeability generated dynamically through fermionic vacuum polarization. Starting from the gauged $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-sigma model, whose dynamics occurs on a curved target space endowed with the Fubini-Study metric, we show that integrating out a Dirac fermion with effective mass induces, at one loop, a non-polynomial magnetic permeability, which after dimensional reduction to $(2+1)$-dimensions yields an effective Maxwell sector takes the form of a logarithmic magnetic permeability. Within this framework, one builds a generalized $\mathds{C}\mathrm{P}^1$-Maxwell model by admitting Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) configurations. Taking this into account, we solved the self-dual equations that describe vortex-like solutions with quantized magnetic flux. Furthermore, one highlights the interactions between the target-space geometry and the induced permeability.

### [69] [Probing Lorentz symmetry violation via the Casimir effect in rectangular cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07938)
*M. B. Cruz,E. R. Bezerra de Mello,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies the Casimir effect for a real scalar field in a rectangular waveguide with Dirichlet boundary conditions, using it as a probe of Lorentz symmetry violation introduced via a fixed background four-vector $u_\\mu$ in a modified Klein-Gordon theory. The authors compute the vacuum energy for four specific orientations of $u_\\mu$ (temporal or aligned with spatial axes) and find direction-dependent corrections to the Casimir energy that reflect anisotropic dispersion relations, while preserving mode separability and the universal structure of the spectral kernel.
\n\n
本文研究了在具有Dirichlet边界条件的矩形波导中，实标量场的Casimir效应作为Lorentz对称性破缺的探针，其中Lorentz破缺通过修改的Klein-Gordon理论中引入一个固定的背景四矢量 $u_\\mu$ 实现。作者计算了 $u_\\mu$ 在四种特定取向（时间方向或与空间轴对齐）下的真空能，发现Casimir能量出现了依赖于方向的修正，反映了各向异性的色散关系，同时保持了模式可分离性和谱核的普适结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how Lorentz symmetry violation—introduced through a fixed background vector $u_\\mu$ in a modified Klein-Gordon Lagrangian—affects quantum vacuum fluctuations in confined geometries. The Casimir effect provides a sensitive experimental and theoretical platform to detect such symmetry-breaking effects, especially those that are anisotropic and geometry-dependent, which may arise in quantum gravity or effective field theories beyond the Standard Model.
\n\n
动机在于探索通过修改的Klein-Gordon拉格朗日量中引入固定背景矢量 $u_\\mu$ 所导致的Lorentz对称性破缺如何影响受限几何中的量子真空涨落。Casimir效应提供了一个敏感的实验与理论平台，用于探测此类对称性破缺效应，特别是那些具有各向异性且依赖于几何结构的效应，这些效应可能源于量子引力或超出标准模型的有效场论。

Method: The authors consider a real scalar field obeying Dirichlet boundary conditions on a rectangular cavity, governed by a Lorentz-violating Klein-Gordon equation: $(\\partial^2 + m^2 + u_\\mu \\partial^\\mu)^2 \\phi = 0$ (or equivalent formulations). They analyze four canonical configurations where the background vector $u_\\mu$ is aligned with the time axis or one of the three spatial axes. For each case, they solve for the modified mode frequencies, derive the regularized vacuum energy via zeta-function or cutoff regularization, and examine how the Casimir energy depends on the orientation of $u_\\mu$ relative to the cavity.
\n\n
作者考虑一个在矩形腔中满足Dirichlet边界条件的实标量场，其动力学由Lorentz破缺的Klein-Gordon方程描述：$(\\partial^2 + m^2 + u_\\mu \\partial^\\mu)^2 \\phi = 0$（或等效形式）。他们分析了四种典型构型，其中背景矢量 $u_\\mu$ 分别沿时间轴或三个空间轴之一对齐。针对每种情况，求解修正后的模式频率，通过zeta函数或截断正规化方法导出正规化的真空能，并考察Casimir能量如何依赖于 $u_\\mu$ 相对于腔体的取向。

Result: The Lorentz-violating background induces anisotropic modifications to the field’s dispersion relation, leading to orientation-dependent shifts in the mode spectrum and Casimir energy. Despite these changes, the eigenmode structure remains separable, and the functional form of the spectral kernel retains its universal character. The resulting Casimir energy exhibits explicit dependence on the direction of $u_\\mu$, providing a measurable signature of Lorentz symmetry breaking in confined systems.
\n\n
Lorentz破缺背景导致场的色散关系出现各向异性修正，从而引起模式谱和Casimir能量的取向依赖性偏移。尽管如此，本征模式结构仍保持可分离性，且谱核的函数形式保留其普适性。所得Casimir能量显式依赖于 $u_\\mu$ 的方向，为受限系统中Lorentz对称性破缺提供了可观测的信号。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that Casimir setups in confined geometries can serve as precise probes of Lorentz symmetry violation, particularly for anisotropic modifications induced by a fixed background field. The direction-sensitive corrections to the vacuum energy offer a clean theoretical signature that could, in principle, be tested in precision experiments, thereby linking tabletop quantum field theory measurements to fundamental questions about spacetime symmetry.
\n\n
该研究表明，在受限几何中的Casimir装置可作为Lorentz对称性破缺的精确探针，尤其适用于由固定背景场引起的各向异性修正。真空能中对方向敏感的修正提供了一种清晰的理论信号，原则上可在精密实验中检验，从而将桌面尺度的量子场论测量与时空对称性的基本问题联系起来。

Abstract: We investigate the Casimir effect as a probe of Lorentz symmetry violation for a real scalar field confined to a rectangular waveguide with Dirichlet boundary conditions. The field dynamics is governed by a Lorentz-violating extension of the Klein-Gordon theory involving a fixed background four-vector $u_μ$. Focusing on four representative configurations in which the background is aligned with the temporal direction or with one of the spatial axes of the cavity, we derive the modified mode spectra and the corresponding vacuum energies. We show that these configurations induce anisotropic modifications of the dispersion relations that depend explicitly on the orientation of the background vector relative to the cavity geometry, while still preserving mode separability. The resulting Casimir energy acquires characteristic direction-dependent corrections that encode the breaking of Lorentz symmetry, without altering the universal functional structure of the spectral kernel. Our analysis provides a controlled and transparent framework for isolating Lorentz-violating effects in confined geometries and highlights Casimir systems as sensitive probes of anisotropic physics and fundamental spacetime symmetries.

### [70] [Homogeneous Anisotropic Black Branes with Bianchi VI$_h$ Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07993)
*Markus A. G. Amano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper presents a new class of exact vacuum black brane solutions in five-dimensional Einstein gravity with negative cosmological constant, featuring homogeneous horizons with Bianchi VI$_h$ symmetry. These generalize the Solv (Bianchi VI$_{-1}$) geometry via a continuous anisotropy parameter $h$. The authors reduce the field equations to a cohomogeneity-one system to solve analytically for the metric. Although not asymptotically (locally) AdS, thermodynamic properties are studied, yielding anisotropic entropy–temperature scaling. A separate branch of Ricci-flat, hyperscaling-violating vacuum solutions is also found when the cosmological constant vanishes.
\n\n
本文提出了一类新的五维爱因斯坦引力中具有负宇宙学常数的真空黑膜解，其视界具有Bianchi VI$_h$对称性的均匀结构。这些解通过连续各向异性参数$h$推广了已知的Solv（Bianchi VI$_{-1}$）几何。作者将场方程约化为cohomogeneity-one系统，并解析求得了度规。尽管这些解并非渐近（局部）AdS，但作者仍分析了其热力学性质，得到了各向异性全息系统中的熵与温度的标度关系。此外，当宇宙学常数为零时，还发现了一支新的Ricci-flat、hyperscaling-violating真空解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to explore gravitational solutions with non-trivial spatial anisotropy and homogeneous but non-isotropic horizon geometries, particularly within the context of holography. Bianchi classifications offer a systematic way to study such homogeneous spacetimes, and extending known solutions like the Solv geometry (Bianchi VI$_{-1}$) to a continuous family parameterized by $h$ allows for a deeper understanding of how anisotropy affects black brane thermodynamics and potential dual field theories. Additionally, investigating the $\Lambda = 0$ limit reveals novel Ricci-flat geometries with hyperscaling violation, enriching the landscape of exact solutions in general relativity.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于探索具有非平凡空间各向异性以及均匀但非各向同性视界几何的引力解，特别是在全息原理背景下。Bianchi分类为研究此类均匀时空提供了一种系统方法，而将已知的Solv几何（Bianchi VI$_{-1}$）推广为由连续参数$h$标记的解族，有助于深入理解各向异性如何影响黑膜热力学及其可能的对偶场论。此外，考察$\Lambda = 0$极限揭示了具有hyperscaling violation的新颖Ricci-flat几何，丰富了广义相对论中精确解的景观。

Method: The authors employ a symmetry-based ansatz consistent with Bianchi VI$_h$ homogeneous spatial slices, reducing the five-dimensional vacuum Einstein equations with cosmological constant $\Lambda = -6/L^2$ to a cohomogeneity-one ordinary differential equation (ODE) system. By exploiting the homogeneity of the horizon, they simplify the PDEs to ODEs along the radial direction. The resulting system is solved analytically, yielding an exact metric depending on the anisotropy parameter $h$. Thermodynamic quantities such as temperature and entropy are computed via standard black brane techniques (e.g., surface gravity and horizon area). In the $\Lambda \to 0$ limit, they separately analyze the field equations to uncover a new class of Ricci-flat, hyperscaling-violating solutions.
\n\n
作者采用与Bianchi VI$_h$均匀空间切片一致的对称性假设，将五维含宇宙学常数$\Lambda = -6/L^2$的真空爱因斯坦方程约化为一个cohomogeneity-one常微分方程（ODE）系统。通过利用视界的均匀性，他们将偏微分方程简化为沿径向的常微分方程。所得系统被解析求解，得到依赖于各向异性参数$h$的精确度规。温度和熵等热力学量通过标准黑膜技术（如表面引力和视界面积）计算。在$\Lambda \to 0$极限下，他们单独分析场方程，揭示了一类新的Ricci-flat、hyperscaling-violating解。

Result: The main results are: (1) an exact analytic black brane solution in $AdS_5$ with homogeneous Bianchi VI$_h$ horizon geometry, continuously interpolating between different anisotropic geometries as $h$ varies; (2) derivation of thermodynamic scaling laws $S \sim T^{\\frac{2}{1+h}}$ (for $h > -1$), indicating anisotropic holographic duals; (3) discovery of a new branch of vacuum, Ricci-flat solutions with hyperscaling violation in five dimensions when $\Lambda = 0$, characterized by metrics of the form $ds^2 = dr^2 + r^{2\\theta/d} \\left( e^{2\\alpha x} dy^2 + e^{-2\\alpha x} dz^2 + dx^2 + dt^2 \\right)$ with hyperscaling violation exponent $\theta$ related to the anisotropy.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 在$AdS_5$中构造出具有均匀Bianchi VI$_h$视界几何的精确解析黑膜解，当$h$变化时可连续插值不同各向异性几何；(2) 推导出热力学标度律$S \sim T^{\\frac{2}{1+h}}$（对于$h > -1$），表明其对应各向异性全息对偶；(3) 当$\Lambda = 0$时，在五维中发现一支新的真空Ricci-flat解，具有hyperscaling violation，其度规形式为$ds^2 = dr^2 + r^{2\\theta/d} \\left( e^{2\\alpha x} dy^2 + e^{-2\\alpha x} dz^2 + dx^2 + dt^2 \\right)$，其中hyperscaling violation指数$\theta$与各向异性相关。

Conclusion: This work expands the catalog of exact black brane solutions with non-isotropic homogeneous horizons in AdS gravity, providing a tunable family of geometries governed by the Bianchi VI$_h$ parameter $h$. These solutions offer a concrete gravitational framework for studying anisotropic strongly coupled systems via holography, with explicit thermodynamic scaling. The identification of hyperscaling-violating Ricci-flat solutions in the flat-space limit further demonstrates the richness of vacuum Einstein gravity beyond isotropic or asymptotically AdS settings.
\n\n
本工作扩展了AdS引力中具有非各向同性均匀视界的精确黑膜解目录，提供了一族由Bianchi VI$_h$参数$h$调控的可调几何。这些解为通过全息原理研究各向异性强耦合系统提供了具体的引力框架，并具有明确的热力学标度。在平直空间极限下发现的hyperscaling-violating Ricci-flat解进一步表明，真空爱因斯坦引力在超越各向同性或渐近AdS情形时仍具有丰富的结构。

Abstract: We construct a new family of exact vacuum black brane solutions to five-dimensional Einstein gravity with a negative cosmological constant, characterized by a homogeneous horizon with Bianchi VI$_h$ symmetry. This construction generalizes the known Solv (Bianchi VI$_{-1}$) geometry via a continuous anisotropy parameter, $h$. By reducing the field equations to a cohomogeneity-one system, we derive the metric analytically. These homogeneous solutions are not asymptotically (locally) AdS, but nevertheless we analyze the thermodynamics, establishing scaling relations between entropy and temperature with anisotropic holographic system in mind. Additionally, we identify a new branch of Ricci-flat, hyperscaling-violating vacuum solutions in the case where the cosmological constant vanishes.

### [71] [Error-correcting codes over the Mordell-Weil groups of extremal rational elliptic surfaces and the $E_8$ lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08102)
*Shun'ya Mizoguchi,Takumi Oikawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper constructs the $E_8$ lattice using classical error-correcting codes over Mordell-Weil groups of rational elliptic surfaces with maximal-rank (rank 8) singularity lattices, leveraging Oguiso-Shioda's classification. This approach generalizes standard code-based lattice constructions like Construction A and Construction A$_{\rm C}$ into a Lie algebraic framework.
\n\n
本文利用经典纠错码在具有最大秩（秩为8）奇点格的有理椭圆曲面的Mordell-Weil群上构造了$E_8$格，借助Oguiso-Shioda分类完成。该方法将Construction A和Construction A$_{\rm C}$等标准码基格构造推广到李代数框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from seeking deeper connections between algebraic geometry, coding theory, and lattice theory—specifically, to realize the exceptional $E_8$ root lattice through geometric and arithmetic structures arising from rational elliptic surfaces. The authors aim to extend classical code-to-lattice constructions (e.g., Construction A) by incorporating the rich structure of Mordell-Weil lattices and their relation to singularity lattices in the context of Oguiso-Shioda’s classification.
\n\n
动机源于寻求代数几何、编码理论与格理论之间的深层联系——特别是通过有理椭圆曲面所导出的几何与算术结构来实现例外的$E_8$根格。作者旨在将经典码到格的构造（如Construction A）加以推广，融入Mordell-Weil格及其与Oguiso-Shioda分类中奇点格关系的丰富结构。

Method: The method relies on the structure theorem for Mordell-Weil lattices of rational elliptic surfaces: when the singularity lattice has maximal rank 8, the Mordell-Weil group is either cyclic or a direct sum of cyclic groups. Using Oguiso-Shioda’s complete classification of such surfaces, the authors define error-correcting codes over the natural ring of the Mordell-Weil group. These codes are then used to "glue" the orthogonal components of the singularity lattice, resulting in the full $E_8$ lattice. This procedure extends Construction A-type methods by replacing the base field/group with modules over rings derived from elliptic surface geometry.
\n\n
该方法依赖于有理椭圆曲面Mordell-Weil格的结构定理：当奇点格具有最大秩8时，Mordell-Weil群为循环群或其直和。作者利用Oguiso-Shioda对此类曲面的完整分类，在Mordell-Weil群的自然环上定义纠错码。这些码随后用于“粘合”奇点格的正交分量，从而得到完整的$E_8$格。该过程通过将Construction A类方法中的基域/群替换为源自椭圆曲面几何的环上的模，实现了推广。

Result: The paper successfully constructs the $E_8$ lattice uniformly across all cases in Oguiso-Shioda’s classification by gluing singularity lattices via codes over Mordell-Weil groups. This yields a unified, geometrically motivated realization of $E_8$ that subsumes and generalizes classical code lattice constructions within a Lie-theoretic and arithmetic-geometric context.
\n\n
本文成功地在Oguiso-Shioda分类的所有情形下，通过Mordell-Weil群上的码粘合奇点格，统一构造出$E_8$格。这提供了一种统一且几何动机明确的$E_8$实现方式，将经典码格构造纳入李理论与算术几何的框架中并加以推广。

Conclusion: This work establishes a novel bridge between the theory of rational elliptic surfaces, error-correcting codes, and exceptional Lie algebras by showing that the $E_8$ lattice can be systematically built from codes over Mordell-Weil groups. It positions Construction A-like methods within a broader algebraic-geometric paradigm, suggesting potential extensions to other root lattices and deeper links between coding theory and modular forms or string compactifications.
\n\n
本工作通过展示$E_8$格可系统地由Mordell-Weil群上的码构建，建立了有理椭圆曲面理论、纠错码与例外李代数之间的新桥梁。它将Construction A类方法置于更广泛的代数几何范式中，暗示了向其他根格推广的可能性，以及编码理论与模形式或弦紧化之间更深层的联系。

Abstract: We construct the $E_8$ lattice from classical error-correcting codes over the Mordell-Weil groups of rational elliptic surfaces that have a singularity lattice of rank 8 (maximal) for all cases of Oguiso-Shioda's classification. By the structure theorem of the Mordell-Weil lattice of rational elliptic surfaces, if the rank of the singularity lattice is maximal, then the Mordell-Weil group is a cyclic group or a direct sum of them. The singularity lattices are glued together by a code over their natural ring to form the $E_8$ lattice. Such constructions of the $E_8$ lattice from codes can be seen as a Lie algebraic extension and further generalization of known code lattice constructions such as Construction A and Construction A${}_{\rm C}$.

### [72] [WKB-asymptotics for multipoint Virasoro conformal blocks and applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08194)

These results generalize Zamolodchikov's elliptic recursion and enable numerical computations in minimal string theory, with consistency verified against exact 5-point blocks and AGT-based series expansions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: The WKB analysis of the classical BPZ equation provides a powerful and systematic tool to compute asymptotic Virasoro conformal blocks at large intermediate dimensions. This approach bridges integrable structures in 2D CFT (like elliptic recursion) with modern techniques such as the AGT correspondence, opening avenues for numerical and analytical studies of non-perturbative observables in minimal string theory and related models.
\n\n
对经典BPZ方程的WKB分析为计算大中间维度下Virasoro共形块的渐近行为提供了一种强大而系统的方法。该方法将二维共形场论中的可积结构（如椭圆递归）与现代技术（如AGT对应）相联系，为极小弦理论及相关模型中非微扰观测量的数值与解析研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We study multipoint Virasoro conformal blocks on the sphere in the comb channel. We arrive at the asymptotic expression for these blocks at large intermediate dimensions, applying WKB method for "classical BPZ equation", which is used to study (classical) Virasoro blocks via monodromy method. Several applications of this asymptotic are discussed, such as the possibility to generalize Zamolodchikov's elliptic recursion and numerical evaluation of amplitudes in minimal string theory. Our expressions pass nontrivial checks, such as agreement with known exact expressions for 5-point blocks in special cases and the usual series expansion of Virasoro blocks computed using AGT correspondence.

\n\n
本文利用全息方法研究了重子富集热等离子体的输运性质，其对偶体是带有高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet, GB）修正和弦云背景的荷电AdS黑洞。文章系统分析了拖曳力、喷注淬火参数、屏蔽长度、径向轮廓和能量损失等关键观测量如何随GB耦合、重子/味密度、温度和角频率变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Holographic duality provides a non-perturbative framework to compute real-time transport coefficients. Incorporating Gauss-Bonnet corrections accounts for finite coupling effects beyond supergravity approximation, while the string cloud models flavor degrees of freedom, enabling study of baryon and flavor density dependence.
\n\n
动机源于在有限重子密度和有限’t Hooft耦合下理解强耦合类QCD等离子体，传统微扰方法在此失效。全息对偶提供了计算实时输运系数的非微扰框架。引入高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）修正是为了刻画超引力近似之外的有限耦合效应，而弦云模型则用于描述味自由度，从而研究重子密度和味密度的影响。

Method: The authors employ gauge/gravity duality (AdS/CFT correspondence). The boundary theory is a baryon-rich thermal plasma dual to a bulk geometry: a charged AdS black hole with Gauss-Bonnet higher-derivative curvature corrections and a string cloud source. They compute:
- Drag force via the Nambu–Goto action for a trailing string,
- Jet quenching parameter $\\hat{q}$ from the expectation value of a light-like Wilson loop,
- Screening length from the maximal separation of a static quark-antiquark pair,
- Radial profile and energy loss of a rotating quark by solving equations of motion for a rotating string ansatz in the corrected background.
All quantities are evaluated as functions of Gauss-Bonnet coupling $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$, chemical potential (baryon density), flavor density (string cloud density), temperature $T$, and angular frequency $\\omega$.
\n\n
作者采用规范/引力对偶（AdS/CFT对应）。边界理论是一个重子富集的热等离子体，其对偶体为带有高斯-博内高阶曲率修正和弦云源的荷电AdS黑洞。他们通过以下方法计算：
- 利用Nambu–Goto作用量计算拖曳弦的拖曳力，
- 通过类光Wilson圈的期望值计算喷注淬火参数 $\\hat{q}$，
- 从静态夸克-反夸克对的最大分离距离确定屏蔽长度，
- 通过在修正背景中求解旋转弦假设下的运动方程，得到旋转夸克的径向轮廓和能量损失。
所有物理量均作为高斯-博内耦合 $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$、化学势（重子密度）、味密度（弦云密度）、温度 $T$ 和角频率 $\\omega$ 的函数进行评估。

Result: Key results include:
- Drag force and jet quenching parameter $\\hat{q}$ increase with Gauss-Bonnet coupling $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$, baryon chemical potential $\\mu_B$, and flavor density $n_f$.
- Screening length decreases with $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$, $\\mu_B$, and $n_f$.
- Radial profile of rotating quark decreases with $\\mu_B$, $n_f$, temperature $T$, and angular frequency $\\omega$, but increases with conjugate momenta and $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$.
- Energy loss grows with $\\mu_B$, $n_f$, velocity $v$, and $\\omega$, but is suppressed by $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$.
These trends indicate that finite coupling and finite density enhance energy dissipation and reduce coherence length scales in the plasma.
\n\n
主要结果包括：
- 拖曳力和喷注淬火参数 $\\hat{q}$ 随高斯-博内耦合 $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$、重子化学势 $\\mu_B$ 和味密度 $n_f$ 增大；
- 屏蔽长度随 $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$、$\\mu_B$ 和 $n_f$ 减小；
- 旋转夸克的径向轮廓随 $\\mu_B$、$n_f$、温度 $T$ 和角频率 $\\omega$ 减小，但随共轭动量和 $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$ 增大；
- 能量损失随 $\\mu_B$、$n_f$、速度 $v$ 和 $\\omega$ 增大，但被 $\\lambda_{\\text{GB}}$ 抑制。
这些趋势表明，有限耦合和有限密度增强了等离子体中的能量耗散，并缩短了相干长度尺度。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that finite 't Hooft coupling (via Gauss-Bonnet correction) and finite baryon/flavor densities significantly modify transport properties in strongly coupled plasmas. The enhancement of drag and jet quenching suggests stronger interactions at finite density and finite coupling, relevant for modeling quark-gluon plasma in heavy-ion collisions at intermediate energies (e.g., RHIC BES). The suppression of energy loss by GB coupling highlights the role of higher-derivative gravity corrections in regulating dissipation.
\n\n
本研究表明，有限’t Hooft耦合（通过高斯-博内修正）和有限重子/味密度显著改变了强耦合等离子体的输运性质。拖曳力和喷注淬火的增强表明在有限密度和有限耦合下相互作用更强，这对中等能量重离子碰撞（如RHIC BES）中夸克-胶子等离子体的建模具有重要意义。GB耦合对能量损失的抑制凸显了高阶导数引力修正对耗散过程的调控作用。

Abstract: In this work, holographic approach has been used to analyse the transport properties of baryon rich back-reacted thermal plasma with finite 't Hooft coupling correction. The dual bulk geometry is charged AdS black hole with higher derivative Gauss-Bonnet (GB) correction and string cloud. Specially, we have studied the nature of drag force, jet quenching parameter, screening length, radial profile and energy loss with respect to different parameters. The drag force and jet quenching parameter are enhanced with GB coupling, baryon and flavor density whereas the screening length reduces with these parameters. The radial profile and energy loss of the rotating quark has also been studied and it is observed that the radial profile decreases with increase in baryon potential and flavor density, temperature and angular frequency, whereas it is enhanced with conjugate momenta and GB coupling. Further, the energy loss of the quark grows with potential and flavor density, velocity and angular frequency and it is suppressed with GB coupling.

</details>


### [74] [Topological Fields in $4d$ Higher Spin Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08334)
*P. T. Kirakosiants*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies topological fields in 4d higher spin theory, demonstrating their finite degrees of freedom and constructing a gauge-invariant cubic action coupling physical and topological higher spin fields.
\n\n
本文研究了四维高自旋理论中的拓扑场，证明其具有有限自由度，并构建了一个耦合物理与拓扑高自旋场的规范不变三次作用量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Topological fields in higher spin theories are poorly understood despite their potential role in consistent formulations of interacting higher spin systems. Clarifying their dynamical content (i.e., showing they carry finitely many degrees of freedom) and enabling their consistent interaction with physical higher spin fields via gauge-invariant actions is essential for advancing higher spin gravity and related holographic dualities.
\n\n
尽管拓扑场在高自旋理论中可能对构建自洽的相互作用体系至关重要，但目前对其理解仍不充分。明确其动力学内容（即证明其仅携带有限自由度），并构造出能使其与物理高自旋场通过规范不变作用量一致耦合的机制，对于推进高自旋引力及相关全息对偶理论至关重要。

Method: The authors analyze the field equations of topological sectors in $4d$ higher spin theory to count physical degrees of freedom. They then construct gauge-invariant functionals by leveraging the unfolded formalism and BRST-like techniques common in higher spin theories, ultimately deriving an explicit cubic vertex that couples physical and topological higher spin fields while preserving gauge invariance.
\n\n
作者通过分析四维高自旋理论中拓扑扇区的场方程来计算其物理自由度数目。随后，他们利用高自旋理论中常用的展开形式（unfolded formalism）和类BRST技术，构造规范不变泛函，并最终导出一个显式的三次顶点，该顶点在保持规范不变性的同时耦合了物理与拓扑高自旋场。

Result: The topological higher spin fields are shown to possess only a finite number of local degrees of freedom, justifying their "topological" designation. A fully gauge-invariant cubic action involving both physical and topological higher spin fields is explicitly constructed, providing a consistent interaction term within the higher spin framework.
\n\n
拓扑高自旋场被证明仅具有有限数目的局域自由度，从而验证了其“拓扑”命名的合理性。作者显式构建了一个包含物理与拓扑高自旋场的完全规范不变三次作用量，为高自旋框架内提供了一致的相互作用项。

Conclusion: This work establishes that topological fields in $4d$ higher spin theory are non-dynamical in the conventional sense but still admit consistent interactions with physical fields through gauge-invariant vertices. This opens avenues for incorporating topological sectors into complete higher spin theories and their holographic duals.
\n\n
本工作表明，四维高自旋理论中的拓扑场在常规意义上是非动力学的，但仍可通过规范不变顶点与物理场发生一致的相互作用。这为将拓扑扇区纳入完整的高自旋理论及其全息对偶体系开辟了新路径。

Abstract: The equations for topological fields in the $4d$ higher spin theory are considered. It is shown that these fields contain a finite number of degrees of freedom that justifies their naming. The issue of construction of gauge invariant functionals is addressed, and a gauge-invariant cubic action is constructed for the interacting physical and topological higher spin fields.

### [75] [Effects of fermions in one-loop propagators in the Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo-Jarvis gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08460)
*Santiago Cabrera,Marcela Peláez,Matthieu Tissier*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes the one-loop quark propagator in the Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo-Jarvis (CFDJ) gauge with dynamical quarks, showing that the coupling, gluon mass, and gauge parameter freeze in the infrared, supporting the framework's infrared safety. The quark dressing function Z(p) exhibits distinct concavity behavior for finite gauge parameters compared to Landau gauge, potentially aligning better with lattice data.
\n\n
本文在包含动力学夸克的情况下，计算了Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo-Jarvis（CFDJ）规范下的一圈夸克传播子，表明耦合常数、胶子质量与规范参数在红外区冻结，支持该框架的红外安全性。夸克波函数重整化因子$Z(p)$在有限规范参数下相比Landau规范展现出不同的凹凸性，可能更符合格点数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous studies of the Curci-Ferrari model focused on the pure Yang-Mills sector or used the Landau gauge; this work aims to extend the analysis to include dynamical quarks and finite gauge-fixing parameters in the CFDJ gauge to assess its viability as an infrared-safe perturbative framework for QCD with a massive gluon.
\n\n
先前对Curci-Ferrari模型的研究主要集中在纯Yang-Mills部分或使用Landau规范；本文旨在将分析扩展至包含动力学夸克并在CFDJ规范中引入有限规范固定参数，以评估其作为具有质量胶子的QCD红外安全微扰框架的可行性。

Method: The authors perform a one-loop calculation of the quark propagator within the CFDJ gauge using an infrared-safe renormalization scheme. They analyze the renormalization group flow of the strong coupling $g$, the gluon mass $m$, and the gauge parameter $\\xi$, and compute the quark dressing function $Z(p)$ for both Landau ($\\xi = 0$) and finite-$\\xi$ gauges.
\n\n
作者在CFDJ规范下采用红外安全的重整化方案，对夸克传播子进行一圈计算。他们分析了强耦合$g$、胶子质量$m$和规范参数$\\xi$的重整化群流，并计算了Landau规范（$\\xi = 0$）与有限$\\xi$规范下的夸克波函数重整化因子$Z(p)$。

Result: The coupling, gluon mass, and gauge parameter all freeze below a finite energy scale, confirming infrared stability. The quark dressing function $Z(p)$ changes concavity when moving from Landau to finite-$\\xi$ gauges, suggesting improved agreement with lattice QCD results in nonvanishing gauges.
\n\n
耦合常数、胶子质量和规范参数均在某一有限能标以下冻结，证实了红外稳定性。当从Landau规范过渡到有限$\\xi$规范时，夸克波函数重整化因子$Z(p)$的凹凸性发生变化，表明非零规范参数下可能与格点QCD结果有更好的一致性。

Conclusion: The CFDJ gauge with dynamical quarks provides a consistent infrared-safe perturbative framework for QCD with a massive gluon. If validated by lattice simulations, it could serve as a foundation for future nonperturbative studies of the quark-gluon vertex and related Green’s functions.
\n\n
包含动力学夸克的CFDJ规范为具有质量胶子的QCD提供了一个自洽的红外安全微扰框架。若经格点模拟验证，该框架可作为未来对夸克-胶子顶点及相关Green函数进行非微扰研究的基础。

Abstract: We present the one-loop computation of the quark propagator in the Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo- Jarvis (CFDJ) gauge, extending previous analyses to include dynamical quarks. Using the infrared- safe renormalization scheme, we study how finite gauge parameters affect the infrared behavior of QCD correlation functions. The coupling, gluon mass, and gauge parameter are found to freeze below a finite energy scale, confirming the infrared stability of the framework. The quark dressing function Z(p) shows a change in concavity between the Landau and finite-ξ cases, suggesting that nonvanishing gauges may better reproduce lattice trends. These results establish the CFDJ gauge as a possible infrared-safe setting candidate for perturbative QCD with massive gluons. In the case of a consistency check from lattice calculations, it could provide a basis for future studies of the quark-gluon vertex and related observables.

### [76] [Gravitational formulation of stress-tensor deformed field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08481)
*Yunfei Xie,Yun-Ze Li,Lixin Xu,Song He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores stress-tensor deformations in quantum field theory (QFT) coupled to Einstein gravity, showing that while such deformations are non-local in $d>2$, they become local when expressed on the deformed saddle-point metric. It constructs completions using Palatini $f(R)$ gravity and an eigenvalue method for Ricci-based theories, and applies them to various deformations including generalized Nambu-Goto, $\det T$, ModMax, Born-Infeld, and root-$T\bar T$ flows. In free theories, quantum corrections generate an Einstein-Hilbert term with controlled higher derivatives.
\n\n
本文研究了耦合爱因斯坦引力的量子场论（QFT）中的应力张量形变，表明尽管在 $d>2$ 时这些形变是非局域的，但当用形变后的鞍点度规表达时，其流变为局域。文章通过Palatini $f(R)$ 引力和基于Ricci理论的本征值方法构建了两种完备化方案，并将其应用于广义Nambu-Goto、$\det T$、ModMax、Born-Infeld以及root-$T\bar T$ 形变等模型。在自由场论中，量子修正生成了具有受控高阶导数项的Einstein-Hilbert项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stress-tensor deformations like $T\bar{T}$ offer insights into emergent gravity and holography but are generally non-local in dimensions $d>2$, limiting their geometric interpretation. The authors aim to understand how coupling a seed QFT to dynamical gravity can restore locality and provide a geometric framework for such deformations, especially beyond two dimensions.
\n\n
应力张量形变（如 $T\bar{T}$）为涌现引力和全息对偶提供了深刻见解，但在 $d>2$ 维中通常是非局域的，限制了其几何诠释。作者旨在探究将种子QFT与动力学引力耦合如何恢复局域性，并为这类形变（尤其在二维以上）提供几何框架。

Method: The authors couple a seed QFT to Einstein gravity with deformation parameter $\\lambda$ and evaluate the gravitational path integral at the metric saddle point. They expand around a fixed reference background to isolate the leading bilocal stress-tensor deformation governed by the graviton Green's function. Locality is recovered by re-expressing the flow on the deformed saddle-point metric. Two constructive completions are then developed: (1) Palatini $f(R)$ gravity and (2) an eigenvalue method for general Ricci-based gravity theories. These are applied to specific deformations: scalar generalized Nambu-Goto, $\\det T$, 2D multi-scalar ModMax/Born-Infeld, and 4D root-$T\\bar{T}$/$T\\bar{T}$ flows of Maxwell theory. An off-shell quantum analysis in free field theory computes leading corrections.
\n\n
作者将种子QFT与含形变参数 $\\lambda$ 的爱因斯坦引力耦合，并在度规鞍点处计算引力路径积分。围绕固定参考背景展开，分离出由引力子Green函数决定的主导双局域应力张量形变项。通过在形变后的鞍点度规上重写流，恢复局域性。随后构建两种完备化方法：(1) Palatini $f(R)$ 引力；(2) 针对一般Ricci型引力理论的本征值方法。这些方法被应用于特定形变：标量广义Nambu-Goto、$\\det T$、二维多标量ModMax/Born-Infeld模型，以及四维Maxwell理论的root-$T\\bar{T}$/$T\\bar{T}$ 流。在自由场论中，通过壳外量子分析计算主导修正。

Result: The leading deformation is universally bilocal in the stress tensor with kernel given by the graviton propagator, but becomes local on the deformed metric. Constructive completions yield known nonlinear electrodynamics (ModMax, Born-Infeld) from $T\\bar{T}$-like flows in 2D and 4D. In free theories, quantum corrections generate an Einstein-Hilbert term with higher-derivative corrections under control.
\n\n
主导形变在应力张量中表现为普适的双局域形式，其核由引力子传播子给出，但在形变度规上变为局域。所构建的完备化方案从2D和4D中的 $T\\bar{T}$ 类流成功导出已知的非线性电动力学（ModMax、Born-Infeld）。在自由场论中，量子修正生成Einstein-Hilbert项，并伴随受控的高阶导数修正。

Conclusion: Stress-tensor deformations coupled to dynamical gravity admit a geometric interpretation via saddle-point metrics, restoring locality in $d>2$. The framework unifies various nonlinear field theories through gravitational completions and reveals how quantum effects in free theories naturally induce gravitational dynamics, suggesting a pathway toward emergent gravity from QFT deformations.
\n\n
与动力学引力耦合的应力张量形变可通过鞍点度规获得几何诠释，在 $d>2$ 中恢复局域性。该框架通过引力完备化统一了多种非线性场论，并揭示了自由场论中的量子效应如何自然诱导引力动力学，为从QFT形变中实现涌现引力提供了新路径。

Abstract: Stress-tensor deformations suggest a geometric origin of emergent gravity but are typically non-local for $d>2$. We couple a seed QFT to Einstein gravity with deformation parameter $λ$ and evaluate the gravitational path integral at the metric saddle. Around a fixed reference background, the leading deformation is universal: a bilocal term quadratic in the stress tensor with kernel set by the graviton Green's function, plus a systematic higher-order expansion. Expressed on the saddle-point (deformed) metric, the flow becomes local. We then provide two constructive completions on deformed backgrounds--Palatini $f(R)$ gravity and an eigenvalue method for general Ricci-based theories--and apply them to scalar generalized Nambu-Goto and $\det T$ deformations (arbitrary $d$), two-dimensional multi-scalar ModMax and Born-Infeld models, and four-dimensional root-$T\bar T$ and $T\bar T$ flows of Maxwell theory yielding ModMax and Born-Infeld electrodynamics. In free field theory, an off-shell analysis further shows that the leading quantum correction generates an Einstein-Hilbert term with controlled higher-derivative terms.

</details>


### [77] [Parity-dependent Casimir forces and Hall currents for a confined Dirac field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08601)
*Aitor Fernández,César D. Fosco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates the Casimir effect for a massless Dirac field confined between two parallel thin walls in $d+1$ dimensions under even (symmetric) and odd (antisymmetric) boundary conditions with respect to reflection about the midplane. The symmetric configuration yields an attractive Casimir force, while the antisymmetric one produces repulsion, consistent with a parity-based theorem for fermionic Casimir effects. Additionally, the authors examine parity-sensitive vacuum fluctuation phenomena: correlations between wall-localized currents and the induced bulk current in an external electric field, revealing a symmetry-inherited transverse (Hall-like) current in $2+1$ dimensions.
\n\n
本文研究了在$d+1$维时空中，受限于两平行薄壁之间的无质量Dirac场在关于中平面反射对称（偶）和反对称（奇）边界条件下的Casimir效应。对称构型产生吸引性的Casimir力，而反对称构型则导致排斥力，这与将宇称与费米子Casimir效应符号关联的普适定理一致。此外，作者还考察了两种对宇称敏感的真空涨落现象：局域在壁上的电流之间的关联，以及外加电场下诱导的体电流；特别地，在$2+1$维情形下，发现了一种横向（类Hall）诱导电流，其空间分布继承了限制势的对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how discrete symmetries—particularly parity under reflection about the midplane—affect quantum vacuum phenomena in fermionic systems. While the scalar Casimir effect is well-studied, the fermionic case exhibits richer structure due to spinor boundary conditions and their connection to parity. The authors aim to test a general theorem linking the sign of the fermionic Casimir force to the parity of the field configuration and extend the analysis to related vacuum fluctuation observables that also encode parity information.
\n\n
动机源于理解离散对称性——特别是关于中平面反射的宇称——如何影响费米子系统中的量子真空现象。尽管标量Casimir效应已被广泛研究，但费米子情形由于旋量边界条件及其与宇称的联系而展现出更丰富的结构。作者旨在验证一个将费米子Casimir力符号与场构型宇称关联的普适定理，并将分析拓展至其他同样编码宇称信息的真空涨落可观测量。

Method: The authors consider a massless Dirac field in $d+1$-dimensional spacetime confined between two parallel thin walls. They impose two distinct boundary conditions corresponding to even and odd parity under reflection about the midplane. Using mode summation or Green’s function techniques (implied by standard Casimir calculations), they compute the Casimir energy and force. They then analyze vacuum current-current correlations localized on the walls and calculate the induced bulk current in the presence of a static external electric field, particularly focusing on the $2+1$-dimensional case where topological responses like the Hall effect may emerge.
\n\n
作者考虑$d+1$维时空中的无质量Dirac场，被限制在两平行薄壁之间。他们施加了两类边界条件，分别对应于关于中平面反射的偶宇称和奇宇称。通过模态求和或Green函数方法（标准Casimir计算所采用），计算Casimir能量与力。随后，他们分析局域在壁上的真空电流-电流关联，并计算在外加静态电场下诱导的体电流，特别聚焦于可能出现类Hall拓扑响应的$2+1$维情形。

Result: The key results are: (1) The even-parity boundary condition leads to an attractive Casimir force, while the odd-parity condition yields a repulsive force, confirming the parity-sign theorem for fermionic Casimir effects. (2) The correlation function between currents on the two walls depends sensitively on the parity of the configuration. (3) In $2+1$ dimensions, an external electric field induces a transverse (Hall-like) bulk current whose spatial profile mirrors the symmetry (even or odd) of the confining boundary conditions.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 偶宇称边界条件导致吸引性Casimir力，而奇宇称条件产生排斥力，验证了费米子Casimir效应中宇称与力符号关联的定理；(2) 两壁上电流之间的关联函数对构型宇称高度敏感；(3) 在$2+1$维中，外加电场会诱导出横向（类Hall）体电流，其空间分布镜像反映了限制边界条件的对称性（偶或奇）。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that parity plays a decisive role in determining the nature of the fermionic Casimir force and related vacuum fluctuation phenomena. The sign of the force, current correlations, and the symmetry of induced currents are all governed by the reflection parity of the boundary conditions. This underscores the profound influence of boundary-induced symmetry breaking on quantum vacuum structure in fermionic systems, with potential implications for topological materials and quantum field theory in confined geometries.
\n\n
本研究表明，宇称在决定费米子Casimir力及相关真空涨落现象的性质中起着决定性作用。力的符号、电流关联以及诱导电流的对称性均由边界条件的反射宇称所支配。这凸显了边界诱导的对称性破缺对费米子系统中量子真空结构的深刻影响，对拓扑材料和受限几何中的量子场论具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We study a massless Dirac field subjected to two alternative boundary conditions on two parallel thin walls, in d + 1 dimensions. The two configurations correspond to the system being even or odd under reflection about the midplane between the two walls, and lead to qualitatively different behaviors. The even (symmetric) configuration produces an attractive Casimir force, whereas the odd (antisymmetric) one yields repulsion, in agreement with a general theorem linking parity to the sign of the fermionic Casimir effect. We complement this result by studying two phenomena associated with the vacuum fluctuations responsible for the Casimir interaction, both of which are also sensitive to parity: the correlation between currents concentrated on the walls, and the induced bulk current under the influence of an external electric field. For the latter we show that, in 2 + 1 dimensions, an induced transverse (Hall-like) current arises, whose spatial profile inherits the symmetry of the confining potential.

</details>


### [78] [Cluster Bootstrap for Cosmological Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08670)
*Shruti Paranjape,Marcos Skowronek,Marcus Spradlin,Anastasia Volovich,He-Chen Weng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that cosmological wavefunction coefficients for $n$-site chain and loop graphs in a cubic scalar theory in de Sitter spacetime are governed by symbol alphabets drawn from $A_{2n{-}2}$ and $B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster algebras, respectively, and obey corresponding cluster adjacency properties. This is established via a combinatorial correspondence between graph tubings and polygon triangulations. The result extends to general power-law FRW cosmologies in the $ε$ expansion and enables a bootstrap determination of de Sitter symbols for $n \leq 4$.
\n\n
本文证明了在de Sitter时空中，立方标量理论的$n$-点链图和圈图所对应的宇宙学波函数系数的symbol alphabet分别由$A_{2n{-}2}$和$B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster变量的子集给出，并满足相应的cluster adjacency性质。这一结论的关键在于建立了图“tubing”与多边形“triangulation”之间的精确组合对应关系。该结果可推广至一般幂律FRW宇宙学的$ε$展开中，并作为bootstrap输入唯一确定了$n \leq 4$时的de Sitter symbol。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the recent application of cluster algebra structures—originally developed in mathematics and particle physics—to cosmological observables. Understanding whether cosmological wavefunction coefficients exhibit cluster-algebraic properties like symbol alphabets and adjacency could reveal hidden mathematical structures and provide powerful non-perturbative constraints for the Cosmological Bootstrap program.
\n\n
动机源于近期将cluster代数结构（最初发展于数学和粒子物理）应用于宇宙学观测量的研究。探究宇宙学波函数系数是否展现出如symbol alphabet和adjacency等cluster代数性质，可能揭示隐藏的数学结构，并为Cosmological Bootstrap计划提供强有力的非微扰约束。

Method: The authors establish a precise bijection between graph tubings appearing in the kinematic flow equation for wavefunction coefficients and triangulations of polygons encoding compatibility in cluster algebras of type $A$ and $B$. This combinatorial identification allows them to map the analytic structure of cosmological correlators onto known cluster algebra frameworks. They then use these cluster adjacency constraints as input for the Cosmological Bootstrap to fix symbols for low-point ($n \leq 4$) wavefunction coefficients using physical requirements such as locality, unitarity, and regularity in the soft limit.
\n\n
作者建立了出现在波函数系数kinematic flow方程中的图“tubing”与编码$A$型和$B$型cluster代数相容性的多边形“triangulation”之间的精确双射。这一组合对应使得他们能将宇宙学关联函数的解析结构映射到已知的cluster代数框架上。随后，他们将这些cluster adjacency约束作为Cosmological Bootstrap的输入，结合局域性、幺正性和软极限下的正则性等物理要求，唯一确定低点（$n \leq 4$）波函数系数的symbol。

Result: The main results are: (1) $n$-site chain graphs correspond to symbol alphabets in $A_{2n{-}2}$ cluster variables with associated adjacency; (2) loop graphs correspond to $B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster variables with analogous properties; (3) these structures persist to all orders in the $ε$ expansion for general power-law FRW backgrounds; and (4) for $n \leq 4$, the de Sitter wavefunction symbols are uniquely fixed by physical principles combined with cluster adjacency.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) $n$-点链图对应于$A_{2n{-}2}$ cluster变量中的symbol alphabet并满足相应adjacency；(2) 圈图对应于$B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster变量并具有类似性质；(3) 这些结构在一般幂律FRW背景下的$ε$展开中对所有阶都成立；(4) 对于$n \leq 4$，de Sitter波函数的symbol可由物理原理与cluster adjacency共同唯一确定。

Conclusion: This work establishes a deep connection between the combinatorics of cosmological perturbation theory and cluster algebras, extending the reach of algebraic structures seen in scattering amplitudes to cosmological wavefunctions. The cluster adjacency property provides a powerful new constraint for the Cosmological Bootstrap, enabling exact determination of low-point correlators without explicit diagrammatic computation.
\n\n
本工作建立了宇宙学微扰论组合结构与cluster代数之间的深刻联系，将散射振幅中出现的代数结构推广至宇宙学波函数。cluster adjacency性质为Cosmological Bootstrap提供了强有力的新约束，使得无需显式费曼图计算即可精确确定低点关联函数。

Abstract: We show that cosmological wavefunction coefficients associated with $n$-site chain and loop graphs for a cubic scalar theory in de Sitter spacetime have symbol alphabets given by subsets of $A_{2n{-}2}$ and $B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster variables, respectively, and satisfy the associated cluster adjacency properties. The key step in proving this is identifying a precise connection between graph "tubings" that appear in the kinematic flow equation and polygon "triangulations" that encode the combinatorics of cluster compatibility. Our results imply that cosmological wavefunction coefficients in a general power-law FRW cosmology satisfy cluster adjacency to all orders in the $ε$ expansion. We use this information as bootstrap input to show that de Sitter symbols for $n \leq 4$ are uniquely determined by simple physical constraints.

</details>


### [79] [A proof of conservation laws in gravitational scattering: tails and breaking of peeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08705)
*Geoffrey Compère,Sébastien Robert*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes a refined definition of asymptotically flat spacetimes that aligns with physical expectations at null infinity and gravitational scattering. It establishes three antipodal matching conditions at spatial infinity relating the dual mass aspect, shear tail, and peeling behavior, and recasts them as asymptotic conservation laws on the boundary hyperboloid.
\n\n
本文提出了一种与类光无穷远（null infinity）和引力散射物理性质一致的渐近平直时空定义。作者在空间无穷远处建立了三个对极匹配条件（antipodal matching conditions），分别涉及对偶质量矩（dual mass aspect）、剪切尾部（shear tail）的主导项，以及类时与类光无穷远处剥落性质（peeling properties）与空间无穷远处量之间的非平凡关联，并将这些恒等式重新表述为定义在边界双曲面（boundary hyperboloid）上的渐近守恒律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing definitions of asymptotically flat spacetimes often fail to simultaneously satisfy consistency with both future/past null infinities ($\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$) and spatial infinity ($i^0$), particularly in capturing the correct behavior of gravitational radiation and matter interactions. The authors aim to resolve this tension by constructing a framework that respects known scattering properties and ensures smooth matching between asymptotic regions.
\n\n
现有的渐近平直时空定义通常难以同时满足与未来/过去类光无穷远（$\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$）和空间无穷远（$i^0$）的一致性，尤其在描述引力辐射和物质相互作用的正确行为方面存在不足。作者旨在通过构建一个尊重已知散射性质并确保不同渐近区域之间光滑匹配的框架来解决这一矛盾。

Method: The authors introduce a new definition of asymptotically flat spacetimes based on controlled fall-off and regularity conditions near spatial infinity, compatible with the Bondi–Sachs formalism at null infinity. They analyze the asymptotic structure using a hyperboloidal foliation approaching $i^0$, and derive matching conditions by comparing expansions of geometric quantities (e.g., shear and mass aspect) from $\\mathscr{I}^+$ and $\\mathscr{I}^-$ in the limit toward $i^0$. These are then expressed as conservation laws on the unit hyperboloid $\\mathbb{H}^3$ that forms the boundary at spatial infinity.
\n\n
作者基于在空间无穷远处受控的衰减与正则性条件，提出了一种新的渐近平直时空定义，该定义与类光无穷远处的Bondi–Sachs形式相容。他们采用双曲面叶状结构（hyperboloidal foliation）逼近 $i^0$，并通过比较从 $\\mathscr{I}^+$ 和 $\\mathscr{I}^-$ 出发、在趋近 $i^0$ 极限下几何量（如剪切和质量矩）的展开式，推导出匹配条件。这些条件随后被表述为定义在作为空间无穷远边界的单位双曲面 $\\mathbb{H}^3$ 上的守恒律。

Result: Three precise antipodal matching conditions are derived: (1) the dual mass aspect at $\\mathscr{I}^+$ equals the antipodal dual mass aspect at $\\mathscr{I}^-$; (2) the leading tail of the shear satisfies an analogous antipodal relation; and (3) a non-trivial identity linking the peeling behaviors at $\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$ to the leading asymptotic data at $i^0$. These are reformulated as conserved charges on $\\mathbb{H}^3$, providing a unified description of asymptotic symmetries and memory effects.
\n\n
作者推导出三个精确的对极匹配条件：(1) $\\mathscr{I}^+$ 处的对偶质量矩等于 $\\mathscr{I}^-$ 处对极点的对偶质量矩；(2) 剪切的主导尾部满足类似的对极关系；(3) 一个非平凡恒等式，将 $\\mathscr{I}^\\pm$ 处的剥落行为与 $i^0$ 处的主导渐近数据联系起来。这些条件被重新表述为 $\\mathbb{H}^3$ 上的守恒荷，为渐近对称性和记忆效应提供了统一描述。

Conclusion: The work provides a consistent and physically motivated framework for asymptotically flat spacetimes that bridges null and spatial infinities. The derived antipodal matching conditions and their interpretation as conservation laws deepen the understanding of infrared structures in gravity, with implications for soft theorems, memory effects, and the holographic description of asymptotically flat spacetimes.
\n\n
本工作提供了一个自洽且物理动机明确的渐近平直时空框架，成功连接了类光无穷远与空间无穷远。所导出的对极匹配条件及其作为守恒律的诠释，深化了对引力红外结构的理解，对软定理（soft theorems）、记忆效应（memory effects）以及渐近平直时空的全息描述具有重要意义。

Abstract: We propose a definition of asymptotically flat spacetimes that is consistent with both null infinities and compatible with known properties of gravitational scattering, incoming and outgoing radiation, and interactions with matter. For this class of spacetimes, we prove three antipodal matching conditions at spatial infinity: one for the so-called dual mass aspect, one for the leading tail of the shear, and one that non-trivially relates the peeling properties of the spacetime at past and null infinities to the leading tail and mass aspect at spatial infinity. Furthermore, we reformulate these identities as asymptotic conservation laws defined on the boundary hyperboloid at spatial infinity.

### [80] [The Cluster Evolutionary Reference Ensemble at Low-$z$ (CEREAL) Sample of Galaxy Clusters I: X-ray Morphological Properties and Demographics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06785)
*Laurel White,Michael McDonald,Steven W. Allen,Marshall W. Bautz,Michael Calzadilla,Gordon P. Garmire,Julie Hlavacek-Larrondo,Ralph Kraft,Adam B. Mantz,Taweewat Somboonpanyakul,Alexey Vikhlinin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper introduces the CEREAL sample—a low-redshift (z~0.15) ensemble of 169 galaxy clusters selected from the Planck SZ catalog and observed with Chandra—to provide an unbiased reference for studying high-redshift cluster evolution. The sample shows a higher fraction of non-cool core systems compared to X-ray-selected samples, with cool core fractions of 39% and strong cool core fractions of 13%, and no mass dependence in dynamical state or cool core presence.
\n\n
本文介绍了CEREAL样本——一个由Planck SZ星表选出、经Chandra观测的169个低红移（$z\\sim0.15$）星系团集合，旨在为高红移星系团演化研究提供无偏参考。该样本相比X射线选样显示出更高比例的非冷核系统，冷核比例为39%，强冷核比例为13%，且动力学状态或冷核存在性无质量依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Evolutionary studies of galaxy clusters at $z\gtrsim2$ require reliable low-redshift comparison samples. However, most existing low-z samples are X-ray selected, which biases them toward relaxed, cool core systems and hinders accurate evolutionary inference. To address this selection bias, the authors construct a new low-redshift reference sample with a well-understood selection function based on the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) effect.
\n\n
对红移$z\\gtrsim2$星系团的演化研究需要可靠的低红移对比样本。然而，现有大多数低红移样本是X射线选样的，这使其偏向于弛豫态和冷核系统，从而阻碍了准确的演化推断。为解决这一选择效应偏差，作者基于Sunyaev-Zel'dovich（SZ）效应构建了一个具有清晰选择函数的新低红移参考样本。

Method: The authors construct the CEREAL sample by selecting 169 galaxy clusters from the Planck SZ catalog and obtaining uniform, high-resolution Chandra X-ray follow-up. They use X-ray surface brightness concentration ($c_\\mathrm{SB}$) as a proxy for cool core strength and centroid shift ($w$) to quantify dynamical relaxation. Statistical analysis is performed to determine fractions of cool core, strong cool core, and relaxed systems, and to test for mass dependence and the incidence of bright central X-ray point sources.
\n\n
作者从Planck SZ星表中选取169个星系团，通过统一、高分辨率的Chandra X射线后续观测构建CEREAL样本。他们使用X射线表面亮度集中度（$c_\\mathrm{SB}$）作为冷核强度的代理量，并用质心偏移（$w$）量化动力学弛豫程度。通过统计分析确定冷核、强冷核及弛豫系统的比例，检验其是否具有质量依赖性，并评估明亮中心X射线点源的发生率。

Result: The CEREAL sample exhibits a cool core fraction of $0.39_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$, a strong cool core fraction of $0.13_{-0.03}^{+0.03}$, and a dynamically relaxed fraction of $0.42_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$. These values indicate significantly more non-cool core systems than in traditional X-ray-selected samples. No mass dependence is found in cool core or relaxed fractions. Bright central X-ray point sources ($L_\\mathrm{nuc,~2-10~keV} > 10^{43}$ erg s$^{-1}$) are rare (0.7% of massive low-z clusters) but occur more frequently in cool cores.
\n\n
CEREAL样本的冷核比例为$0.39_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$，强冷核比例为$0.13_{-0.03}^{+0.03}$，动力学弛豫比例为$0.42_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$。这些数值表明其非冷核系统显著多于传统X射线选样。冷核或弛豫比例未发现质量依赖性。明亮中心X射线点源（$L_\\mathrm{nuc,~2-10~keV} > 10^{43}$ erg s$^{-1}$）在大质量低红移星系团中很罕见（0.7%），但在冷核中心出现频率更高。

Conclusion: The CEREAL sample provides a minimally biased, SZ-selected low-redshift reference for evolutionary studies of galaxy clusters. Its properties—particularly the higher fraction of non-cool core systems and lack of mass dependence in dynamical state—highlight the limitations of X-ray-selected samples and underscore the need for SZ-based selection in future cluster cosmology and evolution studies.
\n\n
CEREAL样本为星系团演化研究提供了一个几乎无偏、基于SZ效应选择的低红移参考样本。其特性——尤其是更高的非冷核比例和动力学状态无质量依赖性——凸显了X射线选样的局限性，并强调未来星系团宇宙学与演化研究需采用SZ选样方法。

Abstract: With rapid improvements in the assembly of large samples of galaxy clusters, we are approaching the ability to study clusters at $z\gtrsim2$. Evolutionary studies comparing these distant clusters to the clusters in our local universe depend heavily on the reliability of low-redshift cluster samples, most of which are subject to X-ray selection effects, biasing them to relaxed, cool core clusters. Here, we introduce the Cluster Evolutionary Reference Ensemble At Low-$z$ (CEREAL) sample, composed of Chandra X-ray observations of 169 galaxy clusters that have been selected from the Planck Sunyaev-Zel'dovich catalog. CEREAL has a simple and well-understood selection function, spans an order of magnitude in mass at $z\sim0.15$, and has uniform, high-resolution X-ray follow-up. We present the full sample and provide results based on X-ray surface brightness properties, finding significantly more non-cool core systems than in X-ray-selected samples. We use surface brightness concentration (c$_\mathrm{SB}$) as a proxy for cool core strength and centroid shift ($w$) to measure dynamical state. Over the full sample, we find a cool core (c$_\mathrm{SB} > 0.075$) fraction of $0.39_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$, a strong cool core (c$_\mathrm{SB} > 0.155$) fraction of $0.13_{-0.03}^{+0.03}$, and a dynamically relaxed ($w<0.01$) fraction of $0.42_{-0.04}^{+0.04}$. We find no mass dependence in the fraction of clusters that appear relaxed or have cool cores. We quantify the rarity of X-ray-bright central point sources (L$_\mathrm{nuc,~2-10~keV} > 10^{43}$ erg s$^{-1}$), finding them to be intrinsically rare ($0.7_{-0.5}^{+1.2}$\% of massive, low-z clusters) with a notable increase in occurrence rate at the centers of cool cores.

### [81] [Signatures of Extended Dark Energy Parametrisations in Structure Formation under Background Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06805)
*Greco A. Peña,Mario H. Amante,Javier Chagoya,Cristian Barrera-Hinojosa,C. Ortiz,Graeme Candlish*

Abstract: We study structure formation in alternative cosmological models constrained by background observations, including $Λ$CDM, wCDM, the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder parametrisation and a flexible Chebyshev expansion of the dark energy equation of state. The models are constrained using baryon acoustic oscillations, cosmic microwave background, cosmic chronometers and strong lensing measurements. Using the best-fitting parameters, we generate cosmology-dependent initial conditions and perform N-body simulations to analyse the matter power spectrum, halo mass function and halo density profiles. Although all models remain broadly consistent with $Λ$CDM at the background level, differences in the physical matter density $Ω_{0m}h^2$ and in the expansion history $H(z)$ lead to distinct growth histories that are amplified by non-linear evolution. We find a clear hierarchy in the power spectrum amplitude and in $σ_8$, with the Chebyshev and CPL models exhibiting enhanced small-scale power, earlier halo formation at $z\gtrsim2$ and a migration of excess toward higher masses at late times. The wCDM model displays milder and partially compensating effects driven by its different expansion history. When expressed in terms of the scaled radius $r/R_{200c}$, halo density profiles show a high degree of universality across cosmologies, indicating that internal halo structure is largely governed by the same gravitational dynamics. These results demonstrate that even modest background-level variations in $w(z)$ can translate into coherent non-linear signatures, highlighting the constraining power of large-scale structure observables in extended dark energy models.

*BICEP/Keck Collaboration,:,P. A. R. Ade,Zeeshan Ahmed,Mandana Amiri,Denis Barkats,Ritoban Basu Thakur,Colin A. Bischoff,Dominic Beck,James J. Bock,Hans Boenish,Victor Buza,Brianna Cantrall,James R. Filippini,Antonio Fortes,Min Gao,Christos Giannakopoulos,Neil Goeckner-Wald,David C. Goldfinger,Stephen Gratton,James A. Grayson,Annsley Greathouse,Paul K. Grimes,Grantland Hall,George Halal,Mark Halpern,Emma Hand,Sam A. Harrison,Shawn Henderson,Thuong Hoang,Johannes Hubmayr,Howard Hui,Kent D. Irwin,Jae Hwan Kang,Kirit S. Karkare,Sinan Kefeli,J. M.
