Nguyen,Roger O'Brient,Scott Paine,Anika Patel,Matthew A. Petroff,Anna R. Polish,Thomas Prouve,Clement Pryke,Carl D. Reintsema,Steffen Richter,Thibault Romand,Maria Salatino,Alessandro Schillaci,Benjamin Schmitt,Robert Schwarz,Chris D. Sheehy,Baibhav Singari,Ahmed Soliman,Tyler St Germaine,Aaron Steiger,Bryan Steinbach,Rashmi Sudiwala,Grant Teply,Keith L. Thompson,Carole Tucker,Anthony D. Turner,Clara Vergès,Abigail G. Vieregg,Albert Wandui,Alexis C. Weber,Justin Willmert,Chin Lin Wong,Wai Ling K. Wu,Hung-I Yang,Cyndia Yu,Lingzhen Zeng,Cheng Zhang,Silvia Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper presents the first constraints on multipole-dependent cosmic birefringence using BICEP/Keck Array (BK18) CMB polarization data. The authors analyze photon coupling to an axion-like pseudoscalar field in an Early Dark Energy (EDE) model, which induces a scale-dependent rotation $\\beta(\\ell)$ of CMB polarization and generates non-zero EB correlations. Using a step-function parametrization for $\\beta(\\ell)$, they find no evidence for such rotation, with constraints $|\\Delta\\beta| < 0.15^\\circ$ (68% CL). They also constrain the axion-photon coupling strength $g$, obtaining $g = 0.11 \\pm 0.37$ (68% CL) for the best-fit EDE fraction $f_{\\rm EDE} = 0.087$.
\n\n
本文利用BICEP/Keck阵列（BK18）的CMB偏振数据，首次对多极依赖的宇宙双折射效应（cosmic birefringence）施加了限制。作者分析了Early Dark Energy（EDE）模型中光子与类轴子赝标量场的耦合，该耦合通过Chern-Simons相互作用导致CMB偏振发生尺度依赖的旋转$\\beta(\\ell)$，并产生非零的EB关联。采用$\\beta(\\ell)$的阶跃函数参数化，未发现显著信号，限制为$|\\Delta\\beta| < 0.15^\\circ$（68%置信度）。同时，对轴子-光子耦合强度$g$进行约束，在最佳拟合EDE占比$f_{\\rm EDE} = 0.087$下得到$g = 0.11 \\pm 0.37$（68%置信度）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmic birefringence—rotation of the plane of CMB polarization due to parity-violating interactions—offers a powerful probe of new physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly involving axion-like particles (ALPs). While isotropic birefringence has been previously constrained, a multipole-dependent rotation $\\beta(\\ell)$ can arise in specific early-universe scenarios such as Early Dark Energy (EDE) models where a pseudoscalar field couples to photons via a Chern-Simons term. Such a scale-dependent signal would leave unique imprints in CMB EB and TB cross-correlations, providing a novel observational window into parity violation and dark sector dynamics. This work aims to test these predictions using high-sensitivity, multi-frequency CMB polarization data from BK18.
\n\n
宇宙双折射——由宇称破坏相互作用引起的CMB偏振面旋转——是探测超出标准模型新物理（尤其是涉及axion-like particles, ALPs）的有力工具。虽然此前已有对各向同性双折射的限制，但在某些早期宇宙模型（如Early Dark Energy, EDE）中，赝标量场通过Chern-Simons项与光子耦合，可导致多极依赖的旋转$\\beta(\\ell)$。这种尺度依赖的信号会在CMB的EB和TB交叉关联中留下独特印记，为研究宇称破坏和暗区动力学提供新的观测窗口。本文旨在利用BK18高灵敏度、多频段CMB偏振数据检验这些理论预言。

Method: The analysis uses the BK18 CMB polarization dataset combining BICEP2, Keck Array, and BICEP3 observations at 95, 150, and 220 GHz. The authors construct a phenomenological model for the multipole-dependent birefringence angle $\\beta(\\ell)$ as a step function: $\\beta(\\ell) = \\beta_0$ for $\\ell < \\ell_{\\rm step}$ and zero otherwise. They compute the modified CMB polarization spectra incorporating this rotation, which mixes E and B modes and generates non-zero EB cross-spectra. Using the BICEP/Keck likelihood framework—which includes robust foreground modeling (e.g., dust and synchrotron) and multi-frequency cross-spectra (EE, BB, EB)—they perform a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis to constrain both the step amplitude $\\beta_0$ and the axion-photon coupling constant $g$ in the context of an EDE model with fixed $f_{\\rm EDE}$ values.
\n\n
该分析使用BK18 CMB偏振数据集，整合了BICEP2、Keck阵列和BICEP3在95、150和220 GHz的观测。作者构建了一个唯象模型，将多极依赖的双折射角$\\beta(\\ell)$参数化为阶跃函数：当$\\ell < \\ell_{\\rm step}$时$\\beta(\\ell) = \\beta_0$，否则为零。他们计算了包含此旋转修正后的CMB偏振谱，该旋转混合E模和B模并产生非零EB交叉谱。利用BICEP/Keck似然框架（包含稳健的前景建模，如尘埃和同步辐射，以及多频段交叉谱EE、BB、EB），通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法，同时约束阶跃幅度$\\beta_0$和在固定$f_{\\rm EDE}$值下的EDE模型中的轴子-光子耦合常数$g$。

Result: The analysis finds no statistically significant evidence for multipole-dependent cosmic birefringence. For the step-function model of $\\beta(\\ell)$, the constraint on the rotation amplitude is $\\beta_0 = -0.04^{+0.15}_{-0.14}$ degrees (68% CL), consistent with zero. For the EDE-motivated axion-photon coupling, assuming the Planck 2018 best-fit EDE fraction $f_{\\rm EDE} = 0.087$, the coupling strength is constrained to $g = 0.11 \\pm 0.37$ (68% CL). These results are consistent with previous isotropic birefringence limits and represent the first direct constraints on scale-dependent birefringence from CMB data.
\n\n
分析未发现多极依赖宇宙双折射的统计显著证据。对于$\\beta(\\ell)$的阶跃函数模型，旋转幅度的限制为$\\beta_0 = -0.04^{+0.15}_{-0.14}$度（68%置信度），与零一致。对于EDE模型驱动的轴子-光子耦合，在假设Planck 2018最佳拟合EDE占比$f_{\\rm EDE} = 0.087$的情况下，耦合强度被限制为$g = 0.11 \\pm 0.37$（68%置信度）。这些结果与此前各向同性双折射的限制一致，并代表了CMB数据对尺度依赖双折射的首次直接约束。

Conclusion: This work establishes the first observational limits on multipole-dependent cosmic birefringence using high-precision CMB polarization data. The null detection supports the standard cosmological model and places new constraints on parity-violating interactions involving axion-like fields in Early Dark Energy scenarios. The methodology developed—combining multi-frequency EB spectra with a flexible $\\beta(\\ell)$ parametrization—provides a template for future tests of fundamental symmetry violations with next-generation CMB experiments like CMB-S4 and LiteBIRD.
\n\n
本工作利用高精度CMB偏振数据，首次建立了对多极依赖宇宙双折射的观测限制。零结果支持标准宇宙学模型，并对Early Dark Energy场景中涉及类轴子场的宇称破坏相互作用施加了新约束。所发展的方法——结合多频段EB谱与灵活的$\\beta(\\ell)$参数化——为未来CMB-S4和LiteBIRD等下一代CMB实验检验基本对称性破缺提供了模板。

Abstract: We present the first constraints on multipole-dependent cosmic birefringence using CMB polarization data from the BK18 dataset, which combines observations from BICEP2, Keck Array, and BICEP3 at frequencies of 95, 150, and 220 GHz. Photon coupling to an axion-like field leads to the rotation of CMB polarization, inducing non-zero EB cross-correlations. We show that a multipole-dependent rotation beta(l) imprints a distinct signature in the polarization spectra that can be constrained. Specifically, we consider an Early Dark Energy (EDE) scenario in which a pseudoscalar field couples to photons through a Chern-Simons interaction, generating a polarization rotation with multipole dependence. We introduce a phenomenological beta(l) as a step function, obtaining constraints on the step function size consistent with zero, with uncertainties less than 0.15 degrees (68% CL). In addition, using multi-frequency EE, BB, and EB cross-spectra, along with robust BICEP/Keck foreground treatment and likelihood framework, we derive constraints on the axion-photon coupling amplitude g for several choices of EDE parameters. For the baseline best-fit value f_EDE = 0.087 from the Planck 2018 analysis, we obtain g = 0.11 +/- 0.37 (68% CL), consistent with previous limits.

</details>


### [83] [Empirical signatures of velocity and density cascades in the Local Universe probed by CosmicFlows4 dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06867)
*Yves Grosdidier,Hélène M. Courtois*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates the multiscale statistical properties of reconstructed cosmic velocity and density fields from CosmicFlows4 data out to $z \lesssim 0.08$, identifying two distinct scaling regimes, quantifying intermittency via Universal Multifractal formalism, and revealing strong non-Gaussianity and a possible transition toward large-scale homogeneity.
\n\n
本文研究了来自 CosmicFlows4 数据、红移范围至 $z \lesssim 0.08$ 的重构宇宙速度场与密度场的多尺度统计性质，识别出两个不同的标度律区域，利用 Universal Multifractal 形式量化间歇性，并揭示了强烈的非高斯性及向大尺度均匀性过渡的可能迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the nature of cosmic structure across scales—particularly whether scaling laws, intermittency, and homogeneity emerge in the observed nearby universe—and to test theoretical expectations from turbulence-inspired models of gravitational structure formation using high-quality observational reconstructions.
\n\n
动机在于理解宇宙结构在不同尺度上的本质——特别是观测到的近邻宇宙中是否出现标度律、间歇性与均匀性，并利用高质量的观测重构数据检验受湍流启发的引力结构形成模型的理论预期。

Method: The authors compute absolute structure functions of arbitrary order $q$ in configuration space from the CosmicFlows4 3D velocity and density-contrast fields within $\simeq 350~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$. They estimate scaling exponents $ζ(q)$, apply the Universal Multifractal formalism to characterize intermittency, and analyze probability density functions (PDFs) of field increments, including skewness and Lévy-stability.
\n\n
作者在约 $\simeq 350~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$ 范围内，从 CosmicFlows4 的三维速度场和密度对比场出发，在位形空间中计算任意阶 $q$ 的绝对结构函数，估计标度指数 $ζ(q)$，采用 Universal Multifractal 形式刻画间歇性，并分析场增量的概率密度函数（PDF），包括偏度与 Lévy 稳定性。

Result: Two scaling regimes are found: a small-scale regime dominated by reconstruction smoothing with nearly linear $ζ(q)$, and a larger-scale regime ($45–250~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$) exhibiting nonlinear $ζ(q)$, $ζ_ρ(1)\simeq0.3$ ($D_ρ\approx3.7$), $ζ_v(1)\simeq0.4$, and a correlation function $ξ(r)\sim r^{-1.4}$ implying $D_2\simeq1.6$. Increment PDFs are Lévy-stable and non-Gaussian; velocity increments show negative skewness, indicating asymmetric cascade dynamics favoring compressive flows.
\n\n
发现两个标度律区域：小尺度区域受重构平滑主导，$ζ(q)$ 几乎呈线性；大尺度区域（$45–250~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$）则表现出非线性的 $ζ(q)$，其中 $ζ_ρ(1)\simeq0.3$（对应 $D_ρ\approx3.7$）、$ζ_v(1)\simeq0.4$，相关函数满足 $ξ(r)\sim r^{-1.4}$，暗示 $D_2\simeq1.6$。增量 PDF 呈 Lévy 稳定且高度非高斯；速度增量呈现系统性负偏度，表明级联动力学具有不对称性，倾向于压缩性流动。

Conclusion: The observed non-linear scaling, multifractality, and non-Gaussian statistics support a turbulent-like, intermittent picture of cosmic structure formation on intermediate scales, while the emergence of power-law correlations over $[45,250]~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$ may signal the onset of large-scale homogeneity, consistent with the cosmological principle at sufficiently large scales.
\n\n
观测到的非线性标度律、多重分形性与非高斯统计支持在中间尺度上宇宙结构形成具有类似湍流的间歇性图像，而 $[45,250]~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$ 范围内幂律相关性的出现可能标志着大尺度均匀性的开端，与足够大尺度下的宇宙学原理一致。

Abstract: Aims: We aim to characterise the multiscale statistical properties of the reconstructed velocity and density fields of the nearby universe, identify possible scaling regimes, quantify intermittency, and assess indications for the transition toward large-scale homogeneity within the range probed by current data. Methods: We analyse the CosmicFlows4 three-dimensional velocity and density-contrast cubes using absolute structure functions of arbitrary order, $q$. The analysis is performed within a volume extending to $z \lesssim 0.08$ ($\simeq 350~\mathrm{Mpc}$ $h^{-1}$). Structure function scaling exponents $ζ(q)$ are estimated from configuration-space statistics. Intermittency is characterised using the Universal Multifractal formalism, and probability density functions of increments are examined. Results: Two regimes are detected. Small separations are dominated by reconstruction smoothing and show nearly linear $ζ(q)$ behaviour. At larger separations, a scaling regime appears with $ζ_ρ(1)\simeq0.3$ ($D_ρ\approx3.7$) and $ζ_v(1)\simeq0.4$. The correlation function follows $ξ(r)\sim r^{-1.4}$ over $[45,250]~\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$, implying $D_2\simeq1.6$. Non-linear $ζ(q)$ and Lévy-stable increment PDFs indicate intermittency and strong non-Gaussianity. Velocity increments show a systematic negative skewness suggestive of a cascade-like asymmetry associated to amplification of negative, compressive gradients.

### [84] [Estimating the completeness of the QUBRICS Survey with 3501 QSO redshifts from Gaia DR3 spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06907)
*Matteo Porru,Stefano Cristiani,Francesco Guarneri,Giorgio Calderone,Andrea Grazian,Konstantina Boutsia,Andrea Trost,Valentina D'Odorico,Guido Cupani,Catarina M. J. Marques,Francesco Chiti Tegli,Fabio Fontanot*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The QUBRICS survey has significantly expanded the sample of bright, high-redshift QSOs in the southern hemisphere. Using an independent Gaia DR3 QSO sample, the authors evaluate the completeness and recall of QUBRICS' machine-learning-based selection methods (XGB and PRF). They find high recall (89% for XGB, 66% for PRF) and estimate a spectroscopic completeness of 82%, which is crucial for robust cosmological analyses with QSOs. The study also provides new redshifts for 1223 QSOs to enhance future selection algorithms.
\n\n
QUBRICS巡天显著扩充了南天区明亮高红移QSO的样本。作者利用一个独立的Gaia DR3 QSO样本，评估了QUBRICS基于机器学习的选源方法（XGB和PRF）的完备性和召回率。他们发现其召回率很高（XGB为89%，PRF为66%），并估计光谱完备性为82%，这对于使用QSO进行稳健的宇宙学分析至关重要。该研究还为1223个新QSO提供了可靠的红移，以改进未来的选源算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to address the historical northern-hemisphere bias in QSO identification and to validate the statistical robustness of the QUBRICS survey's novel QSO selection pipeline. Since QSOs are fundamental tracers for cosmological studies (e.g., measuring Baryon Acoustic Oscillations or the growth of structure), an accurate quantification of the survey's completeness and recall is essential to avoid systematic biases in downstream analyses.
\n\n
主要动机是解决历史上QSO证认中的北天区偏向问题，并验证QUBRICS巡天新颖QSO选源流程的统计稳健性。由于QSO是宇宙学研究（例如测量重子声学振荡Baryon Acoustic Oscillations或结构增长）的基本示踪体，因此准确量化巡天的完备性和召回率对于避免下游分析中的系统性偏差至关重要。

Method: The authors use an independent sample of 3501 QSOs from Gaia DR3 with low-resolution spectra as a benchmark. They cross-match this sample with the input datasets used by QUBRICS' two machine learning classifiers: eXtreme Gradient Boosting (XGB) and Probabilistic Random Forest (PRF). By focusing on QSOs with $z>2.5$ that were unclassified in the original QUBRICS input data (i.e., not pre-identified as QSOs), they directly measure the recall (the fraction of true QSOs correctly identified as candidates) for each method. Completeness is then estimated based on the ratio of confirmed QSOs to the total expected population.
\n\n
作者使用一个包含3501个具有低分辨率光谱的Gaia DR3 QSO的独立样本作为基准。他们将此样本与QUBRICS使用的两种机器学习分类器——eXtreme Gradient Boosting (XGB)和Probabilistic Random Forest (PRF)——的输入数据集进行交叉匹配。通过聚焦于在原始QUBRICS输入数据中未被分类（即未被预先证认为QSO）且红移$z>2.5$的QSO，他们直接测量了每种方法的召回率（即被正确识别为候选体的真实QSO的比例）。然后，基于已证认QSO与总预期数量的比率来估计完备性。

Result: For the XGB method, 136 out of 152 ($89\\%$) unclassified, high-redshift QSOs in its footprint were correctly identified as candidates. For the PRF method, 46 out of 69 ($66\\%$) were correctly identified. Combining these results, the authors estimate a final spectroscopic completeness of $82\\%$ for the QUBRICS survey's high-redshift QSO sample. Additionally, they provide new, reliable redshifts for 1223 QSOs, with a median redshift of $z=2.1$ and median magnitude $G=17.8$.
\n\n
对于XGB方法，在其天区覆盖范围内，152个未被分类的高红移QSO中有136个（$89\\%$）被正确识别为候选体。对于PRF方法，69个中有46个（$66\\%$）被正确识别。综合这些结果，作者估计QUBRICS巡天高红移QSO样本的最终光谱完备性为$82\\%$。此外，他们还为1223个QSO提供了新的可靠红移，其中值红移为$z=2.1$，中值星等为$G=17.8$。

Conclusion: The QUBRICS survey's machine-learning-based selection methods, particularly XGB, demonstrate high efficiency and reliability in identifying high-redshift QSOs in the southern sky. The quantified completeness of 82% provides a solid foundation for using the QUBRICS QSO catalog in precision cosmological studies, ensuring that potential selection biases are well understood and accounted for. The new redshift data will further refine future QSO selection algorithms.
\n\n
QUBRICS巡天基于机器学习的选源方法，特别是XGB，在南天区证认高红移QSO方面表现出高效率和可靠性。所量化的82%完备性为在精确宇宙学研究中使用QUBRICS QSO星表奠定了坚实基础，确保潜在的选源偏差得到充分理解和校正。新的红移数据将进一步优化未来的QSO选源算法。

Abstract: QSOs are essential for investigating the structure and evolution of the Universe. Historically, their identification has been concentrated in the northern hemisphere, primarily due to the sky coverage of major astronomical surveys. The QUBRICS survey, started in 2019 to address this asymmetry, has identified more than 1300 new bright (i<19.5) high-redshift (2.5<z<6) QSOs in the southern sky. We aim to quantify, using an independent QSO sample, the completeness and recall of the QUBRICS QSO selection methods, based on XGB (eXtreme Gradient Boosting) and PRF (Probabilistic Random Forest), since completeness is a fundamental metric for ensuring the statistical robustness of QSO-based cosmological investigations. A subset of Gaia DR3 sources with low-resolution spectra was analyzed, obtaining a sample of 3501 QSOs. To determine how many QSOs were correctly identified as candidates, we crossmatched this independent sample with the datasets used for selection: 894 QSOs with z>2.5 fell within the XGB dataset footprint, of which 152 were unclassified and thus eligible for completeness testing. Similarly, 675 QSOs with z>2.5 were within the PRF dataset footprint, including 69 unclassified objects. The XGB correctly identified as candidates 136 (89%) of the 152 QSOs with z>2.5 present in its dataset as unclassified objects. The PRF correctly identified as candidates 46 (66%) of the 69 QSOs with z>2.5 present in its dataset as unclassified objects. These findings confirm the high efficiency of the QUBRICS selection methods (recall=89%) and provide the completeness estimate for spectroscopically confirmed QSOs (82%), necessary for cosmological studies using QUBRICS data. This work also provides reliable redshifts for 1223 new QSOs (median redshift z=2.1 and magnitude G=17.8), that will help improve the performance of future selections.

</details>


### [85] [The Impact of Dark Matter on Gravitational Wave Detection by Space-based Interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07158)
*Yuezhe Chen,Pan-Pan Wang,Bo Wang,Rui Luo,Cheng-Gang Shao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This review explores how gravitational wave (GW) observations—particularly with future space-based detectors like LISA—can probe dark matter through its influence on compact-object dynamics, gravitational lensing, and direct field couplings. These effects may reveal dark matter’s distribution and particle nature.
\n\n
本文综述了引力波（GW）观测——特别是未来空间探测器如LISA——如何通过暗物质对致密天体动力学、引力透镜效应以及场与探测器的直接耦合来探测暗物质。这些效应可能揭示暗物质的分布及其粒子性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While dark matter's existence is well-established observationally, its fundamental particle identity remains elusive. Gravitational wave astronomy, especially in the low-frequency regime accessible to space-based interferometers like LISA, opens a new observational window to test dark matter models through its macroscopic gravitational and potential non-gravitational interactions with GW sources and detectors.
\n\n
尽管暗物质的存在已被观测充分证实，但其基本粒子身份仍不清楚。引力波天文学，尤其是在LISA等空间干涉仪可探测的低频波段，为通过暗物质与引力波源及探测器之间的宏观引力（甚至可能的非引力）相互作用来检验暗物质模型开辟了新的观测窗口。

Method: The paper reviews three primary mechanisms by which dark matter can imprint signatures on gravitational wave signals: (1) dynamical effects on compact binaries—such as orbital modifications due to dark matter spikes, dynamical friction, and perturbations in extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs); (2) gravitational lensing by large-scale or clumpy dark matter distributions that alter waveform amplitude and phase; and (3) direct interactions between ultralight dark matter fields (e.g., axion-like particles) and the detector hardware or laser interferometry, potentially inducing oscillatory signals. The analysis synthesizes theoretical modeling, numerical simulations, and prospects for data analysis with future missions.
\n\n
本文综述了暗物质在引力波信号中留下印记的三种主要机制：(1) 对致密双星系统的动力学效应——例如由暗物质尖峰（dark matter spikes）、动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）和极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）中的扰动引起的轨道修正；(2) 由大尺度或团块状暗物质分布引起的引力透镜效应，改变波形的振幅和相位；(3) 超轻暗物质场（如类轴子粒子）与探测器硬件或激光干涉仪的直接相互作用，可能产生振荡信号。分析综合了理论建模、数值模拟以及未来任务的数据分析前景。

Result: The review demonstrates that current and upcoming gravitational wave observatories—especially LISA—can constrain dark matter properties such as its density profile around black holes, its clustering scale, and the mass-coupling parameters of ultralight fields. Specific observables include anomalous orbital decay rates in EMRIs, lensing-induced waveform distortions, and resonant detector responses to coherent dark matter fields.
\n\n
该综述表明，当前和未来的引力波天文台——尤其是LISA——可以限制暗物质的性质，例如黑洞周围的密度轮廓、成团尺度以及超轻场的质量-耦合参数。具体可观测量包括EMRIs中异常的轨道衰减速率、透镜引起的波形畸变，以及探测器对相干暗物质场的共振响应。

Conclusion: Gravitational wave astronomy provides a powerful and complementary probe of dark matter, bridging astrophysical structure and particle physics. With precise waveform modeling and multi-messenger strategies, future low-frequency GW observations could uncover both the macroscopic distribution and microscopic nature of dark matter.
\n\n
引力波天文学为暗物质提供了一种强大且互补的探针，连接了天体物理结构与粒子物理。通过精确的波形建模和多信使策略，未来的低频引力波观测有望揭示暗物质的宏观分布及其微观本质。

Abstract: The existence of dark matter is supported by multiple astrophysical observations, yet its particle nature remains unknown. The development of gravitational wave astronomy, especially with future space-based detectors such as LISA, provides new opportunities to study the interactions between dark matter and compact-object systems. This review summarizes the main dark matter candidates and their macroscopic distributions, and highlights three mechanisms through which dark matter can affect gravitational wave observations: (1) modifications to compact-object orbits and the dynamics of systems such as extreme mass-ratio inspirals, including dark matter spikes, dynamical friction, and potential perturbations; (2) gravitational lensing effects induced by the spatial distribution of dark matter, altering waveform amplitudes and phases; and (3) direct couplings between ultralight dark matter fields and detectors. As low-frequency gravitational wave detection techniques are proposed and continue to develop, these effects may offer a novel avenue for probing the properties of dark matter, and combining precise waveform modeling with multi-messenger observations could reveal insights into its microscopic structure.

</details>


### [86] [Study of the cosmological tensions and DESI-DR2 in the framework of the Little Rip model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07398)
*Safae Dahmani,Imad El Bojaddaini,Amine Bouali,Ahmed Errahmani,Taoufik Ouali*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates the $H_0$ and $S_8$ tensions using a Little Rip (LR) dark energy model, which extends $\\Lambda$CDM with an additional parameter $\\beta$. The authors perform MCMC statistical analysis with modern datasets (CMB, BAO, PantheonPlus, DESI-DR2, SNIa). They find a positive correlation between $H_0$ and $\\beta$, partial alleviation of the Hubble tension (<3σ) when using only early-universe data (CMB+BAO), but not when including late-time probes like PantheonPlus. Bayesian evidence shows the LR model is preferred only for CMB data alone, and the best-fit region shifts toward quintessence-like behavior when including DESI-DR2.
\n\n
本文通过引入一个带有额外参数 $\\beta$ 的 Little Rip（LR）暗能量模型来研究 $H_0$ 和 $S_8$ 张力问题。作者利用 MCMC 方法结合现代观测数据（CMB、BAO、PantheonPlus、DESI-DR2、SNIa）进行统计分析。结果发现 $H_0$ 与 $\\beta$ 呈正相关；仅使用早期宇宙数据（CMB+BAO）时，哈勃张力可缓解至小于 $3\\sigma$，但加入晚期探针（如 PantheonPlus）后则不再缓解。贝叶斯证据表明，LR 模型仅在单独拟合 CMB 数据时优于 $\\Lambda$CDM，且在包含 DESI-DR2 数据时最佳拟合区域趋向于 quintessence 场行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the persistent cosmological tensions—specifically the $H_0$ tension (discrepancy in the Hubble constant between early- and late-universe measurements) and the $S_8$ tension (disagreement in matter clustering amplitude)—which challenge the standard $\\Lambda$CDM model. The authors explore whether a late-time dark energy model featuring a future singularity (the Little Rip) can alleviate these tensions without invoking early-universe physics, by introducing a minimal extension with one extra parameter $\\beta$.
\n\n
动机源于持续存在的宇宙学张力问题——特别是 $H_0$ 张力（早期与晚期宇宙对哈勃常数测量的不一致）和 $S_8$ 张力（物质成团幅度的分歧），这些对标准 $\\Lambda$CDM 模型构成挑战。作者探索一种具有未来奇点（Little Rip）的晚期暗能量模型是否能在不引入早期宇宙新物理的前提下缓解这些张力，该模型仅通过引入一个额外参数 $\\beta$ 对 $\\Lambda$CDM 进行最小扩展。

Method: The authors employ a phenomenological Little Rip (LR) dark energy model defined by an equation of state that leads to a future abrupt event but avoids a finite-time singularity. The model introduces a single new parameter $\\beta$ beyond $\\Lambda$CDM. They perform a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis using multiple observational datasets: Planck CMB, BAO, PantheonPlus supernovae, DESI-DR2 BAO, and recent SNIa data. Model comparison is conducted via the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC) and Bayesian evidence (Bayes factors) to assess whether the LR model provides a statistically significant improvement over $\\Lambda$CDM.
\n\n
作者采用一个唯象的 Little Rip（LR）暗能量模型，其状态方程导致未来突变事件但避免有限时间奇点。该模型在 $\\Lambda$CDM 基础上仅引入一个新参数 $\\beta$。他们利用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法，结合多种观测数据集：Planck CMB、BAO、PantheonPlus 超新星、DESI-DR2 BAO 以及近期 SNIa 数据进行分析。通过赤池信息准则（AIC）和贝叶斯证据（Bayes factors）进行模型比较，以评估 LR 模型是否在统计上显著优于 $\\Lambda$CDM。

Result: The analysis reveals a positive correlation between $H_0$ and the LR parameter $\\beta$. When fitting only early-universe data (CMB or CMB+BAO), the Hubble tension is reduced to below $3\\sigma$. However, this alleviation disappears when late-time data (e.g., PantheonPlus) are included. The inclusion of DESI-DR2 data shifts the best-fit parameters toward a quintessence-like regime ($w > -1$). Bayesian model comparison indicates that the LR model is only favored over $\\Lambda$CDM when fitting CMB data alone; for combined datasets, it does not provide a compelling improvement. No significant resolution of the $S_8$ tension is reported.
\n\n
分析结果显示 $H_0$ 与 LR 参数 $\\beta$ 呈正相关。仅拟合早期宇宙数据（CMB 或 CMB+BAO）时，哈勃张力可降至 $3\\sigma$ 以下；但加入晚期数据（如 PantheonPlus）后，这种缓解消失。引入 DESI-DR2 数据后，最佳拟合参数向 quintessence 类区域（$w > -1$）偏移。贝叶斯模型比较表明，LR 模型仅在单独拟合 CMB 数据时优于 $\\Lambda$CDM；对于组合数据集，未显示出显著改进。文中未报告对 $S_8$ 张力的显著缓解。

Conclusion: The Little Rip dark energy model offers limited success in addressing cosmological tensions. While it marginally alleviates the $H_0$ tension with early-universe data alone, this effect is not robust when late-time probes are included. The model does not resolve the $S_8$ tension, and Bayesian evidence supports $\\Lambda$CDM over the LR extension for most combined datasets. The shift toward quintessence suggests the LR framework may effectively interpolate between phantom and quintessence behaviors, but it does not provide a compelling alternative to $\\Lambda$CDM under current data constraints.
\n\n
Little Rip 暗能量模型在解决宇宙学张力方面效果有限。尽管它在仅使用早期宇宙数据时能轻微缓解 $H_0$ 张力，但当包含晚期探针后该效果不再稳健。该模型未能解决 $S_8$ 张力，且贝叶斯证据表明在大多数组合数据集中 $\\Lambda$CDM 仍优于 LR 扩展。向 quintessence 的偏移表明 LR 框架可能有效插值于 phantom 与 quintessence 行为之间，但在当前数据约束下，它并未构成对 $\\Lambda$CDM 的有力替代。

Abstract: We present an analysis that investigates the $H_0$ and $S_8$ tensions by considering a dark energy model. The latter is a late-time model characterized by a future abrupt event known as the Little Rip (LR) model and characterised by one extra parameter, $β$, compared to the standard model, $Λ$CDM. To test this approach, we perform a statistical analysis by the MCMC method using the most recent observational data. We obtain a positive correlation in ($H_0$, $β$) plane. We also note that the Hubble tension is less than $3σ$ when using early measurements, i.e., Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data, and when combining it with Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) data, but it is no longer so when we combine early and late measurements (i.e. PantheonPlus (PP)). In addition, we test the model with DESI-DR2 combined with CMB and recent SNIa measurements. We notice that our model shifts toward the quintessence field. For a complete statistical analysis, we use the Akaike Information Criteria and Bayesian analysis of the evidence. According to Bayes factors, we find that the LR model provides an improved fit only to CMB data.

</details>


### [87] [Symmetry-Protected Momentum Exchange between Dark Matter and Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07879)
*Mohid Farhan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper constructs a theoretically robust interacting dark energy model where dark energy is a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson from a softly broken $U(1)_S$ symmetry, and dark matter is an inert scalar doublet stabilized by a $Z_4$ symmetry. Their interaction occurs solely through derivative couplings (momentum exchange), with no background energy transfer. Despite significant momentum coupling, the resulting suppression of $σ_8$ saturates above the level needed to fully resolve cosmological tensions, revealing an intrinsic limit in such symmetry-protected models.
\n\n
本文构建了一个理论自洽的相互作用暗能量模型：暗能量是源于软破缺全局对称性 $U(1)_S$ 的 pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson，而暗物质是由离散 $Z_4$ 对称性稳定的惰性标量二重态。二者仅通过导数耦合（动量交换）相互作用，背景能流为零。尽管动量交换效应显著，结构增长幅度 $σ_8$ 的压低存在饱和值，无法完全解决当前低红移宇宙学张力，揭示了此类对称性保护模型在结构抑制上的内在极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from persistent cosmological tensions—particularly the $S_8/σ_8$ discrepancy between CMB-inferred and weak lensing measurements—and the theoretical challenge of constructing radiatively stable interacting dark energy models. The authors aim to explore whether symmetry principles can yield viable, natural models of dark sector interactions that avoid fine-tuning while addressing observational anomalies.
\n\n
动机源于持续存在的宇宙学张力——尤其是 CMB 推断与弱引力透镜测量之间的 $S_8/σ_8$ 差异——以及构建辐射稳定（radiatively stable）相互作用暗能量模型的理论挑战。作者旨在探索对称性原理是否能够产生自然且可行的暗区相互作用模型，在避免精细调节的同时解释观测异常。

Method: The authors construct a UV-complete particle physics model where dark energy emerges as a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson from a complex scalar singlet with a softly broken global $U(1)_S$, and dark matter is an inert scalar doublet protected by a discrete $Z_4$ symmetry. Renormalizable portal couplings are forbidden by the requirement of radiative stability for the dark energy field, leaving only derivative (momentum-exchange) interactions. They implement this interaction self-consistently into the Boltzmann code CLASS by modifying the perturbed fluid equations to include momentum transfer while preserving zero background energy exchange, then compute linear observables like the matter power spectrum and $σ_8$.
\n\n
作者构建了一个紫外完备的粒子物理模型：暗能量来自一个带有软破缺全局对称性 $U(1)_S$ 的复标量单态，表现为 pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson；暗物质则是由离散 $Z_4$ 对称性保护的惰性标量二重态。为保证暗能量场的辐射稳定性，可重整化门户耦合被禁止，仅保留导数型（动量交换）相互作用。他们将该相互作用自洽地嵌入 Boltzmann 求解器 CLASS 中，通过修改扰动流体方程以包含动量转移（同时保持背景能流为零），进而计算物质功率谱和 $σ_8$ 等线性观测量。

Result: The model predicts no energy transfer at the background level but modifies the evolution of cosmological perturbations via momentum exchange. Despite allowing large momentum coupling strengths, the suppression of the clustering amplitude $σ_8$ saturates at a level insufficient to fully reconcile the $S_8$ tension between Planck CMB and low-redshift probes. This saturation arises intrinsically from the structure of derivative interactions and the underlying symmetries.
\n\n
该模型在背景层级无能量转移，但通过动量交换修改宇宙学扰动的演化。尽管允许较大的动量耦合强度，结构聚团幅度 $σ_8$ 的压低存在饱和值，不足以完全调和 Planck CMB 与低红移观测之间的 $S_8$ 张力。这种饱和效应本质上源于导数相互作用的形式及底层对称性结构。

Conclusion: Symmetry-protected interacting dark energy models with pure momentum exchange exhibit a fundamental upper bound on their ability to suppress structure formation. This intrinsic limitation provides a theoretically controlled benchmark: while such models are natural and radiatively stable, they cannot fully resolve current low-redshift cosmological tensions, suggesting that more complex dark sector dynamics or alternative mechanisms may be required.
\n\n
纯动量交换的对称性保护相互作用暗能量模型在抑制结构形成方面存在根本上限。这一内在限制提供了一个理论可控的基准：尽管此类模型具有自然性和辐射稳定性，却无法完全解决当前低红移宇宙学张力，暗示可能需要更复杂的暗区动力学或替代机制。

Abstract: We present a particle physics motivated realization of interacting dark energy in which a radiatively stable dark energy sector couples to weakly interacting massive particle dark matter through pure momentum exchange. The dark energy field arises as a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson from a complex scalar singlet charged under a softly broken global $U(1)_S$, while dark matter is identified with an inert scalar doublet stabilized by a discrete $Z_4$ symmetry. This symmetry structure allows renormalizable dark matter-dark energy portal operators; however, requiring the dark energy field to emerge as a radiatively stable pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone Boson necessitates their absence, leaving derivative interactions as the leading coupling. As a result, energy transfer between the dark sectors is absent at the background level, while momentum exchange modifies the evolution of cosmological perturbations. We implement the resulting interacting dark energy model self-consistently in the Boltzmann code CLASS and study its impact on the growth of structure. We find that, despite sizeable momentum exchange, the suppression of the clustering amplitude $σ_8$ saturates above the level required to fully resolve current low-redshift tensions. Our results demonstrate that symmetry-protected, momentum-exchange-only dark sector interactions possess an intrinsic limit on structure suppression, providing a theoretically controlled benchmark for interacting dark energy scenarios.

</details>
